---
name: Kunoza umutekano wawe bwite
goal: Gushiraho ikibanza c’ubuhinga bwa none gitekanye, gishikamye kandi gikora neza.
objectives: 


  - Gutahura ingene ubuhinga bwa none bukora no guhitamwo neza
  - Kuronka ubwigenge bw'ubuhinga muri Linux
  - Gushira mu ngiro uburyo bwiza bwo gucungera umutekano kuri mudasobwa y'umuntu ku giti ciwe
  - Kwongera umutekano wo gusura urubuga no gukoresha telefone ngendanwa biciye ku bikoresho vy'inkomoko yuguruye n'imiterere ibereye
  - Gushira mu ngiro uburinzi bukenewe ku rubuga rwo muhira


---

# Intambwe yo kwegera ubusegaba bwa digitale



Mu isi aho ibikoresho vya digitale biri hose ariko bikaba ari bike cane, kwiga ingene wokingira ibidukikije vyawe bwite vy’ubuhinga bwa none ni ngombwa. Yaba ari mudasobwa yawe, umucukumbuzi wawe, telefone yawe canke urubuga rwo mu nzu, imwe yose muri izo Elements irashobora kuba irembo ry’ubuzima bwite bwawe. Iryo shure rigufasha gusubira kugenzura ibikoresho vyawe vy’ubuhinga bwa none.



Si ukumenya gusa ingendo nziza: ni ugutahura ivyo ukoresha, ingene ubikoresha, n’ico ivyo bisobanura ku mutekano wawe. Iryo shure rya SCU202 ritanga intangamarara yimbitse ku vyerekeye ubuhinga bw’ishimikiro bw’imirongo y’ibikorwa, rikakumenyesha ikoreshwa ry’ibikorwa rya Linux, rikakuyobora mu gushinga ahantu h’akazi hahamye, hakora neza kandi hakomeye.



Mu bice vyose vy’amashure,uzobona ingene wogenzura ubutungane bwa porogarama ushiramwo, gupfuka neza amakuru yawe, gukoresha neza umucukumbuzi wawe na telefone yawe ata makuru menshi ashobora gusohoka, no gukomeza umutekano w’urubuga rwawe rwo muhira.



Iryo shure ryibanda ku bakoresha bo hagati bashaka kuja kure mu kumenya neza ibikoresho vyabo vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Ishingiye ku buryo bukora, bwibanda ku kwigenga n'ubusegaba, kugira ngo umuntu yubake ingeso z'ubuhinga bwa none zitekanye kandi zifise ubumenyi, hakurikijwe ijambo "*Ntukizere, Suzuma*".



+++

# Imenyekanisha


<partId>8b696bba-e6f6-47d9-ba30-fe4b75636b88</partId>



## Incamake y'amashure


<chapterId>7bf90137-7387-462d-884f-fe48e812b739</chapterId>



Murakaze mu nyigisho ya SCU202, ikurikirana ivyigwa vya SCU101, bizokujana kure mu kumenya neza umutekano w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none mu gushimika ku busegaba bw’umuntu ku giti ciwe, ku kurinda ubuzima bwite, no ku gucunga neza amakuru yawe bwite. Aha niho hari incamake y'ivyo uzobona mu gihe cose c'amashure ya SCU202.



### Igice ca 1 - Intangamarara



Ivyigwa bitangura no gusubiramwo muri make ivyiyumviro bivugwa muri SCU101 bizotuma umenya neza ingingo ngenderwako z’ishimikiro zikenewe kugira ngo ushobore kwegera neza ibikurikira.



### Igice ca 2 - Kuva ku gukanda gushika ku nzira: kumenya neza Linux



Iki gice kizana uburyo bwa GNU/Linux, inkingi y’ubusegaba bwa digitale. Uzobona itandukaniro riri hagati ya Linux, Windows na macOS, ubone amateka aryoshe cane ya Linux n’amaporogarama y’ubuntu, kandi utahure igituma Linux akenshi ihuriye n’umutekano n’umwidegemvyo.



Inyuma, uzomenya ingene wohitamwo uburyo bwo gutanga Linux bujanye n’ivyo ukeneye be n’ibidukikije vyo ku biro. Ubwa nyuma, uzotera intambwe zawe za mbere na Ubuntu biciye mu nzira ido n’ido yo gushiramwo no gutunganya.



![Image](assets/fr/064.webp)



### Igice ca 3 - Gukingira mudasobwa yawe


Muri iki gice, uzomenya ingene wokomeza umutekano wa mudasobwa yawe. Tuzokwegera uburyo bwo kurinda neza uburyo ushobora gushikamwo no gutandukanya uko ukoresha. Uzotahura akamaro ko guhindura sisitemu n’amaporogarama kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zishobora gushika.



Uzomenyerezwa kandi kugenzura ubutungane n’ukuri kw’amaporogarama yashizwe kuri interineti kugira ngo wirinde kwanduzwa canke guhungabanywa, hamwe no gukoresha neza ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru yawe bwite n’ivyo ufise. Ubwa nyuma, uzobona igituma n’ingene wosukura amakuru y’amadosiye yawe kugira ngo ukinge ubuzima bwite bwawe kuri Internet.



![Image](assets/fr/235.webp)



### Igice ca 4 - Umucukumbuzi: OS iri muri OS



Muri iki gihe, ama browser y’urubuga ari hose mu buzima bwacu bwa misi yose, kandi akenshi ni yo abanza guterwa n’ibitero vyo kuri internet. Muri iki gice, turasubiramwo amateka y’ibikoresho vyo gukoresha amakuru n’ingene vyateye imbere.



Uzoheza ubone icegeranyo c’ibikoresho vy’uguhindura n’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none, ivyiza n’ibibi vyavyo, hamwe n’ingene wobikora kugira ngo ukingire ubuhinga bwawe bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwawe uko bishoboka kwose.



![Image](assets/fr/098.webp)



### Igice ca 5 - Gusubira kugenzura telefone yawe



Muri iki gihe, amatelefone yacu y’ubuhinga bwa none ni ugushiramwo ubuzima bwacu bwite n’ubw’umwuga, ivyo bikaba bituma bihambaye cane ko tugenzura umutekano wayo. Tuzokwihweza mu buryo burambuye uburyo butandukanye bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa, ivyiza vyabwo n’aho bugarukira, mu gihe tuzobona uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa kugira ngo usubire kuronka ubusegaba bwose ku gikoresho cawe.



Uzoheza wige uburyo bwiza bwo gucungera umutekano wa misi yose, kuva ku guhindura amakuru gushika ku gutandukanya amakuru yawe bwite n’ay’umwuga. Ubwa nyuma, uzobona ibikoresho vyo guhanahana amakuru bitekanye be n’ibindi bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bufunguye kugira ngo ushobore kwongereza ubuzima bwite n’umutekano wa telefone yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/142.webp)



### Igice ca 6 - Gukingira urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere



Igikoresho cawe co muhira ni ikintu gihambaye cane iyo bije ku bijanye n’umutekano. Tuzotangura turabe ingene urubuga rwo mu karere rukora, imbere y’uko tuja ku ntambwe ngirakamaro zijanye no kurucungera neza.



Uzomenya ingene wohitamwo no gutunganya router itekanye, gucapura urubuga rwawe, gukomeza urubuga rwawe rwa Wi-Fi, no gukoresha ibikoresho vyo kugenzura kugira ngo ubone ningoga ibintu vyose bitari vyo.



![Image](assets/fr/193.webp)



### Igice ca 7 - Igice ca nyuma



Kugira ngo uheze ivyigwa, uzoshobora kugerageza ikizame ca nyuma kugira uronke icemeza cawe no kugenzura ko utahura ingingo zaganiriweko.



![Image](assets/fr/274.webp)



Woba witeguriye gufata neza umutekano wawe w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none, gukomeza ubusegaba bwawe bwite no kwizigira ubuzima bwite bwawe bwo kuri internet? Reka tugende!



*N.B.: Niwahura n’amajambo utamenyereye mu gihe c’amashure, usabwe kuraba [urutonde rw’amajambo](https://planb.network/resources/urutonde rw’amajambo) kugira ngo ubone insobanuro



## Ivyiyumviro vy'ingenzi vya SCU101


<chapterId>26cfac35-a3bb-4657-95b3-8508bedfa903</chapterId>



Imbere yo gutangura inyigisho ya SCU202, ndashaka gusubiramwo muri make ivyiyumviro nyamukuru vyavuzwe mu nyigisho iheruka("SCU101") muri iki gice.



Ikindi kandi, nimba ukiri uwutangura gukoresha mudasobwa kandi utarafata SCU101, ndagusavye cane gutangura n’iryo shure rya mbere imbere y’uko uja kuri iri. Ivy’ishimikiro vyavuzwe muri SCU101 ntibizosubirwamwo hano. Sinzosubira rero ku migenzo y’ishimikiro y’umutekano, canke ku gukoresha VPN, abacungera amajambo banga, canke kwemeza ko umuntu ari uwundi. Kandi naho biri ukwo, ivyo vyiyumviro vyose ni ngombwa kumenya neza imbere y’uko tuja ku mikoreshereze iteye imbere, ivyo tuzobivugako mu bigabane bikurikira.



Ivyigwa vya SCU101 vyari ivyigwa vy’intango vyagenewe gushinga urufatiro rukomeye mu bijanye n’isuku ry’ubuhinga bwa none ku batangura n’abakoresha ubuhinga bwa none. Intumbero yayo yari iyo gutuma umutekano wa misi yose, ubuzima bwite n’ubusegaba bwa digitale bitera imbere.



https://planb.network/courses/99c46148-7080-4915-a7e0-9df0e145cd47

### Gushakisha kuri interineti bitekanye



Akenshi gukoresha Internet ni co kintu nyamukuru umuntu yinjiramwo mu bijanye n’iterabwoba ryo kuri Internet. Muri SCU101, twabonye ko ari ngombwa kuguma turi maso cane cane iyo umuntu ariko arakura amakuru. Gukuraho amadosiye gusa avuye mu bibanza vyizewe, kandi uhitemwo porogarama zifunguye, akenshi zikaba zironka inyungu mu gukorera mu mucyo cane no kugenzura abantu.



Ikindi kintu ciza cavuzwe muri iyo nyigisho cari kijanye n’ama cookies, ni ukuvuga utwo dudosiye dutoduto tubikwa kuri orodinateri yawe iyo usuye imbuga ngurukanabumenyi. Ukwiye kwama ubifuta canke ubigabanya kugira ngo ukinge ubuzima bwite bwawe.



Muri rusangi, gukoresha urubuga rwo kuri Internet mu buryo butekanye bisaba ko umuntu yiyubara: wirinde gukanda ku mbuga zitazwi, wirinde gufyonda ku mbuga ziteye amakenga, kandi ukoreshe urubuga rutekanye kandi rujanye n’igihe.



![Image](assets/fr/268.webp)



### Gutahura VPNs no gukingira uruja n'uruza rwawe rwa Internet



SCU101 yarakumenyesheje iciyumviro ca VPN (Reseau privé virtuel). Mu majambo y’ingirakamaro, VPN irapfuka uruja n’uruza rwawe rwa internet mu gukora umugende utekanye hagati y’igikoresho cawe na server iri kure. Ariko rero, VPN zose si zimwe: ushire imbere abatanga ubuhinga buboneka, bwizigirwa bemera kwiyandikisha ata mazina, nka Mullvad, ProtonVPN canke IVPN. Izo VPN zigufasha kugira ubuzima bwite bwiza ataco ukorakoranya amakuru yawe bwite ataco ukeneye.



Ikindi kandi, twari twabonye ko ku nzira za Wi-Fi za bose, iyo nzira y’uguhuza igaragara cane. Ni co gituma gukoresha VPN ari ngombwa. Niba udashobora gukoresha imwe, huza gusa ku mbuga za HTTPS kugira ngo ukinge amakuru yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/269.webp)



### Gukoresha neza mudasobwa yawe



Umutekano kandi bisigura kumenya ubuhinga bwawe bwo gukoresha (OS). Mwarasuzumye OS zitatu nyamukuru: Windows, macOS na Linux, imwe yose ifise ivyiza vyayo vy’umutekano. Kuri Windows cane cane, antivirus iri ku gihe ni nkenerwa kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kumenya no guhagarika porogaramu mbi.



![Image](assets/fr/270.webp)



SCU101 kandi yarakugabishije ko utokwigera ushiramwo ama USB atazwi muri mudasobwa yawe, kuko yoshobora kuba arimwo ibintu bibi bishobora kwanduza sisitemu yawe.



### Gukingira ibitero vyo kuri interineti no gucunga amakuru y'inyuma



Igice nyamukuru c’amahugurwa ya SCU101 cari ugutahura ibitero vyo kuri internet. Virusi ntiziboneka gusa: akenshi zisaba ko ugira ico ukoze ataco wipfuza, nk’ugukuraho dosiye yanduye canke gufungura urubuga rw’ubuhendanyi muri e-mail.



Kimwe mu bitero bikunze kuboneka ni phishing, aho ubutumwa bw'ubuhendanyi bwoherezwa kugira ngo baguremeshe gutangaza amakuru y'agaciro. Igihe uhanganye n’ivyo bitero, nusuzume mu buryo butunganye uwubirungikiye, kandi wirinde gukanda ku mahuza canke gufungura ibintu bifatanye n’ivyo bitero bivuye ku bintu bitazwi canke biteye amakenga.



Ikindi kintu gikomeye gitera ubwoba ni ransomware, ibuza amakuru yawe mu kuyashiramwo amakuru y’ibanga kandi isaba incungu. Kugira ngo ushobore guhangana n’ivyo, ni ngombwa ko uhora ukora backup y’amakuru yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/271.webp)



### Gukingira neza amasandugu yawe y'ubutumwa



SCU101 cane cane yashimikiye akamaro ko gucungera e-mail yawe, irembo ry’izindi konti zawe zose zo kuri Internet. Igikapu c’ubutumwa gishobora guhungabanywa kiratuma abo basuma bashobora gusubiramwo amajambo y’ibanga y’amakonti yawe hafi yose biciye ku buryo busanzwe bwo gusubizaho ubutumwa bwo kuri e-mail.



Rero warabonye akamaro ko guhingura amaderesi y’ubutumwa bwo kuri interineti atekanye kandi yihariye. Ni vyiza kugira e-mail yihariye Address yabikiwe kugira ngo ushobore gusubiza konti yawe, itandukanye n’iya Address yawe nyamukuru.



![Image](assets/fr/272.webp)



### Akamaro k'abacungera ijambobanga



Umutekano wa digitale ushingiye cane ku buryo amajambo y’ibanga yawe ameze. SCU101 yasiguye igituma gukoresha umucungerezi w’ijambobanga ari ngombwa: ivyo bikoresho bigufasha gukora generate no kubika amajambobanga agoranye, yihariye kandi atari yo ku gikorwa cose ukoresha.



Abacungera ijambobanga barakworohereza cane igikorwa, kubera ko ubwirizwa kwibuka ijambobanga rimwe gusa ry’ingenzi ku bandi bose.



![Image](assets/fr/273.webp)



### Ivyemezo bibiri (2FA)



Ubwa nyuma, SCU101 yarakumenyesheje uburyo bwo kwemeza ko umuntu ari uwundi (2FA). Iryo hame rigizwe n’ugukora ivyemezo mu ntambwe zibiri zitandukanye: ijambobanga ryawe risanzwe n’ikindi kintu ca kabiri, nk’itegeko ry’igihe gito ryakozwe n’ikoreshwa nka Google Authenticator canke Authy, canke urufunguzo rw’ibikoresho nka YubiKey.



2FA irinda neza cane amakonti yawe: naho ijambobanga ryawe ryoba ryarashizwe mu kaga, ukuronka amakuru biraguma bidashoboka ata kintu ca kabiri. Menya ko amakode yoherezwa kuri SMS canke kuri e-mail adatekanye cane, kuko ashobora gufatwa canke guhindurwa.



___



Ivyo vyibutsa vy’ishimikiro bizokora nk’ishimikiro ry’inyigisho zacu za SCU202, aho tuzoja cane mu kumenya neza ubuhinga bwo gucungera umutekano wo kuri internet, kugira ngo turinde neza ubusegaba bwawe bwite, ubuzima bwite bwawe n’amakuru yawe bwite muri rusangi.



# Kuva ku gukanda gushika ku nzira: kumenya neza Linux


<partId>e28895b3-2b09-4811-8031-5abc1f14fde2</partId>



## Linux, Windows, macOS: ni ikihe kigubereye?


<chapterId>598cdecb-f90c-4382-b13c-0ba5a9dfeede</chapterId>



Reka dutangure iri shure rya SCU202 n’ivy’ishimikiro: ubuhinga bwo gukoresha mudasobwa yawe (OS). Si vyo gusa bigena uguhitamwo kwawe kw’ibikoresho, ariko kandi n’umutekano wawe, ukworoha gukoresha n’ubushobozi bwo guhindura imashini yawe uko ushaka.



Imbere yo kwinjira mu vy’ubuhinga bwa Linux mu bice bikurikira, birahambaye ko dutahura itandukaniro rikomeye riri hagati y’izo nzira zitatu zisanzwe: Windows, macOS na GNU/Linux. Muri iki kigabane, tuzokwiga umuti umwumwe wose, tumenye aho ukora neza n’aho udakora neza, hanyuma duhitemwo neza ivyo ukeneye.



### Sisitemu yo gukoresha ni iki?



Sisitemu ikoresha ni urutonde rwa porogarama nyamukuru zikora nk’umuhuza hagati y’uwuzikoresha, ibikoresho (na vyo nyene ari porogarama) n’ibikoresho, ni ukuvuga mudasobwa yawe. Ni porogarama y’ishimikiro Layer ishoboza gukoresha ibikoresho vya mudasobwa (processeur, mémoire, disques, périphériques, n’ibindi).



Mu majambo nyayo, iyo sisitemu irakira, igakora hanyuma igasubiza ivyo usaba biva kuri porogarama yawe, ikoresheje neza ibikoresho vya orodinateri uko bishoboka kwose. Igenzura ugushirwa mu ngiro kwa porogarama nyinshi icarimwe, igenzura ibihimba vya PC, igenzura amasano, iremera gucunga amadosiye, kandi igenzura umutekano w’amakuru biciye ku buryo bwo kwemerera no kwemeza ko ari ukuri.



![Image](assets/fr/001.webp)



Iyo ata n’uburyo bwo gukoresha, porogarama imwe imwe yose yobwirizwa kuba ifise uburyo bwayo bwite bwo kuvugana n’ivyo bikoresho, ivyo bikaba bituma gukorana hagati ya porogarama zitandukanye hafi bidashoboka. Uruhara rwayo rero ni ngirakamaro.



Uko ni ko nyene mudasobwa za kera zakora. Uburyo bwa mbere bwo gukoresha, GM-NAA I/O, ntibwabonetse gushika mu 1956. Bwazanye ubuhinga bwo gukora ibintu mu bice, ivyo bikaba vyatuma ibikorwa bigenda neza. Mu myaka ya 1960 harabonetse ubuhinga bwo gukora porogarama nyinshi no gusangira umwanya hakoreshejwe CTSS (1961) na Multics (1969), ivyo vyatumye abakoresha benshi bashobora gukorana icarimwe n’ubuhinga bumwe. Hanyuma mu myaka ya 1970, uguhingura Unix kwahinduye cane ubuhinga bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none kubera uburyo bwo gutwara ibintu, uburyo bwo gukora ibikorwa vyinshi n’uko bworoshe.



![Image](assets/fr/004.webp)



### Uburyo nyamukuru bwo gukoresha n'imigabane yabo kw'isoko



Ubu, isoko ry’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none riganzwa n’imiryango itatu ikomeye: **Windows, MacOS na GNU/Linux**.



Dushingiye ku mibare iriho ubu, Windows iracari ifise igice kinini c’ibikoresho bishirwa kuri mudasobwa z’abantu, ikaba ifise umugabane w’isoko ushika ku bice 71%. Ukwo kuganza ni kubera ihuriro ry’ibintu vy’amateka, ubutunzi n’ubuhinga:





- Kuva mu myaka ya 1990, Windows yarashizweho ku buryo busanzwe kuri mudasobwa nyinshi zigurishwa, ivyo bikaba vyatumye abantu benshi bayimenya. Microsoft yaciye yihuta gushinga amasezerano menshi y’ubuhinga bwa none (amasezerano abahinguzi ba PC bashiramwo Windows imbere y’igihe), gutyo bituma habaho ukudakora bigoye guhagarika.





- Naho iyo ngendo iriko iratera imbere buhoro buhoro, Windows yarishizeho nk’ikigereranyo mw’isi y’abahinga kuva kera cane. Uretse imice yihariye nk’ubuhinga, hafi ubucuruzi bwose buracari kuri mudasobwa zikoresha Windows.





- Igitigiri kinini c’abakoresha cararemesheje abahinguzi gushira imbere guhingura porogarama zabo za Windows, kugira ngo zishike ku bantu benshi. Mu gusubiza, ikidengeri gikura c’ibidukikije vy’ibikorwa gikwegera abakoresha bashasha, kigatuma haba uruziga rw’ingeso nziza.





- Ubwa nyuma, ubwo butegetsi burakomezwa kandi n’ishusho ibonwa y’imirongo ihanganye: Linux akenshi ibonwa ko ari ubuhinga bwinshi cane ku bantu bose (kandi iguma itamenyekana na benshi), mu gihe macOS, ifatanye gusa n’ibikoresho vya Apple, akenshi ibonwa ko izimvye.



macOS, muri ico gihe, ifise umugabane w’isoko ugera kuri 16%, kandi muri rusangi itoranywa kubera ko ikora neza n’ibikoresho vya Apple. Ihitamwo ry’iyi nzira y’ugukoresha ryakomejwe mu myaka iheze n’ubushobozi bwa Macs, bivuye ku gushiramwo ama chips ya Apple Silicon. Iryo hinduka rikomeye ryatumye habaho uguheba amaprocesseur ya Intel x86 bagakoresha ubuhinga bwa ARM, bukora neza cane mu bijanye n’ubushobozi n’inguvu zikoreshwa.



Linux iguma ari ntoyi kuri mudasobwa z’abantu (hafi 4%), ariko iganza ku ma server (hafi 63%) no ku ma supercomputer (100%), kubera ukudahungabana kwayo n’ubushobozi bwayo.



![Image](assets/fr/002.webp)



*Isoko Ndamukiza 2025: [Imibare y'Isi Yose - Umugabane w'Isoko rya OS](https://gs.



Linux nayo irashizwemwo cane mu bikoresho vy’imbere nk’ama router, ama televiziyo ahuye, amatelefone ngendanwa (Android ishingiye ku ntungamubiri ya Linux) mbere no mu bijanye n’imiduga. Windows iguma ifise ubushobozi bukomeye mu bucuruzi, mu gihe macOS ikunda cane abahinga mu bikorwa bimwebimwe.




→ **Igihambaye:** Kernel ni co gice nyamukuru c’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha: icungera ukuntu umuntu ashobora gushika ku bikoresho (processeur, memory, peripherals), igaca imanza mu gukora ibikorwa icarimwe, igashitsa amategeko y’umutekano kandi itanga Interface imwe kuri porogarama zipfuka uburemere bw’imirongo y’ubuhinga bwa none. Mu yandi majambo, ikora nk’ikiraro hagati y’ibidukikije vya porogarama (amasomero, abashoferi, ibikoko, ibikorwa, ibikoresho vy’uburongozi, Interface y’ibishushanyo, n’ibindi) n’ibikoresho.



### Windows: yoroshe gukoresha kandi irahuye



Windows ni ubuhinga bwo gukoresha bwakozwe na Microsoft. Ishirwa kuri mudasobwa nyinshi z’abantu ku giti cabo kw’isi. Mu mateka, vyarashimishijwe kubera ko vyoroshe gukoresha kandi bikaba vyumvikana Interface. Ariko rero, iyo ntumbero irateye amakenga ubu: Interface ya macOS na yo nyene irashikira cane, kandi ama distribution menshi ya Linux arafise Interface ibereye abantu bose (ivyo tuzobisubirako mu bice bikurikira).



Ku bakoresha batazi canke abafise ivyo bakeneye bike (ibikorwa vyo mu biro, ubuhinga bwinshi, gusura urubuga), Windows ishobora kuba ahantu horoshe kwinjira, wungukira ku nyandiko nyinshi n’ukwiga vyihuta. Ariko mu vy’ukuri, ikintu kimwe gusa Windows ishobora gusumba macOS na Linux ni imikino ya videwo.



![Image](assets/fr/005.webp)



Kimwe mu bintu nyamukuru bikomeye kuri Windows ni ubutunzi bw’ibidukikije vyayo: hafi porogarama zose z’ubudandaji (amasuite y’ibiro, porogarama z’umwuga, imikino ya videwo n’abashoferi b’ibikoresho) zihuye na Windows. Ku bakoresha barondera umuti witeguye gukoreshwa ufise imiterere mikeyi, ivyo bishobora kuba uguhitamwo guhuye n’ubwenge.



Ariko rero, ukwo gushikira abantu biraza n’igiciro. Windows ni ubuhinga bw’umuntu ku giti ciwe, bushingiye ahantu hamwe, ata kode y’inkomoko ya bose. Nta kugenzura kwigenga gushoboka, ivyo bikaba bigaragaza imipaka igaragara mu bijanye n’uguseruka n’umutekano. Ikindi kandi, gukusanya amakuru (telemetry) birakwiragiye cane muri Windows kandi akenshi bikoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe, ata kwemera nyakuri canke ubushobozi bwo kuyagenzura.



Ku bijanye n’umutekano, Windows ni co kintu nyamukuru gikoreshwa na malware. Kuba izwi cane be n’utunenge tumwetumwe tw’imiterere yayo mu vya kahise birasigura igice c’ivyo bintu. Nta gukeka ko hariho utwigoro twakozwe mu myaka iheze (cane cane na Windows Defender na UAC), ariko muri rusangi iguma yateguwe cane kugira ngo yorohe gukoreshwa kuruta gukomera no kugenzura abayikoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/007.webp)



Mu vyiyumviro vyanje, Windows ifise ikibanza nyamukuru kitavugwa: irashobora kuba itekanye, ariko ikaba ari ntoyi kuruta Linux na macOS; iremeza ko umuntu ashobora kugenzura, ariko ni bike cane kuruta Linux; ntabwo ari ububasha nk’ubwa macOS, canke ngo bube bworoshe nka Chrome OS canke ubuhinga bumwe bumwe bwa Linux bushobora gukoreshwa n’abatangura. Ni average mu mice yose, ataco ari kibi vy’ukuri mu bijanye n’ivyo (kiretse ubuzima bwite, ku buryo busanzwe).



![Image](assets/fr/006.webp)



Ku bijanye n’ubusegaba bwa digitale n’ubuhinga, Windows iraca yerekana ningoga aho igarukira. Icogereranyo caco gishingiye ku bucuti butagira uburinganire hagati y’uwukoresha n’uwusohora, ku nyungu y’uwo wa nyuma. Ku bashaka cane gutahura, guhindura no gukingira mudasobwa yabo, si ubuhinga bwiza cane. Ni co gituma tutazoguma tuvuga cane kuri Windows muri SCU202.



### macOS: ubufatanye n'ugutuma bigenda neza



macOS ni uburyo bwo gukoresha bwakozwe na Apple ku mudasobwa zayo za Mac.Ni uburyo burazwe kuri Unix, biciye ku buryo bwa NeXTSTEP, bwaronswe na Apple mu 1997.



![Image](assets/fr/008.webp)



Uwo mushinge ukomeye utanga ugushikama kwiza, gucunga neza ubutunzi n’ubwubatsi butekanye cane. Ivyongeweko n’igishushanyo ca Interface giteye igomwe cane, cakozwe kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gukoresha neza.



![Image](assets/fr/003.webp)



Kimwe mu bintu bikomeye bikomeye vya macOS ni ugushiramwo mu buryo buhagaze ibikoresho n’ibikoresho. Apple ni yo igenzura uruhererekane rwose, kuva ku mibumbe y’ivyo bikoresho gushika ku bintu bitobito vya Interface. Ico bivamwo ni uburyo bwo kwizigirwa muri rusangi, bufise ibibazo bikeyi kandi butunganijwe neza kugira ngo bukore neza.



Ariko rero, iyo nzira yo gukorana irafise akaga ko gukomeza gukingirwa mu bidukikije vya Apple. macOS ni ubuhinga bufise igice c’ubuhinga (bufise ahanini kode y’inkomoko yugarijwe) bukoreshwa gusa ku bikoresho vyakozwe na Apple. Abakoresha ntibashobora gucungera ivyo bahinduye, amahitamwo y’imiterere ya sisitemu canke amahitamwo y’ibihimba vy’ibikoresho. Ivyuma biragoye guhindura canke gusanura, kandi akenshi birakingirwa na porogarama.



![Image](assets/fr/009.webp)



Ku bijanye n’ubuzima bwite, naho macOS idatera cane nk’iya Windows, iguma iboshe ku nzira y’ubwenge yo gukusanya amakuru, gukorana n’ibicu no kwizigira ibikorwa bihurikiye hamwe. Ivyinshi mu bikorwa vy’ubuhinga biteye imbere vy’iyi sisitemu bishingiye ku guhuza ubudasiba n’ibidukikije vya Apple (iCloud, App Store, Siri...), ivyo bikaba bigabanya ubwigenge bw’uwukoresha.



macOS ishobora gushimisha abakoresha baha agaciro ubushobozi, ugushikama n’ugutekanirwa kw’urutonde rwinjijwe neza, ataco bakeneye kwisuka mu bintu vy’ubuhinga. Ku rundi ruhande, ku bijanye n’ubusegaba bwa digitale no kugenzura ibidukikije vyawe vy’ubuhinga bwa none, birafunze cane, bishingiye cane ku sosiyete imwe, kandi ntibibereye guhindura neza ibintu. Ni co gituma tutazobivugako cane muri iri shure rya SCU202.



### GNU/Linux: umwidegemvyo, ubugenzuzi n'umutekano



GNU/Linux itandukanye cane n’izindi zibiri zabanje kubera uburyo bwayo bwo gukoresha ubuntu kandi bufunguye. Udakunze Windows canke macOS, Linux ntiyitegurwa n’ishirahamwe rimwe, ahubwo ihingurwa n’abahinguzi bo kw’isi yose. Uwo murongo w’abanyagihugu utanga icemezo c’uguseruka, umutekano n’uguhinduranya. Linux itanga ububasha bwose ku bakoresha bayo, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora guhindura neza aho akora. Ivyo biraryoshe cane cane ku bakoresha bateye imbere, abahinguzi canke abashaka kumenya neza ibidukikije vyabo vy’ubuhinga bwa none.



Ivyiza vya Linux ni ugukomera kwayo, ugushikama kwayo n’umutekano wayo wo hejuru. Kubera ko ari open source, kode yayo irashobora gusuzumwa n’uwuyikoresha canke ishirahamwe ryose, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane ingorane zo gukoresha porogarama mbi canke backdoors. Linux irakomeye cane, muri rusangi ikoresha ibikoresho bike kuruta Windows, kandi irabereye cane cane mu gukoresha ibikoresho bitari vyinshi canke gukoresha cane nk’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none, uburongozi bwa server canke umutekano wo kuri internet.



![Image](assets/fr/010.webp)



Ariko rero, Linux nayo iratanga ibintu bimwe bimwe bigoranye ku batangura. Umubare munini w'ibikoresho vya Linux bishobora gutera urujijo ku bakoresha batamenye. Na vyo nyene, ugukoresha neza iyo sisitemu mu ntango, naho vyorohejwe n’ugusangira bimwebimwe, vyoshobora gusaba ko umuntu yiga imbere y’igihe kugira ngo ayimenye neza, canecane iyo umuntu yihweje ukuntu akoresha ubudasiba umurongo w’iherezo (umurongo w’amabwirizwa). Kandi ivyo nivyo gusa iki gice ca mbere c’amashure ya SCU202 kivuga!



### Ni ubuhe buryo bwo gukoresha ukwiye guhitamwo?



Amahitamwo yawe azovana ahanini n'ivyo ukeneye n'ivyo witega:




- Niba uriko urarondera uburyo bworoshe, uburyo bwinshi bwo gukoresha ibikoresho n’ubuhinga (na cane cane ku mikino y’amasanamu), hamwe n’ugukoresha ibintu rusangi, Windows yoshobora kuba ari uburyo bwiza. Ariko rero, urakeneye kumenya aho igarukira mu bijanye n’ingene ikora, umutekano n’ubuzima bwite;
- Niba uriko urarondera ubufatanye bwiza hagati y’ibikoresho vyawe na sisitemu yawe, Interface itunganijwe kandi ikoreshwa neza n’umutekano mwiza cane ata nkenerwa y’imiterere iteye imbere, kandi ukaba usanzwe ufise canke wipfuza kwemera sisitemu y’ibidukikije ya Apple, macOS ni ikintu gisanzwe;
- Ubwanyuma, nimba uriko urarondera umutekano, ugushikama n'ubushobozi hejuru ya vyose kandi ushaka no kugenzura cane ibidukikije vyawe vya digitale, mu gihe witeguye gutanga umwanya mu kwiga uko ukoresha sisitemu yawe, Linux ni uburyo bwiza cane, cane cane mu gihe ubwigenge bw'ubuhinga n'ubusegaba bwa digitale ari vyo bibanza.



Mu bice bikurikira vy’iki gice ku bijanye n’imirongo y’ibikorwa, nzoba ndiko ndagutwara cane muri Linux, kubera ko ishobora gutuma ushobora kugenzura cane ibidukikije vyawe vy’ubuhinga bwa none.



## Inkomoko ya GNU/Linux


<chapterId>9dbf749d-daae-493b-ab96-93a322df011d</chapterId>



Imbere yo kuraba ivyerekeye GNU/Linux n’ikibanza iyo sisitemu ifise mu buhinga bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none, birahambaye ko umuntu akurikirana inkomoko yayo kugira ngo atahure ico igereranya. Muri iki gice, turasubira kuraba imizi ya GNU/Linux mu mateka, mu vy’ubuhinga no mu vy’ubuhinga, biciye mu iragi rya Unix, Genesis y’umugambi wa GNU, iremwa ry’umubiri wa Linux n’uguseruka kw’umuhari w’ubuhinga bwa none.



### Iragi rya Unix



Ivuka rya Linux ntirishobora gutahurwa tutavuze umuvyeyi wayo ataco akora: Unix. Unix yashinzwe mu mpera z’imyaka ya 1960 no mu ntango z’imyaka ya 1970 na Ken Thompson, Dennis Ritchie na bagenzi babo bo muri AT&T Bell Labs, Unix yatumye habaho ihinduka rikomeye mu mateka y’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha. Mu ntango yateguwe muri *Assembler*, hanyuma isubirwamwo muri *C* na Dennis Ritchie mu 1973, Unix yashizeho umushinge w’umurongo mushasha wa OS ushingiye ku guhinduranya n’ukworohereza.



![Image](assets/fr/011.webp)



Ubwo buryo buraboneka mu ngingo ngenderwako y’ishimikiro yashizwe ahabona na Doug McIlroy:



> Kora ikintu kimwe kandi ugikore neza.

Unix ishobora kubonwa nk'iterambere rya, n'inyishu ku, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha Multics, ubuhinga bwabwo bufata. Multics yari umugambi watangujwe mu 1964, ivyamwa vy’ubufatanye hagati ya MIT, General Electric na AT&T Bell Laboratories. Ken Thompson na Dennis Ritchie (abaremye UNIX) bagumye bacungera cane umugambi wa Multics gushika mu 1969, igihe ishirahamwe ryabo ryava mu gutegura.



Muri ico gihe niho Unix yaseruka, mu ntango yitwa "*UNICS*" bisobanura "*Ibikorwa vy'amakuru n'ubuhinga bw'ibarabara*", bihushanye cane n'"*Ibikorwa vy'amakuru n'ubuhinga bw'ibarabara*", ni ryo jambo ry'inyongera ry'ikirundi risobanura Multics. Ubu buryo bushasha burashigikira ukworoha, uguhinduranya n’ugukora neza, bitandukanye n’ugusobanuka birenze urugero kwa Multics.



Kuva mu myaka ya 1970, Unix yarateye imbere mu bijanye n’ubushakashatsi, imbere y’uko ikwiragizwa cane muri kaminuza kuva mu 1975, atari kubera amategeko agenga ivy’ubudandaji yashizwe kuri AT&T. Ivyo vyatumye yemerwa mu ma laboratwari menshi, nka Berkeley, aho ishami rya BSD (*Itanga porogarama za Berkeley*) ryavukiye. Muri ico gihe nyene, AT&T yatanguye kumenyekanisha Unix mu myaka ya 1980, bituma habaho ukwiyongera kw’amaverisiyo y’ubuhinga adahuye (System V, Xenix, SunOS, AIX, Solaris, HP-UX, n’ibindi).



![Image](assets/fr/012.webp)



*Isoko: Amateka ya Unix-yoroshe, na Eraserhead1, Infinity0 na Sav_vas, ishusho yava ku kigereranyo c'amateka ya Unix cakozwe na Éric Lévenez, [Ivyabona vya Yehova]



Uguca ibice hagati y’ayo mashami (BSD ku ruhande rw’inyigisho, na System V cane cane ku ruhande rw’inganda) kwatumye habaho urujijo rwinshi kandi n’ugukorana kw’imirongo bigabanywa. Kugira ngo barondere igikoresho gikomeye, gishobora gutwara, kitagira amafaranga, umuryango waratanguje ibikorwa vyinshi, harimwo umugambi wa GNU mu 1983, hanyuma hakurikiraho ugutegura umurongo wa Linux mu 1991, ivyo bikaba vyari vyuzuye ikinogo cari gisigaye kubera ukubura umurongo w’ubuntu mu bidukikije vya GNU. Ivyo ni vyo vyari intango y’ubuhinga bwa GNU/Linux.



### Umugambi wa GNU



Umugambi wa GNU (ijambo ry'inyongera risobanura "*GNU's Not Unix*") watangajwe ku mugaragaro na Richard Stallman kw'igenekerezo rya 27 Nzero 1983, mu matsinda yihariye y'amakuru. Iciyo gihe, Stallman yari agikora mu kigo ca MIT kijejwe ivy’ubwenge bukora. Ku wa 5 Nzero 1984, yarahevye igikorwa ciwe ku bushake kugira ngo abone ko iyo kode yariko arandika idashobora gusabwa n’umukoresha wiwe. Yaciye atangura gutegura GNU, afise intumbero yo guhingura uburyo bwo gukoresha ku buntu, ni ukuvuga uburyo bwubahiriza umwidegemvyo une w’ishimikiro: gukora ku buntu, kwiga ku buntu, guhindura ku buntu no gusubira gutanga ku buntu.



![Image](assets/fr/013.webp)



Uretse imice yayo y’ubuhinga, umugambi wa GNU uri mu gice c’ubuhinga bwa filozofiya bwarazwe n’umuco w’abanyaruyeri wo mu myaka ya 1970: umuco ushingiye ku gusangira ubumenyi, gukorana n’urunganwe no kuronka ku buntu kode y’inkomoko. Richard Stallman yaripfuje kuzigama impwemu yo gukorana n’abandi yari ihambaye mu misi ya mbere y’ubuhinga bwa none, igihe abahinguzi bari bakitanga mu mwidegemvyo kode y’inkomoko y’ibikoresho vyabo. Umugambi wa GNU ntugamije gusa gutanga uburyo bwo gukoresha ku buntu, ariko ni ukugwanira iciyumviro ca politike n’inyifato runtu c’ubuhinga bwa none: ubumenyi bushikira bose, ata n’umwe afise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha canke gufunga. Intumbero ni ukubuza abakoresha kuba imbohe z’amaporogarama badashobora gutahura canke guhindura, no guteza imbere ubuhinga bwo kwidegemvya.



Ivyo ari vyo Stallman yashinze *Free Software Foundation* (FSF) mu mwaka w’1985, ishirahamwe ryihaye guhimiriza no guteza imbere gukoresha no kurema porogarama z’ubuntu.



![Image](assets/fr/014.webp)



GNU yihuta gutanga urutonde rw'ibikoresho vy'ingenzi kuri sisitemu yayo:




- GCC (umukozi wa C)
- glibc (ububiko bwa C busanzwe)
- coreutils (amabwirizwa y'ishimikiro)
- Emacs (umuryango w'umuhinduzi w'inyandiko)
- bash (umusemuzi w'umurongo w'itegeko)
- GDB (Debugger)



![Image](assets/fr/018.webp)



Amatafari amwe amwe yo hanze na yo nyene arashizwemwo, nka X Window System, moteri y’uguhingura TeX na microkernel ya Mach, ikoreshwa n’umugwi wa server ya GNU Hurd (hamwe, Mach na Hurd zirangura uruhara rumwe n’urw’umurongo wa Unix wa kera, ariko mu nyubakwa ya microkernel + server). Uwo mugambi wo gusubirira kernel wari uhambaye cane ariko wari ugoye cane. Ntizokwigera ikora neza, isige umwanya ku kernel ya Linux.



![Image](assets/fr/019.webp)



Ivyinshi muri GNU vyateguwe n’abakozi b’intahemuka, bamwe mu bihe vyabo vy’uburuhukiro, abandi baterwa inkunga n’amashirahamwe, amashure makuru canke amashirahamwe. Mu mpera z’imyaka ya 1980, FSF yaratanguye gukoresha abahinga mu bijanye n’iterambere kugira ngo igikorwa cihute. Amashirahamwe amwe amwe, nka Cygnus Solutions (mu nyuma yaje kuba igice ca Red Hat), yaragize uruhara runini mu kubungabunga no kumenyekanisha porogarama za GNU zidafise amahera.



Igihe Linus Torvalds yasohora kernel yiwe ya Linux mu 1991, yari ihuye neza n’ibidukikije vyari vyaramaze kuremwa na GNU, kandi yerekanye ko ari ngirakamaro cane kuruta kernel ya Mach + Hurd. Ihuriro rya GNU na Linux ryatumye bishoboka ku ncuro ya mbere kugira ubuhinga bwo gukoresha bushitse, bufise ubuntu kandi bukora neza: **GNU/Linux**, ni ukuvuga ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’umugambi watangujwe na Stallman hafi imyaka cumi imbere y’aho.



### Ivuka rya kernel ya Linux



Inkuru y’umurongo wa Linux itangura mu mwaka w’1991, na Linus Torvalds, uwo gihe yari umunyeshure w’ubuhinga bwa mudasobwa muri kaminuza ya Helsinki muri Finilande. Kubera ko Torvalds atashimishijwe n’imipaka ya Minix, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha Unix busanzwe bwakozwe na Andrew S. Tanenbaum ku bw’intumbero z’inyigisho, yaciye atangura gukora kernel yiwe bwite yo gukoresha mudasobwa yiwe bwite, afise intumbero gusa yo kwiga mu gukora. Ku wa 25 Myandagaro 1991, yaratangaje ku mugaragaro umugambi wiwe ku rubuga rwa Usenet, avuga yifata ruto ko ukiri umugambi w’intango kandi ko ari uwugerageza. Mu ntango z'umwaka w'1992, verisiyo 0.12 y'uwo mugambi yarasohotse hakoreshejwe uruhusha rwa GNU GPL ku buntu.



![Image](assets/fr/016.webp)



Iyi kernel, mu ntango yitwa Freax, hanyuma ihindurwa izina Linux (ugucapura kwa "Linus" na "Unix"), ntiyatevye gukwegera abandi bahinga b'abanyamwete. Umuryango mpuzamakungu waravyuka ubwawo kugira ngo ushireho umusanzu ku bijanye n’inkomoko y’ibintu bishobora gushikirizwa ku buntu. Udakunze GNU, Linux mu ntango ni kernel gusa: igice ca porogarama gijejwe gucunga ibikoresho vy’imashini. Ifatanijwe n’ibikoresho n’ibikorwa vyamaze gutegurwa n’umugambi wa GNU, iyo kernel iraheza igatanga ubuhinga bwo gukoresha ku buntu kandi bukora neza. Iryo huriro ryitwa "GNU/Linux" kugira ngo rishimike ku gukorana hagati y'iyo migambi ibiri. Mu rurimi rusangi, ariko, iyi sisitemu ikoreshwa muri rusangi yitwa gusa "Linux".



![Image](assets/fr/017.webp)



→ ***Tux***: ikimenyetso n’ikimenyetso c’umurongo wa Linux, cakozwe mu 1996 na Larry Ewing akoresheje porogarama ya GIMP.



### Inkomoko yuguruye n'ubuhinga bwa porogaramu y'ubuntu



Uko Linux yagenda irakundwa cane mu myaka ya 1990, haradutse impaka z'ingengabitekerezo ku majambo "porogarama y'ubuntu" na "inkomoko yuguruye", atari kubera insobanuro zibiri z'ijambo "*ubuntu*".



Naho Richard Stallman na FSF bashigikira cane iciyumviro c’ubuhinga bwa porogarama y’ubuntu ishingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako z’inyifato runtu ("*ubuntu nk’uko biri mu mwidegemvyo*"), abandi bakinyi bashigikira uburyo bushingiye ku vy’ukuri, bushingiye ku buhinga bwibanda ku guseruka no ku buhinga bw’ubuhinga bw’akarorero kafunguye. Mu mwaka w'1998, harashizweho umugambi w'ubuhinga bufunguye (OSI), ushizeho ijambo "open source" kugira ngo ryishimire cane urwego rw'amashirahamwe, rishimika ku nyungu z'ubutunzi n'ubuhinga aho gushimika ku vyiyumviro vy'ingengabitekerezo.



Richard Stallman aranegura ku mugaragaro ikoreshwa ry'ijambo "inkomoko yuguruye", abona ko ritagira aho ribogamiye cane, mbere ko ritagiramwo politike. Ashimika ku jambo "porogarama y'ubuntu" kugira ashimike ku vy'uko ikibazo nyamukuru atari ic'ubuhinga, ahubwo ari ic'imibano: ic'umwidegemvyo w'abakoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/015.webp)



*Isoko: Nataniyeli Welch



Itandukaniro hagati y'ayo majambo abiri rero riri mu ntumbero nyamukuru: umuhari w'amaporogarama y'ubuntu utera imbere mbere na mbere filozofiya y'umwidegemvyo w'umuntu ku giti ciwe n'uw'abantu bose ku bijanye n'amaporogarama, mu gihe inkomoko yuguruye ahanini iha agaciro ubuhinga bwiza, uguseruka n'ugukorana nk'uburyo bwo kuronka igicuruzwa ciza.



Naho zitandukanye mu vy’ubuhinga, izo nzira zibiri zisangiye agaciro nk’uguseruka, gusuzuma kode y’inkomoko, ubwigenge bw’abaguzi, n’ubushobozi bw’abakoresha ba nyuma bwo gutahura, guhindura no kunoza ibikoresho vyabo vya porogarama. Na n'ubu, izo ntandukaniro zituma habaho impaka n'uguzirikana mu miryango y'abahinga, cane cane Bitcoin.



### Ingaruka ku muco no ku mibano



GNU na Linux si inkuru y’uguterimbere gusa mu vy’ubuhinga: ingaruka zavyo ku mico kama no ku mibano ni ngirakamaro nk’uko nyene. Ukwiragira kwabo kwa mbere kwari ahanini biciye kuri Internet, biciye mu mahuriro y’ubuhinga n’urutonde rw’abarungika ubutumwa, hanyuma vyihuta biciye mu gukwiragiza, ni ukuvuga amakoraniro y’amaporogarama yari yaratunganijwe imbere y’igihe akikuje umurongo wa Linux. Kera mu mwaka w’1993, hariho ubuhinga bwo gutanga amakuru nka Slackware na Debian kugira ngo ubuhinga bwa GNU/Linux bushobore gushikirwa n’abantu benshi.



Ubu buryo bushingiye ku kibano, bufunguye kandi bukorana buratuma Linux itera imbere ningoga, mu buryo bwegerejwe kandi bugira uruhara. Uwukoresha wese arashobora gutanga umusanzu mu mugambi, haba mu gushiramwo amakode, mu gukora inyandiko canke mu kugerageza. Ivyo bikorwa vyinshi vy’ugukorana bigereranya ubuhinga bushasha bwo mu kibano mw’isi y’ubuhinga bwa none.



Nk’uko twabibonye mu kigabane ca mbere, iragi rya Linux uno musi rirarenga kure cane mudasobwa z’abantu: iraganza isoko ry’amaserver ya Internet, itanga ububasha ku mudasobwa zikomeye cane, ni yo ishingirako ubuhinga bwa Android buha ububasha amamiliyaridi y’amatelefone y’ubuhinga bwa none kw’isi yose, kandi mbere iri mu mutima w’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none vy’ubuhinga bwa none, ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none vy’ubuhinga bwa none (ro).



GNU/Linux ni ikintu kirenze cane ubuhinga bwo gukoresha gusa: ni filozofiya, ubuhinga, umuco n’imibano bishingiye ku gufungura, gukorana n’umwidegemvyo w’ubuhinga bwa none. Ivyo vyiza birabandanya guhindura cane uburyo dufata inda, dukoresha no gusangira ubuhinga bwa none muri iki gihe.



Mu gihe c'iyi ragi ry'ubuhinga, ubu birashoboka gusuzuma mu majambo nyayo ingene izo ngingo ngenderwako zishirwa mu ngiro mu bijanye n'ubuhinga bwa mudasobwa y'abantu bwite. Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, turaza gutohoza ahantu hanini h’ugukwirakwiza Linux (canke GNU/Linux), kugira ngo dutahure uko vyateye imbere n’ingene bikoreshwa, no kugira ngo tugufashe guhitamwo iyo ihuye neza n’ivyo ukeneye.



## Incamake y'ugukwiragiza Linux


<chapterId>868f44d7-69ce-4493-b65e-daff00f3eb54</chapterId>



Igiharuro ca Linux (kenshi kivugwa mu ncamake "*distro*") ni uburyo bwo gukoresha bushitse bushingiye ku ntumbero ya Linux (kandi kenshi bufise Elements ya GNU), bushizwemwo porogarama zihuye, amasomero, inyandiko zo gutangura n'ibikoresho vyo gucunga, kugira ngo haboneke ikibanza giteguwe gukoreshwa. Ugukwiragiza Linux rero ntikugarukira ku ntumbero gusa, ahubwo guserukira ugushiramwo ibintu vyose bikenewe kugira ngo mudasobwa ikoreshe kandi ikoreshe (canke ikindi gikoresho cose co gukoresha mudasobwa).



Buri Linux itangazwa irimwo :




- **Linux kernel**, ivugana n'ibikoresho kandi igacungera ibikoresho vya sisitemu (CPU, ububiko, amadisike, n'ibindi)
- **umukoresho wo gufungura**, nka *GRUB*, kugira ngo ufungure sisitemu
- **uburyo bwo gutangura** bushobora gutuma ibikorwa bitangura ku gihe co gutangura: *uburyo*, *OpenRC*, *SysV init*, canke *runit* bivanye n'amahitamwo y'ubuhinga bwo gukwiragiza
- a **uburyo bwo gucunga amapaki**, bushobora kugufasha gushiramwo, guhindura no gukuraho porogaramu. Ivyo bimenyerewe cane ni *APT* (Debian, Ubuntu), *RPM/DNF* (Fedora, RHEL), *Pacman* (Arch), *Zypper* (openSUSE) canke *APK* (Alpine)
- kuri interineti **ububiko bwa porogaramu**, bushira hamwe verisiyo zemejwe z'ibikorwa biriho
- **umugwi w'ibikoresho vya sisitemu** (igikoko, abahinduzi, abakoranya, imirongo y'urubuga, n'ibindi) kandi kenshi ibidukikije vy'ibiro vyatunganijwe mbere (*GNOME*, *KDE Plasma*, *XFCE*, n'ibindi)
- inyandiko z'imiterere, inyandiko na, mu bihe bimwe bimwe, ibikorwa vyo gufasha



![Image](assets/fr/050.webp)



Ico gikorwa co gukoranya ni co kijanye n’ugukwirakwiza kwose, guhitamwo ibice vyaco bishingiye ku filozofiya yavyo (ukworoha, ukworoha, umutekano, ugushikama, ubuhinga bushasha, n’ibindi), abantu bigenewe (abatangura, abacuruzi, abakozi, ibibanza vy’akazi, imashini zishizwemwo, etc.) n’ingendo yavyo yo gutegura (ro* lease re* cle or). Nk’akarorero, Arch Linux yibanda ku kworosha imiterere n’uguseruka kw’ubuhinga, mu gihe Ubuntu yibanda ku bumenyi bw’abakoresha n’uguhuza n’ibindi (ariko ivyo tuzobigarukako mu gice ca nyuma c’iki gice).



→ **Iciyumviro:** Gukwirakwiza *rolling release* bishiramwo ama verisiyo ya porogarama nshasha igihe nyene ashobora kuboneka, bikaba bituma habaho uburyo buhora bujanye n’igihe ariko bushobora kuba butaguma bushikamye. Ku rundi ruhande, ugukwirakwiza *gushikamye* kwohereza amaverisiyo ya porogarama iyo verisiyo nini isohotse, bikaba vyemeza ko hariho ukwizigirwa kwinshi kubera ubushasha.



Kuba hariho ibice vy’ugukwiragiza bituma abakoresha bashobora kwungukira kuri sisitemu ya Linux yiteguye gukoreshwa, ataco bakeneye gusubira kwubaka n’amaboko igice cose ca porogarama. Ivyo bigereranya inyungu nini cane mu bijanye n’igihe, ugushikama n’umutekano. Kandi, ku bijanye n’ubwubatsi, ugukwiragiza bikoresha ubuhinga bw’ibikoresho Layer butangwa n’umurongo wa Linux. Iyi Layer ituma ubuhinga bwo gukoresha bushobora gukorana n’ibikoresho vyinshi bitandukanye, ata nkenerwa yo guhindura porogarama zijanye n’igice kimwekimwe cose. Ukwo guhinduranya canke gusubirira ibihimba vya sisitemu kandi bituma vyoroha guhindura canke gusubirira ibihimba vya sisitemu ataco bimaze gusubira kwubaka sisitemu yose.



Gutahura itandukaniro riri hagati y’ibice vya Linux rero ni intambwe ihambaye mu guhitamwo ikibereye ivyo ukeneye, ubuhinga bwawe n’ivyo usabwa. Ivyo ni vyo tuzoba turiko turaraba muri iki kigabane.



### Inkomoko ya kahise k'ugukwiragiza Linux



Ivyo bikoresho vya mbere vya Linux vyabonetse inyuma y’aho Linus Torvalds asohoye kernel ya Linux muri Nzero 1991. Ico gihe, Linux yari kernel gusa: kugira ngo umuntu aronke ubuhinga bushitse, abakoresha bategerezwa gukoranya n’amaboko ibice bitandukanye bisabwa (kenshi bikurwa mu mugambi wa GNU), ivyo bikaba vyasaba urugero rwo hejuru rw’ubuhinga bwa technical. Gushiramwo system bisigura gukoranya kernel wewe nyene, gutunganya imigabane, guhitamwo ibikoresho, gucunga dependencies za software... Muri make, igikorwa gikomeye, kigenewe abatanguje.



Kugira ngo Linux ishobore gukoreshwa cane, imigambi myinshi iriko iraseruka vuba, n’iciyumviro co gukoranya ubuhinga bwiteguye gukoreshwa buva ku ntumbero ya Linux n’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bihuye.



Ivyo bikorwa vya mbere ni vyo vyatumye Linux ivuka:





- Gashyantare 1992: Linux y'agateganyo ya MCC**



Yateguwe muri kaminuza ya Manchester, MCC Interim Linux ifatwa nk’iya mbere cane itanga Linux. Intumbero yayo ni iyo kworohereza gushiramwo system kuri PC isanzwe. Iza mu buryo bw’ama disquette makeyi kandi irimwo ibikoresho bikeyi vyo gutuma Linux ikora ningoga.





- Gicurasi 1992: Sisitemu ya Linux (SLS)**



Igikoresho ca SLS ni co ca mbere gitanga ugushiraho ibintu vyose bifise ubuhinga bwo gukoresha idirisha (X Window), igikoko, igikoresho co gukoranya n’ibindi bikoresho vyatunganijwe imbere y’igihe. Intumbero yayo ni ugutanga ubuhinga bumeze nka Unix bushobora gukoreshwa na bose.



![Image](assets/fr/049.webp)



Mu misi yayo ya mbere, SLS yari iteye imbere cane, ariko abayikoresha ntibatevye gutangaza amajambo y’ugunegura ukudashikama kwayo be n’ingingo zimwe zimwe zo kuyibungabunga. Ivyo vyatumye abahinguzi benshi batangura imigambi isa n’iyo, haba mu gutuma SLS itera imbere canke mu kuyisubirira. Gutyo niho hatanguye igiti kinini c’ugusangira Linux n’ugucapura kwavyo mu miryango.



SLS ntaco ikiriho. Verisiyo yayo ya nyuma izwi ni iyo mu mpera za 1994.





- Nyakanga 1993: Ivyuma**



Patrick Volkerding yatanguje Slackware mu buryo bumwe bumwe mu mpanuka, akosora no kunoza ibibazo muri SLS nk’igice c’umugambi w’ishure muri kaminuza ya leta ya Minnesota. Biciye mu guhindura vyinshi no gutuma ibintu bigenda neza, verisiyo yiwe yahinduwe ya SLS yaje kuba umurongo wa Linux wigenga vy’ukuri, ushobora gushimisha abantu bose bavunitse umutima kubera imipaka ya SLS. Amaze kwemererwa na kaminuza yiwe, yarasohoye igitabu ca mbere yasohoye mw’izina rya Slackware kw’igenekerezo rya 17 Nyakanga 1993.



![Image](assets/fr/048.webp)



Slackware niho yaciye ihinduka Linux ikoreshwa cane mu myaka ya 1990. Ubwubatsi bwayo bworoshe, inyandiko z’ibihimba vy’umubiri, kwubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako za Unix n’ukubura ibintu bitaboneka vyatumye iba ikigereranyo ku bakoresha bateye imbere barondera uburyo buke kandi bubonerana.



Slackware iracariho n’ubu, bikaba ari yo nzira ya kera cane ya Linux iguma ikoreshwa. Ni n’inkomoko y’ibice vyinshi biva ku bindi, bikora umuryango munini wa mbere w’ibice vya Linux: Slackware.





- Kanama 1993: Debiyani**



Muri ico gihe nyene, Ian Murdock yatanguje ugukwiragiza Debian, mu mpwemu itandukanye cane n’imigenzo y’ico gihe, cane cane iyo ikoreshwa n’ugukwiragiza nka SLS, akenshi itunganywa n’umuntu umwe. Murdock yasanze Debian ari umugambi w'abanyagihugu, uteguwe mu buryo bufunguye, mu mpwemu y'ubuhinga bwa none n'umugambi wa GNU. Udakunze izindi nzira nyinshi za Linux, Debian ni nzira idakoreshwa mu bucuruzi.



![Image](assets/fr/047.webp)



*Ian Murdoki. Inkomoko: [Ilya Schurov CC BY-SA 2.0] (amafoto/ivoyager/2398462112/).*



Ku bijanye n’ubuhinga, Debian yaritandukanije kuva mu ntango n’uburyo bwo gupakira, uburyo bwo gukurikirana ivyagezwe, kandi ikiruta vyose n’ugushiraho umucungerezi w’ibipapuro akora cane, *dpkg*, yuzuzwa ningoga na *APT* automated softwares of manageable mu 1998, bishobora gutuma habaho ubuhinga bwo gucungera amapaki mu 1998.



![Image](assets/fr/046.webp)



*Debiyani 1.3 (1997). Inkomoko: Ububiko bw'Ikwirakwiza Linux*



Mu ntango, uwo mugambi warashize mu ngiro ivyemezo vyawo vy’inyifato runtu mu gusohora *Debian Social Contract* n’Ingingo ngenderwako z’Ikoreshwa rya Porogarama z’Ubuntu za Debian (DFSG), kugira ngo hashingwe itegeko ritomoye ryerekeye umwidegemvyo w’amakode n’uguseruka. Yatewe inkunga n'ishirahamwe ry'amaporogarama y'ubuntu, Debian yaciye yigenga mu gushinga ishirahamwe ritagira inyungu ry'amaporogarama mu nyungu za bose (SPI) mu 1997.



Debian rero yabaye imwe mu nkingi z’ubuhinga n’ingengabitekerezo z’isi ya GNU/Linux, umushinge wavukiyemwo amajana y’ibikoresho bikomeye, harimwo Ubuntu, Linux Mint, Kali Linux na Raspberry Pi OS.





- 1994: Inkofero itukura Linux**



Marc Ewing yasohoye verisiyo ya mbere ya Red Hat Linux mu 1994. Ivyo vyatumye havuka ugukwiragiza kwogira uruhara runini mu gutuma Linux igira ubuhinga. Ewing yashimishijwe n'isi yose ya Unix, yararemye verisiyo ya Linux itunganijwe, ishobora gukoreshwa, ashiramwo igikoresho gihambaye: *Red Hat Package Manager* (RPM), cahuje uburyo bw'amapaki y'amaporogarama kandi kikayorohereza gushiramwo, kuvugurura no gukuraho, cane cane mu bidukikije vy'umwuga. Uwo murongo wobaye urugero rwemewe cane.



Mu mwaka w’1995, Bob Young, uwashinze ishirahamwe ryitwa AAC Corporation ryitaho cane ibikoresho vya porogarama za Linux, yaraguze ishirahamwe rya Marc Ewing. Ivyo bigo bibiri bihuriye hamwe vyatumye havuka Red Hat Software. Bompi hamwe, barateguye uburyo bwo gukora ubucuruzi bw’intango: ugukwiragiza porogarama zifunguye zifatanijwe n’ugufasha no gutanga icemezo ku bucuruzi. Uwo murongo w’ubudandaji wacitse ikigereranyo, kandi ushobora kuwusanga mu migambi myinshi iri mu bidukikije vya Bitcoin.



![Image](assets/fr/045.webp)



*Bob Abakiri bato na Mariko Ewing. Umufotozi: Candice C Cusic/AP*



Mu mwaka w’2003, Red Hat yaracitse ingamba: ishami ry’abanyagihugu ryacitse Fedora, laboratwari y’ubuhinga bushasha ifise urugendo rw’iterambere ryihuta, mu gihe ishami ry’ubudandaji ryahinduwe Red Hat Enterprise Linux (RHEL), ryemewe, rishikamye, ry’igihe kirekire ry’ugukwiragiza ryagenewe ibikorwa remezo vy’ubudandaji mu mwaka w’2000. Kuva ico gihe, Fedora yarakoreshejwe nk’ikibanza co kugeragezako ubuhinga buzoheza bushizwemwo cane muri RHEL. Iryo shirahamwe, Red Hat yarashoboye guhuza ubuhinga bwo gukorana n’abanyagihugu n’ubuhinga bwo gukorana n’inganda.



Ivyo bimenyetso vy’ubutsimvyi vyashinze imiryango ikomeye ya Linux y’ubu, imwe yose muri yo ikaba yarateguye uburyo bwayo bwite bw’ubuhinga n’ubuhinga bwa filozofiya.



### Uyu musi imiryango ikomeye yo gukwiragiza Linux



#### Umuryango wa Debian



Uyu muryango wubakiwe hirya no hino y'umucungerezi w'amapaki ya APT n'uburyo bw'amapaki ya `.deb`. Debian igaragara kubera uburyo bwayo bukomeye bwo gukoresha porogaramu z'ubuntu n'uburyo bukomeye bwo gucunga ubufasha.



![Image](assets/fr/044.webp)



Ubuntu, ikomoka kuri Debian, imenyekanisha Linux biciye mu buryo bworoshe bwo gushiramwo no gukoresha. Ubuntu ifise uburyo bwinshi buzwi, nka Kubuntu (ibidukikije vya KDE) na Xubuntu (XFCE). Ibindi bikoresho bihambaye bishingiye kuri Debian ni Linux Mint (navyo biva kuri Ubuntu), Kali Linux (umutekano wa mudasobwa), na Raspberry Pi OS ku mudasobwa ntoya za Raspberry Pi.



Uyu muryango ni wo tuzokwibandako cane mu nyuma, kuko uzana hamwe bimwe mu bikoresho vya Linux bihuye kandi bikundwa cane kugira ngo bikoreshwe kuri mudasobwa z’abantu ku giti cabo.



#### Umuryango w'inkofero itukura



Ishingiye ku buryo bwa RPM (*Red Hat Package Manager*), uwo muryango rero urimwo Fedora, ubuhinga bushasha bwo gukwiragiza abantu bukora nk’ishimikiro ry’ubuhinga rya Red Hat Enterprise Linux (RHEL), ubuhinga bwo gukwiragiza bw’ubudandaji bugenewe amashirahamwe kandi buzwi cane kubera ugushikama kwabwo kw’igihe kirekire.



![Image](assets/fr/043.webp)



Ivyimburwa vyinshi bikomeye biva ata guca ku ruhande kuri RHEL, bifise intumbero yo gutanga ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha ku buntu kandi buhuye, ata n’amahera y’infashanyo y’ubudandaji. Muri izo, CentOS yaramaze igihe kirekire ifise ikibanza gihambaye nk’igishushanyo c’abanyagihugu ca RHEL, gushika Red Hat ihinduye kamere yayo mu 2020 ikaba CentOS Stream, igishushanyo co hagati ya Fedora na RHEL. Iryo cemezo ryatumye habaho ama forks mashasha nka AlmaLinux na Rocky Linux.



Ibindi bikoresho bihambaye biva muri uwo muryango ni Oracle Linux, ifise ivyiza vyihariye ku bidukikije vyo mu gicu, na ClearOS, ikoreshwa ry’ubuhinga bwa SMB rifise server y’urufunguzo n’ibikoresho vy’uruhome rw’umuriro.



#### Umuryango wa Arch Linux



Umuryango wa Arch Linux utandukanye n’ubuhinga bunyuranye cane n’ubw’ugukwiragiza ibintu bitari ku ruhande. Ni ivy'agaciro gatoyi, kandi vyakozwe hakurikijwe ingingo ngenderwako y'"*KISS*" ("*Bigumye Vyoroheje, Bibe Ivy'Ikijuju*"). Arch Linux itanga uburyo bw’ishimikiro, butagiramwo ibintu vyinshi, uwubukoresha ategerezwa kwubaka n’amaboko bivanye n’ivyo akeneye.



![Image](assets/fr/041.webp)



Ubu buryo bushingiye ku *rolling release* model, aho amapaki aguma avugururwa, ataco akeneye gusubira gushiramwo sisitemu igihe cose hasohotse ikintu gikomeye. Umucungerezi w’amapaki ya Pacman arihuta kandi ntaremereye, bituma vyoroha gushiramwo no guhindura porogarama, kandi AUR (*Arch User Repository*), ububiko bw’abanyagihugu, buratanga uburyo bwo gukoresha amapaki menshi cane atari yemewe n’ay’iterambere.


Arch Linux igenewe cane cane abakoresha bateye imbere bashaka gucungera ibidukikije vyabo vyose, mu gihe bemera ibintu bimwe bimwe bigoranye mu gushiramwo no gucungera. Ico gisabwa mu buryo bw’ubuhinga catumye habaho ugusangira ibintu vyinshi biva ku bindi bigamije gutuma ikoreshwa ryayo rigira demokarasi.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/arch-linux-7a3dc8a8-629b-4971-bb0d-4eab94f93973

Izwi cane ni Manjaro, igumya ishingiro ry’ubuhinga rya Arch mu gihe itanga gushiramwo vyoroshe, ibidukikije vy’ibiro vyatunganijwe mbere n’ingendo y’ugusohora itevye gatoyi kugira ngo ivyagezwe bibe bimeze neza.



![Image](assets/fr/042.webp)



#### Umuryango wa Slackware



Slackware iguma ari intahemuka ku ngingo ngenderwako za Unix za kera, ishimikiye cane ku kworoha, uguseruka n’ugushikama. Udakunze ubuhinga bwa none bukoresha ubuhinga bwo gucunga porogarama, Slackware yizigira ubuhinga bwa `.tgz` butagira umuti w’ivy’ubuhinga, bisaba ubumenyi bwiza bw’ibidukikije vyayo n’ibice vyayo.



Ubu buryo buke, bufatanijwe n’ugushikama kwinshi, butuma Slackware iba ugukwiragiza gukundwa n’abakoresha bazi utuntu n’utundi canke abahinga mu vy’ubuhinga bwa Unix, cane cane mu bihe aho ubushobozi bwo kumenya imbere y’igihe no kugenzura ari ngirakamaro (amaserver, ubuhinga bushizwemwo, ibidukikije bihambaye cane, n’ibindi).



![Image](assets/fr/040.webp)



Slackware yavyaye uburyo bwinshi bwo gukwiragiza, bumwe muri bwo bushaka guhindura ikoreshwa ryayo mu gihe bugumya impwemu yayo: Salix, Porteus, Slackel...



Naho umuryango uri muto kuruta Debian canke Red Hat, umuryango wa Slackware uguma ari ikigereranyo c’amateka n’ubuhinga mu gisata ca GNU/Linux.



#### Umuryango wa Gentoo



Ishami ry’umugambi wa Enoch Linux waremwe mu 1999, Gentoo yaremwe na Daniel Robbins n’intumbero yo guhingura uburyo bwo gukwiragiza bushobora guhindurwa cane, ata binaries zari zateguwe mbere, kandi bubereye ibikoresho vy’ukoresha. Ihinduwe izina ryitwa Gentoo (inyuma y’igikoko citwa penguin ca Papouasie, kimwe mu bikoko vyihuta cane), ugukwiragiza gushingiye ku gukoranya amapaki kuva ku ntango, bikaba bishoboza gukora neza cane bivuye ku gukoresha *Portage*, uburyo bwo gucunga amapaki bwahumekewe n’ivyambu vya BSD. Gentoo igenewe abakoresha bazi utuntu n’utundi barondera ubushobozi, ubugenzuzi n’uburemere, kugiciro c’igihe kirekire co gushiramwo no gusanasana.



![Image](assets/fr/038.webp)



Hariho ibintu vyinshi biva kuri vyo vyaremewe kugira ngo bikoreshwe neza: Funtoo, Linux y’umutuku (Sabayon), Linux yo kubara, Pentoo, n’ibindi.



Ubwa nyuma, ChromeOS, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha bwateguwe na Google ku bikoresho vyayo vya Chromebook, bwakomotse mu ntango kuri Gentoo, naho kuva ico gihe bwaciye buvako cane.



![Image](assets/fr/039.webp)



Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku miryango y’ugukwiragiza Linux no kwiyumvira amashami ya buri imwe, ndagusavye kuraba iki kigereranyo ciza cane kandi gitomoye cane kuri Wikimedia: [*Igihe c’ugukwiragiza Linux*](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1b/Linux).



### Ni uwuhe murongo wa Linux wohitamwo?



Guhitamwo ukwiragira kwa Linux bivana n’ivyo ukeneye, urugero rwawe rw’ubuhinga n’ivyo ushaka gukoresha. Aha niho hari amahitamwo y’ibikoresho bikoreshwa cane canke vyihariye, n’ivyiza n’ibibi vyavyo nyamukuru.



#### Gukwirakwiza muri rusangi no gushikira





- Ubuntu**:



Yateguwe na Canonical itanguzwa mu 2004, Ubuntu ni imwe mu nzira zizwi cane kw'isi. Ishingiye kuri Debian, itanga urugendo rwo gusohora rudasanzwe, n’amaverisiyo ya LTS (*Long Term Support*) agumaho imyaka itanu. Ubuntu iratandukanye n’ibindi bikoresho vyiza cane, umuryango munini n’inyandiko nyinshi, bikaba bituma iba ihitamwo ryiza cane ku batangura. Nkako, tuzokoresha Ubuntu mu gihe cose c'amahugurwa ya SCU202, kuko ari inzira ikomeye yo kwinjira mw'isi ya GNU/Linux. Ubuntu ishiramwo ibidukikije vy'ibiro vya GNOME ku buryo busanzwe, n'ibintu bikeyi bihinduwe.



![Image](assets/fr/020.webp)



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/ubuntu-78a3be56-5d51-4ec3-8629-0dd27c352ab5



- Linux **:



Yatangujwe mu mwaka w’2006, Linux Mint ni ugukwiragiza gukomoka kuri Ubuntu, kwagenewe gutanga ubundi buryo busanzwe, bwegereye ubuhinga bwa Windows. Itanga ibidukikije vyinshi vy'ibiro, harimwo Cinnamon, Fork ya GNOME yakozwe cane cane n'umugwi wa Mint, itanga Interface igaragara, ya kera kandi imenyerewe.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/linux-mint-da44852e-513f-4004-949a-8fde60c1bca5

Mint igaragara kubera ukworoha kwayo, ukubaho kwayo kw’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwinshi n’igikoresho co guhindura neza. Ku rundi ruhande, yizigira cane ibikorwa remezo vya Ubuntu, bikaba bituma yizigira amahitamwo y'ubuhinga ya Ubuntu (cane cane ku rugero rwa kernel n'ububiko). Mint irabereye cane cane abakoresha batari abahinga, canke abashaka ubuhinga bwiteguye gukoreshwa butasaba kwiga cane.



![Image](assets/fr/021.webp)





- Zorini OS**:



Zorin OS yaremwe mu mwaka w’2008 n’umugwi w’abanya Irlande, ikaba yibanda cane ku bakoresha Windows na macOS barondera guhindukira neza bakaja kuri Linux. Ishingiye kuri Ubuntu LTS kandi itanga Interface ishobora kwigana Windows canke macOS bivanye n’ivyo ukunda.



Gushiramwo biragenda neza, porogarama z'ingenzi zirashirwaho mbere, kandi verisiyo ya "Lite" iratuma ukoresha iyo sisitemu ku mashini za kera. Hariho integuro zimwe zimwe, nka "Pro", zitari ku buntu (hafi €50), ariko verisiyo y'ubuntu iracariko irakora neza. Zorin OS ni ihitamwo ryiza ku barondera ahantu hamenyerewe, hahuriweko neza ata n’imwe ikoreshwa n’amaboko.



![Image](assets/fr/022.webp)





- OS y'intango**:


Yatangujwe mu 2011, OS y'intango ni ugukwiragiza gushingiye kuri Ubuntu kwibanda cane cane ku mibumbe n'uguhuza kwa Interface. Ibidukikije vyayo vy’ibiro vya Pantheon, vyahumekewe na macOS, ni bike, biraryoshe kandi biragenda neza. Ariko rero, iyo sisitemu iguma idashobora guhindurwa nk’iyindi mirongo, kandi abakoresha bamwebamwe bateye imbere boshobora kwumva ko bafise aho bageze kubera amahitamwo ya Interface be n’imiterere yayo y’ugufunga n’ibigirankana. Ni vyiza ku bakoresha bakunda ivy’ubwiza barondera uburyo bworoshe kandi buhuye bwo gukoresha ku musi ku musi.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/elementary-os-757a20be-22b5-484c-a032-2bdd909860ac


![Image](assets/fr/023.webp)





- Pop!OS**:



Pop!OS yakozwe n’ishirahamwe ry’Abanyamerika ryitwa System76, na yo nyene ishingiye kuri Ubuntu. Igenewe abakoresha mudasobwa n’abayikora, ifise Interface GNOME yahinduwe (kandi ubu hakaba hariho ibidukikije vyo mu nzu vyitwa COSMIC). Pop!OS ishiramwo ivyiza vy'ama GPU ya NVIDIA ku buryo busanzwe, kandi ifise uburyo bwo gucunga idirisha ry'ibara ry'agahama. Ubuhinga buraguma bworoshe gukoresha, ariko kandi buratanga ibikorwa vy’ubuhinga biteye imbere bitari mu gasandugu. Igenewe abakoresha bo hagati, abanyeshure canke abahinga bashaka ubuhinga bukora neza batabwirizwa gutunganya ibidukikije vyabo n’amaboko.



![Image](assets/fr/024.webp)



*Isoko: [Na Allman - Igikorwa kiwe bwite, CC BY-SA 4.0]



#### Ugukwiragiza hagati n'ubushobozi bwinshi





- Fedora** (Ikibanza c'akazi canke KDE:



Fedora ni urubuga rushigikiwe n’inkofero itukura, rushingiye ku buhinga bushasha (Wayland, PipeWire, Flatpak...). Ikoresha uburyo bwa RPM n'umucungerezi w'amapaki `dnf`. Igihe gisohoka vuba cane, bisigura ko sisitemu yawe yama iri ku rugero rwo hejuru, ariko uzokenera kuguma ubona ibintu bishasha. Ni ugukwiragiza kwiza ku bategura canke abakoresha ubuhinga barondera uburyo bugezweho.



![Image](assets/fr/025.webp)


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/fedora-8c17b6ca-5acb-4825-a069-4474375534b0


- openSUSE** (Igikoko canke Isimbuka):



openSUSE iboneka nk'ugusohoka guhinduka canke gukwirakwiza guhamye. Irafise igikoresho ca YaST co gutunganya sisitemu, kandi ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bwinshi n'ibidukikije vyinshi vy'ibishushanyo. Bisaba ubumenyi bukeyi, ariko biguma bikomeye kugira ngo bikoreshwe ku musi ku musi.



![Image](assets/fr/026.webp)





- Debiyani**:



Debian iriho mu mashami menshi, harimwo *Stable* (yizewe cane, ariko ni porogaramu ya kera) na *Testing* (iyigezweho cane, ariko ntaco igaragaza). Ikoresha `apt` kandi izwi kubera uburindutsi bwayo, filozofiya y’ubuntu n’uguhuza cane. Debian ni ihitamwo ryiza ku bakoresha barondera ugushikama, abarongozi ba sisitemu...



![Image](assets/fr/027.webp)


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/debian-d09a57ec-8372-40ca-bcff-499415209e1f


- Imanjaro**:



Ishingiye kuri Arch, Manjaro ituma Arch Linux ishobora gukoreshwa. Iyi distribution itanga ugushiraho ibishushanyo, ibikoresho vyo mu nzu n’ugufasha neza kw’ibikoresho. Ivyahinduwe birasubirwamwo kugira ngo bibe vyiza cane. Manjaro irabereye abakoresha bo hagati barondera ubuhinga bwa none bwa Arch Linux, ataco bakeneye gutunganya vyose n’amaboko.



![Image](assets/fr/028.webp)





- Linux**:



Arch Linux ni ubuhinga bukeyi, bushobora gukomeza guhindurwa, bushikirizwa ata Interface canke porogarama zidakenewe. Bisaba gushiramwo n’amaboko, ariko itanga ubugenzuzi bwose n’inyandiko nziza cane (Arch Wiki). Ukwo gukwiragiza ni ngirakamaro ku bakoresha bateye imbere bashaka kumenya neza vyose.



![Image](assets/fr/029.webp)



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/arch-linux-7a3dc8a8-629b-4971-bb0d-4eab94f93973

#### Gukwiragiza bidasanzwe



- Kali Linux**:


Kali Linux ni urubuga rushingiye kuri Debian rwagenewe kugerageza kwinjira no kugenzura umutekano. Harimwo amajana y’ibikoresho vya pentest. Ukwo gutanga ntikubereye vy’ukuri nk’uburyo nyamukuru bwo gukoresha ku musi ku musi.



![Image](assets/fr/030.webp)





- Inkukuma OS**:



Parrot OS nayo ikomoka kuri Debian. Itanga ikibanza co gukora pentesting, umutekano w’ibitero n’ukurinda ubuzima bwite. Ishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bwinshi kuruta Kali, iyo distribution irabereye kandi gukoreshwa mu buryo busanzwe ku musi ku musi, ifise ibikoresho vy’umutekano vyinjijwe imbere y’igihe.



![Image](assets/fr/031.webp)





- Imirizo**:



Tails ni Debian, ishingiye ku buzima bwite bwibanda ku gukwiragiza ubuzima. Ivyo vyose bica mu rubuga rwa Tor, kandi nta kintu na kimwe kibikwa hagati y’ibihe vy’abakoresha. Ni ugukwiragiza kwiza ku gukoresha rimwe gusa (itangazamakuru, ubukangurambaga, uruvyaro rwa seed Bitcoin...).



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/tails-15108901-f15d-4f7f-a001-b02b1dcd60c8

→ **Iciyumviro:** Ugukwiragiza ubuzima ni ubuhinga bwo gukoresha Linux bushobora gukoreshwa ataco buvuze kuri USB canke kuri CD, ataco bushize kuri disiki ya Hard.



![Image](assets/fr/032.webp)





- Ibibazo OS**:



Qubes OS ishingiye kuri Fedora kandi ikoresha ubuhinga bwa Xen kugira ngo ikoreshe mu bice. Porogarama yose ikoreshwa mu mashini y’ivy’impwemu iri ukwayo. Ni ubwubatsi butekanye cane, ariko busaba amafaranga menshi kandi buragoye kubufata.



![Image](assets/fr/033.webp)





- Umugozi w'umwirabura**:



BlackArch ni umurongo w'ivy'ubuhinga bwa none (nka Kali kuri Debian). Itanga ibikoresho vy’umutekano birenga 2800. Ni ugukwiragiza kwuzuye cane, ariko kwabikiwe abakoresha bateye imbere bamaze kumenya isi ya Arch, kandi bakeneye ivyo bikoresho vyihariye (abashakashatsi b’umutekano, aba pentesters...).



![Image](assets/fr/034.webp)





- PureOS**:



PureOS ni ugukwiragiza gukomoka kuri Debian kwateguwe na Purism, ku buntu rwose (kwemezwa na FSF). Ishimikiye cane ku buzima bwite, ifise porogarama z’ubuntu gusa kandi ata n’imwe iriho.



![Image](assets/fr/035.webp)




https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/pureos-2b6d5fe8-62f8-4a62-b898-4e0530ed408a


- Igikoresho ca Pi OS**:


Raspberry Pi OS (yahora yitwa Raspbian) ni ugukwiragiza kwatunganijwe neza ku mudasobwa ntoya za Raspberry Pi. Ishingiye kuri Debian, n'amapaki yasubiwemwo ku bw'ubwubatsi bwa ARM. Ishobora gukoreshwa mu migambi y’inyigisho, mu bipimo vy’ubuhinga bwa none canke mu bikoresho bitobito vy’umuntu ku giti ciwe.



![Image](assets/fr/036.webp)





- Ni nde**:



Whonix ifatanya Debian n'urubuga rwa Tor mu nyubakwa y'ama VM abiri (irembo + ikibanza co gukoreramwo). Ni ugukwiragiza gushingiye ku mutekano, ariko bivana n’uguhindura ibintu mu buryo bw’impwemu. Ni vyiza ku bakeneye vy’ukuri kwiherera.



![Image](assets/fr/037.webp)



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/whonix-06f9172c-2962-412e-9487-b665d8ca9f59

Iyi panorama iraguha icegeranyo c'ibidukikije vy'ugukwirakwiza Linux, bikagufasha guhitamwo ugukwirakwiza guhuye neza n'ubuhinga bwawe n'intumbero zawe.


Mu gice gikurikira ca SCU202, tuzokwihweza neza ibidukikije vya Linux bikora, dutangure n’ibidukikije vy’ibishushanyo bigize ishimikiro ry’imigenderanire yawe ya misi yose n’uburyo.


## Ibidukikije vya Linux


<chapterId>ecfac353-a31b-48fb-b2af-2abbeeac5f2b</chapterId>


Mu sisitemu ya GNU/Linux, ibidukikije vyo ku biro birafise uruhara ruhambaye cane mu bumenyi bwawe bwo gukoresha. Ni igishushanyo Layer gishoboza gukorana na sisitemu, bishingiye ku bimenyetso vy’amashusho bimenyerewe: amadirisho, menyu, ibishushanyo, ibipande n’ibikoresho vyashizweho imbere y’igihe.


Muri iki gice, nzoba ndiko ndatohoza imiterere n’uruhara rw’ibidukikije vy’ibiro, ibice vyavyo bisanzwe, imiryango nyamukuru iriho, ibigenderwako vyo guhitamwo n’ukuntu bishirwa mu bikoresho vya Linux bikundwa cane.


### Ibiro ni ibiki?


Ibidukikije vyo ku biro (canke "*DE*" ku *Ibidukikije vyo ku biro*) vyerekeye umugwi wa porogarama zigize igishushanyo cuzuye Interface c'umurongo w'ibikorwa. Kuri Windows na macOS, ikibanza kimwe co gukoresha mu biro kiratangwa ku buryo busanzwe, kikaba kiri muri sisitemu, ata bushobozi bwo kugihindura cose (hariho gusa ibipande bimwebimwe vyo guhindura igice ca Interface). Ku rundi ruhande, ubuhinga bwa Linux burafise ibice vyinshi cane, bufata ibidukikije vyo ku biro nk’igice cigenga gishobora gusubirizwa mu mwidegemvyo.


Mu Linux, birahambaye gutandukanya neza ibice vyose: kernel (igenzura imigenderanire n'ibikoresho), server y'iyerekanwa (ikora nk'umuhuza hagati y'ibikorwa, abashoferi b'ibishushanyo, n'ibikoresho biciye ku kernel), n'ubwa nyuma ibidukikije vy'ibiro ubwavyo, bishingiye kuri cohever- ku wukoresha. Iryo tandukaniro rishobora rimwe na rimwe kutagaragara neza, kuko ama distribution menshi ya Linux azana n’ibidukikije vy’ibiro vyashizweho mbere rimwe na rimwe bikaba birimwo umuhinguzi wayo bwite wa Wayland, uwo na we agaca akora nk’umukozi w’iyerekanwa.



![Image](assets/fr/052.webp)



### Ibice bisanzwe vy'ibidukikije vy'ibiro



Ibidukikije vyo ku biro mu gukwiragiza Linux si igikorwa kimwe, ariko ni urutonde rw’ibice vya porogarama bihuye bitanga igishushanyo cuzuye Interface co gukorana na sisitemu ikoresha. Ivyo bihimba bishingiye ku bice vyinshi vya porogarama, bifise imiterere gutya:





- Umuyobozi w'idirisha**: ashushanya imipaka y'idirisha, agacungera uko ashirwa, guhindura ingano, n'ingaruka z'ihinduka... Nk'akarorero: Mutter (GNOME), KWin (KDE Plasma), Xfwm (Xfce).





- Umucungerezi wa dosiye**: aragufasha guca mu giti c'ububiko, gukopa, kwimura, canke gukuraho dosiye mu buryo buboneka. Ingero: Igikoko c'amazi (GNOME), Igikoko c'amazi (KDE), Igikoko c'amazi (Xfce).





- Ikigo c'imiterere**: iki ni urutonde rw'ibikoresho bishoboza umukoresha guhindura amaparametere ya sisitemu ataciye ku murongo w'amabwirizwa: ukuntu asa, urupapuro rwo ku ruhome, uburongozi bw'umukoresha, urubuga, ibikoresho vyo ku ruhande...





- Sisitemu applets**: ibi ni ibishushanyo bitobito n'ibice bikorana mu mwanya w'ibikorwa (canke "uruzitiro"), nk'ugucungera ijwi, urugero rwa bateri, guhuza urubuga, isaha...





- Igipande canke urupapuro rw’ibarabara**: umurongo uboneka, kenshi hejuru canke hasi y’ibarabara, urimwo urutonde nyamukuru, amaporogarama ya sisitemu, inzira ngufi, ahantu h’imenyekanisha, n’ibindi.





- Umuyobozi w'ikiringo**: akora igihe atanguye, yerekana igicapo co kwinjira maze agatanguza ikiringo c'ibishushanyo catowe. Akarorero: GDM (GNOME), SDDM (KDE), UmucoDM (Xfce).





- Umuyobozi w'amatangazo**: acungera kwerekana amatangazo ya sisitemu (ubutumwa, imburi, ivyagezwe, n'ibindi). Nk’akarorero: dunst, Plasma-imenyesha, xfce4-imenyesha.





- X11 composer (ntibikenewe)**: yongerako ibishushanyo (ibitutu, uguseruka, ibishushanyo) mu bidukikije aho umuyobozi w'idirisha adashigikira gukora. Nk’akarorero: kompton, pikom.





- Server y'iyerekanwa**: iyi ni porogaramu ikora ivy'uguhanahana amakuru hagati ya sisitemu (biciye kuri kernel n'abashoferi b'ibishushanyo) n'ibikorwa vy'ibishushanyo. Igaragaza amadirisho ku rubuga kandi igacungera ivyo winjiza kuri klavye n’imbeba. Serveri yerekana kenshi ni igice gitandukanye c'ibidukikije vy'ibiro, ariko uburyo bwinshi buriko burakoresha Wayland, uburyo bugezweho aho uruhara rwa server yerekana rushobora gufatwa n'umuyobozi w'idirisha (nk'akarorero Mutter munsi ya GNOME canke KWin munsi ya KDE). Ivyo rero vyitwa "Gukoranya Wayland".



Ivyo vyose Elements bishingiye ku bikoresho vy’ibishushanyo, ni ukuvuga, ububiko bw’ibitabu bwa porogarama butanga ibice vy’ishimikiro vyo guhingura ibishushanyo: amabuto, menus, ivyicaro vy’inyandiko... Ivyo bikoresho bibiri nyamukuru vya Linux ni:




- GTK (*Igikoresho ca GIMP*): gikoreshwa na GNOME, XFCE, Umunyu, MATE...
- Qt: ikoreshwa na KDE, LXQt...



![Image](assets/fr/054.webp)



### Incamake y'ibidukikije vy'ibiro vya Linux



![Image](assets/fr/053.webp)



#### GNOME



Yatangujwe mu 1997, isohoka ubwa mbere mu 1999, GNOME ("*Ibidukikije vy'Ikigereranyo c'Ikintu c'Urusobe rwa GNU*") ishingiye ku bubiko bw'ibitabu bwa GTK kandi igamije kugabanya ugushihana hagati y'ukoresha na Interface biciye mu gutegura ibintu vyoroshe cane. Kuva GNOME 3, umushinge wayo, GNOME Shell, yarahevye imvugo ngereranyo ya kera y'ibiro vyuzuye ibishushanyo: aho gukoresha ibibanza vyinshi vy'akazi biboneka icarimwe, abakoresha bahindukira bakaja ku gihitamwo kimwe c'ibikorwa aho bacungera amadirisho, ibiro vy'ubuhinga, n'ibikoresho vy'ibikorwa.



![Image](assets/fr/051.webp)



Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, umuhinga mu vyo gukora indirimbo Mutter afatanya uburongozi bw’idirisha n’ikirundo ca Wayland, mu gihe aguma akorana na X11 kubera XWayland. Ku mburabuzi, ibidukikije bitanga Nautilus yo gusesangura dosiye, GNOME Terminal ku murongo w'amabwirizwa, n'urupapuro rw'imiterere rwo hagati. Amahitamwo yo guhindura GNOME arafise aho agarukira.



Iyi ni yo nzira y'ubuhinga bwa Fedora Workstation, Ubuntu n'izindi nzira nyinshi zikoreshwa kuri mudasobwa.



#### Ubuhinga bwa KDE



Umugambi wa KDE watangujwe mu 1996, n’uburyo bwa mbere bw’ibidukikije vyayo vy’ibiro vyasohotse mu 1998. Mu 2014, harashizweho itandukaniro hagati y’ibidukikije vy’ibiro n’ibindi bice vy’umugambi. Ivyo bikoresho vy'ibiro vyitwa "Plasma".



KDE Plasma ishingiye kuri Qt 6, urutonde rw'ibikoresho vy'ubuhinga bwa C++, no kuri KDE Frameworks, urutonde rw'amasomero y'ibice bifasha gutegura ibikorwa vy'ubuhinga buhuriweko. Umuyobozi wayo w’idirisha, KWin, na we nyene akora nk’umuhinga w’indirimbo wuzuye wa Wayland: akora ibikorwa vy’amaso (ugupfukiranya, uguseruka, uguhinduka), ugucapura igicapo n’ukwihutisha kwa GPU, n’ibimenyetso vy’ugukorako vyinshi biciye ku libinput.



![Image](assets/fr/055.webp)



Kimwe mu bintu bitandukanya KDE Plasma ni ikibanza cayo c’imiterere, kigaragaza igishushanyo Interface ku miterere hafi yose: inyifato y’ibiro vy’ukuri, inzira ngufi zo kw’isi yose, uburyo bwo gukora neza, uburongozi bw’ububasha, imiterere y’urubuga, ukugaragara kw’idirisha... Nta nyandiko manually configuration edited destop destop, the need to be guhindura uko ushaka.



KDE Plasma ikoreshwa mu gukwiragiza vyinshi, harimwo Kubuntu, OpenSUSE Tumbleweed, Fedora KDE Spin na Manjaro KDE.



#### Xfce



Xfce ni ikibanza c'ubuntu, gifunguye, cakozwe mu 1996 na Olivier Fourdan. Intumbero yayo ya mbere, ikiriho n’ubu, yari iyo gutanga uburyo bworoshe, bworoshe kandi bwihuta bwo gukoresha ibidukikije vy’ibiro biremerera nka GNOME canke KDE. Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Xfce ishingiye ku bikoresho vya GTK, ivyo bikaba biyikwegeranya na GNOME mu buryo bumwe bumwe, ariko kandi bikayitandukanya mu vy’ubuhinga bwayo.



Xfce ifata uburyo bwa kera bw’ibishushanyo Interface, bufise ibiro bikoreshwa n’ibishushanyo, urutonde rw’ibikorwa, umurongo w’ibikorwa, n’ibipande bishobora guhindurwa. Ivyo vyose vyakozwe kugira ngo bikoreshe neza ibikoresho, haba mu bijanye n’ubushobozi bwa RAM be n’ubushobozi bwa processeur. Ivyo bituma ari umuti mwiza kuri mudasobwa za kera, zidakomeye cane, canke gusa ku bakoresha barondera uburyo bugenda neza, bushikamye kandi bukora neza.



![Image](assets/fr/056.webp)



#### LXQt



LXQt ni ikibanza c’ibiro gifise uburemere buke gigenewe gutanga igishushanyo cuzuye Interface mu gihe gikoresha ibikoresho bikeyi vya sisitemu. Ni vyiza canecane ku mashini za kera canke zidakomeye cane.



LXQt ni ingaruka y’uguhuza imigambi ibiri itandukanye mu 2013: LXDE (yateguwe mu ntango n’ububiko bw’ibitabu bwa GTK+) na Razor-qt (ibidukikije bisa n’ivyo bishingiye kuri Qt). Ukwo gufatanya kwavyaye LXQt, n’intumbero yo guhuza utwigoro mu gihe wungukira ku bubasha n’ubuhinga bwa none bw’inzego za Qt, zihuye neza n’iterambere ry’imirongo ya Linux kuruta GTK+ 2, ikoreshwa na LXDE.



![Image](assets/fr/057.webp)



#### Umutobe



Cinnamon ni ikibanza ca none co gukoresha mu biro vyateguwe kandi bibungabungwa n’umugwi w’abakwiragiza Linux Mint. Yatangujwe mu 2011 nk’inyishu itaziguye ku mahinduka akomeye yashizweho na GNOME 3, abonwa ko ari uguhungabanya cane na bamwe mu kibano.



Mu ntango, Cinnamon yari Fork yoroshe ya GNOME Shell, ariko buhoro buhoro yarabohotse muri GNOME kugira ngo ibe ikibanza c’ibiro cuzuye, mu gihe yariko irabandanya kwizigira amasomero ya GTK (cane cane GTK 3).



Intumbero yayo nyamukuru ni ugutanga Interface ya kera, ishobora gutahurwa, mu kubandanya kwa GNOME 2 na Windows: urutonde rw’ibikorwa ruri hasi ibubamfu, umurongo w’ibikorwa, ahantu h’imenyekanisha, n’ibiro bishobora gukoreshwa. Ubu buryo bwo gukingira buraryoshe cane cane ku bakoresha bashasha canke abava kuri Windows, bazoca babona ningoga ivyo bakoresha.



![Image](assets/fr/058.webp)



#### MUGENZI



MATE ni Fork ya GNOME 2, yatangujwe mu 2011, inyuma y’ukuza kwa GNOME 3 n’iyindi Interface itandukanye cane (GNOME Shell). MATE yavutse ku cipfuzo co kuzigama uburyo bwa kera bw’ibidukikije vya GNOME 2, mu gihe bibungabunga kandi bikabihindura bishasha.



Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, MATE ishingiye ku masomero ya GTK 3 (inyuma yo gukoresha GTK 2 igihe kirekire), kandi igumya imiterere y’ibice: umucungerezi wa dosiye (Caja), umurongo w’ubugenzuzi, terminal, umuhinduzi w’inyandiko... Ivyo bihimba vyose ni amaforogo y’ibikoresho vya GNOME 2, biguma bivugururwa kugira ngo bigume bihuye n’imirongo y’ubuhinga bwa none.



Interface yayo ishingiye ku nzira y’ubuhinga bwa kera: urupapuro rumwe canke zibiri (menu, ahantu ho gutangura ningoga, isaha, ahantu ho gutangaza), urudandazwa rufise ibishushanyo, n’imitunganirize y’idirisha rireremba.



![Image](assets/fr/059.webp)



### Ivyangombwa vyo guhitamwo



Guhitamwo ibidukikije vyawe vya GNU/Linux si ikintu c’ubusa: bigena ubumenyi bw’ukoresha, ubushobozi bwa sisitemu, n’uguhuza kwa porogarama. Buri DE ishingiye ku mahitamwo y’ubuhinga (amasomero, ubwubatsi, umucungerezi w’idirisha...) bigira ico bikoze ku kuntu isa, inyifato, ubushobozi, mbere n’ibisabwa vy’ibikoresho. Aha ni ho hari ingingo nyamukuru umuntu akwiye kwitwararika igihe ahitamwo neza.



#### Ibikorwa vy'ibikoresho



Ibidukikije vyose vy'ibiro bifise ikirenge c'ibikoresho bitandukanye. Ivyo bipimwa mu bijanye n’ugukoresha RAM, ugukoresha CPU, n’igihe co gutangura:




- Ku mashini za kera canke zidakomeye cane (CPU y’umurongo umwe, RAM iri munsi ya 2 GB...), ndabagira inama yo gukoresha ibidukikije bifise uburemere buke cane nka LXQt, LXDE canke Xfce. Batanga igishushanyo cuzuye Interface, ariko ata ngaruka z’amashusho canke ibivako bikomeye;
- Ibidukikije vyo hagati, nka MATE canke Cinnamon, bisaba ibikoresho bishasha gatoyi (4 gushika kuri 6 GB RAM ni vyo vyiza), ariko biguma bibereye;
- Ibidukikije vy'ubu, vy'ubutunzi nka GNOME canke KDE Plasma biratunganye cane, ariko bisaba ibikoresho vyinshi, cane cane iyo ingaruka z'ibishushanyo zishobojwe. Birabereye ku mashini ziherutse gusohoka.



#### Ubwiza n'ivyo ukunda



Buri DE itanga filozofiya yihariye ya Interface:




- GNOME ikunda gukoresha mu buryo bworoshe, ifise Interface itunganye, ata biro canke ibishushanyo vya kera, n'uburyo bwo gukora bushobora gutera ubwoba abatangura
- KDE Plasma irashobora guhindurwa cane, gushika no ku bintu bitobito. Irafise ukuntu igaragara mu gihe ca none, ibishushanyo bigendagenda, n’iyindi Interface iri hafi cane ya Windows 1.
- Cinnamon na MATE bitanga ubumenyi bwa kera: urutonde rwo hasi ibubamfu, umurongo w’ibikorwa, ibishushanyo vyo ku biro. Cinnamon iraboneka cane mu gihe ca none, MATE iraremereye
- Xfce na LXQt zigamije kworosha no gukora neza, n'ubwiza buzigamye ariko bushobora guhindurwa



#### Ikoreshwa ry'intumbero



Ikoreshwa nyamukuru rya mudasobwa na ryo nyene rizogira ico rihinduye ku mahitamwo yawe:




- Ku bijanye n'ibiro n'ibikoresho vyinshi, ibidukikije vyose birabereye
- Ku kibanza co gukoreramwo c'iterambere, ivyo ukunda biratandukanye: abahinguzi bamwebamwe barashima ubukerebutsi bwa Xfce, abandi bakunda ibikoresho vyo gukorana bitangwa na KDE .
- Ku bikorwa vyinjijwe canke vy’abakozi bifise Interface ntoyi, canke ku mashini za kera cane, LXQt, LXDE canke Xfce ni zo zonyene zishobora guhitamwo .



#### Uguhuza n'ugusangira kwatowe



Igikoresho cose ca GNU/Linux gikunda ibidukikije vy’ibiro, akenshi bikaba vyinjijwe neza, bigeragezwa neza, biza n’ibikoresho vyihariye, kandi bishirwaho ku buryo busanzwe. Birashoboka kwama ushiramwo ikindi kibanza co kuri mudasobwa, ariko ivyo bishobora gutuma porogarama isubiramwo, amakimbirane yo gutunganya, canke ubumenyi bw'abakoresha butagenda neza. Ihitamwo ryawe ry’ibidukikije vy’ibiro rero rishobora guterwa n’iry’ugukwirakwiza kwawe kwa Linux, canke, ibihushanye n’ivyo, uguhitamwo kwawe kw’ibidukikije vy’ibiro vyihariye bishobora kuyobora ihitamwo ryawe ry’ugukwirakwiza.



Urashobora kubona ko hariho ugutanga, kwaba gucungiwe n'umugwi w'umugambi canke n'abatanga intererano bo hanze, birimwo ibidukikije vy'ibiro bitandukanye n'ivyo mbere (nk'akarorero Kubuntu, Lubuntu, Xubuntu...).



Aha niho hari ibidukikije vy'ibiro vy'ibice nyamukuru:





- Ubuntu → GNOME





- Kubuntu → Plasma ya KDE





- Xubuntu → Xfce





- Lubuntu → LXQt





- Linux Mint → Igitabu c'umunyu (igitabu nyamukuru), ariko kandi na MATE na Xfce





- Fedora → GNOME (integuro y'ingenzi), ariko itanga ama Spins menshi yemewe:
 - Fedora KDE Guhindukiza → KDE Igishushanyo
 - Fedora Xfce Guhindukiza → Xfce
 - Fedora LXQt Guhindukiza → LXQt
 - Fedora Mudarasini → Mudarasini
 - Fedora UMUGENZI-Igikoresho co guhindura → UMUGENZI
 - Fedora SoaS, i3, n'ibindi → ibidukikije vyihariye





- Debian → GNOME (mburabuzi), ihitamwo rya KDE, Xfce, LXQt, umunyu, MATE mu gihe co gushiramwo





- Manjaro → KDE Plasma, GNOME canke Xfce bivanye n'ivyo vyasohotse; n'ibindi bitabu vy'abanyagihugu bishobora kuboneka na Cinnamon, MATE, LXQt, i3, n'ibindi.





- Zorin OS → Zorin Ibiro, ishingiye kuri GNOME (Verisiyo y'Ibanze) na Xfce (Verisiyo y'Ibanze)





- OS y'intango → Pantheon, ibidukikije vy'intango bishingiye kuri GTK





- Pop! OS → GNOME yahinduwe na Interface COSMIC, vuba izosubirizwa na verisiyo ya Rust





- openSUSE → guhitamwo ku gushiramwo hagati ya KDE Plasma (inkuru yunze ubumwe), GNOME, Xfce, MATE, n'ibindi.





- Arch Linux → ntitanga ibidukikije vy'imbere, rero ukeneye gushiramwo ivyo uhisemwo





- Kali Linux → Xfce (ivya kera kuva muri 2019), kandi itanga KDE, GNOME, i3, MATE, n'ibindi.





- OS y'inkukuma → MATE (mburabuzi), ubundi buryo bufise KDE Plasma





- Imirizo → GNOME





- Qubes OS → Xfce





- BlackArch → i3 umuyobozi w'idirisha (si ibidukikije vy'ibiro vyuzuye)





- PureOS → GNOME





- Whonix → KDE Plasma (uburyo nyamukuru), ubundi buryo buboneka na Xfce



Mu gusozera, nta kibanza kimwe ciza kuruta ibindi vyose co gukoresha mu biro, ahubwo ni ikintu kimwe gusa gihuye neza n’ibikoresho vyawe, ivyo ukoresha be n’ivyo ukunda. Ni ibisanzwe mbere kugerageza DEs nyinshi imbere yo kuronka iyo itanga ugusenyera ku mugozi umwe hagati y’ubwiza, ubuhinga, n’ubushobozi.
