Iki gice kizoba caraguhaye ugutahura neza ico ari co ibidukikije vy’ibiro, ibice nyamukuru bigize, itandukaniro riri hagati y’imiti nyamukuru iriho, n’ingingo ngenderwako zihambaye zo guhitamwo. Mu gice gikurikira, uzoshobora gutera intambwe zawe za mbere ukoresheje Ubuntu, ubuhinga bwo gukwiragiza bushobora gukoreshwa mu buryo bwinshi ku bantu bose.



## Gutangura na Ubuntu: vyose ukeneye kumenya


<chapterId>7cea476d-f759-4c7e-8ca5-8b35bc79c682</chapterId>



Uyu musi, Ubuntu ni imwe mu nzira zishobora gushika kuri GNU/Linux: ibidukikije vya GNOME vyiza, ububiko bwinshi, ivyagezwe vy’umutekano vyishura n’umuryango munini. Ni co gituma nahisemwo gushikiriza uku gutanga.



Ariko rero, kugira ngo umenye neza gushiramwo ivyuma vyawe ku biro bisaba gutahura uburyo nyamukuru bwo gukoresha iyo sisitemu: gucunga amapaki, umurongo w’amabwirizwa, umutekano w’ishimikiro, n’ingene wobikora ku musi ku musi. Muri iki gice, nzogutwara intambwe ku yindi, kuva ku gutunganya ivy’intango gushika ku gushiramwo ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga n’iterambere, kugira ngo umenye neza ko ufise urubuga rwuzuye, rutekanye kandi rukora neza.



### Gushiramwo ubukwiragiza Ubuntu



Imbere y'uko ukoresha Ubuntu, ukeneye kuyishira ku mashini yawe. Iyi ntambwe yoshobora gusa n’iyiteye ubwoba nimba utigeze uyikora, ariko muri iyi misi biroroshe cane kuyikora.



Ibintu vyinshi birashoboka, bivanye n'ingene mudasobwa yawe imeze:




- Niba ufise mudasobwa ifise Windows imbere y'igihe, urashobora gushiramwo Ubuntu iruhande ya Windows (*"dual boot"*), canke ugasubirira system yawe yose Niba uhisemwo *dual boot*, urashobora guhitamwo system yo gukoresha uzotangura igihe cose ufunguye. Uyu ni umuti wo guhitamwo nimba ushaka gusa kugerageza Ubuntu mu gihe uguma ufise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha Windows .
- Niba ufise imashini nshasha idafise ubuhinga bwo gukoresha, ushobora gushiramwo Ubuntu nk'uburyo nyamukuru .



Mu bihe vyose, uburyo bwo gushiramwo bukurikira ingingo ngenderwako nyene z’ubuhinga, izo turiko turabona.



#### Kuvanaho Ubuntu



Dosiye yo gushiramwo Ubuntu iza mu buryo bw’ishusho ya ISO, dosiye irimwo vyose ukeneye kugira ngo ufungure no gushiramwo sisitemu. Kugira ngo uyironke, [genda ku rubuga rwemewe](https://ubuntu.com/gukuraho/gukoresha).



![Image](assets/fr/060.webp)



Hariho verisiyo 2 za Ubuntu:




- LTS (*Infashanyo y'igihe kirekire*)
- Verisiyo nshasha



Itandukaniro rikomeye hagati ya verisiyo ya LTS na verisiyo itari LTS ya Ubuntu ni igihe co gushigikira n'ugushikama. Verisiyo ya LTS irashigikirwa imyaka 5. Ku rundi ruhande, verisiyo itari LTS ishigikirwa gusa amezi 9, rero urakeneye guhindura sisitemu yawe ubudasiba. Ku rundi ruhande, verisiyo nshasha itari LTS irimwo ibintu vyose bishasha. Ndabagira inama yo gukoresha verisiyo ya LTS nimba uriko uratangura, kuko igumaho kandi isaba guhindura bike cane. Ariko rero, urashobora guhitamwo verisiyo nshasha itari LTS niwabishaka: ntaco izogira kuri porogarama isigaye.



Fyonda gusa kuri buto ya "*Gukuraho*" kugira ngo ubone ishusho ya Ubuntu ISO.



#### Rema urufunguzo rwa USB rushobora gutangura



Kugira ngo ushire Ubuntu kuri mudasobwa yawe, ukeneye gutuma ishusho ya ISO ishobora gufunguka ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa USB. Urufunguzo ruzokora nk’ibikoresho vyo gushiramwo.



Nimushiremwo umuduga wa USB ufise nibura 8 GB (wirinde, ibirimwo bizokurwaho), hanyuma mukoreshe igikoresho nka [BalenaEtcher](https://www.balena.io/etcher) kugira ngo mukore ubuhinga bwo gufungura amakuru buva ku ishusho ya ISO. Hitamwo gusa dosiye ISO, urufunguzo rwa USB, hanyuma ukande kuri "*Flash*".



![Image](assets/fr/061.webp)



#### Gufungura kuva ku rufunguzo rwa USB



Ubu rero ukeneye gufungura mudasobwa yawe atari kuri disiki ya Hard, ahubwo ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa USB. Subiramwo imashini yawe maze winjire muri menu y’ugutangura canke BIOS/UEFI. Ivyo bikorwa kenshi mu gukanda urufunguzo umaze gufungura mudasobwa yawe (kenshi `F2`, `F10`, `F12`, `DEL`, `ESC`). Suzuma ingene ushobora gushika kuri iyi menyu ku mashine yawe.



Mu nzira y'ugutangura, hitamwo urufunguzo rwa USB (rushobora kuboneka munsi y'izina ry'umuhinguzi w'urufunguzo canke nk'"USB"). Hanyuma uhitemwo "*Gerageza canke Shiraho Ubuntu*". Mudasobwa izoca ifungura muri Ubuntu mu buryo bwa "live": ivyo bigufasha kugerageza system ataco uhinduye, canke gutanguza installer ataco uhinduye.



#### Amagenamiterere y'intango



Uwushiramwo azotanga iciyumviro:




- Hitamwo ururimi rwawe n'isaha yawe
- kwihuza n'urubuga rwa Wi-Fi
- Hitamwo ubwoko bw'ugushiraho (ubwa mbere canke bwagutse) bivanye n'uko ushaka sisitemu ntoyi canke ifise porogaramu nyinshi zashizweho mbere
- nimba woshiramwo canke kutashiramwo porogaramu y'uwundi muntu (abashoferi b'ibishushanyo, ama codecs, n'ibindi)



#### Hitamwo ubwoko bwo gushiramwo



Umaze gutanguza Ubuntu, umuhinga wo gushiramwo Ubuntu arakuyobora intambwe ku yindi. Kurikiza intambwe yose maze uhitemwo uburyo bubereye wewe. Intambwe ihambaye kuruta izindi zose ni iyo yerekeye ubwoko bw’ugushiraho. Bivanye n’ingene umeze, hari ibintu bitatu bishobora gushika:





- Gushiramwo iruhande ya Windows (*ugufungura kabiri*)**



Niba mudasobwa yawe isanzwe irimwo Windows, Ubuntu izoca imenya ubwo nyene iyo installation maze itanga iciyumviro co gufungura kabiri kuri sisitemu 2 zikoreshwa:




- Uwushiramwo azogabanya igice ca Windows kugira ngo abone umwanya
- Ubuntu izoshirwa muri iki kibanza c'ubusa, n'imigabane yayo bwite
- Hazoshirwamwo umuyobozi w'ivy'ugufungura (GRUB), azogufasha guhitamwo hagati ya Windows na Ubuntu igihe cose mudasobwa ifunguye .



Hitamwo iyi nzira nimba ushaka kuguma ukoresha Windows ku bikorwa bimwe bimwe (nk'imikino ya videwo) mu gihe uriko uravumbura Linux.



Kugira ngo ivyo ubikore neza, ndagusavye ko wobanza gukora igice kitagenewe kuri disiki uhisemwo muri Windows, hanyuma ugahitamwo n’amaboko ico gice igihe ushiramwo Ubuntu. Kugira ngo ubikore, fungura Disk Manager muri Windows, ukande iburyo kuri disk iriko irabazwa hanyuma uhitemwo "*Gabanya ijwi*". Hanyuma ugaragaze ubunini wipfuza kubika kuri Ubuntu (ndagusavye ko ukoresha 80 GB kugira ngo ukoreshe neza).





- Gusubirira Windows**



Niba ushaka gukoresha Ubuntu gusa, ushobora guhitamwo gukuraho disiki yose:




- Iyi nzira ifuta amakuru yose asanzweho, harimwo na Windows .
- Ubuntu buzoca buba uburyo bwonyene bushizwe kuri iyo mashini .



Hitamwo iyi nzira gusa iyo wipfuza guhindura 100% ukaja kuri GNU/Linux. Ibuka gukora backup y’amakuru yawe ya Windows imbere y’uko uyafuta burundu.





- Gushiramwo kuri mudasobwa idafise ikintu



Nimba imashini yawe ata sisitemu irimwo na gato, canke nimba warahanaguye disiki imbere y’igihe, gushiramwo birabandanya nk’uko vyari vyifashe imbere. Ubuntu izokwishiramwo nk'uburyo nyamukuru maze ihite itunganye imigabane ikenewe.



Uzoca usabwa gushinga konti y’ukoresha (izina, ijambobanga, izina ry’imashini). Hitamwo ijambobanga rikomeye: rizogufasha kwinjira muri sisitemu, gushiramwo porogarama canke guhindura amasetingi ahambaye



Ku bindi bisobanuro ku bijanye n'ivyo gushiramwo Ubuntu, ushobora kandi kuraba iyi nyigisho:



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/ubuntu-78a3be56-5d51-4ec3-8629-0dd27c352ab5

Igihe installation irangiye, nukureho urufunguzo rwa USB iyo usabwe, hanyuma wongere ufungure. Ubu Ubuntu buzoba bushizweho kandi bwiteguye gukoreshwa ku mashine yawe.



Urasangwa, ubu ufise ubuhinga bwa GNU/Linux bushitse!



![Image](assets/fr/062.webp)



### Imiterere ya sisitemu y'intango



Igihe umufasha wo gushiramwo azoheza, winjire n'uwukoresha mushasha maze ufungure terminal:



```bash
Ctrl+Alt+T
```



![Image](assets/fr/063.webp)



#### Gusubiramwo



Amashusho ya ISO arimwo amapaki yakonje amayinga menshi imbere y'uko asohoka, rero wama uhuza urutonde maze ukoreshe amapaki mbere:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt full-upgrade
sudo apt autoremove --purge
```



Itegeko rya mbere rihindura urutonde rw’amapaki yo mu karere, rikakuraho amaverisiyo mashasha maze rikayashiramwo; ica kabiri gisukura ibintu vyose biva ku bindi bitagikenewe.



→ Itegeko rya `sudo` rikora igikorwa gifise uburenganzira bw’umuyobozi kandi risaba ijambobanga ryawe kugira ngo ryemeze.



![Image](assets/fr/064.webp)



Ushobora rero gusubira gufungura mudasobwa yawe:



```bash
sudo reboot
```



#### Ububiko bwa porogaramu n'imirongo: gutahura aho porogaramu ikomoka



Muri Ubuntu, porogaramu irashirwaho kandi igasubirwamwo biciye ku buryo bw’ububiko buzwi. Ububiko ni umukozi arimwo ibihumbi vy’amaporogarama (porogarama, amasomero, abashoferi...), vyose bitunganijwe hakurikijwe amategeko atomoye. Izo mpapuro zigenzurwa, zigashirwako umukono kandi zigakwiragizwa ubwazo biciye ku mucungerezi w'impapuro `apt`.



Ububiko bwose bugabanywamwo ibice. Ku mburabuzi, Ubuntu ikoresha ibice bine nyamukuru:




- main**: porogaramu y’ubuntu icungiwe ku mugaragaro na Canonical. Ingero: Firefox, Ibiro vy'uburenganzira, bash
- restricted**: porogaramu zitari izo ku buntu zikenewe kugira ngo ibikoresho bikore neza. Ingero: abashoferi ba NVIDIA, porogaramu ya Wi-Fi, ama codecs y'umunyagihugu
- universe**: porogaramu y’ubuntu ibungabungwa n’abanyagihugu. Ingero: GIMP, Igishushanyo c'Irangi, Ubushizi bw'amanga
- multiverse**: porogaramu zitegekanijwe n’amategeko (uburenganzira bwo gukoresha, uruhusha rudakoreshwa ubuntu). Uko bishobora kuboneka bivanye n’igihugu. Ingero: amajwi/amasanamu amwe amwe, Steam



Igice kimwekimwe cose gishobora rero guca mu mihora canke amashami menshi: `gusohora`, `umutekano`, `uguhindura`, `ugusubira inyuma`, n'ibindi, bihuye n'ingene ivyo bivugururwa bimeze.



### Intambwe zambere ku murongo w'itegeko



Igishushanyo Interface gituma gukoresha Ubuntu bishoboka, ariko ku bikorwa bimwe bimwe vy'uburongozi, terminal iguma ari igikoresho gikora neza kandi gikomeye kuruta ibindi vyose. Munsi ya Ubuntu, igikoko mburabuzi ni **Bash** (*SHell*), igikoko c'ubuntu kiva mu muco wa Unix.



Gukoresha terminal bigufasha gukoresha amadosiye ataco uhinduye, gutunganya neza sisitemu, gucunga amapaki, gukora ibikorwa canke gusuzuma ingorane. Aha niho hari amabwirizwa y’ingenzi uzokenera kugira ngo utangure.





- Erekana ububiko buriho:



```bash
pwd
```



Iri tegeko ryerekana inzira y'ububiko urimwo ubu. Ni ngirakamaro cane nimba ushaka kuguma ukurikirana aho uri mu giti c'ububiko.



![Image](assets/fr/065.webp)





- Urutonde rw'ibirimwo mu bubiko



```bash
ls -lah
```



Iri tegeko ritanga urutonde rw'amadosiye n'ububiko mu bubiko buriho mu buryo burambuye:




- `-l`: "*long*" uburyo, bugaragaza uruhusha, ubunini, umukoresha, itariki...
- `-a`: nayo yerekana amadosiye yihishije (ayo atangura n'akadomo).
- `-h`: "*umuntu-ashobora gusoma*", yerekana ubunini mu buryo bushobora gusomwa (KB, MB...).



![Image](assets/fr/066.webp)



Impinduka:



```bash
lsblk
```



Igaragaza igiti c'imiterere y'amadisiki n'imigabane ihuye na sisitemu yawe. Ivyo ni ngirakamaro cane mu kumenya umuduga wa USB, nk’akarorero.





- Guhindura ububiko:



```bash
cd /path/to/directory
```



`cd` bihagaze kuri "*hindura ububiko*". Ivyo bituma ushobora kwihindukiza igiti ca dosiye. Nk'akarorero, n'itegeko `cd Music`, uzoba uri mu bubiko `/Music`.



![Image](assets/fr/067.webp)





- `cd ~`: igaruka ku bubiko bw'inzu.
- `cd -`: igaruka ku bubiko bwa kera.





- Rema ububiko



Kugira ngo ureme ububiko bushasha imbere muri ubu, koresha itegeko:



```bash
mkdir name
```



Gusa hindura "izina" mu izina ry'ububiko bwawe bushasha.



![Image](assets/fr/068.webp)





- Kopa dosiye:



Kugira ngo ukope dosiye, koresha itegeko `cp`, ukurikize izina rya dosiye (utegerezwa kuba uri mu bubiko aho dosiye iri), hanyuma inzira ija ku bubiko buja.



```bash
cp file.txt destination
```



![Image](assets/fr/069.webp)





- Kwimura canke guhindura izina rya dosiye:



```bash
mv file.txt /new/directory/
```



Itegeko `mv` rigufasha kwimurira canke guhindura izina rya dosiye canke ububiko. Niwatanga inzira ija mu bundi bubiko inyuma y'izina rya dosiye, dosiye izokwimurirwa. Niwatanga izina rishasha mu bubiko bumwe, dosiye izohindurwa izina.



![Image](assets/fr/070.webp)





- Gukuraho dosiye canke ububiko:



```bash
rm file.txt
```



Imburi: iri tegeko ntirijana amadosiye mu gitereko c'ibikoresho.



![Image](assets/fr/071.webp)





- `-r`: gukuraho bisubira inyuma (ku bubiko).
- `-f`: ihatira gukuraho ata kwemeza (biteye akaga).



Kugira ngo wirinde amakosa n'iri tegeko, ndagusavye kwongerako ubutumwa bwo kwemeza ku buryo busanzwe. Gusa ukore muri terminal yawe:



```bash
echo "alias rm='rm -i'" >> ~/.bashrc
source ~/.bashrc
```



Uzosabwa kwemeza imbere y’uko usiba vyose.





- Gukuraho ikibanza



Kugira ngo ukureho terminal maze utangure n'igicapo kitagira ikintu, wandike:



```bash
clear
```





- Gushitsa itegeko nk'umuyobozi:



```bash
sudo command
```



Ijambo ry'ingenzi `sudo` (*superuser do*) riguha uburenganzira bwo gukora itegeko mu gihe gito ufise *umuzi* (umuyobozi wa sisitemu) uburenganzira. Uzosabwa ijambobanga ryawe kugira ngo wemeze iki gikorwa. Urabe maso: ntukigere ukoresha `sudo` utatahuye ico itegeko rikora.



Impanuro: guhindukira ku muzi w'igikoko (igihe c'umuyobozi), wandike:



```bash
sudo -i
```



Ivyo bifungura terminal yuzuye ifise uburenganzira bw'imizi. Koresha n’ubwenge kandi ntuzokwigere ukoresha igihe kirekire.





- Raba imfashanyo y'itegeko:



```bash
man command_name
```



Itegeko `umuntu` (*igitabu*) rifungura inyandiko zose z'itegeko. Kugendagenda n'imfunguruzo z'umwampi maze usohoke n' `q`.



Akarorero:



```bash
man cp
```



Kugira ngo ubone incamake yihuse, koresha:



```bash
cp --help
```



Aya mategeko y'intango ni vyo vyose ukeneye kugira ngo ukore ibikorwa vyinshi vy'ishimikiro muri terminal yawe. Iyo wimenyereje gatoyi, uzoronka ubwigenge n’umuvuduko.



Mu bice bikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene twokoresha terminal kugira ngo ducunge sisitemu, amapaki, n’ibikoresho vy’umutekano.



### Ubuyobozi bw'amapaki: APT, Snap na Flatpak



Ku sisitemu ya GNU/Linux nka Ubuntu, gushiramwo porogarama, gusubiramwo no gukuraho bishirwa hamwe biciye mu sisitemu zo gucunga amapaki. Udakunze Windows, aho ukura amadosiye `.exe' canke `.msi', Ubuntu ikoresha ibikoresho nka APT, Snap canke Flatpak kugira ngo ivyo bikorwa bikore, bikaba vyemeza ko ubuhinga bugenda neza.



#### APT: Uburyo bwa Debian



APT (*Igikoresho c'amapaki ateye imbere*) ni umuyobozi w'amapaki nyamukuru ya Ubuntu. Ifata amapaki mu buryo bwa `.deb`, avuye mu bubiko buzwi. Buri paki irimwo porogarama, ibivako n’amakuru y’imbere. Reka turabe amabwirizwa y’ishimikiro, dukoresheje umuhinduzi w’amashusho wa GIMP nk’akarorero.



Kugira ngo urondere mu bubiko umuzigo uriho (utegerezwa, vy'ukuri, gusubirira "gimp" n'izina rya porogaramu wipfuza):



```bash
apt search gimp
```



![Image](assets/fr/072.webp)



Kugira ngo ushiremwo porogaramu n'ibindi vyose biyishingiyeko:



```bash
sudo apt install gimp
```



![Image](assets/fr/073.webp)



Igihe gushiramwo birangiye, uzosanga ibikorwa mu rutonde rw'ibikorwa vya Ubuntu, biri hasi ibubamfu bwa Interface.



![Image](assets/fr/074.webp)



N'ikiruta ivyo: urashobora kandi kwandika izina rya porogaramu ushitse muri terminal (muri iki gihe, "gimp") kugira ngo uyifungure.



![Image](assets/fr/075.webp)



Kugira ngo ukureho porogaramu, ushobora gukoresha itegeko rikurikira (usubirira "gimp" n'izina rya porogaramu wipfuza gukuraho):



```bash
sudo apt remove gimp
```



Ushobora kandi kwongerako `--purge` ku itegeko ryawe kugira ngo usibe amadosiye y'imiterere ajanye na porogaramu:



```bash
sudo apt remove --purge gimp
```



![Image](assets/fr/076.webp)



Kugira ngo uhindure urutonde rw'amakuru y'amapaki ariho (`uvugurure`) no gushiramwo verisiyo nshasha (`uvugurure`), ushobora gukoresha aya mabwirizwa abiri akurikira:



```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade
```



![Image](assets/fr/077.webp)



→ APT iranyaruka, iraremereye, kandi yinjijwe neza cane muri Ubuntu. Ku maporogarama yose ari mu bubiko buzwi, ubu ni bwo buryo bwiza.



#### Snap: amapaki y'ibikoresho bivuye muri Canonical



Snap ni uburyo bw’amapaki bwateguwe na Canonical, bwateguwe kugira ngo bube ubw’isi yose, butandukanye n’uburyo nyamukuru kandi bwigenga. Ivyo bisigura ko igishushanyo cose gishiramwo ivyo kivyifatamwo kandi kigakora mu bidukikije vy’umusenyi.



Ivyo bituma bishoboka ko porogarama ziguma zigezweho ataco zitwaye kuri sisitemu, kandi zikora ku bikoresho vyose vya Linux bifasha Snap. Ku rundi ruhande, bifata igihe kirekire kugira ngo utangure, bishobora gutuma umuntu ateranya ibintu bimwe bimwe bidakenewe, kandi gukorana n’ibindi bikoresho bimwe bimwe ntibigenda neza.



Kugira uronde umuzigo wa Snap mu bubiko bwa Snap (aha kuri porogaramu ya Spotify):



```bash
snap find spotify
```



![Image](assets/fr/078.webp)



Kugira ngo ushiremwo porogaramu:



```bash
sudo snap install spotify
```



Iyo installation irangiye, uzosanga executable muri menyu y'ibikorwa vya Ubuntu, iri hasi ibubamfu bwa Interface. Canke, mbere vyoroshe: ushobora kwandika izina rya porogarama uyifungure (muri iki gihe, "spotify") kugira ngo uyifungure.



![Image](assets/fr/079.webp)



Kugira ngo uvugurure amapaki yose ya Snap yashizweho:



```bash
sudo snap refresh
```



Kugira ngo usibe porogaramu:



```bash
sudo snap remove spotify
```



![Image](assets/fr/080.webp)



→ Porogaramu za Snap zishirwa mu bubiko bwa `/var/snap` zigashirwako nk’uburyo bw’amadosiye butandukanye.



#### Flatpak: ubundi buryo bw'ibice



Flatpak ni ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha amapaki y'isi yose, bwateguwe n'abanyagihugu (Red Hat, GNOME...). Igamije gutsinda imipaka y’imiterere ya kera, mu gihe itanga uburyo bwiza bwo gucunga uruhusha kuruta Snap. Igikoresho cose gikora mu gasandugu k’umusenyi, ariko gifise ubuhinga bwiza bwo kugenzura.



Kugira ngo ushiremwo Flatpak n'ubufatanye bwayo bw'ibishushanyo:



```bash
sudo apt install flatpak gnome-software-plugin-flatpak
```



Kwongera ububiko bw'abanyagihugu (Flathub):



```bash
flatpak remote-add --if-not-exists flathub https://flathub.org/repo/flathub.flatpakrepo
```



Kugira ngo ushiremwo porogaramu biciye kuri Flatpak, koresha itegeko rikurikira (muri aka karorero, kugira ngo ushiremwo porogaramu ya VLC):



```bash
flatpak install flathub org.videolan.VLC
```



![Image](assets/fr/081.webp)



Muri make:



| Format       | Origin       | Isolation | Size | Performance | Permission Control |
| ------------ | ------------- | --------- | ------ | ------------ | ------------------- |
| APT / `.deb` | Debian        | ❌         | ✅      | ✅            | 🟡                  |
| Snap         | Canonical     | 🟡        | ❌      | ❌            | 🟡                  |
| Flatpak      | Community     | ✅         | 🟡     | 🟡           | ✅                   |

#### Ikigo ca porogaramu: uwushiramwo ibishushanyo



Ubuntu irimwo porogaramu yitwa *App Center*, ikora nk’igishushanyo Interface co kurondera, gushiramwo no gukuraho porogaramu mu buryo bworoshe, ata gukoresha imirongo y’amabwirizwa nk’uko twabibonye. Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, App Center ikora nk’igipfukisho ku barongozi b’amapaki. Bishobora rero:




- Gushiramwo .deb amapaki ukoresheje APT
- Shiraho amapaki ya Snap avuye mu bubiko bwa Snap



Rero App Center store si uburyo bwo gushiramwo ibintu mu buryo bwayo bwite, ahubwo ni Interface ihuriza hamwe kandi igahuza inkomoko nyinshi za porogarama, ifise ubuhinga bwo kurondera, amakuru adondora n’amabuto yo gushiramwo ibintu ashobora gukoreshwa n’abatangura.



![Image](assets/fr/082.webp)



### Gucungera no kuvugurura



Kugira ngo ubone ko sisitemu yawe iguma itekanye kandi itekanye, Ubuntu ihita ikoresha ivyagezwe bihambaye biciye ku gikorwa citwa `unattended-upgrades`. Iyi serivisi ikora mu nyuma kandi igashiramwo ibice vy’umutekano vyasohowe n’ugukwirakwiza, ataco winjiramwo.



#### Suzuma uko serivisi imeze



Kugira ngo umenye neza ko ubu buryo bukora:



```bash
sudo systemctl status unattended-upgrades
```



Ushobora kubona igisohoka kigaragaza ko serivisi `ikora (iriko irakora)`.



![Image](assets/fr/083.webp)



Niba atarivyo, ushobora kubikoresha n'amaboko:



```bash
sudo systemctl enable --now unattended-upgrades
```



Iyi serivisi irinda sisitemu yawe ubugoyagoye bushasha buvumbuwe, ataco ukeneye kugenzura n’amaboko ko hariho ivyahinduwe buri musi. Ni ngirakamaro cane cane ku bibanza vy'akazi bitagenzurwa cane, nka mudasobwa z'abantu, kuko bitanga icemezo c'ivy'umutekano.



→ **Ibuka:** `unattended-upgrades` zigarukira ku mapaki y'umutekano ava mu bubiko bwa `umutekano`. Ntikoresha rero ivyagezwe bishasha vya porogarama, ivyo uzobwirizwa kubikora n’amaboko.



#### Kuvugurura sisitemu yose n'amaboko



Naho ibice bihambaye vyoshirwaho ubwavyo, birahambaye ko uhora ukoresha ivugurura ry'amaboko kugira ngo wungukire ku verisiyo nshasha za porogaramu n'ibice bitavugwa n'ivugurura ritagira uwubicungera`. Kugira ngo ubikore, koresha itegeko:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt full-upgrade
```





- `apt update` ihuza urutonde rw'amapaki ariho
- `apt full-upgrade` ishiraho verisiyo nshasha, naho ivyo vyoba bisobanura guhindura ibintu bimwe bimwe (bitandukanye n'ivyo `upgrade`, ari vyo bikomeye)



![Image](assets/fr/084.webp)



Inyuma y'ivugurura, ushobora gusukura amadosiye adakenewe ukoresheje:



```bash
sudo apt autoremove --purge
```



Iri tegeko rikuraho amapaki ya kera n'amadosiye y'imiterere ajanye.



Niba warashizeho porogaramu biciye ku bacungezi b’amapaki ya Snap canke Flatpak, ushobora gukoresha aya mabwirizwa abiri kugira ngo uyavugurure na yo nyene:



```bash
sudo snap refresh
flatpak update
```



#### Gusubira gutangura inyuma y'ibindi bivuguruwe



Ivyiyumviro bimwe bimwe bihambaye, nk’ivyo kuri Linux kernel canke libc (ububiko bw’ururimi rwa C rusanzwe bukoreshwa na porogarama nyinshi), bitangura gukora gusa inyuma y’aho imashini yawe isubiye gufungura. Kugira ngo umenye nimba gusubira gutangura ari vyiza, shiramwo igikoresho ca `needrestart`:



```bash
sudo apt install needrestart
```



Hanyuma wiruke:



```bash
sudo needrestart
```



Iyi porogarama izosuzuma ibikorwa vyose canke ibikorwa vyose bikiriko birakoresha verisiyo za kera z’amasomero canke kernels, maze ikubwire nimba bisabwa gusubira gufungura kugira ngo ukoreshe ivyo bishasha.



![Image](assets/fr/085.webp)



Gutuma ubuhinga bwawe n’ubuhinga bwawe biguma bigezweho ni ikintu gihambaye cane iyo bije ku bijanye n’umutekano wa mudasobwa. Kugira ubuhinga bwa Linux bugezweho ni ikimenyamenya c’ugushikama, umutekano n’ubushobozi.



### Uruhome rw'umuriro n'ugukomera kw'urubuga



Uruhome rw'umuriro ni igikoresho co gucungera umutekano mudasobwa yinjira n'isohoka. Kuri Ubuntu, uzoyikoresha mu kuyungurura uruja n'uruza kugira ngo wemere gusa amakuru yemewe no guhagarika ayashobora kuba ari mabi. Ivyo bibuza abantu bo hanze kwinjira mu nzu batabisavye, nk’akarorero, kugira ngo urushirize gukingira amakuru yawe na sisitemu yawe.



Ukimara gushiramwo Ubuntu, gucungera amakuru y’urubuga rw’imashini yawe ni intambwe ihambaye. Ubuntu irimwo uruhome rw'umuriro rusanzwe: UFW (*Uruhome rw'umuriro rudakomeye*). Iragufasha gucunga amahuzu yinjira n’asohoka ukoresheje ubugenzuzi bwiza, ataco ukeneye kwandika n’amaboko amategeko agoranye.



#### Gukoresha uruhome rw'umuriro



Ku mburabuzi, UFW irashizweho, ariko ntikora. Kugira ngo uyikoreshe:



```bash
sudo ufw enable
```



![Image](assets/fr/086.webp)



Iyo imaze gukoreshwa, ushobora kugenzura uko imeze n'amategeko ariho ubu ukoresheje:



```bash
sudo ufw status verbose
```



![Image](assets/fr/087.webp)



Ku mbuga, UFW ifata ubuhinga bwo kwanka amahuzu yinjira atasabwe mu gihe yemera uruja n’uruza rusohoka, ivyo bikaba ari ugusenyura neza umutekano/imikorere y’imashini y’umuntu ku giti ciwe y’intumbero rusangi.



#### Kwemerera serivisi



Niba ukeneye gutuma serivisi ishobora gushikirwa kure (nk'umukozi wa SSH), utegerezwa kuyiha uburenganzira:



```bash
sudo ufw allow 22/tcp comment 'SSH'
```





- `22` ni icuma mburabuzi ca serivisi ya SSH
- `tcp` ni porotokole ikoreshwa
- Ihitamwo rya `ibitekerezo` rigufasha kwongerako ibisobanuro bisomwa kugira ngo vyorohe gusobanura amategeko mu nyuma



Ushobora kugenzura itegeko na:



```bash
sudo ufw status numbered
```



![Image](assets/fr/088.webp)



#### Sigura amategeko hakurikijwe urutonde rwa IP (ikoreshwa ryo mu karere)



Birashoboka ko ushobora guhagarika uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ibikorwa bimwebimwe ku rutonde rw'amaderesi IP, bishobora kuba ngirakamaro mu rubuga rw'aho hantu (LAN):



```bash
sudo ufw allow from 192.168.1.0/24 to any port 6881 proto tcp
```



Ivyo bituma TCP ishobora guhuzwa ku cambu 6881 gusa bivuye ku nzira `192.168.1.0/24` (mu bisanzwe ni inzira ya Wi-Fi yo mu nzu yawe).



#### Igishushanyo Interface: GUFW



Niba udakunda cane iyo terminal, hariho igishushanyo Interface citwa GUFW, kigatuma vyoroha gucunga amategeko y’uruhome rw’umuriro ukoresheje amabuto, urutonde rumanuka, n’ibisandugu vy’ibiganiro. Gushiramwo:



```bash
sudo apt install gufw
```



Iyo umaze kuyishiramwo, uyifungure biciye ku rutonde rw’ibikoresho. Uzoshobora gukoresha uruhome rw'umuriro, kwemerera canke guhagarika ibikorwa no kubona amahuzwa yayunguruwe mu gihe nyaco.



![Image](assets/fr/089.webp)



→ **Ivyiza:** Naho woba utashize ahabona ibikorwa vy’urubuga vyose ku isi yo hanze, uruhome rw’umuriro ruracari ngirakamaro mu kubuza ubwoko bumwe bumwe bw’ugucapura canke gushikira. Kandi wibuke guhagarika ibikorwa bidakenewe kandi wama ushiramwo porogarama yawe y’urubuga. Ukwo gukomera kw’urubuga rw’aho hantu ni umurongo wa mbere wo kwikingira mu nzira yagutse y’umutekano, ariko ivyo tuzobigarukako mu nyuma mu nyigisho.



### Uguhuzwa na interineti n'uburongozi bw'urubuga



Mu Ubuntu, uburongozi bw’urubuga bukorwa na *NetworkManager*, igikorwa gishira hamwe amahuzu y’intsinga, Wi-Fi, VPNs, modems, n’ibindi. Ivyo bikoresho vyose hamwe, bituma vyoroha gukoreshwa buri musi kandi bikaba bikomeye mu bibazo bikomeye cane (amaserveri, amakonfigurasiyo y’amaboko, n’ibindi).



#### Uburongozi biciye ku gishushanyo Interface



Ku bakoresha benshi, igishushanyo Interface kiri muri GNOME (Imiterere ya sisitemu → Urubuga/Wi-Fi) kirahagije cane. Biguha uburenganzira bwo:




- Kwihuza n'urubuga rwa Wi-Fi ruriho
- Gucungera amahuzwa y'intsinga, abaserukira canke VPNs
- Raba uko urubuga rwose ruri ubu Interface



Ubu buryo bwo gucunga busanzwe burapfuka vyinshi mu bikenewe vya kera vya mudasobwa y’umuntu ku giti ciwe.



![Image](assets/fr/090.webp)



#### Gukoresha iherezo na nmcli



Ku bijanye no gutorera umuti ingorane canke gushika kure, itegeko `nmcli` rigufasha gukoresha *NetworkManager* uhereye ku murongo w'itegeko.





- Kugaragaza urubuga rwabonetse:



```bash
nmcli device status
```





- Gupima imihora ya Wi-Fi iri hafi



```bash
nmcli device wifi list
```





- Kugira ngo wihuze n'urubuga rwa Wi-Fi



```bash
nmcli device wifi connect "wifi_name" password "password"
```



### Gushiramwo porogaramu z'ingenzi



Igihe ubuhinga bwawe bw’ishimikiro bumaze gukora, intambwe ikurikira ni ugushiramwo porogarama ukeneye. Ubuntu itanga uburyo bwinshi bwo gushiramwo (APT, Snap, Flatpak), ivyo twabivuze mu buryo burambuye haruguru. Aha, dukoresha APT igihe cose bishoboka kugira ngo tuzigame ubufatanye bw’imvukira n’uburyo.



#### Umucukumbuzi w'urubuga



Ku mburabuzi, Ubuntu irimwo verisiyo ya Snap ya Firefox. Iyi nzira itanga ukwitandukanya neza (ari vyiza mu bijanye n’umutekano), ariko bituma igihe co gutangura kigenda buhoro, gukoresha ibikoresho vyinshi, n’imipaka imwe imwe y’ugushiramwo sisitemu (ugucungera amadosiye, insasanuro...).



Niba ukunda verisiyo kavukire `.deb`, ushobora kuyishiramwo ukoresheje PPA yemewe ya Mozilla:



```bash
sudo add-apt-repository ppa:mozillateam/ppa
sudo apt update
sudo apt install firefox
```



Hanyuma, kugira ngo ubuze sisitemu gusubira kuri verisiyo ya Snap mu gihe c'ivugurura:



```bash
sudo apt-mark hold firefox
```



Ibi bihagarika verisiyo ya `.deb` ishizweho ubu. Izobandanya guhindurwa, ariko izoguma muri iyo nzira.



![Image](assets/fr/091.webp)



Turaza kuraba mu buryo burambuye ama browser mu kigabane kizokurikira, kugira ngo bigufashe guhitamwo iyo ibereye ivyo ukeneye, no kuyitunganya neza.



#### Imeyili



Thunderbird ni umukiriya w’ubutumwa bufunguye, na yo nyene yateguwe na Mozilla. Ishigikira amakonti ya IMAP/POP, ingengabihe, ivyungura n’ugushiramwo amakuru OpenPGP.



```bash
sudo apt install thunderbird
```



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/thunderbird-91d02325-0361-4641-b152-8975890284a8
#### Ibiro



LibreOffice ni ibiro vy'ubuntu vyuzuye kuruta ibindi vyose. Itanga ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha ijambo, Excel na PowerPoint, ikaba ihuye neza cane n’imiterere y’ibiro vya Microsoft (.docx, .xlsx, .pptx).



```bash
sudo apt install libreoffice
```



Niba wipfuza gushiramwo ibintu vyinshi:



```bash
sudo apt install libreoffice-writer libreoffice-calc libreoffice-impress
```



Izo mpapuro zitatu zivuga ivy’ingenzi: gukora amajambo, gukora urupapuro rw’ibara n’ugushikiriza.



![Image](assets/fr/092.webp)



Hariho n’izindi nzira, nka OnlyOffice (yegereye Ibiro vya Microsoft vya Interface), Ibiro vya WPS (ivy’umuntu, ariko bigenda neza cane), canke Calligra Suite (umugambi wa KDE). Ivyo bishobora gushirwako biciye kuri Flatpak, Snap canke bikakurwa ku mbuga zavyo.



#### Ivyuma vyinshi



VLC ni igikoresho co gukina amakuru, gishobora gukina amajwi/amasanamu menshi ata yindi codecs:



```bash
sudo apt install vlc
```



Ubuntu ntitanga ama codecs amwe amwe (MP3, H.264...) ku buryo busanzwe, kubera imvo zijanye n'amategeko. Iyi nkuru ikurikira yongerako ibi bihambaye Elements:



```bash
sudo apt install ubuntu-restricted-extras
```



#### Ibishushanyo n'imiterere



Ku bijanye no guhindura amafoto no gushushanya, hariho ibimenyetso bibiri vy'inkomoko yuguruye:



```bash
sudo apt install gimp inkscape
```



GIMP ni porogaramu iteye imbere yo guhindura amafoto, igereranywa na Adobe Photoshop, Inkscape na yo ni porogaramu y’ibishushanyo vy’ibishushanyo, igereranywa na Adobe Illustrator.



Ku bijanye no guhindura amasanamu, urashobora gushiramwo Kdenlive, ikaba ari nziza, ishobora gutahurwa kandi ibereye abatangura n’abateye imbere:



```bash
sudo apt install kdenlive
```



Ku bijanye no guhindura amajwi, hariho Audacity



```bash
sudo apt install audacity
```



Ku bijanye no gufata amajwi, gutangaza canke gukora amasanamu, hariho OBS Studio



```bash
sudo apt install obs-studio
```



#### Ibikoresho vyo guteza imbere



Niba uri umuhinguzi, ushobora gushiramwo ibidukikije vy'ishimikiro vya C/C++, Git, n'ibindi bikoresho n'iri tegeko:



```bash
sudo apt install build-essential git curl
```



Gushiramwo VSCode



```bash
sudo snap install code --classic
```



Uretse ibi bikoresho bikeyi vy’ishimikiro, ndagusavye kandi gushiramwo ibikoresho vy’umutekano vy’ingenzi bihuye n’ingene ukoresha, cane cane umucungerezi w’ijambobanga na VPN:



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

Ubwa nyuma, kugira ngo dusozere iki kigabane, ng’ibi ibintu vyiza bikeyi umuntu yokurikiza ku musi ku musi:





- Koresha itegeko rya `sudo` gusa igihe bikenewe cane. Iri tegeko riduza uburenganzira bwawe bwo gukora igikorwa nk'umuyobozi. Ikosa rya `sudo` (nk'akarorero `rm -rf`) rishobora gutera ingaruka kuri sisitemu yose. Ushobora kandi kwirinda guhindukira ukaja mu buryo bw'imizi (`sudo -i`) mu bihe birebire, kiretse iyo bikenewe cane;





- Naho Ubuntu ikoresha ubwayo ibice bimwe bimwe vy'umutekano biciye ku `unattended-upgrades` service, ivyo ntibifata porogaramu zose. Ushobora gukora ivugurura ry'amaboko ryose ubudasiba:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade
```



N'iki gice ku vy'ishimikiro vya Ubuntu, ubu ufise ibidukikije vya Linux bikora, bihoraho bibereye gukoreshwa buri musi. Urazi gushiramwo porogarama, gutunganya urubuga rwawe, kuguma ukoresha ubuhinga bwawe, no gufasha biciye ku nzira y’amabwirizwa.



Ukwo kwigenga mu buryo bw’ubuhinga ni wo mushinge w’ingenzi wo kwegera igice gisigaye c’iyi nyigisho yizigiye. Mu gice gikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano w’aho ukorera maze dushire mu ngiro ingingo za mbere zitomoye zo gukomeza ubushobozi bwawo bwo kwihangana.






# Gukingira mudasobwa yawe


<partId>7fda3e41-ff0e-4fa0-8bd5-350d9ad5bbec</partId>



## Kwemeza n'ugucapura


<chapterId>c8350e86-5581-4d51-8207-fd4ee48502a7</chapterId>



Umutekano wa mudasobwa yawe utangura n’ivyiyumviro bibiri bihambaye mu mutekano wo kuri interineti: kwemeza n’ugucapura. Izo nzira zibiri ni zo zishingirako gukingira neza imashini yawe, kuzigama ubuzima bwite bwawe no kumenya neza ubusegaba bwawe bwa digitale. Muri iki gice, tuzokwihweza mu buryo bwimbitse ingene wocungera ivyo bintu kuri mudasobwa yawe.



### Gukingira mudasobwa yawe



Gukingira uburenganzira bwo gukoresha mudasobwa yawe mu buryo bw’umubiri no mu buryo bwa porogarama ni co gishingiyeko umutekano wayo. Imashini idakingiye irashobora guhinduka bitagoranye aho umuntu yinjira canke igatuma amakuru y’agaciro asohoka, mbere n’aho ata n’umwe afise Internet. Waba ukoresha Windows, macOS canke Linux, hariho ingingo nyinshi z’ishimikiro ukeneye gushiramwo kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo gushika ku rubuga ata wemerewe.



#### Ijambobanga rya sisitemu



Ijambobanga ry’ikiganiro (iryo usabwa igihe utanguye canke igihe uvyutse mu mva) ni ryo nzitizi ya mbere ku kugerageza kwinjira. Bibuza uwundi muntu gushika ku makuru yawe canke gukoresha nabi sisitemu yawe iyo imashini yawe yibwe canke isigaye ata wuyicungera.



Iri jambobanga ritegerezwa kuba rikomeye:




- Bitegerezwa kuba bihagije. Muri iki gihe (Kamena 2025), ndasaba ko habaho inyuguti 20 n’imiburiburi;
- Itegerezwa gufatanya inyuguti nini n’into, imibare n’inyuguti zidasanzwe;
- Bikwiye kuba ivy’imburakimazi uko bishoboka kwose, kandi ntibibemwo amahuza yose aja kuri Elements y’ibidukikije vyawe bitaziguye canke bitaziguye, nk’izina, itariki canke ahantu.



![Image](assets/fr/201.webp)



*Isoko: [Imirongo y'imizinga](https://www.imirongo y'imizinga.com/)*



Ijambobanga ritoroshe nta gukeka ko rigoye kwibuka. Ndabahimiriza rero gukoresha umucungerezi w’ijambobanga nka Bitwarden canke KeePass.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

Ubwa nyuma, nuhindure iryo jambobanga ubudasiba—inyuma y’amezi 3 canke 6—na canecane nimba imashini yawe ikoreshwa ahantu abantu bose bakoresha canke aho abantu bakoresha telefone ngendanwa.



#### Gukingira BIOS/UEFI



Umutekano wa mudasobwa yawe ntutangura iyo ubuhinga bwo gukoresha bumaze gutangura, ahubwo utangura kuva mu ntango. Imbere y’uko Windows, Linux canke macOS mbere zikora, porogarama yinjijwe muri motherboard, yitwa BIOS canke UEFI, bivanye n’uruvyaro rw’imashini yawe, ifata ububasha ku mashini kugira ngo itanguze hardware maze itanguze igikorwa co gufungura.



BIOS (*Igikoresho c’Ishingiro c’Injira/Isohoka*) ni co cabanjirije UEFI (*Iporogarama y’Igihugu Interface*). Muri iki gihe, UEFI ni co kigereranyo kiri kuri mudasobwa zose zo muri iki gihe.



Ku mburabuzi, ukwinjira muri ivyo bipimo ntibirinzwe. Umuntu atera afise uburenganzira bwo gushika ku mashine yawe (mu kibanza rusangi, mu gihe habaye ubusuma canke mbere mu gihe gito ataco uzi) yoshobora kwinjira muri Interface UEFI maze agahindura ibintu bihambaye. Yashobora, nk’akarorero:




- Guhindura urutonde rwo gufungura kugira ngo ukoreshe ku nguvu uburyo bwo hanze buvuye ku rufunguzo rwa USB
- Guhagarika uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano nka Secure Boot
- Gushiramwo porogaramu mbi muri mudasobwa yawe...



Kugira ngo wikingire ivyo bitero bitari mu nzira, birahambaye ko ufunga uburenganzira bwo kwinjira muri BIOS/UEFI ukoresheje ijambobanga. Iryo jambobanga ritandukanye n’ijambobanga rya sisitemu yawe kandi ribuza umuntu adashobora kwinjira muri BIOS/UEFI ata wemerewe.



Kugira ngo uyikoreshe, bizovana n'umuderi wa motherboard yawe, ariko muri rusangi ukeneye:




- Subiramwo mudasobwa yawe
- Ubwo nyene inyuma y'ugufungura, kanda ningoga urufunguzo rwo gushika kuri BIOS/UEFI rwihariye ku mashini yawe (`Del`, `F2`, `F10`, `Esc`...)
- Mu Interface iboneka, nurondere amahitamwo y’ijambobanga ry’umutekano canke ry’umuyobozi .
- Shiraho ijambobanga rirerire, ridasanzwe kandi ridasanzwe, hanyuma uribike
- Bika ivyo wahinduye hanyuma wongere utangure mudasobwa



![Image](assets/fr/203.webp)



**Imburi:** iyo utakaje iri jambo banga, uzobuzwa kandi uzobwirizwa gusubiramwo motherboard. Rero, nubone ko ubika iryo jambobanga mu kibanza co gucungera ijambobanga canke ahantu hatagira umutekano.



Ikindi, fungura "Secure Boot" nimba iriho kandi itarakora. Ubu buryo burabuza kode itashizweko umukono canke ihinduwe gukora igihe co gutangura. Ikoreshwa mu guhagarika bootkits na rootkits, ubwoko bw’ibintu bibi bishobora kwanduza boot ya mudasobwa, mbere n’imbere y’uko OS itangura gukora.



Gukingira UEFI ni ikintu gikunda kwirengagizwa ariko gihambaye cane co kurinda imashini yawe ibitero biteye imbere. Ni kimwe mu bihome bikeyi bikingira ukwinjira mu mubiri canke gukoresha nabi imbere y’urutonde.



#### Gucungera uburenganzira bwo gukoresha mudasobwa



Gukingira ikibanza co gukoreramwo ntibigarukira ku gukingira porogarama gusa: iyo umuntu w’umunyaruyeri aronse uburenganzira bwo gushika ku mashine yawe, arashobora guca ku nzitizi nyinshi canke agatuma iyo porogarama ihungabana ataco uzi. Ivyo ni ko biri canecane ku ma laptops, yoroshe gutwara, ariko kandi ku gikoresho cose gisigaye mu kibanza gisangiye, kifunguriwe abantu bose canke mbere gishobora gushikirwa n’abandi bantu gusa.



Kimwe mu bitera ingorane (ariko bikaba bifatwa nk’ibidahambaye) ni ugusiga mudasobwa ata wuyicungera, mbere n’iminota mikeyi, mu bibanza vya bose nk’amasomero, amakoraniro, ahantu hafunguye no mu bibanza vy’amahoteli. Ivyo si ingorane gusa yo kwiba: mu masegonda makeyi, umuntu w’umunyaruyeri arashobora gufatanya inkoni ya USB mbi, akashiramwo porogarama y’ubutasi, agahindura amaparametere y’ugufungura kugira ngo ahate gufungura hanze, canke agafata amakuru y’ivyemezo mu gutera igikoresho citwa hardware keylogger.



Muri iyo nzira nyene, ndabagira inama yo kudakoresha ibikoresho vyo hanze canke ibikoresho vyo hanze udashobora kugenzura. Irinde kwinjiza muri mudasobwa yawe inkoni za USB, ama drive ya Hard yo hanze, ama chargeur canke ama dongle iyo inkomoko y’ivyo bintu itazwi (bishasha canke vy’umuntu wizigira). Ibikoresho bimwebimwe bisa n’ibitagira akamaro bishobora kuba birimwo ama circuits ashobora gukora amabwirizwa mabi igihe nyene bishizwemwo. Ku rundi ruhande, ntugurize ibikoresho vyawe bwite canke ngo ubisige ata wubicungera ahantu umuntu ashobora kubironka: vyoshobora guhindurwa n’ibindi bikoresho bishobora gukoreshwa nabi.



Kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo kwiba, urashobora gukoresha PC yo ku biro ubuhinga bwo gufunga. PC nyinshi z’abahinga zifise ikibanza co gucungera umutekano citwa Kensington, kikaba gituma umuntu ashobora gufata umugozi w’icuma ku kintu kidahinduka. Ivyiyumviro bitandukanye biraboneka kandi ku ma laptops. Birumvikana ko ivyo bikoresho bitatanga uburinzi bushitse ku busuma, mugabo birahagije kugira ngo umuntu ahagarike ibitero vy’akaryo.



![Image](assets/fr/202.webp)



Vyongeye, wama uzimya imashini yawe iyo uri kure yayo, canecane iyo uri ahantu hatagira umutekano. Udakunze standby yoroshe, gufunga burundu bibuza OS gukora, kandi bikarinda ibitero bimwe bimwe bitera RAM. Iratuma kandi umutekano wawe wa BIOS/UEFI ukora.



Ubwa nyuma, imwe mu ngingo zihambaye cane ushobora gufata kugira ngo wikingire ubusuma ni ugukoresha ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru yose kuri disiki. Ivyo bikingira amakuru yawe mu gutuma adashobora kuyaronka ata jambobanga, naho iyo disiki yoba yakuwemwo maze igashirwa mu yindi mashini. Kuri sisitemu zimwe zimwe, ubu bubiko bukoreshwa mburabuzi:




- macOS ikoresha ububiko bwa dosiye
- Windows ikoresha BitLocker, ariko gukoresha kwayo bivana n’imashini na verisiyo ya OS .
- Ivyiyumviro vya Linux ntivyihuta gupfuka disiki, kiretse iyo iyo nzira yatowe mu gihe co gushiramwo. Ushobora gukoresha LUKS kugira ngo ushiremwo amakuru kuri disiki


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/luks-13d9928b-08b1-478c-a1b4-67617978584a

Mu bihe vyose, ijambobanga ryo gukuraho ritegerezwa kuba rikomeye, ritandukanye n’ijambobanga rya sisitemu, kandi rikabikwa mu mucungerezi w’ijambobanga ry’umutekano. Niba uriko urakoresha disiki y’inyuma canke urufunguzo rwa USB rurimwo amakuru y’agaciro, nuzirikane kandi kuyapfuka umwumwe wese ukoresheje ibikoresho nka VeraCrypt.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/veracrypt-d5ed4c83-7c1c-4181-95ea-963fdf2d83c5

### Ingingo ngenderwako y'agateka gatoyi



Ingingo ngenderwako y’uburenganzira bukeyi ni itegeko ry’ishimikiro mu mutekano wo kuri interineti, rivuga ko ikigo cose (umuntu akoresha, porogarama ya porogarama, uburyo bwo gukora, n’ibindi) gikwiye gusa kugira uburenganzira bukenewe cane kugira ngo gishobore gukora ibikorwa vyaco. Mu yandi majambo, ntukigere utanga uburenganzira bwinshi kuruta uko bikenewe, kuko uburenganzira bwose bwongereweko bwongera uburebure bw’igitero c’urwo rutonde.



Mu majambo nyayo, kuri mudasobwa yawe bwite, ivyo bisigura ko konti yawe nyamukuru y’ukoresha idategerezwa kuba ifise uburenganzira bw’umuyobozi ku bikorwa vya misi yose: gusura urubuga, gusuzuma imeyili, gukora ibikorwa vyo mu biro, n’ibindi. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo ikoreshwa ahantu hazitiwe, ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutera akaga buzoba buke.



Kuri Windows, benshi mu bakoresha barafise konti y’umuyobozi ku buryo busanzwe, naho ivyo ari umugenzo mubi. Ndagusavye gukora konti y'ukoresha isanzwe yo gukoresha buri musi, maze ugasiga konti y'umuyobozi ku bikorwa biyikeneye vy'ukuri. Iyo ugerageje gukora igikorwa gisaba uburenganzira bwo hejuru, Windows izogusaba gusa kwinjiza ijambobanga ry'umuyobozi aho gukanda gusa ku buto "*EGO*".



![Image](assets/fr/204.webp)



Mu nsi ya Linux, iyo ngingo y’agateka gatoyi cane irakoreshwa neza. Ku mburabuzi, ufise konti y'ukoresha ifise uburenganzira buke, kandi ushobora kuduza uburenganzira bwawe mu gihe gito ukoresheje itegeko `sudo`. Birashoboka kandi gutunganya `sudo` kugira ngo yemere amabwirizwa amwe amwe gusa bivanye n'ukoresha (biciye muri `/etc/sudoers`).



![Image](assets/fr/064.webp)



Kuri macOS, naho konti ya mbere yaremwe kenshi ifise uburenganzira bwo gutwara, iyo sisitemu ikoresha uburyo busa na `sudo`: ukeneye kwemeza ibikorwa vyawe ukoresheje ijambobanga ry’igikorwa cose gihambaye. Naho biri ukwo, birashoboka cane gukora konti y’ukoresha isanzwe no kubika konti y’umuyobozi kugira ngo ukoreshe rimwe na rimwe, ivyo ndabihanura nimba mudasobwa ikoreshwa n’abantu benshi.



Ukwo gucapura ntikugarukira ku bantu bakoresha gusa. Porogaramu nyinshi zisaba uburenganzira bwo hejuru ku gushiramwo, hanyuma zikabandanya zikorana n’ubwo burenganzira iyo zitagikenewe. Ndaguhanura rero, aho bishoboka hose, guhitamwo porogarama zikora mu buryo bw’ukoresha, gukuraho porogarama utagikoresha, no kuba maso ku bijanye n’ugusaba gushirwa hejuru kw’uburenganzira.



### Ivyigwa vyinshi: ibidukikije bitandukanye



Uretse gutandukanya amakonti y’abarongozi n’amakonti asanzwe, uburyo bwiza bwo kwuzuza ni uguhingura ibiganiro vy’abakoresha bitandukanye kuri mudasobwa imwe kugira ngo ugabanye ikoreshwa bivanye n’ingene bimeze. Ubwo buryo bushingiye ku nsiguro yoroshe: mu gucapura ibikorwa vyawe mu bidukikije bitandukanye, ugabanya igitero c’ibidukikije vyose kandi ugabanura ingaruka z’ikintu cose co mu mutekano.



Uburyo bwose bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none buratuma umuntu ashobora gukora amakonti menshi ku mashini imwe. Izo konti imwe yose irafise ikibanza ciwe bwite: amadosiye, amaporogarama, amasetingi n’ibiganiro vy’urubuga ntibisangira hagati yayo, kiretse iyo vyemewe mu buryo butomoye.



Nk’akarorero, woshobora gutunganya ibiganiro vyawe gutya:




- Konti yihariye igikorwa cawe c’umwuga, aho ushiramwo gusa porogarama ukeneye cane (amasuite y’ibiro, ibikoresho vyo gukorana, ubutumwa bw’umwuga...). Iki kiganiro ntigitegerezwa gukoreshwa mu gusura urubuga ku buntu canke mu kugerageza porogarama;
- Konti yo gukoresha umuntu ku giti ciwe, ikoreshwa mu gusura urubuga rwa misi yose, mu gukorana n’abandi, mu gukurikirana amakuru, canke mu gushiramwo porogarama z’abaguzi. Iyi ni yo session ishobora guterwa cane n’ibitero vy’umucukumbuzi canke ibintu biteye amakenga;
- Konti yagenewe ibikorwa bihambaye, nk’ugusaba amakonte ya banki, gucunga amakete yawe ya Bitcoin, canke ikindi gikoresho cose gisaba umutekano mwinshi. Iyi konti ikwiye gukoreshwa gusa muri ivyo bikorwa, hakaba harimwo porogarama zishizwemwo zigarukira ku vyo bikenewe cane, kandi hakaba harimwo n’imiterere y’urubuga ikomeye kuruta;
- Konti y’umushyitsi canke ibujijwe cane, igenewe gusa gukoreshwa rimwe na rimwe n’abagize umuryango, nk’akarorero. Iyi konti itegerezwa kuba idafise uburenganzira bwo kuyirongora kandi ikaba ifise uburenganzira buke bwo kuyironka.



Hariho ivyiza vyinshi vyo gukoresha iyo nzira. Ica mbere, amaporogarama ashizwe mu kiganiro ntashobora guhungabanya ay’abandi (kiretse iyo umuntu ashizwe hejuru y’agateka). Ica kabiri, iyo ikiganiro giteye akaga, nk’akarorero biciye ku buhinga bubi bwavuye kuri interineti, ingaruka muri rusangi ziri mu mipaka y’iyo konti. Ivyo bisigura ko inyandiko zawe z’ubudandaji canke ibitabo vyawe vya Bitcoin bizoguma bidashobora gushikirwa n’ibintu bibi iyo bibitswe mu kindi kiganiro, kiri ukwaco neza.



Kuri Linux, ukwo gutandukanya gushobora gukomezwa n’uburyo nka AppArmor canke SELinux, bushobora gukoreshwa mu kurushirizaho kugabanya uburenganzira bwo gushika ku kiganiro cose.



![Image](assets/fr/205.webp)



Ni ngombwa kumenya ko multisession idasubirira gukoresha konti itari umuyobozi, canke gukoresha ingingo ngenderwako y'agateka gatoyi. Irawuzuza mu kwongerako Layer y’ukwitandukanya kw’ubwenge, yoroshe gushinga kandi ikora neza cane ku muryango w’abanyavyaha canke mu gukoresha abahinga.



Ubwa nyuma, ubundi buryo, bukomeye kuruta ariko bukora neza cane, ni ugutanga orodinateri itandukanye ku bijanye n’ikoreshwa ryose, nk’akarorero: laptop imwe ikoreshwa gusa mu bikorwa vy’umwuga, iyindi ikoreshwa n’umuntu ku giti ciwe, n’iya gatatu yoroshe kandi icungiwe neza igenewe ibikorwa bihambaye.



### Imashini zitaboneka



Imashini zitaboneka (canke "VMs") zigufasha gukora ibidukikije vyihariye muri mudasobwa yawe. VM yigana mudasobwa yigenga ifise uburyo bwayo bwo gukoresha, ibikorwa vyayo n’imiterere yayo, ariko mu vy’ukuri ikora nk’iporogarama ikora ku mashine yawe nyamukuru.



Ubu buhinga bushingiye kuri hypervisor, ni porogarama icungera uguhingura no gushirwa mu ngiro kw’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Umuti uzwi cane ni VirtualBox, ni porogarama yuguruye, ikoreshwa ku mbuga zitandukanye. Bituma vyoroha gukora VM mu gukanda bike gusa, mu kuyiha ibikoresho vyihariye.



![Image](assets/fr/206.webp)


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/virtualbox-6472f5be-10ce-4a07-8b24-097bfbcedd65

Ku bijanye n’umutekano w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none, kimwe mu vyiza bikomeye vy’amamashini y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none ni ubushobozi bwo gucapura. VM ntisangira amadosiye yayo, imigenderanire canke uburyo bwo gushika ku rubuga n'umurongo w'abashitsi, kiretse utunganije neza ivyo biganiro. Rero iyo VM yandujwe na malware, canke iyo ugerageje porogarama zikomeye ziri muri yo, ingaruka ziguma kuri iyo mashini y’ukuri: sisitemu yawe nyamukuru iguma ari iyo nyene, igihe cose amaparametere y’ukwitandukanya yubahirijwe (nta bubiko busangiye, nta bikoresho vya USB bica kuri VM...).



VM irashobora kugufasha kugerageza porogarama zikekwa: iyo ukuye porogarama ku nzira idashobora kwizigirwa canke ku rubuga ruteye amakenga, urashobora kubanza kuyikoresha muri VM kugira ngo ubone inyifato yayo mu mutekano wose. Ivyo birashobora kandi kuba ngirakamaro igihe uriko urasura imbuga zishobora gutera ingorane: urashobora gutanga VM ku bijanye no kuganira ku bintu bihambaye canke bitazwi, ivyo bikaba bigabanya amahirwe y’ibitero vy’inyandiko mbi canke gukoresha nabi ubugoyagoye bw’umucukumbuzi. Muri make: gukoresha VM bigufasha gutandukanya mu buryo bworoshe ikoreshwa ry’ibintu bimwebimwe n’ibindi bikoresho vyawe.



Ubwa nyuma, birahambaye gutahura ko umutekano utangwa na VMs uvana n’ingene zitunganijwe neza. Ku mburabuzi, abagenzuzi bamwebamwe bemerera uguhana amadosiye hagati y'umushitsi na VM, canke bakemerera gushika ku bikoresho vya USB. Ivyo bikorwa bikwiye guhagarara kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kwitandukanya cane.



### Gutera umusenyi



Sandboxing ni uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano wa mudasobwa bujanye n’ugukoresha porogarama canke igikorwa mu kibanza kiri ukwaco, gifise uburenganzira bwinshi. Intumbero ni uguhagarika cane ukuntu porogarama ikorana n’ibindi bice vyo muri sisitemu. Iyo habaye ikintu co gutera ubwoba, ingaruka zaco zisanzwe ziri muri iyo nzira.



Mu buryo butandukanye n’amamashini y’ivy’impwemu, yigana uburyo bwo gukoresha bushitse bufise ubutunzi bwayo bwite, sandboxing iraremereye, iranyaruka gukoreshwa kandi ntikoresha ubutunzi bwinshi. Ishingiye ku buryo bwo kugabanya uburenganzira bwo kuronka: ku buhinga bwo kwibuka, ku madosiye, ku rubuga, ku bikoresho vyo ku ruhande... Porogaramu y’umusenyi ishobora, nk’akarorero, gusoma dosiye y’igihe gito ariko ntiyigere yinjira ku bubiko bwawe bwite canke kuri sisitemu y’amadosiye.



Aha hariho inyishu zitomoye zo gukora sandboxing, bivanye n'ivyo OS yawe ikoresha:



**Idirisha**




- Windows Sandbox (iboneka gusa muri Windows 10/11 Pro n’Ishirahamwe);
- Sandboxie Plus (inkomoko yuguruye).



**Linukisi**




- Firejail: igikoresho gikomeye, gifise uburemere buke gitandukanya ibikorwa hakoreshejwe imirongo yategekanijwe mbere. Ikora neza n’ibikoresho vyinshi, harimwo Firefox, VLC na Telegram;
- Flatpak: nk’uko twamaze kubibona, iyi si porogarama ya sanboxing ubwayo, ahubwo ni umucungerezi w’amaporogarama afatanya sandboxing: porogarama yose ishizwemwo biciye kuri Flatpak iri ukwayo n’umurongo w’abashitsi ku buryo busanzwe, ifise ubugenzuzi bwiza bw’uburenganzira (ugushika ku mikoro, kamera, urubuga, n’ibindi).



**MacOS**




- Kuri macOS, sandboxing ni ikintu c’akavukire cubatswe muri kernel, ariko gikora gusa iyo kigaragajwe n’uwakoze porogarama. Porogaramu za App Store zihita zishirwa mu gasandugu k’umusenyi, ariko izo zishizweho zivuye ku rubuga (canke zivuye ku murongo w’amabwirizwa) ntizishirwa mu gasandugu k’umusenyi ku buryo busanzwe.



Ubwa nyuma, naho sandboxing itanga uburinzi bwiza bwa Layer, birahambaye gutahura ko atari ugusubirira VM canke uburyo bugabanywe neza.



Ubu ko twamaze kuvuga ibijanye n’umutekano wa mudasobwa yawe biciye mu kwemeza ko ari yo no kuyishira mu bice, mu kigabane gikurikira tuzorabira ku buryo bwiza bwo kuyibungabunga kugira ngo urushirizeho umutekano wayo.



## Kugabanya amakosa biciye mu gusanasana


<chapterId>71d7fd95-ce1d-43d8-9a66-be7b425857fc</chapterId>



Abantu benshi biyumvira ko gushiramwo porogarama zikingira virusi canke guhitamwo ijambobanga ryiza bihagije kugira ngo bakingire mudasobwa yabo. Ariko hariho vyinshi ku mutekano wa mudasobwa kuruta gutunganya rimwe gusa. Ukuri ni ugukomeye kuruta: ibitero vyinshi vyo kuri Internet bikoresha ubugoyagoye buri mu bikoresho n’amaporogarama vya kera. Mu yandi majambo, umutekano wa orodinateri na wo nyene usaba ko udasiba gutunganya imashini yawe.



Muri iki gice, nzogutwara intambwe ku yindi mu buryo bwo kubungabunga neza mudasobwa yawe, no kugabanya ingorane zo gusenyuka.



### Ubuvuguruzi bwa sisitemu



Nk’uko twabibonye mu ntango y’iri shure, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha buracungera ibikoresho (processeur, memory, disques, périphériques, n’ibindi), burashitsa porogarama, buratunganya amadosiye kandi buracungera amahuzu y’urubuga. Ni co gituma ari ikintu gihambaye cane kiri ku mashine yawe.



#### Ni kuki wohindura OS yawe?



Kubera ko igoye cane, nta verisiyo ya OS idafise ubushobozi bwo guhungabana. Aha turiko turavuga ivy’imirongo y’amakode igera ku miriyoni mirongo. Ivyo bihimba vy’umutekano birashobora gukoreshwa n’abatera kugira ngo bakore kode mbi, baronke uburenganzira butaremewe canke ngo bashire mu kaga urutonde rwose. Bimwe muri ivyo bigoranye bivumburwa n’abashakashatsi mu vy’umutekano wo kuri internet mu buryo bubereye, mu gihe ibindi bimaze gukoreshwa n’umwete ata bantu bose babizi: ivyo bizwi kw’izina ry’ibigoranye vy’umunsi zero.



Abagurisha porogarama z’ibikorwa barasohora ubudasiba amakuru mashasha y’umutekano agenewe gukosora izo ngorane. Kudashiramwo izo nkuru ni nk’ugusiga n’ibigirankana urugi rwuguruye kugira ngo umuntu akureho ibitero, naho woba wibaza ko uko ukoresha ibintu ari bike canke ko amakuru yawe ata co amaze.



Si ikibazo co gukosora ibibazo bibonetse gusa, ariko ni ugukora ku bitero vya sisitemu yawe. Uko ama vecteur aba make, niko n’abatera ama levers bake bategerezwa gutera imashini yawe.



Mu buryo bwihariye, ndagusavye ko woshoboza ivyagezwe vyihuta. Ico kintu kiraboneka ku bikoresho vyose vyo muri iki gihe. Nk’akarorero, Windows Update irakora ivyo ku mashini za Windows 10 na 11. Ku macOS, ivyagezwe vy’umutekano bishirwa muri sisitemu y’ivyagezwe. Kuri Linux, bivanye n'ugukwiragira kwakoreshejwe, ibikoresho nka `uguhindura-bitagira uwubicungera` (Debian/Ubuntu) canke `dnf-vyikora` (Fedora) bigufasha gutegura ivy'uguhindura.



Ubwa nyuma, nuzirikane yuko kenshi, ibintu bimwebimwe bihambaye bihindurwa bitangura gukora gusa inyuma yo gusubira gufungura. Ni ngombwa rero ko usubira gufungura imashini yawe ubudasiba, cane cane inyuma y’uguhindura system. Guhindura ubuhinga bwawe bwo gukoresha akenshi bifata iminota mikeyi gusa, ariko ni kimwe mu bintu bifasha cane gukingira ibitero vyinshi.



#### None OS yanje noyihindura gute?



Naho nyene ivyagezwe vyihuta bishobora gukoreshwa kuri sisitemu yawe, biracari bihambaye ko usuzuma n’amaboko, mu bihe bitandukanye, ko ata bihembo bitegerejwe. Reka turabe ingene ivyo wobikora, bivanye n'uko ukoresha:





- Sisitemu ikoreshwa ya Windows*



Windows ifise umuyobozi w'ivugurura yitwa "Ivugurura rya Windows". Ivyo bica bikuramwo ibintu bishasha, ibintu vy’umutekano, abashoferi b’ibikoresho, rimwe na rimwe mbere n’imikorode y’ico gikoresho.



Kugira ngo ugenzure n'amaboko uko ivyagezwe bimeze :



```txt
Settings → Windows Update → Check for updates
```



Ntimwibagire kuraba ko hariho ibintu bishasha bitari vyo muri iyo menu nyene.





- Linux* uburyo bwo gukoresha



Ivyiyumviro vya Linux bishingiye ku buryo bw'amapaki abungabungwa n'abanyagihugu n'abacungera ivyimburwa vyawe. Ivyagezwe bishirwa mu ngiro biciye ku mucungerezi w'amapaki.



Munsi ya Debian (ni ukuvuga Ubuntu) :



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade -y
```



![Image](assets/fr/213.webp)



Niba ushaka gukoresha Interface y'ibishushanyo, kuri Ubuntu hariho igikoresho ca *Software Updater* kigufasha gucunga ivyahinduwe mu buryo bworoshe utaciye muri terminal.



![Image](assets/fr/214.webp)



Munsi y'inkofero itukura (Fedora) :



```bash
sudo dnf upgrade
```



Munsi ya Linux :



```bash
sudo pacman -Syu
```






- MacOS* uburyo bwo gukoresha



Apple ishira hamwe ivyagezwe vyayo mu mirongo ya Interface. Kugira ngo umenye ko biriho:



```txt
Apple menu → System Settings → General → Software Update
```



macOS ihita ikuraho umutekano, sisitemu n'ibikorwa bishasha biciye ku nzira ya "*Automatic Updates*" iri muri iyo menyu nyene.



![Image](assets/fr/212.webp)



### Ivugurura rya porogaramu



Umutekano wa mudasobwa yawe ntuvana gusa n’uburyo ukoresha. Igipande cose ca porogarama ushiramwo kigereranya ahantu hashobora kwinjira ibitero. Porogarama ikimara kuba ifise akaga k’umutekano katakosowe, irashobora gukoreshwa kugira ngo ihungabanye sisitemu yawe canke yibe amakuru yawe.



Hariho porogarama zimwe zimwe zishobora gukora cane kuruta izindi, kuko zikorana n’isi yo hanze canke zigakoresha amadosiye ashobora kuba ari ay’urwanko. Mu bikoresho bihambaye cane harimwo :





- Web browsers*: ni zo zibanza gutera, kuko zikora ibintu bitagenzuwe mu gihe nyaco kandi zifise ahantu hanini cane ho gutera. Ikindi kandi, zifise uruhara runini mu kurinda amakuru yawe bwite. Kandi, ikiruta vyose, zikunda gusubirira porogarama nyinshi zahora zikoreshwa mu karere (aba clients ba e-mail, ama suites y’ibiro, aba media players...). Ariko tuzogaruka kuri iyo ngingo mu gice gikurikira c’inyigisho ya SCU202;





- Abaguzi b’ubutumwa*: baronka ama attachement canke ama links ava hanze adashobora kugenzurwa rero akagira ingorane;





- Ibikoresho vyo guhanahana amakuru* (TeamViewer, Zoom, Signal, Teams...): kubera uburyo bikorana, ni vyo bitera ibitero vy’ubutasi canke bigerageza gukoreshwa kure. Mu buryo bumwe n’ubw’abaguzi ba e-mail, ibikoresho vyo guhanahana amakuru birashobora gukoreshwa nk’ibikoresho vyo kugerageza guhenda canke gukwiragiza ibintu bitari vyo;





- Antivirus, firewall n’ibindi bikoresho vyo kumenya*: ivyo bikoresho muri rusangi birafise uburenganzira bwo hejuru, kuko biguma bipima amadosiye yawe, imigenderanire yawe n’imigenderanire y’urubuga. Ishingiro ry’umukono rya kera, ugutunganya nabi canke ubugoyagoye muri porogarama ubwayo birashobora gutuma porogarama mbi zitamenyekana, canke mbere zikaronka uburenganzira bwo hejuru.



Ego ni ko, ivyo bibazo ntibiva gusa ku bijanye no kuvyitaho nabi, mugabo birahambaye ko umuntu yitwararika canecane guhindura izo porogarama zihambaye cane. Nzorosha hano, ariko birashoboka, n’izindi porogarama zawe zose na zo nyene zikeneye guhindurwa ubudasiba. Reka turabe ingene wobikora nyene, bivanye n’uko ukoresha ubuhinga bwawe.



#### Munsi y'amadirisha



Kuri Windows 11, ubuhinga bwa *Winget* burashirwa muri iyo sisitemu. Iragufasha gutanga urutonde no guhindura porogarama nyinshi zishizwe kuri mudasobwa yawe, uciye kuri terminal. Gusa gukoresha Windows:



```CMD
winget upgrade --all
```



Iri tegeko risaba ububiko bwa bose ku bijanye n’amaverisiyo mashasha ya porogarama ufise, maze rikabihindura ubwavyo.



![Image](assets/fr/211.webp)



Ikibabaje, iri tegeko ntirikora kuri porogaramu zose. Ni co gituma ndagusavye ko wobika urutonde rw’amaporogarama yawe yose kandi ukagenzura n’amaboko ko hariho ibintu bishasha ubudasiba, cane cane ku bikoresho bihambaye. Ku bijanye na porogarama zihambaye cane, nk’ivyo ukoresha mu gukingira virusi canke umucukumbuzi w’urubuga, ndaguhanura ko wokora iyo nsuzuma ku musi ku musi.



#### Munsi ya Linux (Debiyani/Ubuntu)



Inkomezi z’ugukwiragiza Linux ziri mu gucunga porogarama zabo zihuriwe hamwe. Umuyobozi w'amapaki (`APT` mu gihe ca Debian) agumana uburyo n'amaporogarama yose yashizweho biciye mu bubiko buzwi.



Mu buryo bumwe n'ubwo ku bijanye n'ivugurura rya OS, kugira ngo ukore ivugurura ry'isi yose rya porogaramu yawe, genda gusa:



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade
```



Iri tegeko ry'ishimikiro risubiramwo urutonde rw'ibikoresho biriho (`apt update`) hanyuma rigakoresha ivyagezwe bikenewe (`apt upgrade`).



Kugira ngo ubone ivugurura ryuzuye, ushobora gukoresha iri tegeko:



```bash
sudo apt update \
&& sudo apt full-upgrade -y \
&& sudo apt autoremove -y \
&& sudo apt autoclean
```





- `sudo apt full-upgrade` ihindura amapaki yose yashizweho, harimwo n'ayo asaba ko ibindi bishingiyeko vyongerwako canke bikurwaho. `-y` iguha uburenganzira bwo kwishura "egome" ku kwemeza kwose umuyobozi w'amapaki ashobora kugusaba;
- `sudo apt gukuraho -y`: gukuraho ibidakenewe ;
- sudo apt autoclean`: isukura ububiko bw'amapaki ya kera.



![Image](assets/fr/215.webp)



Niba ufise porogaramu zikwiragizwa nk’amapaki ya Flatpak canke Snap, zimwe zirahindurwa ubwazo, ariko ushobora kuzihindura zose n’amaboko ukoresheje itegeko:



```bash
flatpak update sudo snap refresh
```



#### Munsi ya macOS



Porogaramu zishizwemwo biciye ku App Store zishobora guhindurwa bitagoranye muri ibi bikurikira:



```txt
Apple menu → App Store → Update All
```



Ushobora kandi gukoresha ubuhinga bushasha bwikora mu mategeko ya App Store.



Ariko rero, si porogarama zose zishizwe kuri Mac yawe ziva muri App Store. Ku bindi bikoresho, uzobwirizwa kubihindura n’amaboko. Rero, nk’uko bigenda ku bakoresha Windows, ndagusavye ko wobika urutonde rwa porogarama zawe zose kandi ukaguma usuzuma ko hariho verisiyo nshasha, cane cane izo zihambaye nk’umucukumbuzi wawe w’urubuga.



### Gukuraho porogaramu



Uvuye ku bijanye n’umutekano w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none, uko ushiramwo porogarama nke, ni ko n’aho umuntu ashobora kwinjira mu gihugu aba ari make. Porogarama yose ishizwe kuri sisitemu yawe yoshobora kuba irimwo imyobo y’umutekano, naho woba utazokwigera uyikoresha. Ivyo bizwi kw’izina ry’ubutaka bw’igitero: uko buba bunini ni ko n’ingorane zirushiriza kuba nyinshi. Kugabanya iyo nzira mu gukuraho porogarama zidakenewe ni uburyo bworoshe ariko bukora neza bwo kwirinda.



Hari porogarama canke porogarama zimwezimwe zashizweho imbere y’igihe kugira ngo zikoreshwe rimwe gusa, zirashobora kuguma kuri orodinateri yawe amezi menshi zitakoreshwa, mu gihe ziguma zironka amakuru mashasha canke zikorana na sisitemu yawe. Ikibi kuruta, iyo izo porogarama zitagitunganijwe, zishobora kuba zirimwo ibintu bishobora gutuma umuntu agira ingorane.



#### Munsi y'amadirisha



Kugira ngo ubone urutonde rw'ibikoresho vyashizwemwo:



```txt
Settings → Apps → Installed apps
```



Biciye muri uru rutonde rwa porogarama ukureho ikintu cose utagikoresha, canke utazi ico gikoreshwa (inyuma yo gusuzuma vyihuse kuri internet nimba bikenewe). Urabe maso ku bijanye na porogarama za sisitemu, ariko ntukekeranye gukuraho imikino yashizwemwo imbere, ibikoresho vyo kwitaho biteye amakenga canke porogarama zo kwamamaza.



#### Munsi ya Linux (Debiyani/Ubuntu)



Gufungura terminal maze ukoreshe iri tegeko kugira ngo usibe porogaramu:



```bash
sudo apt remove name_of_the_software
```



![Image](assets/fr/216.webp)



Hanyuma ukoreshe iri tegeko kugira ngo ukureho ubwawe ibintu vyose bitagikenewe:



```bash
sudo apt autoremove
```



#### Munsi ya macOS



Munsi ya macOS, hari uburyo 2 nyamukuru: biciye kuri *Launchpad* canke biciye kuri *Finder*. Niba iyo porogarama yavanywe muri App Store, fungura *Launchpad* (kuva muri Dock canke mu bubiko bwa `/Applications`), urondere iyo porogarama, hanyuma ufate urufunguzo rw’Ihitamwo canke ukore igikorwa co gukanda igihe kirekire gushika ibishushanyo bitangura guhungabana. Hanyuma ukande ku musaraba uri iruhande y’ico gikoresho, maze wemeze ko gipfutse.



![Image](assets/fr/210.webp)



Iyo buto yo gukuraho itabonetse, iyo porogarama ntiyashizwe muri App Store. Muri ivyo, koresha *Umurondera*. Ubanza gufunga porogaramu, nimba iriko irakora. Ugurure *Finder*, uje mu bubiko bwa `/Applications`, uhitemwo porogaramu wipfuza gukuraho, hanyuma uyishire mu gitereko c'imyanda co gusubira gukoresha. Ubwa nyuma, n’ushire ubusa mu gitereko c’imyanda kugira ngo urangize gukuraho.



#### Ntukibagire ukwagura umucukumbuzi



Ivyagutse n’ivyongeweko vyo mu mucukumbuzi wawe akenshi birarengagizwa, ariko na vyo nyene bigereranya igitero gikunda gutera. Igikoresho kibi canke ca kera gishobora gufata amakuru yawe yo gusura, kigutera kode canke kigutata mu buryo buteye ubwoba.



Genda mu mirongo y’umucukumbuzi wawe maze uzimye canke usibe ama extensions yose udakoresha canke utazi. Bika gusa ivyo bikenewe cane, bivuye mu bibanza vyizigirwa kandi bikiriho.



### Gukurikirana no kugenzura sisitemu



Umutekano wo kuri Internet kandi urimwo no kugenzura ibikorwa vya sisitemu. Ubwo buryo bwo gukora ibintu bitari vyo buratuma umuntu ashobora kubona inyifato idasanzwe (amasano ateye amakenga, imigenderanire idasanzwe, ukugerageza gushika ku bintu ata wemerewe, n’ibindi) hakiri kare no gufasha imbere y’uko haba ikintu gikomeye.



Iyo ushizeho urutonde rw’igenzura (mbere n’urw’ishimikiro) urashobora kumenya ko hariho porogarama mbi, ama Trojans asinziriye canke porogarama z’ubutasi hakiri kare. Mwene ukwo kugenzura gushobora gukorwa hakoreshejwe ibikoresho vyihariye.



#### Munsi y'amadirisha



Nk’uko twabibonye mu gice ca mbere, Windows mu mateka yarashikiwe cane n’ibitero vya mudasobwa, kubera ukuntu ikoreshwa cane n’ubuhinga bwayo. Ni ngombwa rero kwuzuza uburinzi bw'ishimikiro n'ibikoresho vy'ugupima biteye imbere:





- Microsoft Defender*: kuri Windows, kugira umugera mwiza ni ikintu gikenewe cane. Mu myaka myinshi, Microsoft Defender (yahora yitwa Windows Defender), ari yo nzira yo gukingira virusi yubatswe muri iyo sisitemu, yabonwa ko idashobora kwizigirwa, kandi mu kibanza cayo, hakaba hariho uburyo bwo gutorera umuti ibibazo vy’abandi. Ariko iyo porogarama yarateye imbere cane uko igihe cagenda kirarenga, kandi ubu, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, irahagije kugira ngo itange uburinzi bw’ishimikiro bwo gukoresha umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ivyo bivuzwe, ntidukwiye guha agaciro cane uruhara rwa porogarama zikingira virusi: ni hejuru y’imigenzo yawe bwite y’ubuhinga bwa none ari yo ituma ugira umutekano. Kimwe mu vyiza vya Defender ni uko ikorana na Windows. Uretse uburinzi bw’igihe nyaco, itanga amasanamu yuzuye ushobora gutegura buri ndwi canke ukayakoresha n’amaboko mu bihe bitandukanye.



![Image](assets/fr/007.webp)





- Sysinternals Suite*: iki ni ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none cane bitangwa na Microsoft vyo gupima, gukurikirana no gutorera umuti ingorane za Windows. Ehe ibikoresho nyamukuru biri muri iyi suite:
    - Process Monitor*: ishobora kugufasha kwihweza ibikorwa bikora, ukwinjira muri dosiye, ama register, n’ibindi mu gihe nyaco;
    - Autoruns*: yerekana porogarama zose zatangujwe mu ntango, zigufasha kumenya ningoga porogarama mbi ziguma zikora canke porogarama zidakwiye kuba ziriko zirakora;
    - Process Explorer*: ikurikirana imigenderanire kandi ikamenya inyifato iteye amakenga;
    - TCPView*: igaragaza amahuzu y'urubuga akora (kumenya amahuzu adasanzwe) ;
    - Sigcheck*: igenzura imikono ya digitale ku madosiye kugira ngo ibone kode mbi.



![Image](assets/fr/207.webp)





- GlassWire*: igikoresho co kugenzura urubuga. Ikurikirana amakuru yinjira n’asohoka mu gihe nyaco, kandi ikakumenyesha ibikorwa bidasanzwe.



![Image](assets/fr/208.webp)



#### Munsi ya Linux



Ku mashine ya Linux itunganijwe neza ikoreshwa ku bintu vy’umuntu ku giti ciwe, ingorane ziraba nke. Nyamara, ng'ibi ibikoresho bimwe bimwe vy'ubuhinga bwo kugenzura sisitemu yawe :





- Fail2ban*: igenzura inyandiko za sisitemu ku ngendo zo kwinjira zitashoboye (nk'igerageza ryo kwinjira muri SSH ry'inguvu z'agahomerabunwa). Iyo inyifato iteye amakenga ibonetse, irabuza by’igihe gito IP Address yakoze icaha biciye ku `iptables` ;



![Image](assets/fr/217.webp)





- Lynis*: igikoresho co kugenzura umutekano gisesangura ubuhinga bwawe kugira ngo ubone ko ata n’imwe ikora nabi, ko hariho intege nke zizwi canke ko hariho ukunyuranya n’imigenzo myiza. Itanga raporo yoroshe gusoma, ifise amanota y’umutekano n’impanuro.



![Image](assets/fr/218.webp)


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/lynis-1cf865b3-a352-4dd2-94d2-f17fa65547af

#### Munsi ya macOS



macOS izwi cane kubera umutekano wayo, cane cane kubera amategeko yayo y’ugusinya amaporogarama n’ubwubatsi bupfutse. Ku bijanye n’ugukoresha umuntu ku giti ciwe, imashini igezweho ifise amasetingi y’imbere y’igihe irasanzwe itanga umutekano mwiza. Kugira ngo utere intambwe imbere mu kugenzura sisitemu yawe, ndagusavye :





- KnockKnock*: isuzuma Elements zose zatunganijwe kugira zikore igihe zitangura (abakozi, amadayimoni, ibice vy’umubiri...) maze ikamenya izo zishobora kuba ziteye amakenga, zidashizweko umukono canke zitazwi. Bigufasha kumenya ningoga ububi buguma kuri sisitemu yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/209.webp)



### Insozero: umutekano ni ikintu gihoraho



Umutekano mwiza wa mudasobwa ntushikwako mu gushiramwo ibikoresho vyihariye rimwe, ahubwo ushikwako mu gucungera ubudasiba, mu buryo bukomeye kandi mu buryo bubereye. Gutuma ubuhinga bwawe bwo gukoresha buja ku rugero rwo hejuru, guhindura porogarama zihambaye, gukuraho porogarama zidakenewe no kugenzura neza ubuhinga ni vyo bifadika cane kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kububungabunga neza. Muri rusangi, ibi bikorwa vyiza bikora ku bikoresho vyawe vyose vya digitale: ibintu bihuye, ama server, amatelefone ngendanwa...



Mu kigabane gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene wokwirinda gushiramwo porogarama mbi mu bikorwa, mu kwiga ingene wosuzuma ubutungane n’ukuri kw’amadosiye ukura kuri mudasobwa yawe.




## Ubutungane bwa porogaramu n'ukuri


<chapterId>ffa06aeb-0b90-4271-a385-9a752c1bb5ed</chapterId>



Gushiramwo porogarama kuri mudasobwa yawe vyoshobora gusa n’ikintu kitagira akamaro, mugabo mu vy’ukuri bishobora gutuma mudasobwa yawe igira ingorane zikomeye cane. Nkako, porogarama zishobora guhindurwa canke zigafatwa n’abatera, bagakoresha ako karyo kugira ngo bashiremwo ama virusi, ama Trojans n’ubundi bwoko bw’ibintu bibi muri sisitemu yawe.



Gusuzuma ubutungane n’ukuri kw’amaporogarama imbere y’uko ashirwamwo rero ni umugenzo uhambaye cane wo gucungera umutekano, cane cane iyo bishitse ku maporogarama y’agaciro nk’amasakoshi ya Bitcoin canke abacungera amajambo y’ibanga. Ivyo bituma porogarama zikuwe kuri interineti zihuye neza na neza n’izo zasohowe n’uwazikoze, ata co zihinduye.



Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba ingene wosuzuma ubutungane n’ukuri kw’idosiye, n’ingene woyikora kuri sisitemu yawe.



### Ni kubera iki wosuzuma ubutungane n’ukuri kwa porogarama?



Iyo ukuye porogarama kuri Internet, uba wizigiye ata gukeka ko iyo dosiye izokora ku mashine yawe. Ariko ukwo kwizigira ntigukwiye kwigera kuba impumyi. Ni ngombwa rero gutahura ivyiyumviro bibiri vy’ishimikiro: ubutungane bwa dosiye n’ukuri.



#### Intungane: kumenya neza ko ata mpinduka zabaye



Ubutungane bwa dosiye buratanga icemezo c’uko itahinduwe, n’ibigirankana canke bitagamije, hagati y’igihe yasohowe n’uwayikoze n’igihe wayikuye kuri interineti. N’uguhindura gatoyi gusa birashobora kuba bihagije kugira ngo umuntu yinjize kode mbi muri porogarama.



Ivyo bihinduka ntibiboneka n’ijisho ry’umuntu: dosiye yashizwe kuri interineti ishobora gufunguka no gukora neza neza, mu gihe nyene ikora inyifato mbi. Ni co gituma bihambaye kugenzura ubutungane bwayo hakoreshejwe ibimenyetso vy’intoke vy’ubuhinga bwa none (Hash).



#### Ubuntu: kwemeza ko porogarama ikomoka ku nzira ibereye



Dosiye ishobora kuba idahindutse (itahinduwe), ariko ikaba yasohowe n'ikigo kibi kinyaga akaranga k'uwayiteguye yemewe. Authenticity rero igamije kwemeza ko iyo dosiye vy’ukuri ikomoka ku nzira yemewe, atari ku mubeshi, ku rubuga rw’indorerwamo rutagenzuwe, canke ku munyaruyeri yateye akaga umurongo w’ugukwiragiza.



Ukwo kugenzura inkomoko bishoboka biciye ku mukono wa digitale, uburyo bwo gukingira amakuru buhuza dosiye n’urufunguzo rw’ibanga rw’umuhinguzi. Iyo usuzumye iyo sinyatire ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa bose rw’umuhinguzi (rukwiragizwa biciye ku nzira zitekanye), urashobora kwemera udakeka ko iyo dosiye mu vy’ukuri ikomoka kuri uwo muntu.



Mu kugenzura ukuri (ni ukuvuga ko dosiye yo gushiramwo iva ku nzira ibereye) n’ubutungane (ni ukuvuga ko itahinduwe kuva yasohorwa n’umuhinguzi yemewe), urashobora kumenya neza ko uriko urashiramwo porogarama ibereye.



#### Inyishu z'ubuhinga: Hash n'umukono wa digitale



Kugira ivyo tubishikeko, tuzokoresha ibikoresho 2 vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Ica mbere ni uguhasha. Hash ni urudodo rugufi rw'inyuguti ruharuwe mu buryo bugaragara kandi butamenyekana bivuye ku birimwo dosiye, hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bwa Hash nka SHA-256. Dosiye zibiri zisa cane zizogira Hash imwe nyene, ariko guhindura gatoyi gusa muri iyo dosiye bizotuma Hash ihinduka burundu.



Uwukora iyo porogarama yemewe akenshi atangaza Hash ya dosiye y’intango ku rubuga rwiwe rwemewe. Ku ruhande rwawe, uzoharura aho hantu Hash ya dosiye y’ugushiraho washizeho, kugira ngo ugereranye ivyo bibiri. Iyo ivyo bimenyetso bibiri vy’intoke bihuye, urashobora kwemera udakeka ko iyo dosiye wavuye kuri interineti ari iyo ukuri kandi ko ata co yahinduye.



Igikoresho ca kabiri ni umukono w’ivyuma. Ivyo bigenzura ko porogarama yo gushiramwo ari iyo ukuri. Uwukora iyo porogarama ashira umukono kuri dosiye irimwo Hash n’urufunguzo rwiwe rw’ibanga, kandi urashobora kugenzura iyo sinya ukoresheje urufunguzo rwa bose rujanye n’urwo. Ivyo vyerekana ko iyo dosiye yasohowe n’umuntu akwiriye.



Iyi sisitemu ishingiye ku buhinga bwo gukingira amakuru butaringaniye n’ibikoresho nka GnuPG (umurongo w’amabwirizwa) canke Kleopatra (igishushanyo ca Interface ca Windows). Ivyo bikoresho bitegerezwa kuba vyatunganijwe neza, kandi urufunguzo rwa bose rw’umuhinguzi rutegerezwa gusuzumwa biciye ku nzira itekanye (urubuga rwemewe, urutoke kuri Twitter...). Reka turabe ivyo bishobora gukora.



Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku bikorwa vya Hash vy’ubuhinga bwa none be n’imikono y’ubuhinga bwa none, ndagutumiye ngo ufate inyigisho ya CYP 201 ku buntu itangwa kuri Plan ₿ Network:



https://planb.network/courses/46b0ced2-9028-4a61-8fbc-3b005ee8d70f

### Genzura ubutungane bwa porogaramu n'ukuri



#### Ibisabwa



Niba ukoresha Linux, GPG irashirwaho mbere ku bimenyetso vyinshi. Niba atarivyo, ushobora kuyishiramwo ukoresheje iri tegeko rikurikira:



```bash
sudo apt install gnupg
```



![Image](assets/fr/232.webp)



Ku macOS, nimba utarashiramwo umucungerezi w'amapaki ya Homebrew, ubikore ukoresheje aya mabwirizwa akurikira:



```bash
/bin/bash -c "$(curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Homebrew/install/HEAD/install.sh)"

echo 'eval "$(/opt/homebrew/bin/brew shellenv)"' >> ~/.zprofile

eval "$(/opt/homebrew/bin/brew shellenv)"
```



Hanyuma ushireho GPG n'iri tegeko:



```bash
brew install gnupg
```



Ku bijanye na Windows, iyo udafise GPG, urashobora gushiramwo [Gpg4win](



![Image](assets/fr/219.webp)



#### Gukuraho inyandiko



Kugira ngo utangure, uzokenera inyandiko nyinshi zijanye n’ivyo wipfuza gushiramwo. Muri aka karorero, tuzoba turiko turasuzuma *Sparrow wallet*, umuyobozi w'ibikorwa vya Bitcoin. Ivyo bizoba nk’ivyo ku yindi porogarama yose: ico ukeneye gukora n’ukurondera amadosiye akwiriye yo kugenzura.



Sura urubuga rwemewe rwa [Sparrow wallet mu gice ca "_Gukuraho_"](https://sparrowwallet.com/gukuraho/). Niba wifuza kuraba iyindi porogarama, genda ku rubuga rw’iyo porogarama.



![Image](assets/fr/220.webp)



Ushobora kandi kuja [ku bubiko bwa GitHub bw'umugambi](ibisohoka).



![Image](assets/fr/221.webp)



Gukuraho porogarama y’ugushiramwo porogarama yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/222.webp)



Uzokenera kandi Hash ya dosiye, akenshi yitwa "_SHA256SUMS_" canke "_IKIGANIRO_".



![Image](assets/fr/223.webp)



Kandi n’ushireko umukono wa PGP wa dosiye. Iyi ni inyandiko `.asc`.



![Image](assets/fr/224.webp)



Raba neza ko izo dosiye zose uzishira mu bubiko bumwe kugira ngo ushobore gukora neza intambwe zikurikira.



Ubwa nyuma, uzokenera urufunguzo rwa bose rw'umuhinguzi kugira ngo ugenzure umukono wa PGP. Urufunguzo muri rusangi ruboneka ku rubuga rwemewe rwa porogarama, ku bubiko bwa GitHub bw’umugambi, rimwe na rimwe ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi z’umuhinguzi, canke ku mbuga zidasanzwe nka Keybase.



Ku bijanye na *Sparrow wallet*, ushobora kubona urufunguzo rwa bose rw'umuhinguzi [Craig Raw ku Rufunguzo](https://urufunguzo.io/craigraw). Kugira ngo uyikure kuri terminal, kora itegeko rikurikira:



```bash
curl https://keybase.io/craigraw/pgp_keys.asc | gpg --import
```



![Image](assets/fr/225.webp)



![Image](assets/fr/233.webp)



Kugira ngo umenye neza ko uriko ukoresha urufunguzo rwa bose nyarwo rw'umuhinguzi, atari urwo rwafashwe n'umuhinguzi, ndagusavye gusuzuma amasoko: usuzume ko urutoke rw'urufunguzo ruhuye kuri Keybase, ku rubuga rwemewe rw'umugambi, no ku mbuga zose z'imigenderanire canke imihora y'itumanaho y'umuhinguzi.



#### Gusuzuma umukono



Uburyo bwo kugenzura umukono burasa kuri Windows, macOS na Linux. Wabwirizwa kuba waramaze kwinjiza urufunguzo rwa bose mu ntambwe iheze, ariko nimba utarabikora, ushobora kuruzana ukoresheje iri tegeko rikurikira:



```bash
gpg --import [key_path]
```



Subiriza `[key_path]` n'aho dosiye y'urufunguzo rusangi y'umuhinguzi iri.



![Image](assets/fr/226.webp)



Suzuma umukono ukoresheje iri tegeko rikurikira:



```bash
gpg --verify [file.asc]
```



Subiriza `[dosiye.asc]` n'inzira ya dosiye y'umukono. Ku bijanye na Sparrow, iyi dosiye yitwa "_igisiga-2.0.0-igaragaza.txt.asc_" ku verisiyo 2.0.0.



![Image](assets/fr/227.webp)



![Image](assets/fr/234.webp)



Niba umukono uriho, GPG izovyemeza mu buryo butomoye. Ushobora rero gutera intambwe ikurikira, kuko iyo nzira y’ukugenzura yemeza ko iyo dosiye ari iy’ukuri.



![Image](assets/fr/228.webp)



![Image](assets/fr/235.webp)



#### Gusuzuma Hash



Ubu ko ukuri kwa dosiye irimwo ama hashes kwemejwe, ni igihe co kugenzura ubutungane bwa dosiye y’umushingantahe, bishingiye kuri iyi dosiye yemejwe. Intumbero ni ukugereranya Hash y'umukoresha wawe n'iyo yerekanwa muri dosiye `.asc`. Iyo ivyo bibiri bihuye, ivyo biremeza ko kode ya porogarama itahinduwe mu buryo na bumwe.



Kuri Windows, fungura terminal maze ukoreshe itegeko rikurikira:



```bash
CertUtil -hashfile [file_path] SHA256 | findstr /v "hash"
```



Subiriza `[inzira_ya_dosiye]` n'aho ushizeho.



![Image](assets/fr/229.webp)



Ico kibanza kiragarura Hash iri kumwe n’ivyo bikoresho vyavuye kuri interineti.



![Image](assets/fr/230.webp)



Hanyuma ugereranye igisubizo n'agaciro kahuye muri dosiye "_sparrow-2.0.0-manifest.txt_".



![Image](assets/fr/231.webp)



Ku bijanye nanje, izo nkoko zibiri zirahuye neza cane.



Mu gihe ca macOS na Linux, uburyo bwo kugenzura Hash burakora, rero nta nkenerwa yo kugereranya n’amaboko ibimenyetso bibiri vy’intoke, nk’uko bishobora kuba mu gihe ca Windows.



Gusa gukoresha iri tegeko munsi ya macOS:



```bash
shasum --check [file_name] --ignore-missing
```



Subiriza `[izina_ry'idosiye]` n'izina rya dosiye yemejwe irimwo ama hashes. Nk'akarorero, kuri Sparrow wallet verisiyo 2.0.0:



```bash
shasum --check sparrow-2.0.0-manifest.txt --ignore-missing
```



Niba hashes zihuye, igisohoka gikwiye kuba:



```bash
Sparrow-2.0.0.dmg: OK
```



Munsi ya Linux, itegeko ni nk'iryo:



```bash
sha256sum --check [file_name] --ignore-missing
```



Kandi iyo hashes zihuye, ushobora kuronka:



```bash
sparrow_2.0.0-1_amd64.deb: OK
```



![Image](assets/fr/236.webp)



Ubu urashobora kwizigira ko porogarama waronse ari iyo ukuri kandi ko ari iyo kwizigirwa. Ubu urashobora kuyishira ku mashine yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/237.webp)



Gusuzuma ubutungane n’ukuri ni umugenzo ugororotse cane, mugabo uratanga uburinzi nyabwo kandi bubereye ku bibazo vyinshi cane bijanye no gukura no gushiramwo porogarama.



Mu kigabane gikurikira, tuzokwihweza neza ingene amakuru akoreshwa. Turaza kuraba ingene wokwikingira ingorane zibiri zikomeye: gutakaza amakuru n’ukwiba amakuru.




## Gushiramwo amakuru no kurinda


<chapterId>bcba9b26-72d2-446b-b23c-89927a2e857c</chapterId>



Gukingira amakuru yawe bwite ni igice gihambaye co kumenya ubusegaba bwawe bwa digitale, ubuzima bwite n’umutekano. Ivyago ku makuru yawe ni vyinshi: gufatwa n’abantu, gutakaza ibikoresho canke mbere no gufata amakuru yawe. Mu gushira mu ngiro ubuhinga bwiza bwo gucungera amakuru no gukingira amakuru, urashobora kwirinda vyinshi muri ivyo bintu bishobora gutera ubwoba.
