Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba mu buryo burambuye ingene woshobora gukingira amakuru yawe no kuyapfuka, hamwe no gusukura amakuru y’agaciro ari mu nyandiko zawe.



### Gusubiza inyuma amakuru yawe



#### Kubera iki ukora backup y’amakuru yawe?



Gufata amakuru yawe bwite canke y’ubudandaji ubudasiba ni ingero y’umutekano ihambaye cane, akenshi irarengagizwa gushika bikerewe cane. Mu buryo butandukanye n’ivyo abantu benshi bemera, gucungera amakuru si igikorwa co guhitamwo canke c’ishirahamwe gusa: kirareba umuntu wese akoresha orodinateri. Waba ufise ivyangombwa vy’akazi, amafoto y’umuryango, ivyangombwa vy’umuntu ku giti ciwe canke ibindi vyose bihambaye, ayo makuru arashobora kuzimangana bukwi na bukwi kubera imvo zitari nke:





- Ivyuma bishobora gukora nabi: HDD na SSD zifise ubuzima buke. Ata n’umwe abigabishije, birashobora kunanirwa, bigatuma amakuru adashobora gushikwako.





- Igitero ca mudasobwa: hariho porogarama mbi, cane cane ransomware, zipfuka amadosiye yawe mu karere kandi zigasaba incungu muri Exchange ku rufunguzo rwo gufungura. Ata backup yigenga, uri ku mbabazi zabo.





- Ikosa ry’umuntu: gukoresha nabi, gukuraho mu mpanuka canke guhindura ibintu ataco bigamije bishobora gutuma umuntu atakaza ibintu bidashobora gusubirwamwo.





- Ivyago vy’umubiri: umuriro, amazi yononekaye, ubusuma canke mbere n’ugutera kw’amashanyarazi bishobora gutuma ibikoresho vyawe bidashobora gukoreshwa mu kanya nk’ako gukubita urugohe.



Ni co gituma ukeneye ubuhinga bwo gusubiza inyuma bukomeye, butegekanijwe kandi bukomeye.



#### Uburyo bwa 3-2-1: urugero rukomeye rw'umutekano



Itegeko rya "3-2-1" ni urugero rwemewe mu mutekano w'ubuhinga bwa none. Ishingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako zoroshe ariko zikora cane zituma umuntu yihanganira amakosa n’ibintu bishobora gushika. Ehe ingene bigenda:





- 3 kopi z’amakuru yawe: ivyo birimwo ivy’umwimerere (amadosiye ari kuri mudasobwa yawe) n’izindi kopi zibiri z’ububiko.





- 2 ububiko butandukanye: intumbero ni ukwirinda ingorane y’ibikoresho ishobora gutera ububiko bwawe bwose icarimwe. Nk’akarorero, umuduga wo hanze Hard + igicu; canke NAS + mudasobwa yawe.





- 1 off-site copy: iyo kopi itegerezwa kuba iri kure y’aho uba hakuru (mu nzu y’incuti yawe, kuri server iri kure, mu gicu gitekanye...). Irakurinda ibintu vyo mu karere nk’umuriro canke ubusuma.



Reka dufate akarorero k’umuntu akoresha amakuru yiwe, Alice, ashaka gukingira amakuru yiwe bwite.



Alice abika verisiyo y’amadosiye yiwe kuri laptop yiwe, aho ayakoresha ku musi ku musi. Kugira ngo agire n’imiburiburi ibinyamakuru bibiri bitandukanye, arakunda (nk’akarorero, buri wa mbere) akopa amakuru yiwe yose akayashira ku gicapo ca USB, akayabika i muhira. Kugira ngo Alice yikingire ubusuma bw’amadosiye yiwe iyo yoba yatakaje canke yibwe, irashiramwo iyo nkoni ya USB ikoresheje porogarama zibereye (tuzobona ingene twobikora mu nyuma muri iki kigabane).



Iyo ifise iyo ntunganyo, Alice irasanzwe irindwa n’ibintu vyinshi bitera ubwoba. Ariko rero, hariho ingorane imwe: iyo hoba umuriro canke ubusuma mu nzu yiwe, amakopi yiwe abiri yo mu karere (ordinateri n’urudodo rwa USB) yoshobora kuzimangana icarimwe. Kugira ngo agabanye ivyo bibazo, afata ingingo yo gukoresha ubuhinga bwo kubika amadosiye mu gicu, kandi akabushiramwo amadosiye yiwe ubudasiba.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/proton-drive-03cbe49f-6ddc-491f-8786-bc20d98ebb16

Alice rero yubaha itegeko rya 3-2-1: ifise kopi 3 z’amadosiye yayo (mudasobwa, urufunguzo rwa USB, igicu), ibitswe n’imiburiburi ku bikoresho 2 bitandukanye (disque interne, urufunguzo rwa USB, server yo kure), ifise n’imiburiburi kopi 1 iri hanze y’aho iri (server y’igicu).



Iryo tegeko rituma ashobora kwihangana neza cane: iyo orodinateri yiwe ipfuye, arashobora kugarura amadosiye yiwe akoresheje USB canke mu gicu; iyo uwutanga ububiko bwo mu gicu ashikiwe n’ikibazo gikomeye, aracari n’amadosiye yiwe aho hantu; kandi mbere n’igihe umuntu yivye aho laptop yiwe n’urudodo rwiwe rwa USB vyibwe, arashobora kugarura amakuru yiwe biciye kuri cloud service.



![Image](assets/fr/255.webp)



#### Ikora kugira wirinde kwibagirwa



Uburyo bumwe bwiza bwo kumenya isuku ryiza ry’inyuma ni ugukoresha ubuhinga bwikora. Gutunganya ibikoresho vyawe kugira ngo ama backups akore ubwayo hakurikijwe urutonde (ijoro ryose, buri ndwi...). Ivyo birabuza ukugenzura kandi bikaba vyemeza ko bizobandanya mbere n’igihe woba utaboneka mu gihe gitoyi ku ruhande rwawe.



Mu majambo y’ingirakamaro, hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gukora ama backups yawe. Ushobora, nk'akarorero, gukora inyandiko ya Python ikora ubwayo kugira ngo ikopire amakuru yawe ku buryo bwo hanze. Ni umuti woroshe, ushobora guhindurwa.



Niba ufise NAS, ibikoresho nka *Syncthing* canke *Rclone* bigufasha gukora backups mu rubuga rwawe, udakoresheje Internet.



![Image](assets/fr/253.webp)



Kugira ngo ukoreshe ubuhinga bwo gucungera amakuru mu gicu, urashobora gukoresha porogarama y’ugushiramwo ibintu itangwa n’uwubitanga ubwiwe. Akarorero kamwe ni *Proton Drive*, itanga umukiriya w’uguhuza amadosiye yawe mu gicu. Ushobora kandi guhitamwo porogarama zishobora guhinduka nka *Duplicati*, zigufasha gutegura amakuru y’inyuma y’ibintu vyinshi bikoreshwa kure (Dropbox, Google Drive, Proton Drive, FTP, WebDAV...).



![Image](assets/fr/254.webp)



Ibuka kandi kugerageza ama backups yawe ubudasiba, ni ukuvuga ko ushobora kuyagarura. Backup ntaco imaze iyo yononekaye, idatunganye canke idashobora gusomwa.



Uretse no kumenya neza ko amakuru yawe ashobora gukomera, birahambaye cane ko ukingira ukuntu umuntu ashobora kuyaronka. Nkako, ukwihangana n’umutekano akenshi biratera ingorane: uko ukora kopi nyinshi z’amadosiye yawe, ni ko urushiriza kwongera uburebure bw’igitero cayo, bigatuma rero uwutera ashobora kuyaronka. Ni co gituma gupfuka amakuru yawe ari intambwe ihambaye. Reka turabe ingene twobishira mu ngiro.



### Ugushiramwo amakuru yuzuye kuri disiki zo hanze n'ibinyamakuru



Imwe mu nkingi z’umutekano wa mudasobwa y’umuntu ku giti ciwe ni ugushiramwo amakuru yabitswe. Cane cane, gupfuka amakuru yuzuye nk’ibikoresho vyo mu mutima Hard, inkoni za USB canke amadisike yo hanze bituma, mbere n’igihe habaye ubusuma, ukubura canke uguhungabana kw’ibikoresho, ata makuru ashobora gusomwa ata rufunguzo rwo gufungura.



#### Ni kubera iki ari ngirakamaro?



Iyo ikintu co kubika ibintu kitarimwo amakuru, ushobora gusa kugishira muri orodinateri iyo ari yo yose kugira ngo ushobore guca ubona ibirimwo. Nta nzitizi zihari zo kurinda amadosiye. Ivyo bisigura ko iyo laptop yawe yibwe, canke iyo utakaje urufunguzo rwa USB rworoshe, umuntu afise umugambi mubi yoshobora gushika ku nyandiko zawe bwite.



Uretse ibibazo vy’ubuzima bwite biri mu kaga, amadosiye yawe arashobora kandi guserukira ingorane nyayo y’umutekano. Reka dufate akarorero nyako: nimba ama backups yawe arimwo kopi y’inyandiko zawe z’akaranga, uwugutera yoshobora kuyakoresha kugira ngo akugire nk’umuntu, akugururire amakonti ya banki canke y’amahera y’ibanga mw’izina ryawe, canke mbere aguhe inguzanyo muri banki mw’izina ryawe. Ubwo bwoko bw’ugusohoka kw’amakuru burashobora kugira ingaruka zikomeye, ku muntu ku giti ciwe no ku kazi.



Gushiramwo amakuru yuzuye ni nk’ugufunga: igihe cose ijambobanga ritatanzwe, amakuru aguma adakoreshwa. N’umuterabwoba afise ibikoresho vyihariye vyo gusubiza amakuru ntaco azoshobora gukuramwo ata rufunguzo afise.



#### Ni inyishu izihe z’ubuhinga systeme yawe itanga?





- Linukisi (Debiyani)*



Munsi ya Linux, umuti usanzwe ni LUKS (*Itegeko ry'urufunguzo rwa Linux*). LUKS ni uburyo bwo gucunga umubare w’amajwi bushizwe mu bimenyetso vyinshi. Igihe iyo sisitemu ibanza gushirwako, muri rusangi uzosabwa gupfuka disiki yose ya mudasobwa. Ego ni ko, ndagusavye cane gukoresha iyo nzira. Igihe encryption imaze gukoreshwa, iyo sisitemu izosaba ijambobanga igihe cose ufunguye, mbere n’imbere y’uko OS ifunguka. Ivyo bituma ukuntu umuntu ashobora gushika kuri iyo disiki adashobora guca mu mutekano.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/luks-13d9928b-08b1-478c-a1b4-67617978584a

Niba wipfuza gupfuka disiki y'inyuma canke inkoni ya USB, ivyo bishobora gukorwa kandi ukoresheje umurongo w'amabwirizwa canke ukoresheje igishushanyo Interface. Disiki izobwirizwa guhindurwa, rero amakuru yose ariho azozimangana iyo atabanje gusubirwamwo.



**Biciye ku nzira**



Raba neza ko ufise *cryptsetup*:



```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install cryptsetup
```



Tangana n'ukumenya urufunguzo rwawe rwa USB ukoresheje iri tegeko rikurikira:



```bash
lsblk
```



Ushobora kubona igikoresho nka `/dev/sdb` gifise igice gifatanye, nk'akarorero `/dev/sdb1`. Urabe maso uhitemwo disiki ibereye, kuko izofutwa!



Kugira ngo ushiremwo urufunguzo, koresha iri tegeko kugira ngo utangure gushiramwo:



```bash
sudo cryptsetup luksFormat /dev/sdb
```



Andika "EGO" mu nyuguti nini kugira ngo wemeze igikorwa, hanyuma uhitemwo kandi wemeze passphrase ikomeye. Iri jambobanga rizotuma ushobora gushika ku makuru yawe: wibuke gukora ububiko, kuko iyo utagira, gushika ku makuru y’urufunguzo bizobura ubuziraherezo.



![Image](assets/fr/238.webp)



Gufungura no gufungura ijwi:



```bash
sudo cryptsetup open /dev/sdb encrypted_usb
```



Uzokenera kwinjira muri passphrase yawe kugira ngo ufungure ijwi. `encrypted_usb` ni izina ry'umubumbe wafunguwe.



![Image](assets/fr/239.webp)



Hanyuma ushireho format y’igice casohowe. Ku buryo bwa Linux kavukire:



```bash
sudo mkfs.ext4 /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb
```



Canke, niba ushaka guhuza na Windows:



```bash
sudo mkfs.vfat /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb
```



![Image](assets/fr/240.webp)



Gushira urufunguzo kugira ngo ukoreshe:



```bash
sudo mkdir -p /mnt/usb
sudo mount /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb /mnt/usb
```



Ubu ushobora gushika ku rufunguzo rwawe biciye mu bubiko bwa `/mnt/usb`, no gusoma no kwandika amadosiye nk'uko biri ku yindi nkuru yose.



Kugira ngo ushobore gusenyura no gusubira gupfuka urufunguzo:



```bash
sudo umount /mnt/usb
sudo cryptsetup close encrypted_usb
```



Ushobora rero gukuraho urufunguzo rwawe rwa USB ata nkomanzi.



Kugira ngo ukoreshe muri kazoza umuduga wawe wa USB:



```bash
sudo cryptsetup open /dev/sdb encrypted_usb
sudo mount /dev/mapper/encrypted_usb /mnt/usb
#### … you work on the usb …
sudo umount /mnt/usb
sudo cryptsetup close encrypted_usb
```



![Image](assets/fr/241.webp)



Niba ushaka, ushobora kandi gukoresha uru rukurikirane ukoresheje inyandiko za Python canke Bash.




**Biciye kuri disiki za GNOME:**



Uwundi muti ni ugukoresha porogarama ya GNOME Disks n’igishushanyo cayo Interface, akenshi kikaba coroshe kuruta gukoresha terminal. Mu bisanzwe, iki gikoresho kirasanzwe gishizwe kuri Ubuntu. Niba atarivyo, ushobora kuyishiramwo n'amaboko ukoresheje iri tegeko rikurikira:



```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install -y gnome-disk-utility
```



Kugira ngo ufungure porogaramu, genda kuri menu y'ibikorwa vya Ubuntu maze urondere "*Disks*". Ubusanzwe iboneka ku buryo busanzwe mu bubiko bwa "*Utilities*".



Mu nkingi y’ibubamfu, nurondere urufunguzo rwawe rwa USB. Niba hariho igice gisanzwe kiriho, gihitemwo; niba atarivyo, rema uwundi mushasha: fyonda ku buto "+" buri musi y'urutonde rw'imigabane.



![Image](assets/fr/242.webp)



Hanyuma uhitemwo igice uzoshiramwo amakuru. Fyonda ku kimenyetso c'uruziga, hanyuma uhitemwo "Guhindura igice...".



![Image](assets/fr/243.webp)



Mu:




- Mu "Izina ry'Igitabo", shiramwo izina (nk'akarorero `usb`);
- Hitamwo "Disiki yo mu mutima ikoreshwa na sisitemu za Linux gusa (Ext4)" uburyo;
- Suzuma akazu "Ijambobanga ry'umubare (LUKS)".



![Image](assets/fr/244.webp)



Injira kandi wemeze passphrase ikomeye.



![Image](assets/fr/245.webp)



Wemeze kandi urindire ko igice gihindurwa neza (amakuru yose azokurwaho).



![Image](assets/fr/246.webp)



Iyo iyo nzira irangiye, iyo nzira y’ugucapura iraboneka n’agafunguzo gatoyi. Hitamwo, hanyuma ukande ku ngufuri kugira ngo uyifungure.



![Image](assets/fr/247.webp)



Injira ijambobanga, hanyuma ukande kuri "Gufungura".



![Image](assets/fr/248.webp)



Ijwi rizokwiyongera kandi rishobora gushikirwa n'umucungerezi wa dosiye yawe, kenshi mu bubiko bwa `/media/username/usb`.



![Image](assets/fr/249.webp)



Kugira ngo ukureho urufunguzo rwa USB maze wongere ukoreshe ububiko, wongere ukande ku kimenyetso c'urufunguzo muri GNOME Disks.



Ubwa nyuma, fyonda ku buto bufise ishusho y’umwampi buri hejuru iburyo kugira ngo ukure urufunguzo muri PC yawe neza. Igihe kizoza winjiye, Ubuntu izokwibonera urufunguzo rwawe rwashizwemwo amakuru maze ikagusaba ijambobanga, ataco ukeneye gufungura ama Disiki ya GNOME.



![Image](assets/fr/250.webp)





- Amadirisha:**



Mu nsi ya Windows, umuti w’akavukire uragufasha gupfuka disiki yawe. Biroroshe gukoresha: genda gusa kuri "*Ubuzima bwite n'umutekano*", hanyuma ushire akamenyetso ku gasandugu "*Ugushiramwo amakuru y'ibikoresho*" mu gice c'ibintu vy'ibanga bifise izina nyene. Imfunguruzo zo gusubirana zizoca zibikwa muri konti yawe ya Microsoft ijana.



![Image](assets/fr/251.webp)



Niba ukoresha konti yo mu karere, canke nimba imashini yawe idashigikira iki kintu mu buryo bw’imvukira, urashobora gushinga *BitLocker* n’amaboko (porogarama y’ugushiramwo amakuru ya Microsoft). Ariko kandi hariho n’ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha inkomoko yuguruye nka *VeraCrypt*.



*VeraCrypt* ni porogaramu y’ubuntu, ikoreshwa kuri Windows, Linux na macOS. Ishobora gukoreshwa mu gupfuka disiki yose canke igice, canke guhingura dosiye y'ibikoresho ikora nk'idisiki y'ukuri itekanye. Interface ya VeraCrypt iremeza ko iyo nkuru ishobora gushirwako nk’idisiki isanzwe, ishobora gushikwako gusa inyuma y’ugushingira intahe.



Kugira ngo umenye vyinshi kuri uwo muti, usabwe kuraba iyi nyigisho yuzuye :



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/veracrypt-d5ed4c83-7c1c-4181-95ea-963fdf2d83c5




- OS :**



Ku macOS, ububiko bwa disiki bwa sisitemu bushingiye kuri *FileVault*, ikintu c’akavukire gishobora gushikwako biciye ku mirongo y’umutekano. Niba Mac yawe ifise igice ca Apple Silicon (M1, M2...) canke igice ca T2, ugushiramwo amakuru y’ibikoresho birasanzwe bikora ubudasiba. Ariko rero, gukoresha FileVault birongereza Layer y’umutekano mu gupfuka umubare wose wa sisitemu.



![Image](assets/fr/252.webp)



FileVault imaze gukora, uzokenera guhitamwo uburyo bwo kuyigarura mu gihe ijambobanga ryatakaye: canke ukoreshe konti yawe ya *iCloud*, canke generate urufunguzo rwihariye rwo gusubiza inyuma. Urufunguzo rutegerezwa kubikwa ahantu heza, kuko iyo rwatakaye vyotuma amakuru yawe adashobora gushikwako ubudasiba.


Ku bikoresho vyo hanze vyo kubika (amadisiki Hard, inkoni za USB, n’ibindi), gushiramwo amakuru bikorwa hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bwa disiki. Uzokenera guhindura burundu umuzingo:



- Hitamwo igikoresho, ukande kuri "*Delete*".
- Hitamwo "GUID* Imbonerahamwe y'Imigabane"
- Hanyuma uhitemwo uburyo bwa dosiye bufise amakuru (*APFS* canke *Mac OS yagutse*)
- Hitamwo ijambobanga rikomeye
- Fyonda kuri "*Delete*" hanyuma "*OK*" n'ugushiramwo amakuru birarangiye


Iyo encryption imaze gushirwaho, umuduga wo hanze ushobora guterwa gusa mu kwinjiza iri jambobanga. Iyo sisitemu izoheza ikayifungura mu gihe c’ingurube.


#### Impanuro nke ku bijanye n'ububiko bwawe bwashizwemwo


Imbere yo gushiramwo amakuru, ukeneye gukora ububiko bw’amakuru yose arimwo (kiretse iyo ari ubusa, birashoboka), kuko uburyo bwo gushiramwo amakuru muri rusangi bufuta ibirimwo mu ntango.


Guhitamwo ijambobanga na ryo nyene ni ngirakamaro cane: ritegerezwa kuba rirerire, rikomeye kandi ridasanzwe, kuko ari ryo ryonyene ririnda hagati y’amakuru yawe n’uwundi muntu w’umunyaruyeri. Ukeneye kandi gukora backup, nk’akarorero mu gikoresho co gucungera ijambobanga, kuko bitandukanye n’ibikorwa vyo kuri internet, nta buryo bwo kubigarura buriho. Iyo wibagiwe ijambobanga ryawe, amakuru arazimangana ubuziraherezo.


### Guhitamwo dosiye y'ububiko


Mu bihe bimwebimwe, ntibikenewe canke ngo bibe vyiza gupfuka disiki yose ya Hard canke ibinyamakuru vyo hanze. Muri ivyo bihe, urashobora guhitamwo gukoresha uburyo bwo gukingira amakuru, ivyo bikaba birimwo gukingira gusa amadosiye canke ububiko bumwebumwe burimwo amakuru y’agaciro.


Uburyo bumwe buzwi cane bwo gupfuka amadosiye ni ugukoresha GPG. Ico gikoresho gishingiye ku buhinga bwo gukingira amakuru butagira aho bugarukira: ufise urufunguruzo rubiri, rumwe ni urw’abantu bose, ushobora gutanga ataco ushizeko abaguha amakuru, urundi na rwo rw’ibanga, rutegerezwa kuguma ari ibanga rikomeye. Amadosiye arashirwa mu mfungurwa hakoreshejwe urufunguzo rwa bose rw’uwuyakira, ariko ashobora gufungurwa gusa hakoreshejwe urufunguzo rwiwe rw’ibanga.


Iyi porotokole ni nziza cane mu guhana amadosiye y’agaciro n’abandi ata nkomanzi, ata jambobanga usangira. Ku gukoresha umuntu ku giti ciwe canke rimwe na rimwe, GPG irashoboza kandi gupfuka amakuru mu buryo buhuye: dosiye iraheza irindwa n’ijambobanga ry’umwihariko rizwi na wewe gusa.


Iyindi nzira nziza cane ni Cryptomator. Iyi porogarama y’inkomoko yuguruye iragufasha gukora ububiko: ububiko budasanzwe aho amadosiye yose ashizwemwo ahita ashirwamwo amakuru. Iyi safe ishobora gukorana n’ibikorwa vyo mu gicu nka Dropbox, Google Drive canke Nextcloud ata n’umwe atanga amakuru yigeze abona amakuru atagiramwo amakuru. Iyo porogarama iboneka ku bikoresho vyose, harimwo Android na iOS, kandi ntibisaba ubuhinga budasanzwe kugira ngo umuntu ayikoreshe.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/cryptomator-84e52c76-2253-49fe-81da-e05e90c28d0d


![Image](assets/fr/256.webp)



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/picocrypt-98c213bd-9ace-425b-b012-bea71ce6b38f

Ubwa nyuma, birashoboka kandi gukoresha VeraCrypt mu buryo bw’ibikoresho, bikora dosiye ikora nk’ububiko bufise amakuru, bushobora guterwa nk’idisiki.


Ubu ko umaze kwiga ingene wokingira amakuru yawe bwite ngo ntatakare canke ngo yibwe, ikigabane gikurikira kiraba ikindi kintu gihambaye: ingene wokingira amadosiye yawe bwite ngo ntabe ibitero biciye ku makuru yabo bwite.


## Gusukura amakuru


<chapterId>0869e92e-5488-4e8a-90e6-9b9d1c58a19b</chapterId>


Igihe cose ukoze dosiye ya digitale, yaba ifoto, inyandiko y’ibiro, dosiye y’amajwi canke y’amasanamu, iba irimwo metadata mu nyuma. Aya makuru ntaboneka iyo ufunguye dosiye, ariko arahari, kandi ashobora kubamwo Elements ikomeye cane.


### Ni kuki metadata ari akaga?


Metadata ni amakuru afatanye na dosiye, uruhara rwayo ni ugutanga amakuru yerekeye ibirimwo. Mu ishusho, ivyo bishobora kubamwo itariki n’isaha iyo shusho yafashweko, amakuru nyayo ya GPS, igishushanyo c’icamera canke telefone ngendanwa yakoreshejwe, rimwe na rimwe mbere n’ibintu vy’ubuhinga. Mu nyandiko y’inyandiko, ishobora kubamwo izina ry’umwanditsi, izina ry’ishirahamwe, ID y’igihe c’ukoresha, ibimenyetso vy’igihe co kurema no guhindura, canke mbere ibivugwa imbere mu mutima vyasigaye mu gihe co guhindura.


Ivyo bimenyetso vyoshobora gusa n’ibitagira akamaro, ariko birashobora gukoreshwa n’abanyaruyeri kugira ngo bamenye uwanditse dosiye, bamenye aho umuntu ari, basubire kwubaka ibintu canke ingeso, canke mbere bakoreshe amakosa ya porogarama bishingiye ku verisiyo ya porogarama ikoreshwa.


Reka dufate akarorero nyako: ushize ifoto bivugwa ko ata muntu azi ku rubuga. Niba utakuyeho metadata ya EXIF, gukanda rimwe gusa birashobora kwerekana ama coordinates nyayo ya GPS y’inzu yawe, modele ya telefone yawe n’itariki nyayo iyo foto yafashweko. Na vyo nyene, inyandiko ya PDF yoherejwe ata wuzi umuntu yoshobora kuba irimwo izina ryawe ryose mu bintu vyayo.


Ni co gituma ibinyamakuru bimwebimwe bisohora ibinyamakuru be n’ibinyamakuru bica bikuraho amakuru y’amafoto yawe. Ivyo birimwo X (Twitter), Instagram, Ikimenyetso n’Ikiganiro. Ku rundi ruhande, izindi nzira ntizikuraho metadata na gato: ivyo ni ko bigenda ku mahuriro menshi yo kuri Internet, ku bakiriya benshi bo kuri e-mail, canke mbere iyo ushize ahabona ataco uhinduye ku rubuga.


Ni ikintu gihambaye co gufata: dosiye ikimara kuva mu rwego rwawe rw’ibanga, urakeneye kwiyumvira gusukura amakuru yayo kugira ngo wirinde gutangaza amakuru y’ibanga canke y’agaciro ataco uzi. Reka turabe ingene ivyo wobikora, bivanye n’uko ukoresha ubuhinga bwawe.


### Kuri Linux (Debiyani)


#### Gukoresha igikoresho ca Exif


Uburyo bushitse kandi bwizewe bwo gucunga no gukuraho amakuru y’imbere mu gihugu ni ExifTool, yateguwe na Phil Harvey. Ihuye n’umubare munini w’imiterere ya dosiye (JPG, PNG, PDF, MP3, DOCX...) kandi ishoboza kwerekana no gukuraho amakuru y’imbere.



- Intambwe ya 1: Shiraho ExifTool


Kugira ngo uyishire ku nzira ya Debian (Ubuntu), fungura terminal wandike itegeko:


```bash
sudo apt update
sudo apt install libimage-exiftool-perl
```


Iyi porogaramu ishiramwo `exiftool`, ushobora gukoresha uhereye ku murongo w'amabwirizwa.



![Image](assets/fr/259.webp)





- Intambwe ya 2: Kubona amakuru ya dosiye** (mu gifaransa)



Kugira ngo ubone amakuru yose ari muri dosiye, koresha itegeko rikurikira:



```bash
exiftool name.jpg
```



Subiriza `name.jpg` izina ry'ukuri rya dosiye yawe. Kandi urabe neza ko uri mu bubiko burimwo iri shusho. Nk'akarorero, nimba mfise ifoto y'igishushanyo ca Satoshi Nakamoto mu bubiko bwa `/Downloads`, ndashobora kwerekana amakuru yaco nkoresheje iri tegeko rikurikira:



```bash
cd Downloads
exiftool Satoshi-Nakamoto-Lugano.jpeg
```



![Image](assets/fr/260.webp)



Uzoca ubona urutonde rurerure rw'ibiranga, bishobora kubamwo:




- Itariki n'isaha y'irema
- Aho GPS iri
- Uwukora kamera n'umuderi
- Porogaramu ikoreshwa mu guhindura
- Amakuru yerekeye umwanditsi...



Ivyo biguha inyishu yuzuye y’ivyo ugiye gutangaza canke gutanga.





- Intambwe ya 3: Gukuraho amakuru



Kugira ngo usibe amakuru yose adakenewe muri dosiye, koresha itegeko:



```bash
exiftool -all= name.jpg
```



![Image](assets/fr/261.webp)



Iri tegeko rihita rikora kopi ya dosiye y'umwimerere n'amakuru y'imbere akuweho. Umwimerere uzigama n'ukwaguka `_umwimerere` kwongerewe kw'izina ryayo.



![Image](assets/fr/262.webp)



Niba udashaka kugumana ivy'umwimerere, ushobora kubifuta ukoresheje itegeko:



```bash
exiftool -all= -overwrite_original name.jpg
```



Nitwasubira kuraba amakuru y’ivya dosiye yacu, turashobora kubona ko amakuru yose adakenewe canke y’agaciro yakuweho.



![Image](assets/fr/263.webp)





- Intambwe ya 4: Sukura ububiko bwose



Niba ufise amadosiye menshi yo gukora mu bubiko bumwe, ushobora gukoresha itegeko rusangi nka:



```bash
exiftool -all= *.jpeg
```



Ivyo bikuraho amakuru y'amadosiye yose ya JPEG ari mu bubiko buriho. Ushobora guhindura iyo nzira kugira ngo ihure n'ivyo ukeneye (`*.png`, `*.pdf`...).



![Image](assets/fr/264.webp)



#### Gukoresha MAT2.



Nk’uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha ExifTool, ushobora gukoresha MAT2 (*Igikoresho co gutanga amakuru v2*).





- Gushiramwo MAT2:



```bash
sudo apt install mat2
```



![Image](assets/fr/265.webp)



Iyo umaze kuyishiramwo, ushobora kuyikoresha uhereye ku murongo w'amabwirizwa nk'uku:



```bash
mat2 fichier.pdf
```



![Image](assets/fr/266.webp)



Ku mburabuzi, MAT2 ntihindura dosiye y'umwimerere: irema verisiyo yasukuwe mu bubiko bumwe n'inyuma `-clean` yongeweko.



![Image](assets/fr/267.webp)



Kugira ngo usukure ububiko bwose, nk'ububiko bwa `/Downloads`:



```bash
mat2 ~/Downloads/*
```



### Ibindi bikoresho (Windows na macOS)



Kuri Windows na macOS, hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gukuraho amakuru y’imbere mu nyandiko zawe. Njye mbona, ikintu coroshe ni ugukoresha porogarama y’inkomoko yuguruye [ExifCleaner](https://exifcleaner.com/). Ico gikoresho gifise uburemere buke gifise igishushanyo Interface kandi gishobora gukorana n’imiterere myinshi y’amadosiye mu gukurura no gutera gusa. Mu gutera dosiye imwe canke nyinshi kuri Interface, iyo porogarama ica ikuraho amakuru adakenewe maze igasubirira dosiye z’intango ziri muri ubwo bubiko nyene. ExifCleaner iraboneka kuri Windows, macOS na Linux.



Biroroshe cane gukoresha: gusa ukoreshe porogarama, hanyuma ukureho dosiye imwe canke nyinshi mw’idirisha.



![Image](assets/fr/257.webp)



Rindira umwanya mutoyi mu gihe igikoresho gisukura metadata. Igihe iyo nzira irangiye, uzobona incamake yerekana igitigiri c'amakuru y'intango n'ay'iherezo. Amakuru yose atari ngombwa azoba yarakuweho.



![Image](assets/fr/258.webp)



Gusukura metadata y’amadosiye usangira rero ni akamenyero keza ko gukurikiza iyo bije ku bijanye n’umutekano w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none. Kubera ibikoresho vyoroshe vyashikirijwe muri iki kigabane, ni akamenyero ushobora gushiramwo mu buryo bworoshe ku musi ku musi.



Twashitse ku mpera y’iki gice ku bijanye no gukingira mudasobwa yawe. Mu gice gikurikira, tuzoba turiko turihweza mu buryo bwimbitse imwe muri porogarama zihambaye cane z’imashini yawe: umucukumbuzi w’urubuga. Ni yo yonyene ihuriza hamwe igice kinini c’ibikorwa vyawe vy’ubuhinga bwa none, bikaba biyigira intumbero nyamukuru mu bijanye n’umutekano n’ubuzima bwite.




# Mucukumbuzi: OS iri muri OS


<partId>125c3d99-6aba-4050-bc7c-8543ef8587e4</partId>



## Amateka make y'abagendera mu mazi


<chapterId>ac6d2c23-5883-4564-b6a9-bc109b47f92c</chapterId>



Mucukumbuzi w'urubuga ni porogaramu igufasha gushika ku mbuga n'ibirimwo biri kuri *World Wide Web*. Uruhara rwayo ni ugusobanura indimi zikoreshwa mu guhingura amapaji y’urubuga, cane cane HTML, CSS na JavaScript, kugira ngo bigaragaze ibiri ku rubuga mu buryo busomwa kandi bushobora gukoreshwa. Ikora nk’i Interface hagati y’ukoresha n’abakozi b’urubuga, irungika ibisabwa no kwakira inyishu biciye ku nzira ya HTTP canke HTTPS.



Ariko muri iki gihe, umucukumbuzi yaracitse ikintu kirenze cane igice c’ubuhinga gusa: akenshi ni Interface nyamukuru mu vy’ubuhinga bwa none, cane cane ku bakoresha bashasha. Ni co gituma rimwe na rimwe ifatwa nk'"uburyo bwo gukoresha bwa kabiri" mu buryo bwo gukoresha nyabwo (ubwo twarize mu gice ca mbere ca SCU202). Nkako, ibikorwa vyinshi vyahora bikorwa hakoreshejwe porogarama zidasanzwe zo mu karere ubu birakorwa ataco bimaze kuri Internet biciye ku mucukumbuzi: ivyo kwisamaza, ibikorwa vyo mu biro (ugutunganya amajambo, gukora urupapuro, gutanga amakuru), gucunga ubutumwa kuri e-mail, gutanga ubutumwa, kubika amadosiye no gukorana n’abandi.



Yamara rero ntivyama bifise urwo ruhara nyamukuru. Amateka y’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none arangwa n’ingendo z’ubuhinga bushasha, uguhiganwa mu vy’ubuhinga, rimwe na rimwe n’ugutegeka kw’abantu bamwebamwe. Gukurikirana iyo nkuru bizodufasha gutahura ingene ama browser yacitse ikintu gikomeye cane, n’igituma umutekano wayo ari ikibazo gihambaye cane muri iki gihe.



→ Akenshi umucukumbuzi aravyivangako n’umucukumbuzi. Yamara ivyo bibiri biratandukanye cane. Mucukumbuzi w’urubuga akoreshwa mu kugaragaza imbuga, mu gihe moteri y’ugushaka (ishobora gushikwako biciye ku mucukumbuzi we) ikoreshwa mu kurondera amakuru kuri Internet biciye mu gushiramwo urutonde no gushikiriza amapaji y’urubuga.



### Ivuka n'abagendera mu mazi ba mbere



Amateka y'ibikoresho vy'urubuga atangura n'ivuka ry'urubuga rw'isi yose*, rwavumbuwe na Tim Berners-Lee mu 1989-1990. Ni uburyo bwo gushika ku mapaji arimwo inyandiko, amashusho, amasanamu canke amahuzu biciye kuri Internet, ukoresheje umucukumbuzi w’urubuga. Kugira ngo iyo nzira nshasha ishobore gukoreshwa, mu mpera z'umwaka w'1990 yarakoze urubuga rwa mbere rwo gukoresha, rwitwa "WorldWideWeb", rwashizeho umushinge w'ugukoresha urubuga nk'uko tuzi uno musi. Ishobora kuraba no gukora amapaji y’urubuga, harimwo n’umuhinduzi wa HTML yunze ubumwe. Kugira ngo ntihagire urujijo hagati y'umucukumbuzi n'urubuga ubwarwo, izina ryayo ryahinduwe mu nyuma riba "Nexus".



![Image](assets/fr/093.webp)



Mu 1992, harabonetse izindi nzira nyinshi zo kugerageza. Imwe mu nzira zizwi cane ni Erwise, yateguwe n’abanyeshure bane bo muri Finlande ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bwa X Window System bushingiye kuri Unix. Ni yo yari umucukumbuzi wa mbere afise igishushanyo Interface c’ubwo bwoko bw’ibidukikije. Naho yari ifise akamaro mu vy’ubuhinga, yarashikiwe n’ingorane z’ukubura amahera kandi ntiyabungabungwa inyuma y’aho isohokeye ubwa mbere. Iyindi migambi, nka ViolaWWW, na yo nyene yarabonetse muri ico kiringo.



![Image](assets/fr/094.webp)



1992 kandi niho haremwa Lynx, urubuga rwa kera cane rukiriho kandi rukoreshwa n’ubu. Yateguwe n’umugwi w’abanyeshure bo muri kaminuza ya Kansas.



Ariko mu mwaka w’1993 niho vy’ukuri urubuga rwinjiye mu gihe c’iterambere ryihuse n’ugushika kwa NCSA Mosaic. Iyi browser yakozwe na Marc Andreessen na Eric Bina bo muri NCSA (*Ikigo c’igihugu c’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none*) muri Amerika. Mosaic ni umucukumbuzi wa mbere ashobora gufatanya neza inyandiko n’amashusho mw’idirisha rimwe. Ishobora kwerekana amashusho ataco ihinduye kuri paji z’urubuga (GIF na XBM), igereranya ugutera imbere kw’ubuhinga bw’ubuhinga ugereranyije n’ibikoresho vy’inyandiko nka Lynx. Mosaic kandi yarashizeho ugushigikira amafomu, bica bifungura inzira y’ugukorana nyakuri hagati y’ukoresha n’abakozi b’urubuga. Mosaic yaciye yihuta gushirwa ku bikoresho vyinshi (Windows, Mac, Unix), bituma vyoroha gukwiragiza. Mu mwaka umwe, ryacitse igikoresho gisanzwe co gutohoza urubuga.



![Image](assets/fr/095.webp)



Mu mwaka w’1994, Marc Andreessen yaravuye muri NCSA, ashinga ishirahamwe ry’ivy’itumanaho ryitwa Netscape ari kumwe na Jim Clark. Igice kinini c’umugwi wari warakoze kuri Mosaïque caramwifatanije. Haciye igihe gito, iyo sosiyete iratanguza Netscape Navigator, urubuga rushingiye ku mishinge ya Mosaic, ariko rukora neza kandi rufise ubuhinga bwo gukora neza. Mu mwaka w’1995, Netscape yarateye imbere mu gushiramwo ururimi rwa JavaScript, rwateguwe na Brendan Eich, rwatumye amapaji y’urubuga agira ubushobozi, ni ukuvuga ko ashobora gusubiza ibikorwa vy’abakoresha ataco asubiye gushiramwo.



![Image](assets/fr/096.webp)



Kubera ko Netscape Navigator yoroshe gukoresha, ikaba ishobora gukoreshwa n’ibindi bikoresho kandi yihuta, yaciye yihuta kwishingira intahe nk’ikigereranyo c’urubuga ruriko rurakura. Mu mwaka w’1995, yari ifise ibice 90% vy’isoko, ivyo bikaba ari intango y’igihe ca mbere c’ibikoresho vyo ku rubuga. Ivyo vyatumye Microsoft igira ico ikoze, bituma haba intambara y’abacukumbuzi.



### Kuva ku ntambara z'umucukumbuzi gushika ku myaka y'ubutegetsi bw'umuntu umwe



Ivyo Netscape Navigator yaronse hagati mu myaka ya 1990 ntivyatakaye kuri Microsoft, iyo na yo ikaba yatahuye ningoga akamaro k’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha urubuga muri kazoza k’ubuhinga bwa none. Muri Myandagaro 1995, haciye imisi mikeyi Windows 95 isohotse, Microsoft yarasohoye verisiyo ya mbere ya Internet Explorer, mu ntango yari ishingiye ku ruhusha rw’ubudandaji rw’inkomoko ya Spyglass Mosaic (uburyo bw’ubudandaji bwa Mosaic butandukanye n’ubwo bwateguwe muri NCSA).



Verisiyo ya mbere ya Internet Explorer yari ikiri y’intango, ariko Microsoft yatanguye politike y’iterambere ry’ubukazi. Mu mwaka w’1996, Microsoft yakoresheje Internet Explorer 3.0, yaratanguye kwinjiza umucukumbuzi wayo mu buryo butaziguye muri sisitemu ikoresha Windows, ivyo bikaba vyatumye abakoresha batagikeneye gukuraho umucukumbuzi w’uwundi muntu. Ukwo gukorana kwakomejwe na Internet Explorer 4.0 mu 1997, iyo na yo ikaba yashizeho moteri nshasha y’uguhindura amajambo yitwa Trident. Iyi moteri itera imbere cane umuvuduko wo kwerekana urupapuro kandi ikorana cane na Windows Interface.



![Image](assets/fr/097.webp)



Ingamba za Microsoft zishingiye ku buhinga bwinshi n'ubudandaji:




- gushiramwo Internet Explorer muri Windows (yashizweho mbere y’igihe kandi ishobora gukurwamwo ico gihe);
- umucukumbuzi w’ubuntu, ugereranyije na Netscape, yagumye ari ubudandaji gushika ico gihe;
- kugenzura APIs na sisitemu ikoresha kugira ngo bafashe umucukumbuzi wabo wo muhira mu bidukikije vya Windows.



Mu gihe c’iryo higanwa, Netscape yaciye yihuta gutakaza ikibanza. Mu myaka itanu gusa, umugabane wayo mw’isoko waragabanutse cane. Mu ntango z’imyaka ya 2000, Internet Explorer yari ifise umugabane urenga 95% mw’isoko, ivyo bikaba vyatumye ibindi bikoresho vyose bikoreshwa mu kurondera amakuru biba hafi bike.



![Image](assets/fr/098.webp)



Ukwo gukoresha ibintu bimwe bimwe mu buryo bw’impwemu kwatumye habaho uguteba cane kw’ubuhinga bushasha. Kubera ko ata n’umwe yari asigaye yari asigaye yari afise umuhiganwa akomeye, Microsoft yararetse ko iterambere rya Internet Explorer rihagarara. Hagati ya IE6 (yasohotse mu 2001 na Windows XP) na verisiyo yayo yakurikiye IE7 (mu 2006), nta verisiyo nini yasohotse, naho hariho ubugoyagoye mu vy’umutekano, CSS idahuye n’ivyo W3C ivuga. Ukwo guhagarara kw’ubuhinga bwa none kwatumye urubuga rudahinduka imyaka myinshi, kandi rwahatiye abarukora gukora amakode yihariye ku bikoko vya Trident canke inyifato idasanzwe.



Kubera ko Netscape yari izi ko itazosubira guhangana n’abandi mu vy’ubudandaji, yahisemwo gutanga kode yayo y’inkomoko ku bantu bose mu 1998. Ivyo ni vyo vyavutse umugambi wa Mozilla, ivyo bikaba vyatumye habaho ihinduka rikomeye: ugutegura umucukumbuzi w’ubuntu, wubahiriza amategeko, ashigikiwe n’ishirahamwe ryigenga.



Intumbero y’uyu mugambi ni ugusubira kwubaka burundu umucukumbuzi ku mishinge mishasha, n’umucukumbuzi w’ubuhinga bwa none azokwubaha ingingo ngenderwako z’urubuga rwuguruye. Intumbero yari igaragara: gusubizaho ugufunguka n’ugukorana n’urubuga, mu gihe Internet Explorer yariko iranyiganyiga. Ni muri uwo mugambi, haciye imyaka mikeyi, Mozilla Firefox yavutse.



### Ivugurura ry'ubuhinga: Mozilla Firefox na Safari



Inyuma y’imyaka myinshi ihagaze kubera ububasha bwa Internet Explorer, urubuga rwinjiye mu gihe co gusubira gusubirana ubuhinga mu ntango z’imyaka ya 2000. Iryo hinduka ryatangujwe n’abakinyi babiri bakuru: Mozilla na Apple.



Mu mwaka w’2002, umugambi wa Mozilla, wavutse mu gusohora kode y’inkomoko ya Netscape, waratanguje umucukumbuzi mushasha: Phoenix, yihuta guhindura izina Firebird, hanyuma amaherezo Firefox mu mwaka w’2004 kugira ngo ntihagire amakimbirane yo kwita amazina. Firefox yari ishingiye kuri moteri nshasha rwo guhindura, yitwa Gecko, yagenewe kwihuta, kwaguka kandi, ikiruta vyose, kuba intahemuka ku ngingo ngenderwako z’urubuga zasobanuwe na W3C (*World Wide Web Consortium*). Udakunze Trident, Gecko ishigikira ubuhinga bwa none nka CSS 2.1, DOM na SVG (*Ibishushanyo vy’Imirongo Ishobora Guhindurwa*), hamwe n’ugucungera umutekano gukomeye.



![Image](assets/fr/099.webp)



Firefox kandi yashizeho ubuhinga bushasha bwogira ingaruka ziramvye ku gusura urubuga:




- uburyo bwo kwagura bushingiye ku bice, butuma abakoresha bashobora kwongerako ibintu bishasha bitagoranye batakoze ku mutima w’umucukumbuzi;
- tabbed browsing, izwi cane mu bantu bose, naho nyene isanzwe iriho mu bikoresho vya kera nka Opera;
- ibikoresho vy’ubuzima bwite nk’uguhagarika ibimenyetso biza, umucungerezi w’ijambobanga ryinjijwemwo, n’uburyo bwo gutunganya neza amakuru y’ibanga n’ijambo JavaScript.



Uburemere bwayo buke, uguhinduranya no kwubahiriza ingingo mfatirwako vyakwegereye ningoga abakoresha bateye imbere, abakora urubuga n’umuntu wese arondera ubundi buryo bufunguye kuruta Internet Explorer. Mu mwaka w’2005, Firefox yari yararengeye 10% vy’isoko, ivyo bikaba ari ikintu ciza cane ugereranije n’umucukumbuzi yari yarashizwe imbere y’igihe kuri PC zose zikoresha Windows.



Hagati aho, Apple yariko irategura umurongo wayo w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa macOS. Muri Mukakaro 2003, igitabu Safari carasohotse ku mugaragaro. Ishingiye kuri WebKit, moteri y'uguhindura inkomoko yuguruye ikomoka kuri KHTML, yateguwe mbere n'umugambi wa KDE ku mucukumbuzi wayo wa Konqueror. WebKit irashimwa cane kubera uburyo iyoroshe, yihuta kandi yoroshe gutwara. Apple yashizeho ubuhinga bwinshi bwo gutuma ibintu bigenda neza, cane cane mu bijanye no gukora JavaScript, ivyo bikaba vyariko biraba ikibazo nyamukuru kubera ukuntu ubuhinga bwo gukoresha urubuga bwariko buratera imbere.



![Image](assets/fr/100.webp)



Safari yabaye umucukumbuzi w’imbere ku ma Mac yose guhera kuri Mac OS X Panther (10.3), buhoro buhoro asubirira Internet Explorer ya Mac, iyo Microsoft yahevye mu 2005. WebKit na yo izokoreshwa mu nyuma mu zindi mucukumbuzi nyinshi.



Ivyo bikorwa vyatumye habaho uguhiganwa mu vy’ubuhinga, buhoro buhoro bica bigoyagoya ububasha bwa Internet Explorer, kandi bica bituma habaho uruvyaro rushasha rw’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none vyihuta, vyubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako, kandi vyibanda ku guhinduranya, umutekano n’ubushobozi. Hagati y’umwaka wa 2006 n’uwa 2008, Internet Explorer yaratakaje buhoro buhoro umugabane w’isoko, mu gihe Firefox yishizeho nk’iyindi nzira nyamukuru. Ivyo vyatumye habaho ukuza kw’umukinyi mushasha: Google Chrome.



### Ihinduka ry'isoko: ukuza kwa Google Chrome



Ku wa 2 Nzero 2008, Google yatangaje ko isohoye umucukumbuzi wayo bwite: Google Chrome. Iciyo gihe, Firefox yariko iratera imbere kandi Internet Explorer yari ikiriho, ariko yariko iranegurwa cane kubera ko igenda buhoro, idashikamye kandi isigaye inyuma y’ingingo mfatirwako za none. Google, yizigiye cane urubuga ku bikorwa vyayo (ugushaka, Gmail, Ikarata...), yashaka umucukumbuzi akwiye neza igihe c’ibikorwa vy’urubuga bikomeye.



![Image](assets/fr/101.webp)



Chrome mu ntango yari ishingiye ku nkingi zibiri z'ubuhinga:




- moteri yo guhindura WebKit, yarazwe na Safari na KHTML, yo kwerekana HTML/CSS;
- moteri nshasha ya JavaScript, yitwa V8, yanditswe muri C++ ikoranya kode ya JavaScript mu mabwirizwa y’imashini ku nzira (JIT, ku *Just-In-Time*), igatuma ibikorwa vy’urubuga bikora neza cane.



Ariko igikorwa nyaco ca Chrome kiva ku buhinga bwayo bwo gukora ibintu vyinshi. Buri tab ikora mu buryo bwihariye, ikoresheje ubuhinga bwo gutera umusenyi bubuza urupapuro rw’ububisha guhungabanya umucukumbuzi wose. Ukwo kwitandukanya na kwo nyene kuratuma habaho ugushikama: iyo urupapuro rumwe rupfuye, izindi ziguma zikora. Ikindi kuri ivyo ni Interface y’ibintu bikeyi, ishingiye ku birimwo, ata n’umurongo w’ibirimwo, Address n’umurongo w’ugushaka (*Omnibox*) bihuriweko, n’ibintu bishasha vy’inyuma bicereje.



Ishigikiwe n'ikimenyetso ca Google hamwe n'isekeza ryiza cane ryo kwamamaza, Chrome yararonse umugabane w'isoko ningoga. Ukwihuta kwayo n’uko yoroshe gukoresha vyatumye abayikoresha bayikunda. Mu mwaka w’2012, Chrome yararengeye Internet Explorer mu isoko ry’isi yose ku ncuro ya mbere.



![Image](assets/fr/102.webp)



Mu mwaka w’2013, Google yatangaje ihinduka rikomeye ry’ingene yokora: izokoresha Fork WebKit kugira ngo ireme moteri nshasha yigenga yo guhindura amajambo, yitwa Blink. Iyi Fork isigurwa n’itandukaniro ry’ubuhinga n’imitunganirize na Apple, cane cane ku bijanye n’ubwubatsi bwa moteri n’ugushiramwo ibintu vy’igerageza. Blink yabaye moteri yihariye ya Chrome kuva kuri verisiyo ya 28 gushika ubu, hanyuma iraheza ikoreshwa n'izindi nzira nyinshi zo gukoresha: Opera (yahevye Presto mu 2013), Vivaldi, Brave, Microsoft Edge (kuva muri 2020), n'izindi.



Kuva mu mwaka w’2025, Google Chrome ifise ibice 66% vy’isoko ry’isi yose ku bikoresho vyose (mudasobwa, amatelefone ngendanwa, amatablette), nk’uko bigaragara mu makuru ya StatCounter. Ikurikirwa cane na Safari (ahanini kuri iOS/macOS), Microsoft Edge, na Firefox, umugabane wayo w’isoko uguma ugabanuka. Ubukuru bwa Chrome bwarashitse kandi mu bidukikije vy’amatelefone ngendanwa biciye kuri Android WebView (igice c’ubuhinga gikoreshwa n’ibihumbi vy’ibikoresho), na co nyene kikaba cizigiye Blink.



Chrome yarahinduye cane ubushobozi, umutekano n’ingingo mfatirwako z’ubuhinga bwa none, mu gihe yavyura ingorane nshasha mu gushiramwo no gushiramwo ubuhinga bwo ku rubuga.



### Ugutera imbere kw'amamoteri yo guhindura: kuva kuri Trident gushika kuri Blink



Moteri y’uguhindura ni co gice nyamukuru c’umucukumbuzi w’urubuga. Uruhara rwayo nyamukuru ni ugusobanura amadosiye yakiriwe na server (HTML, CSS, JavaScript, amashusho, imyandikire...) ku generate igishushanyo gikorana Interface. Moteri y’uguhindura ni nk’umusemuzi hagati y’indimi z’urubuga n’igicapo cawe, ihindura imirongo ya kode mu rupapuro ruhuye, rukora kandi rukora.



Mu majambo nyayo, iyo winjije URL mu murongo wa Address:




- Mucukumbuzi yohereza ubusabe bwa HTTP kuri server iri kure;
- Serveri yishura n’inyandiko ya HTML;
- Moteri y’uguhindura isesangura iyo HTML, igakuraho amadosiye ahuye (CSS, JavaScript, amashusho...);
- Yubaka "DOM" (*Icitegererezo c'Ikintu c'Inyandiko*) kigereranya imiterere y'inyandiko;
- Ikoresha amategeko ya CSS kugira ngo ibare ukuntu ikintu cose kigaragazwa (*layout*);
- Ihindura ibishushanyo ikoresheje ikarata y’ibishushanyo n’uburyo bwo gukoresha idirisha.



Iyi nzira yose ikeneye kwihuta kandi igenda neza kugira ngo itange ubumenyi bwiza bw’abakoresha, mbere no ku mapaji atoroshe. Ivyo ni vyo vy’ukuri uruhara rwa moteri y’uguhindura.



Aha niho hari insiguro y'amateka y'ibikoresho nyamukuru vyahinduye iterambere ry'urubuga:



#### Igikoko gitatu (1997 - 2015)



Trident yakozwe na Microsoft ku rubuga rwa Internet Explorer 4, ni moteri yari iganje ku rubuga mu ntango z’imyaka ya 2000, mu mutima w’intambara z’abacukumbuzi. Naho mu misi yayo ya mbere yari ifise ubuhinga bushasha, yaciye yihuta gusubira inyuma mu bijanye no kwubahiriza ingingo mfatirwako za W3C, ivyo bica bituma habaho imbuga nyinshi zatunganijwe gusa kuri Internet Explorer.



Trident kandi yarerekanye ingorane z’umutekano be n’umuduga wa JavaScript ugenda buhoro. Abahinguzi b’urubuga kenshi bategerezwa kwandika kode yihariye kugira ngo bashobore gukora hirya no hino y’ibibazo vyarwo. Microsoft yarayisubirije mu 2015 na EdgeHTML, moteri y’ubuhinga bwa none cane yananiwe guhindura iyo nzira. Trident iguma ari ikigereranyo c’igihe moteri yoshobora gushinga amategeko yayo bwite ku rubuga.



![Image](assets/fr/103.webp)



*Isoko : pcisi.com*



#### Inzoka (1998)



Gecko yakozwe na Netscape, hanyuma ikabungabungwa n’ishirahamwe Mozilla, itanga ubushobozi ku mucukumbuzi wa Firefox. Kuva mu ntango, Gecko yarabaye uwukomeye mu bijanye no kwubahiriza ingingo mfatirwako. Yanditswe mu rurimi rwa C++ kandi ishigikira ama platforms menshi.



Gecko ni yo yatumye habaho ibintu vyinshi bishasha. Ariko rero, ishingiro ryayo ry’amakode rigoye kandi ry’akahise rituma ubwihindurize bumwebumwe bugenda buhoro.



Ku bijanye n’umugabane w’isoko, Gecko ubu iri inyuma cane ya Blink, kuko Firefox ariyo yonyene ikoresha umucukumbuzi munini. Ikoreshwa kandi ku ruhande n’ibikoresho bitazwi cane kandi bikoreshwa cane ari vyo bikoresho vya Firefox: Tor Browser, LibreWolf, Zen Browser, GNU IceCat, Waterfox... Ivyo bituma Gecko iba umushingantahe w’ubudasa ku rubuga, mu gihe Blink ari yo itwara.



![Image](assets/fr/104.webp)



#### KHTML (1998 - 2005)



Yateguwe n'umugambi wa KDE ku mucukumbuzi wayo wa Konqueror, KHTML ni moteri yoroshe, ifise ibice kandi yihuta. Yanditswe mu rurimi rwa C++, yubaha ingingo mfatirwako kandi itanga ishingiro risukuye kandi ry’inyandiko nziza. Iyi moteri ni yo Apple yahisemwo mu 2001 kugira ngo ikore WebKit. KHTML rero ni umukurambere w’ubuhinga bwa Chrome na Safari.



![Image](assets/fr/105.webp)



#### Urubuga (2003)



WebKit ni Fork ya KHTML yatangujwe na Apple kugira ngo ikore umucukumbuzi wayo bwite: Safari. Yabanje gutunganirizwa neza kugira ngo ikore neza kandi ikoreshe macOS, hanyuma ikoreshwa na Google Chrome igihe yasohoka mu 2008. WebKit ishingiye ku bice bibiri:




- WebCore ku guhindura HTML/CSS ;
- JavaScriptCore (izwi kandi nka "Nitro") y'ugushitsa kode ya JavaScript.



WebKit igaragara cane kubera umuvuduko wayo n’ikirenge gitoyi. Ku bijanye na iOS, Apple yategetse ko ikoreshwa ku bikoresho vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa none kubera umutekano n’ugukoresha neza inguvu: mbere na Firefox canke Chrome kuri iPhone zikoresha WebKit munsi y’igipfukisho.



![Image](assets/fr/106.webp)



#### Gupfuka amaso (2013)



Blink ni Fork ya WebKit yatangujwe na Google kugira ngo ikoreshe Chrome (na Chromium), hanyuma ifata vuba cane na Opera, Brave, Vivaldi, mbere na Microsoft Edge kuva mu 2020.



![Image](assets/fr/107.webp)



Muri iki gihe, Blink ni moteri ikoreshwa cane mu guhindura amajambo kw’isi yose. Ariko rero, ubwo busumbasumbane buravyura ikibazo c’ubuhinga bumwe bumwe ku rubuga, ariko ivyo tuzobigarukako mu nyuma.



#### Uruhande rw'Ibikoresho (2015 - 2020)



Igikurikira Trident, EdgeHTML cakozwe na Microsoft kugira ngo Edge ibe iya none, ifise ubushobozi bwo gukora neza kandi ihuye neza. Irimwo bimwe mu bimenyetso vya Trident, ariko ikaba ifise moteri ya JavaScript yahinduwe. Naho ivyo bikorwa vyakozwe, EdgeHTML yarananiwe kwemeza abakoresha n’abakora urubuga. Muri 2020, Microsoft yahisemwo guheba EdgeHTML kugira ngo ikoreshe Blink, itanguza Edge Chromium, yacitse umucukumbuzi wa Blink afise Microsoft Interface Layer.



![Image](assets/fr/108.webp)



Ugutera imbere kw’amamoteri yo guhindura amajambo yerekana amateka y’urubuga: uguhuzagurika hagati y’uguhingura ibintu bishasha n’ugushinga urugero, ukuganza kw’abakinyi bakuru, ukugerageza uburyo bundi bwo guhindura ibintu bushingiye ku nyifato runtu canke ubuhinga. Ubu, hafi amashakisha yose ashingiye kuri Blink, uretse Firefox (Gecko) na Safari (WebKit).



### Blink araganza, Gecko aragwana



Kuva Blink yaremwa muri 2013 no kwemerwa kwayo cane mu bikoresho vyose bikoreshwa na Chromium, iyo moteri yo guhindura ni yo yabaye ihambaye. Mu mwaka w’2025, ntizotanga ubushobozi kuri Google Chrome gusa, ariko kandi izotanga ubushobozi kuri Microsoft Edge (kuva mu mwaka w’2020), Opera, Brave, Vivaldi n’izindi nzira nyinshi zitazwi cane. Ubukuru bwayo burenze 80% vy’isoko ku bikoresho vy’ibiro, na cane cane kuri Android, aho Chrome iza imbere y’igihe.



Ivyo bizana inyungu zimwe zimwe: Blink irakomeye kandi ishigikiwe n’imigwi ikomeye y’abahinga (Google, ariko kandi na Microsoft n’abandi), kandi iratera imbere cane. Blink kandi irafasha mu gutuma habaho uguhuza ibintu bimwe bimwe: abahinguzi b’urubuga barashobora gushimikira ku rubuga rumwe kugira ngo bashikire hafi abakoresha bose. Ariko kandi, ukwo kwibanda ku kintu kurafise ingorane zikomeye mu bijanye n’imiterere.



Ku ruhande rumwe, ishira ku ruhande izindi moteri, cane cane Gecko, zikoreshwa hafi gusa na Firefox. Mu mwaka w’2025, Firefox izogira umugabane w’isoko uri munsi ya 6%, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane ubushobozi bwayo bwo gutuma ijwi ryayo ryumvikana mu biganiro ku bijanye n’iterambere ry’ingingo ngenderwako z’urubuga (W3C, WHATWG). Gecko itunganywa na Mozilla, ishirahamwe ritagira inyungu rifise ubutunzi buke cane kuruta Google. Moteri iguma ishobora guhangana n’ibindi ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bumwe bumwe (cane cane ugukingira ubuzima bwite), ariko irashikirwa n’ugusubira inyuma mu gushirwa mu ngiro API zimwe zimwe zo muri iki gihe. Kandi iki kintu kiri mu nzinguzingu y’ububisha: Gecko ntikora neza cane, ivyo bikaba bituma umubare w’abakoresha ugabanuka, ivyo bikaba bitera intege abahinguzi b’imbuga zabo gukora neza cane kubera Gecko, rero Gecko ntikora neza cane... n’ibindi.



![Image](assets/fr/109.webp)



Ku rundi ruhande, ukwo gushiramwo ibintu vyose bikikije Blink bisigura ko Google de facto igenzura urugero rw’iterambere n’ivy’ubuhinga vy’urubuga. Ariko rero, inyungu zayo z’ubudandaji (kwamamaza, gukurikirana inyifato, uburyo bw’abanyagihugu, n’ibindi) zishobora guhushanya ingingo ngenderwako z’ukutagira aho zibogamiye, ugukorana n’abandi n’ubuzima bwite zari ziburanishijwe mu mateka n’abakinyi nka Mozilla.



Ikindi, kwizigira moteri imwe gusa biratuma habaho ingorane ku bidukikije vyo ku rubuga. Iyo Blink ishizeho ugusubira inyuma, ugushira ahabona canke akaga, ingaruka zigira ico zikoze ku bakoresha bose. Ubutandukane bw’ubuhinga burafise uruhara rwo kwihangana hano, nk’uko nyene bugira uruhara mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha n’ubuhinga bwo kwubaka porogarama.



Ubu, Mozilla irabandanya kugira uruhara runini mu kurwanira urubuga rwuguruye, rwubahiriza ubuzima bwite kandi rushobora gushikwako ata nkomanzi. Firefox iguma ari imwe mu nzira nke zikomeye zidashingiye kuri Chromium, kandi itanga ubuhinga bushasha bwigenga. Ariko ukurokoka kwayo kuva ku bushobozi bwayo bwo kuguma ifise abayikoresha bihagije be n’amahera aramba.



Ubutegetsi bwa Blink rero si ikintu c’ubuhinga gusa: bujanye n’ivya politike, ubutunzi n’imibano mu bijanye n’uburongozi bw’urubuga. Muri ivyo, guteza imbere moteri y’uguhindura vyinshi biguma ari akamenyero keza mu gushigikira urubuga rudafise aho rugarukira, rutekanye kandi rukomeye.



Mu myaka mirongo itatu, umucukumbuzi w’urubuga yarahindutse kuva ku gikoresho coroshe co kuraba gushika ku rubuga rwa porogarama rukomeye, rwinjijwe mu mutima w’ubumenyi bwacu bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none ku musi ku musi. Gutahura iyo nzira y’iterambere ry’amateka biratomora akamaro k’ingene umucukumbuzi akora mu bibazo vy’umutekano n’ubusegaba bw’ubuhinga bwa none.



Mu kigabane gikurikira, Tuzotanga icegeranyo c’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none biriho ubu, kuva ku bikoresho vya kera gushika ku bikoresho vyo muri kazoza, tugereranye ivyiza n’ibibi vyavyo kugira ngo bigufashe guhitamwo neza.



## Incamake y'umucukumbuzi


<chapterId>4a9f71bc-8d76-4ce3-b983-2df1d6e47fb5</chapterId>



Tumaze gutohoza amateka n’iterambere ry’ama browser, ubu turaza kuraba ama browser nyamukuru ariho uno musi. Guhitamwo umucukumbuzi si ikintu kidahambaye cane cane iyo, nk’uko biri kuri twebwe, ikintu ca mbere ari umutekano, ubuzima bwite n’ubusegaba bwa digitale. Buri mucukumbuzi arafise ivyiza vyihariye, ariko kandi arafise intege nke, akenshi zifitaniye isano n’uburyo bw’ubudandaji bwabo canke amahitamwo yabo y’ubuhinga.



Intumbero y’iki kigabane ni ukugufasha guhitamwo umucukumbuzi akwiye neza ivyo ukeneye. Nazitunganije nkoresheje moteri y’uguhindura, ariko urutonde ntirugaragaza ubwoko ubwo ari bwo bwose bw’ugushirwa ku rutonde.



### Mucukumbuzi zishingiye kuri Blink



#### Google Chrome



[Chrome](https://www.google.com/chrome/) inyungu mu gutera imbere vyihuta kandi bikomeza, ahanini birongowe na Google. Imenyekana kubera ubushobozi bwayo bwinshi, umuvuduko, ukuntu ihuye cane n’ingingo mfatirwako z’urubuga rwa none be n’ugushiramwo neza ibikorwa vya Google.



![Image](assets/fr/110.webp)



Ariko rero, mu bijanye n’umutekano n’ubuzima bwite, Chrome iravyura ivyiyumviro bikomeye. Ku buryo busanzwe, umucukumbuzi akorakoranya amakuru menshi ku bakoresha bayo (gucukura, gushaka, amateka...), akoreshwa cane cane mu kwamamaza na Google. Ubushobozi bwo gutandukanya amakuru n’abakurikirana burafise aho bugarukira, kandi guhagarika burundu ugukurikirana biracari bigoye. Kandi, naho Chrome yoba itekanye mu buryo bw’ubuhinga (sandbox ikora neza, guhindura vyihuse...), iguma igenzurwa n’umukinyi akomeye inyungu ziwe z’ubudandaji zidahuye n’ubusegaba nyakuri bw’ubuhinga bwa none.



Ikindi co kwitwararika ni uko kubera iyo nzira y’umuvuduko n’ugusobanuka, Chrome ikoresha ibikoresho vyinshi cane vya system, cane cane RAM.



Google Chrome ishingiye ku mugambi wa Chromium, ariko ni inkomoko yuguruye. Ariko rero, Google yongerako kode nyinshi z’uburenganzira. Rero ntifatwa nk’inkomoko yuguruye yuzuye.



Rero sinzogusaba gukoresha Google Chrome, haba ku giti cawe canke ku kazi (kiretse, vy’ukuri, ubucuruzi bwawe buvana na Google suite). Nkako, hariho uburyo bwiza cane bwo gukoresha Google, haba mu karere no mu gicu. Cane cane, ndabatumiye kumenya ibikorwa bitangwa na Proton :



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/proton-mail-c3b010ce-254d-4546-b382-19ab9261c6a2

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/proton-drive-03cbe49f-6ddc-491f-8786-bc20d98ebb16

#### Intwari



[Brave](https://intwari.com/) ishingiye kuri Blink (nka Chrome), ariko itandukanye cane n’uburyo bwayo bushingiye ku buzima bwite. Ku mbuga, Brave irabuza amatangazo n’abakurikirana, igashiramwo *HTTPS Everywhere*, kandi itanga uburinzi buteye imbere ku bimenyetso vy’intoke n’inyandiko z’abandi. Uburyo bwayo bwo gukora ubucuruzi bushingiye ku kwamamaza kw’ubuzima bwite, ariko ivyo biguma ari ivy’uguhitamwo kandi bishobora guhagarara bitagoranye.



Brave ishingiye kuri Chromium kandi kode yayo yose iraboneka kuri GitHub. Ibice bitobito vyonyene ni vyo bifise igice c’uburenganzira. Muri rusangi, Brave iri hafi cane y’umucukumbuzi w’inkomoko yuguruye.



![Image](assets/fr/111.webp)



Brave ni uburyo bukomeye bwo gusubirira Chrome, bufatanya umuvuduko, umutekano mwiza, ubuzima bwite bwiza ku buryo busanzwe na Interface. Ariko rero, sinzoyigira inama, kubera gusa ishingiye kuri Chromium.



Naho ama browser menshi (harimwo na Brave) ashingiye kuri Chromium mu gihe avuga ko ari uburyo bwo gucungera ubuzima bwite, itohoza ryakozwe muri 2024 ryerekanye ko hariho ubufatanye, ku buryo busanzwe, bwa API yemerera Google kuronka amakuru y’agaciro yerekeye ibikoresho vy’ukoresha (CPU, GPU, Google her services canke RAM), nk’uko. Iyi API, yinjijwe nk’iyindi nzira idashobora gukurwaho muri Chrome, yariho kandi mu bikoresho vyinshi bikomoka kuri Edge, Opera... mbere na Brave.



Naho Brave kuva ico gihe yazimye iyi API, iki kibazo kirerekana neza ukuntu izo nzira zishingiye kuri Chromium, iguma ari umugambi uboshe cane ku bidukikije vya Google. Nk’inyishu, mbere n’ibindi bikoresho vy’ubuzima bwite vya Chromium ntibishobora gutanga ubwigenge bwose canke uburinzi bwose bw’amakuru y’abakoresha.



→ "***fingerprinting***" mu bijanye no gusura kuri internet yerekeza ku buhinga bujanye n'ugukusanya no gusuzuma amakuru yihariye kandi rimwe na rimwe yihariye yerekeye aho ukoresha, kugira ngo umenye kandi ukurikirane ku mbuga zitandukanye, ata gukoresha ibimenyetso bigaragara nk'amakuru y'ibanga. Aya makuru ashobora kubamwo:




- IP yawe Address,
- Uwuguha interineti,
- Aho uri,
- Mucukumbuzi yawe n'imiterere yayo,
- Sisitemu yawe ikoresha,
- Verisiyo ya porogaramu yawe,
- Imyandikire yashizweho,
- Igishushanyo c'igicapo cawe n'ubunini bwaco,
- Uburebure bw'ibara,
- Isaha yawe n'ururimi rwawe,
- HTML5 igitambaro,
- Isesengura ry'ibishushanyo,
- Ukwagura umucukumbuzi wawe,
- n'ibindi...



Kugira ngo umenye nimba urutoke rwawe rw’umucukumbuzi rutuma uba uwudasanzwe canke nimba wifatanya n’abantu benshi, urashobora gukoresha urubuga rukurikira: https://amiunique.org/



#### Vivaldi



[Vivaldi](https://vivaldi.com/), yashinzwe n’uwahoze ari umuyobozi mukuru wa Opera, iriko irashimikira ku bakoresha bateye imbere barondera ubuhinga bwo guhindura ibintu vyimbitse n’ibintu vy’ubuhinga nk’ibipande vyo ku ruhande, umuyobozi w’ibice vy’ubuhinga buhanitse n’ugufata amajambo ateye imbere.



Ku bijanye n’umutekano, Vivaldi irimwo ibintu vyinshi vyo kubuza abakurikirana n’amatangazo, ariko ivyo bikingirwa biguma bigoyagoya gatoyi kuruta Brave. Kandi ntaco igaragara cane mu bintu bimwebimwe, kuko kode yayo y’inkomoko ari inkomoko yuguruye gusa igice. Naho biri ukwo, itanga ubundi buryo bushimishije, butashimikiye cane ku buzima bwite bukomeye kuruta Brave, ariko bushimikiye cane kuri Chrome canke Opera.



![Image](assets/fr/112.webp)



#### Opera



[Opera](https://www.opera.com/) ni urubuga rwa kera, rwamaze igihe kirekire ruriho kuva mu 1995. Ubu rukoresha Blink inyuma yo guheba moteri yarwo (*Presto*). Ifise Interface y’ubu n’ibintu bimwe bimwe bishasha.



Ariko rero, ku bijanye n’ubuzima bwite, Opera iratera impaka cane: yari ifiswe n’ishirahamwe ry’Abashinwa kuva mu 2016, ivyo bikaba vyatumye haba ibibazo ku bijanye n’ukuntu amakuru y’abakoresha yoshobora gukoreshwa nabi. Opera irimwo VPN yunze ubumwe (proxy aho kuba VPN y’ukuri), ariko amategeko y’ubuzima bwite ntasobanutse ku bijanye n’ugucungera inyandiko. Opera na yo ni umucukumbuzi w’ibintu. Ntivyiza rero, canecane igihe ubuzima bwite ari bwo buhambaye.



![Image](assets/fr/113.webp)



#### Mucukumbuzi yihariye



Mucukumbuzi zishingiye ku Blink zirimwo n'izindi mucukumbuzi zo ku ruhande, akenshi zigenewe guhura n'ibintu vy'ikoreshwa vyihariye:





- Arc** :



Yateguwe n'ishirahamwe ry'umucukumbuzi, [Arc](https://arc.net/) itanga uburyo butandukanye cane n'uwukoresha Interface. Isubirira ama tabs ya kera n'uburyo bwa "*ibibanza*", umurongo w'inyuma ubumwe, kandi igashiramwo ibikoresho vy'ubuhinga nk'ibifatwa bishobora gusobanurwamwo n'umuhinduzi w'urubuga woroshe. Ico gishimikiyeko ni ugukoresha, guhindura amashusho n’ugukoresha neza, ivyo bikaba bituma iki gikoresho gikundwa n’abahinga bamwebamwe.



Mu bijanye n’ubuhinga, Arc ishingiye kuri Chromium, ariko iguma ari porogarama y’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Nta guseruka itanga ku bijanye n’ugukusanya amakuru, kandi ingingo ngenderwako zayo z’ubuzima bwite ziguma zidatomoye, cane cane iyo bije ku bijanye n’ugupima amakuru n’uguhuza amakuru mu gicu. Bikwiye rero kwirindwa mu buryo bw’ubusegaba bwa digitale.



![Image](assets/fr/114.webp)





- Igipande** :



[Polypane](https://polypane.app/) igenewe cane cane abahinguzi b’imbere n’abahinguzi ba UX. Igikorwa yayo nyamukuru ni ugushira ahabona icarimwe ingero nyinshi z’urubuga rumwe ku nzira zitandukanye z’ibarabara, kugira ngo igerageze inyifato *yishura* ya Interface mu gihe nyaco. Itanga kandi ibikoresho vyo gushikira, ibikoresho vy’ugushingira intahe HTML/CSS, ibikoresho vy’ugupima amabara n’ibipimo vy’ibikorwa.



Polypane ni umucukumbuzi w’umunyagihugu, yishurwa, ashingiye kuri Chromium, ivyo bikaba bituma ari mwiza cane mu gukoreshwa n’abahinga rimwe na rimwe. Ntiyibereye gukoreshwa mu gusura buri musi, kandi amategeko yayo yerekeye ubuzima bwite arahuye n’amaporogarama y’ubudandaji, nta n’imwe yizeye.



![Image](assets/fr/116.webp)



### Mucukumbuzi zishingiye kuri Gecko



#### Mozila Firefox



[Firefox](https://www.mozilla.org/firefox/new/) ni umucukumbuzi azwi cane akoresha moteri y'uguhindura Gecko. Yateguwe na Mozilla Foundation, Firefox iratandukanye n’ingingo ngenderwako zayo zitomoye z’ubuzima bwite: uburinzi bwo gukurikirana, uburyo buteye imbere bwo kubuza amakuru y’uwundi muntu, ibikoresho vy’amabara bitandukanye, n’ugushiramwo ivyungura vyerekeye umutekano.



Mozilla ni ishirahamwe ridaharanira inyungu, ivyo bikaba biyiha ubwigenge bukeyi ku nyungu z’ubudandaji gusa, naho yoba iguma yizigiye cane mu vy’amahera ubufatanye na Google. Iyi ya nyuma ahanini itanga amahera kuri Mozilla Foundation, ku mugaragaro kugira ngo moteri yayo y’ubushakashatsi igumye ari yo ikoreshwa muri Firefox, gutyo igumye ifise umugabane wayo mw’isoko. Mu buryo butazwi, iyo nzira ituma Google iguma ifise uburyo bwo guhiganwa bugenzurwa: mu gushigikira Mozilla, Google iguma ifise umuhiganwa mutoyi, ivyo bikaba bigabanya ibirego vyo gukoresha nabi ikibanza c’ubukuru kandi bikagabanya ingorane zo guhanwa n’amategeko.



![Image](assets/fr/117.webp)



Firefox ni umucukumbuzi w'inkomoko yuguruye, ikwiragizwa hakurikijwe MPL (*Uruhusha rwa bose rwa Mozilla*). Kode yayo ni ubuntu rwose, irashobora guhindurwa kandi igasubira gukwiragizwa, kandi ni co kintu abantu benshi bava hanze batanga.



Firefox iguma ari ikigereranyo c’umutekano n’ubuzima bwite, naho nyene isigaye inyuma gatoyi y’ibikoresho bikoresha Blink mu bijanye n’ibikorwa bimwebimwe. Ishobora kuba umucukumbuzi mwiza cane, igihe cose itunganijwe neza.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/firefox-11814cec-3415-4ed9-a06e-f6fda5c9510f
#### Mucukumbuzi wa Tor



[Umucukumbuzi wa Tor](https://www.umugambi.org/gukuraho/) ni umucukumbuzi ashingiye kuri Firefox ESR. Ni kimwe mu bisubizo bikomeye cane vyo kutamenyekana kuri internet. Ihindura inzira y’uruja n’uruza biciye ku rubuga rwa Tor, gutyo ikabuza isano ryose hagati y’uwukoresha n’aho urubuga ruja.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/tor-browser-a847e83c-31ef-4439-9eac-742b255129bb

Ikibi ni ukugabanya cane ubushobozi (high latency) n’uguhuza n’imbuga zimwe zimwe. Tor Browser ni nziza cane ku bikorwa bikomeye (itangazamakuru, ubukangurambaga...), ariko ntibereye cane gukoreshwa mu buryo busanzwe bwa misi yose.



![Image](assets/fr/118.webp)



#### Mucukumbuzi ya Mullvad


[Umucukumbuzi wa Mullvad](https://mullvad.net/ru/umucukumbuzi) ni ingaruka y’ubufatanye hagati y’ishirahamwe Tor Foundation na Mullvad VPN. Ishingiye ku mucukumbuzi wa Tor, uwo ubwawo akomoka kuri Firefox ESR. Mullvad Browser yakozwe kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gukoresha neza ubuzima bwiwe bwite. Ku mburabuzi, harimwo uburinzi buteye imbere ku bimenyetso vy’intoke, abakurikirana n’inyandiko z’abandi.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-browser-a16c13d6-8bf9-4cb5-9aa0-85411a9cda0e

Ifise vyinshi mu bijanye n’umutekano n’ubuzima bwite bitangwa na Tor Browser, hariho itandukaniro rimwe: ntihindura inzira y’uruja n’uruza biciye ku rubuga rwa Tor. Kugira ngo wirinde gusohoka kwa IP Address, ushobora kuyikoresha hamwe na VPN (vyiza cane, Mullvad VPN).


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

Mullvad Browser ni umuti mwiza cane nimba uhangayikishijwe n’ubuzima bwite bwawe, waba uri uwutangura canke uwuteye imbere.



![Image](assets/fr/119.webp)



#### Igikoko



[LibreWolf](https://librewolf.net/) ni umucukumbuzi akoreshwa na Firefox yagenewe gutanga urugero rwo hejuru rw'ubuzima bwite. Ikuraho ibintu vyose bishobora gutuma umuntu agira ubuzima bwite, nk’ubuhinga bwo gupima uburebure, gukorana n’ibikorwa vya Mozilla n’ibikorwa vya Pocket.



Ku mburabuzi, LibreWolf ikoresha imiterere y'umutekano ya Firefox (nk'uburyo bwo gukurikirana bukomeye) kandi igahagarika ubufasha bwa DRM. Uwo mugambi wose ni uwufunguye, ushingiye ku kibano, kandi ntushingiye ku mahera iyo ari yo yose ava mu bigo vyigenga. Ndagusaba nimba uriko urarondera Firefox "ikomeye", ifise ububasha bwinshi ku makuru yawe.



![Image](assets/fr/115.webp)



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/librewolf-1783e9dc-9d41-4449-a3cf-ed116849057c

#### Umucukumbuzi wa Zen


[Zen Browser](https://zen-browser.app/) ni umucukumbuzi w’ubuntu kandi yuguruye ashingiye kuri Firefox (moteri ya Gecko), yatangujwe mu 2024. Intumbero yayo ni ugutanga ubuhinga bwo gucukumbuza bugezweho, buteye igomwe, bushobora guhindurwa cane kandi hejuru ya vyose bushingiye ku buzima bwite, ataco bushingiye kuri Chmium.


Zen igaragara kubera uburyo bwayo bukomeye bwo gukoresha Interface n’ubushobozi bwo kuyikoresha, ahanini ihumekewe n’umucukumbuzi wa Arc, ariko ikabohorwa kuri yo kubera kamere yayo y’inkomoko yuguruye na moteri ya Gecko. Birimwo :



- Interface y'ibintu bikeyi, ifise umurongo w'inyuma uhagaze w'ibice, ivyerekanwa bigabanywe, n'uburyo bwa *ahantu h'akazi* bwo gushiramwo ibice vy'ibice hakurikijwe umugambi;
- Uburyo bw’ibigereranyo vya Interface bishobora guhindurwa (*Zen Mods*) bishobora gukoreshwa mu guhindura cane ukuntu umucukumbuzi asa;
- Umurimo w'umwimerere witwa *Glance*, ufungura uruja n'uruza mw'idirisha ry'igihe gito ryoroshe, wirinda uruja n'uruza rw'ibice...


Zen kandi irashigikira ivyungura Firefox, hamwe n'uguhuza biciye kuri konti ya Mozilla.


Kuva ku bijanye n’umutekano n’ubuzima bwite, Zen irafise uburinzi bw’abakurikirana abandi. Mucukumbuzi ubwayo nta makuru yegeranya, kandi iremeza kandi ko telemetry ya Mozilla idakora. Ica kandi ihita yanka ivyemezo vya SSL vya kera canke bitajanye n’amategeko.


Zen Browser ni uburyo bushimishije nimba uriko urarondera ahantu ho gukoresha Gecko ku buntu, harimwo ubuhinga bushasha, hatagiramwo ibintu vyinshi kandi bubaha ubuzima bwite bwawe.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/zen-browser-f1afc500-1933-409a-a2b7-b6c1c43ec285

### WebKit ishingiye ku mucukumbuzi


#### Safari


Mucukumbuzi nyamukuru ikoresha moteri yo guhindura WebKit (si Fork nka Blink) ni Safari. [Safari]() ni umucukumbuzi wa Apple yihariye kuri macOS. Itanga ubufatanye bwiza cane n’ibidukikije vya Apple, ikora neza cane, ubu ikaba irimwo uburinzi bukomeye bwo gukurikirana no gufata urutoke.


Ariko Safari iguma yugaye, igarukira kuri macOS kubera verisiyo yayo y’ibiro, kandi iva ku bidukikije vya Apple. Naho Apple ifise politike ikomeye y’ubuzima bwite, n’uburyo bwayo bwo gukora ubucuruzi bushingiye ahanini ku kugurisha ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none aho gushingira ku kwamamaza, biraguma bitamenyekana ku bijanye n’imigenzo imwe imwe yo mu mutima.


Aha, turiko twibanda ku bikoresho vyo ku biro, ariko birahambaye kumenya ko kuri iOS, Apple isaba ko ibikoresho vyose bikoresha moteri y’uguhindura WebKit (ikintu gishobora guhinduka vuba, ariko, kubera amategeko amwamwe y’i Buraya). Ivyo bisigura ko ama browser nka Chrome, Firefox canke Brave ategerezwa, kuri iOS, gutanga porogarama ishingiye kuri WebKit, atari kuri moteri yabo isanzwe yo guhindura.



![Image](assets/fr/120.webp)



#### Oriyoni



Iyindi nzira iryoshe cane yo gusubirira Safari ni [Orion](https://kagi.com/orion/), umucukumbuzi w’ubuhinga bwa none yagenewe gusa ibidukikije vya Apple, kandi na yo ishingiye kuri WebKit. Intumbero yayo ni ugutanga uburyo bwihuta, buremereye kandi bubaha cane ubuzima bwite, ataco buhinduye ku bintu biteye imbere.



Orion itandukanye na Safari mu buryo bwinshi bw’ubuhinga:




- Ifata politike ikomeye y’ubuhinga bwa zero telemetry: nta makuru yegeranywa canke arungikwa ku buryo busanzwe, harimwo n’igihe co gushiramwo ubwa mbere;
- Harimwo igikoresho co kubuza kwamamaza n’ugukurikirana gishoboka ku buryo busanzwe, kigereranywa mu bushobozi na *uBlock Origin* mu bihe vyinshi;
- Ishigikira mu buryo bw'imvukira gushiramwo no gukoresha ivyungura Chrome na Firefox mu buryo bw'imvukira kuri macOS ;
- Ibikoresho vy’ingirakamaro birimwo uburyo bwa *Focus*(Interface-ubuntu bwo kugendagenda), uburyo bw’inguvu nke n’uburongozi bw’ibice bihagaze.



Orion yose yakozwe n’umugwi wa Kagi (uzwi cane kubera ubushakashatsi butagira amatangazo). Iterambere ryayo riterwa inkunga n’abayikoresha gusa biciye ku nzira ya *Orion+*, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kuronka inyungu zitari nke.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/orion-browser-a5f225d4-946f-425a-8d8e-3a3ec0174a76
### Mucukumbuzi zitagira moteri zihindura



Ubwa nyuma, ndashaka gusozera iyi nsiguro n’ubundi buryo butazwi cane kandi butari bwo: ubuhinga bwo gukoresha amajambo, ubuzwi cane muri bwo ni [Umucukumbuzi wa Lynx](https://lynx.invisible-island.net/).



Lynx ni urubuga rwa kera cane rukiriho (1992). Ikora gusa mu buryo bw'inyandiko kandi ikoreshwa ataco ihinduye mu nzira, ata gishushanyo Interface. Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Lynx ntishigikira JavaScript, CSS canke amashusho, ivyo bikaba bikuraho ugushirwa mu ngiro kwa kode yose ikora kuri paji z’urubuga. Isobanura gusa kode ya HTML idasanzwe, iyo ihindura nk'umwandiko utunganijwe.



Ubu buryo busanzwe buyigira imwe mu nzira zitekanye cane: nta nyandiko mbi ishobora gukora, nta kwamamaza kwinjira mu mutima kugaragazwa, kandi nta makuru ashobora gusohoka biciye ku buryo bwa none (ugufata urutoke ku gipande, gukurikirana JavaScript, n’ibindi) bishoboka.



![Image](assets/fr/121.webp)



Ivyo bigaragara ko bifise aho bigarukira: ukubura rwose uguhindura ibishushanyo, ukudashobora gukoresha imbuga nyinshi zo muri iki gihe (vyinshi muri vyo bivana na JavaScript) n’ubuhinga busanzwe bugenewe abakoresha bazi utuntu n’utundi.



Lynx irashobora kuba iryoshe mu bihe bimwe bimwe vyihariye:




- Gusuzuma amapaji y'urubuga ya HTML atagiramwo JavaScript canke CSS;
- Gusura mu bidukikije vy’ubuhinga buke;
- Gusura mu bidukikije bitekanye cane;
- Gusura ku nzira zigenda buhoro cane canke zidashikamye;
- Ivy’ukwikoresha canke gukaraba.



### Ni uwuhe mucukumbuzi wohitamwo?



Ku bakoresha bashira imbere umutekano n’ubuzima bwite ku buryo busanzwe, batabwirizwa guhindura n’amaboko amasetingi menshi, kandi barondera umucukumbuzi w’intumbero rusangi ku musi ku musi, amahitamwo meza cane mu vyiyumviro vyanje ni LibreWolf na Mullvad Browser. Mu rwego rumwe, nimba udafise ikibazo co gukoresha urufatiro rwa Chromium (naho hari ingorane zirimwo n’ubuhinga butandukanye cane), woshobora kandi kwiyumvira Brave. Nk’uko mubibona, ndakunda moteri y’uguhindura Gecko kubera imvo nyinshi, naho ubu iri inyuma ya Blink mu bijanye n’ubushobozi.



Firefox nayo ni uburyo bwiza cane nk’umucukumbuzi w’intumbero rusangi, igihe cose atunganijwe neza kugira ngo yongere ubuzima bwite.



Ku rugero rwo hejuru rwo kutamenyekana, ku giciro co kugabanya ubushobozi, Tor Browser iguma ari umuti mwiza.



Chrome, naho izwi cane, ntishobora gushirwaho nk’igice c’uburyo bwo gusegaba kwa digitale, kuko Google ishira inyungu zayo z’ubudandaji hejuru y’ukurinda ubuzima bwite. Ni co gituma ntabagira inama yo kuyikoresha.



Muri iki gihe, uguhitamwo kwawe kw’umucukumbuzi kurafise uruhara runini mu mutekano wawe wo kuri Internet no mu buzima bwite bwawe. Rero fata umwanya wo kumenya iyo ihuye cane n’ingorane zawe be n’ivyo ushira imbere.



Ehe incamake yihuta kugira ngo igufashe guhitamwo (ariko rero, wibuke ko iyo ngereranyo ishobora kuba yarateye imbere uko igihe kigenda kirarenga kuva SCU202 yandikwa, kandi isuzuma rya Interface n’ibiyiranga ni ikibazo c’ugukenguruka kw’umuntu ku giti ciwe):



| Browser      | Privacy | Speed | Features | Interface | Open source | Resource consumption |
| --------------- | --------------- | ------- | --------------- | --------- | ----------- | ----------------------- |
| Google Chrome   | 🔴              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🔴          | 🔴                      |
| Brave           | 🟡              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🟢          | 🟡                      |
| Vivaldi         | 🟡              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🔴          | 🟡                      |
| Opera           | 🔴              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🔴          | 🔴                      |
| Arc             | 🔴              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🔴          | 🟡                      |
| Polypane        | 🟡              | 🟡      | 🟢              | 🟡        | 🔴          | 🔴                      |
| Mozilla Firefox | 🟡              | 🟡      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🟢          | 🟡                      |
| Tor Browser     | 🟢              | 🔴      | 🟢              | 🟡        | 🟢          | 🔴                      |
| Mullvad Browser | 🟢              | 🟡      | 🟢              | 🟡        | 🟢          | 🟡                      |
| Safari          | 🟡              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🔴          | 🟡                      |
| Lynx            | 🟢              | 🟢      | 🔴              | 🔴        | 🟢          | 🟢                      |
| LibreWolf       | 🟢              | 🟡      | 🟢              | 🟡        | 🟢          | 🟡                      |
| Orion           | 🟡              | 🟢      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🔴          | 🟢                      |
| Zen Browser     | 🟢              | 🟡      | 🟢              | 🟢        | 🟢          | 🟡                      |

Mu kigabane gikurikira, turaza kuraba uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha urubuga ata nkomanzi, mu gihe ugabanya ukuntu ubuzima bwite bwawe bugaragara.



## Ivyiza mu gukoresha urubuga


<chapterId>ded47ada-0569-4e63-b668-0da042e691d5</chapterId>



Mu gice ca mbere, twaciye mu ndondoro y’ama browser nyamukuru ariho ubu, hamwe n’ivyiza n’ibibi vyayo mu bijanye n’umutekano n’ubuzima bwite.



Ariko rero, mbere n’umucukumbuzi afise umutekano mwinshi cane ntihagije: ingene uwukoresha aguma ari ngirakamaro mu kurinda umutekano wawe wa digitale. Muri iki gice, turaraba mu buryo bwimbitse uburyo bwiza bwo kugabanya ingorane zijanye n’ugukoresha urubuga ku musi ku musi.



### Gukomeza guhindura umucukumbuzi wawe



Mucukumbuzi w’urubuga ni kimwe mu bihimba vya porogarama bigaragara cane muri sisitemu ya mudasobwa. Mu buryo butandukanye n’izindi porogarama nyinshi, ikora ibintu bihinduka biva kuri Internet mu gihe nyaco, ivyo bikaba ari ibintu bidashobora kwizigirwa. Iyo urubuga rwuzuye, umucukumbuzi arakora kode iri kure, iyo kode ikaba ikorana na sisitemu yawe biciye ku moteri y’uguhindura.



Ukwo gusobanuka kw’ubuhinga, hamwe n’aho umuntu ashobora gutera cane, bituma iyo browser iba ikintu gihambaye cane ku batera. Amakosa akomeye mu ma moteri yo guhindura (nka Blink canke Gecko), amasomero y'isesengura ry'amashusho canke abacungezi b'ubwenge bashobora gutuma haba ibitero vyitwa "zero-click" (gusa gusura urubuga rwa booby-trapped maze imashini yawe igahungabana), canke ibitero vya "zero-day" (ubugoyagoye butazwi na vendor).



Kugira ngo ivyo bibazo bigabanuke, abasohora amakuru y’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none barasohora kenshi cane, kenshi buri ndwi, ibintu bishasha bikosora ivyo bintu bishobora gutuma umuntu agira ingorane iyo bimaze kumenyekana. Ivyo bice ntibigarukira kuri Interface canke ku gutera imbere kw’ibikorwa: birazibira n’umwete ibitero vy’ukuri, vyanditswe.



![Image](assets/fr/129.webp)



Ni ngombwa rero:




- gushoboza ivyagezwe vyihuta ku mucukumbuzi wawe no gusuzuma n’amaboko ubudasiba ko ata bishasha biriho;
- canke, niba ukoresha verisiyo ikoreshwa n'amaboko (nk'akarorero biciye kuri `apt`, `flatpak` canke `snap` kuri Linux), ujye uhindura ubudasiba sisitemu yose biciye ku mucungerezi wawe w'amapaki.



Kugira ngo usuzume n'amaboko verisiyo maze ushireho ivugurura:




- muri Firefox: `Ibikubiyemo > Ivyagezwe > Ivyagezwe vya Firefox`;
- umurongo w'itegeko munsi ya Linux (`apt` amapaki):



```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade firefox
```



Guhindura umucukumbuzi wawe, porogarama yawe n’uburyo bwo gukoresha ni kimwe mu ntambwe za mbere nyazo ushobora gutera mu bijanye n’umutekano wo kuri internet.



### Koresha amajambobanga akomeye kandi yihariye



Ku bijanye n’umutekano w’urubuga, rimwe mu makosa asanzwe (kandi ateye akaga) ni ugusubira gukoresha amajambo y’ibanga ku mbuga nyinshi. Ivyo bitera ingaruka ziteye akaga: iyo serivisi imwe gusa ihungabanijwe (ugusohoka kw’amakuru, ubuhendanyi, igitero c’inguvu z’agahomerabunwa...), uwutera ashobora rero kugerageza iryo jambobanga nyene ku zindi nzira, akaronka uburenganzira bwo gushika ku makonti ahambaye nk’ivyo ukoresha kuri e-mail yawe, amakonti ya banki canke ahantu ukora.



Ingingo ya mbere ku bijanye n’amajambo y’ibanga ni ukudasubira kuyakoresha. Konti yose yo kuri Internet ikwiye kurindwa n’ijambobanga ry’umwihariko, ritandukanye rwose n’izindi. Kugira ijambobanga ry’umwihariko kuri konti imwe imwe biratandukanya ibitero bishobora gutera kandi bikagabanya ingaruka zavyo.



Nk'akarorero, niwakoresha ijambobanga rimwe ku rubuga rw'imikino ya videwo no kuri konti yawe ya imeyili, kandi iryo jambobanga rikagira ingorane biciye ku rubuga rw'ubuhendanyi ruhuye n'urubuga rw'urukino, uwo muterabwoba yoshobora rero kwinjira muri konti yawe ya imeyili bitamugoye maze akagenzura izindi konti zawe zose zo kuri interineti.



Ingingo ngenderwako ya kabiri y’ingenzi ni ukugira ijambobanga rikomeye. Ijambobanga rifatwa nk’irikomeye iyo rigoye gukoresha inguvu, ni ukuvuga kurironka mu kugerageza no gukosa. Ivyo bisigura ko amajambo y’ibanga yawe akwiye kuba ari ay’imburakimazi uko bishoboka kwose, maremare, kandi arimwo inyuguti zitandukanye (inyuguti nto, inyuguti nini, imibare n’ibimenyetso).



Gushira mu ngiro izo ngingo ngenderwako zibiri z’umutekano w’ijambobanga (ubudasa n’inkomezi) birashobora kugora ku musi ku musi, kuko bidashoboka gufata mu mutwe ijambobanga ry’umwihariko, ry’imburakimazi kandi rikomeye ry’amakonti yacu yose. Aho niho umucungerezi w'ijambobanga yinjira.



Igikoresho co gucungera amajambo y’ibanga kiratanga amajambo y’ibanga akomeye kandi akabika mu buryo butekanye, ivyo bikaba bigufasha gushika ku makonti yawe yose yo kuri Internet ataco ukeneye kuyafata mu mutwe umwe wese ku giti ciwe. Ukeneye kwibuka ijambobanga rimwe gusa, ijambobanga ry’umukuru, riguha uburenganzira bwo gukoresha amajambobanga yawe yose abitswe muri manager. Gukoresha umucungerezi w’amajambo y’ibanga birakomeza umutekano wawe wo kuri Internet, kuko bibuza gusubira gukoresha amajambo y’ibanga kandi bikazana amajambo y’ibanga ataco bimaze.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

Gukoresha umucungerezi w’ijambobanga birafise ivyiza vyinshi: birorosha ubuzima bwawe bwa misi yose mu gukuraho ivy’ugufata mu mutwe amajambobanga menshi, kandi bikagabanya intege nke nyamukuru yo kwemeza: abakoresha ubwiwe.



Ku bijanye no kwemeza, gukoresha umucungerezi w’ijambobanga bitegerezwa kwuzuzwa n’umuti wo kwemeza ibintu bibiri (2FA), kugira ngo ukoreshwe ku makonti yose ayishigikira. Ivyiza ni uko wokoresha ubuhinga budasanzwe, canke mbere n’ikiruta, igikoresho c’umubiri nka Yubikey.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/authy-a76ab26b-71b0-473c-aa7c-c49153705eb7

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/trezor-u2f-fido2-41d2939e-69b9-4c2e-b836-a2b09de58051

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/ledger-fido-u2f-59f8105b-a0cc-4aff-bc56-048a6a42d39f

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/security-key-61438267-74db-4f1a-87e4-97c8e673533e

### Gukoresha VPN



VPN (*Virtual Private Network*) ni igikoresho co gukora tunnel gipfuka uruja n’uruza rw’urubuga hagati y’igikoresho cawe na server y’umuhuza. Uwo murongo ukora nk’irembo, ugatuma amakuru yose ukoresha kuri Internet aja kuri Internet. Ivyo bituma ISP yawe ibona gusa amakuru apfutse aja kuri VPN, kandi imbuga usura zibona gusa IP Address ya server ya VPN, atari iyawe.



Hariho ivyiza vyinshi vyo gukoresha VPN. Irinda ukuntu ukoresha amakuru yawe ku mbuga zidatekanye (nk’akarorero, Wi-Fi ya bose ku bibuga vy’indege canke mu mahoteli), mu kubuza abandi bantu gufata amakuru yawe. Ihisha kandi IP yawe nyayo Address, ishobora kuba ngirakamaro mu kwirinda gukurikirana ivy’ishimikiro, canke kwigana uruja n’uruza ruva mu kindi gihugu. Ivya nyuma ariko bitari ivya nyuma, VPN ni igikoresho co gukingira ubugenzuzi. Mu bidukikije aho ukuronka ibintu bimwebimwe bibujijwe ku rugero rwa ISP, guhindura uruja n’uruza rwawe kuri server ya VPN iri mu gihugu kitayunguruwe bigufasha gusubira kuronka ku buntu.



![Image](assets/fr/128.webp)



Ku rundi ruhande, bitandukanye n’ivyo abantu benshi bemera, VPN ntitanga ubuzima bw’umuntu. Uwutanga VPN arazi IP yawe nyayo Address, arashobora kwandika amahuzu yawe, kandi akaba umuntu agira gatatu yizigirwa. Ubashinga igikorwa cawe cose co kuri Internet. Iyo uwutanga amakuru ari umunyaruyeri, afise inshingano zitegekanijwe n’amategeko canke afise ubujuju mu vy’ubuhinga, amakuru yawe arashobora gushirwa ahabona.



Ikindi, VPN nta n’uburinzi itanga kuri malware, gukurikirana JavaScript canke amakuru y’abandi. Iyo winjiye muri konti yawe ya Google canke Facebook, gukoresha VPN ntibizobuza izo nzira kukumenya neza. VPNs nazo nyene ntizicungera ibirimwo, kandi ntizizobuza urubuga rwa booby-trapped kugutera biciye ku nzira y’ubugoyagoye bw’umucukumbuzi.



Kandi, ibikoresho vya VPN ntibikwiye gutera urujijo n’urubuga rwa Tor, ari rwo rubuga rwigenga rw’amakuru y’ivyuma kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kumenya neza amazina yiwe. Tor iragenda buhoro, ariko irakomeye cane ku bijanye n’ugucungera kw’isi yose kuruta VPN.



VPN nziza ikwiye kugira politike itomoye yo kudakora amakuru, itanga ubuhinga bwa none (cane cane WireGuard), yemera gukoresha iyo serivisi ata mazina kandi itanga inkomoko yuguruye canke igenzurwa ry’ubuhinga ry’abantu bose. Ivyo mbifise mu muzirikanyi, ndabagira inama y’ibikoresho nka Mullvad canke IVPN.



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mozilla-vpn-f55903d4-aece-4d59-b193-2eb073e59b67
