VPN zihambaye cane zikwiye kwirindwa. Naho zitangaza cane, ziguma ari ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji bishingiye ahantu hamwe, akenshi zishingiye ku butegetsi butagira uburinzi bwinshi, kandi ntabwo zigaragaza neza ingene zikora.



### Gusukura amateka n'ibikuki



Urubuga rwose usura rurandika amakuru y’ibiganiro vyo mu karere kawe kuri mudasobwa yawe, ayo makuru akaba ari ubwoko bubiri nyamukuru: amateka y’ugusura n’amakuru y’ibanga.



Amateka ni urutonde rworoshe rw’ibiharuro vyo mu karere rutanga urutonde rw’imbuga zose zasuwe, n’itariki zazo, izina ryazo rimwe na rimwe n’igihe zasuweko. Bituma vyoroha kuronka urupapuro rwari rwafunguwe mbere. Ariko ku rundi ruhande, bigaragaza ivyo urondera vyose kuri Internet ku muntu wese afise uburenganzira bwo gushika ku kiganiro cawe (harimwo n’ivy’ubuhinga bubi, canke incuti yawe ishaka kumenya vyinshi).



Ku rundi ruhande, ama cookies ni ududosiye dutoduto tubikwa n’umucukumbuzi ku busabe bw’imbuga. Bikoreshwa mu kwibuka igihe cawe (nk’akarorero kuguma uhuye n’urubuga), kubika ivyo ukunda, canke gukurikirana inyifato yawe ku ntumbero z’imibare. Ama cookies amwe amwe arakora (ni ukuvuga ngo ni ngombwa kugira ngo urubuga rukore neza), mu gihe ayandi ari ay’abandi (ashirwaho n’amashirahamwe y’iyamamaza canke abakurikirana kuri paji zasuwe). Ivyo vya nyuma bishoboza gukurikirana urubuga rwose, rimwe na rimwe mu myaka, mu gukurikirana ingeso zawe zo gusura kugira ngo ushireho urutonde rw’ivyo kwamamaza.



Gusukura ubudasiba aya makuru yo mu karere ni uburyo bworoshe ariko bukora neza bwo kugabanya ugukurikirana no kuzigama ubuzima bwite bwawe. Benshi mu bacukumbuzi batanga amahitamwo ya:




- canke gukuraho aya makuru n'amaboko (mu mitunganyirize);
- canke gukuraho igihe cose ufunze umucukumbuzi, canke mu kiringo kinaka (ndagusaba ko ukora ivyo);
- canke gutanguza ibiganiro vy’igihe gito biciye ku buryo bwo gusura mu buryo bwihariye (ibindi kuri ivyo mu gice gikurikira).



Muri Firefox, nk’akarorero, urashobora gutunganya ugukuraho ubwavyo biciye ku Mitunganyirize > Ubuzima bwite n’Umutekano.



Ariko rero, uzirikane ko gukuraho amakuru yawe gusa bidahagije kugira ngo ubone ubuzima bwite bwawe: hariho ubundi buryo buteye imbere bwo gukurikirana, nk’ugufata urutoke (urutoke rwihariye rw’umucukumbuzi wawe, ibikoresho vyawe, IP yawe, uko ukoresha...), bisaba izindi ngingo zo gukingira:




- Koresha umucukumbuzi atanga ubushobozi bwo guhangana n’intoke: Tor Browser na Mullvad Browser ni vyo vyiza kuri ivyo, ahandi ho, ubundi buryo bwiza cane ni LibreWolf, Brave canke Firefox n’ugukomera kw’amaboko;
- Guhagarika canke guhagarika JavaScript igihe cose bishoboka;
- Irinde kwagura ibintu bitari ngombwa;
- Muri rusangi, nufate urutonde rusanzwe, rudahinduka, kugira ngo ushiremwo neza kandi ugabanye ubushobozi bwo kumenyana.



### Gutahura gushakisha mu buryo bwihariye



Uburyo bwo gusura mu buryo bwihariye, buboneka mu bikoresho vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa none (Firefox, Chrome, Brave, Safari...), akenshi ntibitahurwa neza. Si igikoresho co gutuma umuntu atamenyekana, canke ngo agire uburinzi bwo gukurikirana umuntu kuri Internet. Ubu buryo buragabanya gusa kwandika amakuru yo mu karere kuri mudasobwa yawe mu gihe c’ikiganiro gikora.



Mu majambo nyayo, iyo ufunze idirisha mu gushakisha mu bwiherero:




- amateka yo gusura ntazobikwa aho hantu ku gikoresho cawe;
- amakuru yashizweho mu gihe c’ikiganiro azoca asubirwamwo igihe idirisha rizoba ryugarijwe;
- amakuru y’ifomu (ibibanza vyuzuye, amajambobanga) ntazobikwa;
- dosiye z'igihe gito zihujwe na paji z'urubuga zizokurwaho inyuma yo gufunga.



Ariko rero, ubu buryo ntibunyegeza igikorwa cawe kuri Internet: imbuga usura ziracabona IP yawe ya bose Address, zirashobora gukoresha ubuhinga bwo gufata urutoke, kandi ISP yawe, canke umuntu wese ari ku rubuga rwawe rwo mu karere, arashobora kubona imbuga usura.



Ni ngombwa rero ko udashobora kwitiranya gusura urubuga rwiwe bwite n’ukutamenyekana. Kugira ngo ukingire neza ubuzima bwite bwawe bwo kuri Internet, ukeneye gukoresha ibikoresho vy’inyongera nka Tor canke VPN nziza, bivanye n’urugero rw’iterabwoba.



![Image](assets/fr/127.webp)



### Kumenya no kwirinda ubuhendanyi n'ubuhinga bwo gukorana n'abantu



Phishing ni uburyo bwo guhenda abakoresha kugira ngo bamenyeshe amakuru y’agaciro ataco bazi: amakuru yo kwinjira, inomero z’ikarita y’inguzanyo, amakode yo kwinjira, inyandiko z’ibanga. Uwo mubabaro ntushingiye ku nzira y’ubuhinga, ahubwo ushingiye ku gukoresha nabi mu mutwe, gukoresha nabi ukwizigira kw’uwuwukoresha, ukwihuta canke ukubura ubumenyi.



Akenshi, igitero gishingiye ku kwigana ukuntu urubuga rwemewe rusa (banki, ubutumwa, ubuyobozi, iduka ryo kuri Internet, n’ibindi) biciye ku rubuga rw’ikinyoma rufise URL yiyoberanije. Abakoresha bararonka uruja n’uruza rw’ubuhendanyi biciye kuri e-mail, SMS canke porogarama zo gutumako ubutumwa, maze, bizera ko bariko barakorana n’urubuga nyarwo, bakinjiza amakuru yabo yo kwinjira.



Kugira ngo wirinde ivyo bitero igihe uriko urarondera kuri Internet, birahambaye ko ukurikiza ibintu bimwebimwe vy’ishimikiro:





- Sesangura URL**: abatera kenshi bakoresha aderesi ziri hafi cane y’umwimerere (nk’akarorero `micr0soft-support.com`, `paypal-verif.net`, n’ibindi). Hari n’abasubirira inyuguti zisa n’izo mu buryo bw’amaso, bagakoresha inyuguti za Unicode. Suzuma ko Address ihuye neza na neza n’aho witeze, ata n’imwe mu ntango canke mu nyuma iteye amakenga.





- Irinde amahuzu magufi**: ibikorwa nka `bit.ly` canke `t.co` birashobora gupfuka Address ya nyuma. Niwaronka uruja n’uruza rugufi, ushire amakenga canke ukoreshe igikorwa co kwagura URL kugira ngo umenye aho ruja.





- Iyubare ubutumwa butera ubwoba**: ukugerageza guhenda abantu kenshi bikoresha inyiyumvo zikomeye (ukwihutira, ugutera ubwoba, impembo, ugushaka kumenya...). Ikete ryo kuri e-mail rivuga ko konti yawe igiye guhagarara canke ko umuzigo udashobora gushika, birasanzwe ko ari ikintu giteye amakenga.





- Ntukigere urungika amakuru y’agaciro biciye ku nzira yaronse**: Ikigo cemewe ntikizokwigera kigusaba ijambobanga, kode y’ukwemeza canke kopi y’indangamuntu yawe ya scanner biciye ku butumwa bwo kuri e-mail canke SMS yoroshe.



Kandi ng'izi ingingo nkeyi zo kwirinda ushobora gushiramwo mu mucukumbuzi wawe kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo guhenda abantu :





- Ushobora gushika ku mbuga zihambaye biciye ku bimenyetso vyawe**:



Ku bikorwa bihambaye (bijanye n’amabanki, ubuyobozi bw’imisoro, e-mail, n’ibindi), no muri rusangi ku mbuga zose ukoresha ubudasiba, zigama URL yemewe mu bimenyetso vyawe kandi ntukigere ukoresha moteri y’ugushaka canke uruja n’uruza rw’inyuma kugira ngo ushikireyo.



Woba wararonse ubutumwa kuri e-mail buvuye ku biro vy’imisoro burimwo link? Ntukifyondeko. Ahubwo, genda mu kibanza cawe bwite ukoresheje URL wabitse mu bimenyetso vyawe. Muri iki gihe, ama browser yose yo muri iki gihe aratanga umurongo w’ibimenyetso ufise uburenganzira bwo gutunganya amahuzu yawe mu madosiye. Fata umwanya wo kubikora rimwe, usuzume neza URL n’icete ca SSL/TLS, uzoshobora gusesangura ata nkomanzi.





- Wubahe ingendo nziza zo kwemeza ko umuntu ari uwuriho** :



Ni ngombwa kandi gukurikiza ingendo nziza zo kwemeza ko umuntu ari uwuriho kugira ngo ugabanye ingaruka zishobora guterwa n’igitero c’ubuhendanyi. Amategeko abiri ahambaye cane ni ugukoresha amajambo y’ibanga yihariye kuri buri serivisi no gukoresha 2FA.



Reka dufate akarorero: iyo uwugutera ashoboye kuronka ijambobanga rya konti yawe ya Steam, ariko ugakoresha ijambobanga ritandukanye kuri buri konti yawe, ntazoshobora gushika ku bikorwa vy’agaciro nk’ivyo kuri e-mail yawe canke banki. Kandi iyo warakoresheje ubuhinga bwo kwemeza ko umuntu ari we (2FA), rero n’aho woba ufise ijambobanga, uwugutera ntazoshobora kwinjira, kuko atazoshobora gukoresha porogarama yawe ya TOTP (nka Authy, Google Authenticator...).



Uretse izo ngingo, gukoresha umucungerezi mwiza w’ijambobanga nk’umurongo w’ibanga ry’umucukumbuzi na vyo nyene birashobora kugukingira imbuga z’ibinyoma. Nkako, nyinshi muri izo extensions zizobona URL iteye amakenga maze zikanke kwuzuza amakuru yawe, canke mbere zikumenyeshe, ivyo bizotuma udashobora gushikiriza amakuru yawe y’ukwinjira ataco wiyumviriye.





- Suzuma ivyemezo vya SSL/TLS**:



Igishushanyo c’urufunguzo kiri mu murongo wa Address kigaragaza ko hariho uguhuza gupfutse, ariko ntikivyemeza ko urubuga rwemewe. Fyondako kugira ngo usuzume icemeza (ishirahamwe, urwego, ubuyobozi bw’icemeza). ivyiwe birashobora kugufasha nimba ufise amakenga ku bijanye na URL y'urubuga.



Phishing ikora gusa iyo ukanda ningoga cane. Ku bijanye n’ihuriro ryose uronka, nugire akamenyero ko kugenzura mu buryo butunganye, mbere no ku rubuga uzi. Gufata umwanya wawe wo gusuzuma no kugenzura neza ama URL, mbere n’ayo umenyereye, ni kimwe mu bintu vyiza vyo kwikingira ubwo bwoko bw’igitero.



### Suzuma ivyungura vyashizweho



Ivyagutse vy’umucukumbuzi ni ibice vyongerako ibintu (guhagarika amatangazo, guhindura, gufata amajambo, gucunga ijambobanga, Bitcoin Wallets, n’ibindi). Bikora ataco bimaze mu bidukikije vy’umucukumbuzi kandi birashobora gushika ku mapaji yose canke igice cayo usura. Ivyo bituma zigira ububasha, ariko kandi zishobora gutera akaga.



Igikoresho gishobora gufata amakuru yawe bwite, gusoma ibirimwo, gushiramwo kode kuri paji z’urubuga canke mbere gukora JavaScript mu nyuma. Hariho ama extensions aguma afise uburenganzira bwo gufungura ama tabs canke amateka yo gusura, birenze kure ivyo bikenewe kugira ngo akore.



Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo bibazo, shiramwo gusa ivyungura biva ku masoko yemewe (Mozilla Add-ons), wama usuzuma uruhusha rwasabwa, kandi ugumize umubare wavyo ku rugero rutoyi cane. Sukura ama extensions utagikoresha, kandi wiyubare ama clones.



Gusuzuma ubudasiba ama extensions yawe ni ikintu gihambaye mu kubungabunga umucukumbuzi wawe.



### Gutandukanya urubuga rwawe



Gucapura ibikorwa ni umugenzo uhambaye wo kugabanya urugero rw’ugusenyera ku mugozi umwe ku rubuga. Bigizwe n’ugutandukanya mu buryo bw’ubuhinga imikoreshereze yawe itandukanye ya internet: gusura ku giti cawe, ku bijanye n’umwuga, ku giti cawe canke ku giti ciwe.



Intumbero ni yoroshe: gukingira ikintu gifitaniye isano n’igikorwa kinaka (nk’ugusohoka kw’ibifungurwa, igitero canke ubusuma bw’ibiganiro) ngo ntikihumanye ibidukikije vyawe vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Uburyo bwinshi burashobora gukoreshwa, bwonyene canke bufatanye:





- Koresha ama browser atandukanye**: nk’akarorero, Firefox ku bikorwa vy’umuntu ku giti ciwe, Tor canke Mullvad ku bikorwa bihambaye, na Chromium ku bikorwa vy’umwuga. Buri mucukumbuzi akoresha ububiko bwayo bwite, butandukanya rwose amakuru, ibihe n’ibindi. Ivyo kandi biragufasha guhindura amahinduka y’umucukumbuzi n’ivyo ukoresha.





- Rema imirongo myinshi mu mucukumbuzi umwe**: imirongo imwe imwe iraguha uburenganzira bwo kurema imirongo yigenga, imwe yose ifise amateka yayo, ibihe, ivyungura n’imiterere. Ivyo ni umuti udakomeye gatoyi kuruta gukoresha ama browser menshi atandukanye, ariko n’ubu nyene ntaco bimaze.





- Koresha ibikoresho vyubatswemwo**: Firefox itanga [Ibikoresho vy’amakonti menshi] (https://addons.mozilla.org/ru-US/firefox/addon/ibikoresho vy’amakonti menshi/), bigufasha gufungura amabara atandukanye, imwe yose ifise inzira yayo yo kwinjiramwo n’amakuru yayo. Ushobora kandi gushiramwo imbuga zimwe zimwe mu kintu kinaka, kugira ngo zigume zitandukanye igihe cose zifunguwe.



![Image](assets/fr/126.webp)





- Koresha ibidukikije vya sisitemu vyihariye**: Ku bikorwa vy'agaciro cane, ushobora kandi gukoresha umucukumbuzi wawe mu mashini y'ivy'impwemu canke mu gikoresho ca Docker, kugira ngo ugume utandukanye rwose n'ibidukikije vyawe nyamukuru.



### Guhagarika imbuga zahawe uruhusha



Ivyuma bikoreshwa muri iki gihe bituma imbuga zishobora gusaba gukoresha ibintu bihambaye biri ku gikoresho cawe, nk’ivyo gufata amasanamu, mikoro, aho umuntu ari canke amatangazo ya sisitemu. Ivyo bikoresho ni ngirakamaro ku bikorwa bimwebimwe (videoconference, amakarata akora...), ariko kandi birafungura urugi rwo gukoresha nabi iyo bigenzurwa nabi.



Iyo urubuga rugusavye gukoresha kimwe muri ivyo bintu, umucukumbuzi arakwereka ikintu kigusaba ko utegerezwa kwemera. Ariko rero, niwavyemera rimwe gusa utabizi, urwo ruhusha rushobora kuguma rukora ubudasiba mu gihe cose uzosura uru rubuga muri kazoza. Ivyo bisigura nk’akarorero ko urubuga rushobora kwongera gukoresha mikoro yawe canke kamera yawe ataco akubajije, nimba utakuyeho ubwo burenganzira n’amaboko.



Kugira ngo wongere umutekano:




- Gutanga uruhusha gusa iyo bikenewe cane kubera ikintu cemewe;
- Hitamwo uburyo bwo "kwemera rimwe" nimba buhari;
- Gukuraho n'amaboko uruhusha rwatanzwe biciye ku miterere y'umucukumbuzi ku buryo budasanzwe.



![Image](assets/fr/125.webp)



### Suzuma amahuza atekanye (HTTPS)



Igihe cose wohereje amakuru y’ibanga, ay’ibanga canke y’amahera ku rubuga, yaba ijambobanga, inomero y’ikarita y’inguzanyo canke urupapuro rworoshe rwo kwiyandikisha, birahambaye ko ubona neza ko uruja n’uruza hagati y’umucukumbuzi wawe n’urubuga rwawe ruri mu nzira y’ibanga.



Ivyo ni vyo vy’ukuri uruhara rwa HTTPS (*Itegeko ryo gutanga amajambo menshi ry’umutekano*). Iyi porotokole ishingiye ku nzira ya TLS (*Umutekano w'Ivy'Itwara Layer*), ishoboza :




- gupfuka amakuru yahinduwe (nta n’umwe ashobora kuyasoma canke kuyahindura mu gihe ariko aragenda);
- kugenzura ukuri kwa server ya kure biciye ku cete c'ubuhinga bwa none ;
- gukingira ibitero vy’umuntu ari hagati (MITM), bikunze kuboneka ku mbuga za bose canke zishobora guhungabanywa.



Mu majambo nyayo, urubuga rukoreshwa na HTTPS rwerekanwa n'urufunguzo rwugarijwe mu mucukumbuzi wawe Address, akenshi hejuru ibubamfu bwa Interface. Ufyondeye kuri iyi ngufuri yerekana amakuru yerekeye icemeza TLS c’urubuga (ububasha bwo kwemeza, itariki y’uburenganzira, n’ibindi). Urubuga Address na rwo nyene rutangura na `https://`.



![Image](assets/fr/124.webp)



Ku rundi ruhande, iyo urubuga rugikoresha HTTP (ata "S"), iyo nzira ntiba ipfutse. Amakuru yose yinjijwe arashobora rero gufatwa n’umukozi w’ikibi ari hagati yawe n’urubuga: umukoresha w’urubuga, uwutanga uburenganzira bwo gukoresha, ikibanza ca Wi-Fi gifise umutego wa booby, porogarama mbi yo mu karere, n’ibindi.



Mu vy’ukuri, ukwiye kwama usuzuma ayo makuru n’amaboko imbere y’uko winjiza amakuru ku rubuga. Mu bikorwa, ama browser menshi yo muri iki gihe aca atanga ibendera ry’imbuga za HTTP nk’izidatekanye. Ushobora kandi gukoresha uburyo bwo guhatira gukoresha porotokole ya HTTPS mu mategeko y’umutekano w’umucukumbuzi wawe, bikagufasha guhagarika imbuga zitayishigikiye.



Nkako, ni imbuga nke cane muri iki gihe zishobora gushikirwa biciye kuri HTTP gusa. Iryo tegeko ahanini ririko riheba kubera HTTPS, atari kubera imvo zigaragara z’umutekano gusa, ariko kandi kubera ko rihanwa n’abashakashatsi kandi rikamenyeshwa ko rishobora gutera akaga n’abashakashatsi bo muri iki gihe, ivyo bikaba bidatuma abashitsi bavyizigira.



### Guhitamwo moteri y'ubushakashatsi



Nk’uko twamaze kubibona, birahambaye gutandukanya Elements zibiri zikunda gutera urujijo: umucukumbuzi, ariyo porogarama ishizwe kuri mudasobwa yawe (nka Firefox canke Brave) kandi ikoreshwa mu kwerekana amapaji y’urubuga, n’umucukumbuzi, ariyo serivisi yo kuri interineti (nka Google queries) iyo utanga ibisubizo. Izo Elements zibiri zirigenga, naho nyene ama browser akenshi ashiramwo moteri imwe imwe ku buryo busanzwe.



![Image](assets/fr/122.webp)



Ivyo ukoresha mu gushakisha biragira ico bikoze ata guca ku ruhande ku buzima bwawe bw’ibanga. Nkako, ubushakashatsi bwose ukora bushobora kuba :




- ifatanye na IP yawe Address nimba udakoresha Tor canke VPN ;
- ihuye n'ijambobanga ryawe ry'injira n'ijambobanga ryawe nimba uhuye na konti ;
- ibitswe kandi bikasuzumwa kugira ngo haboneke urutonde rw’inyifato;
- ikoreshwa mu kwamamaza canke gusubira kugurisha ku bandi bantu.



Rero moteri nka Google itanga ibisubizo vyihuta kandi bibereye (naho [inyigisho zimwe zimwe zivuga] (https://consumerwatchdog.org/mu-makuru/Wallet-ibibazo-vy’uburyo-bw’ingamba-z’intumbero/) ko Google iriko iragabanya kandi igabanya ubushobozi bwo kugenzura ubuhinga bwawe), ariko. Bing (Microsoft) na Yahoo zikurikirana uburyo nk’ubwo bwo gukoranya ibikorwa vyawe vyo kuri internet kugira ngo zigaburire imihora yabo yo kwamamaza.



Kugira ngo ugabanye uku gukurikirana, turagusavye guhitamwo ubushakashatsi bubaha ubuzima bwite butabika ibimenyetso vy'umuntu ku giti ciwe canke amateka y'ubushakashatsi bwawe:




- [Urupapuro rw'intango](www.urupapuro rw'intango.com/);
- [Ishakisha rya Kagi](ku rubuga rwa Kagi/);
- [Ivyipfuzo](ku rubuga rwacu/);
- [Ikiganiro](ku rubuga rwa interineti);
- [SearXNG](https://docs.searxng.org/) (ishobora kwiyakira).



![Image](assets/fr/123.webp)



Mu ma browser menshi, urashobora guhindura n’amaboko moteri y’ubushakashatsi mu mitunganyirize. Ivyo bigufasha kwirinda Google utahinduye umucukumbuzi wawe.



Ivyiza vyiza vyerekanwa muri iki kigabane ni vyo bishingirako ugucapura mu buryo butekanye kandi bufise ubusegaba. Niwabifata ubudasiba, uzogabanya cane ukuntu ushobora gushikirwa n’ibintu bigutera ubwoba.



Ubu ko twabonye ingene ama browser n’ama orodinateri akoreshwa, mu gice gikurikira turaza kuraba ingene twosubira kugenzura telefone yacu.






# Gusubira kugenzura telefone yawe


<partId>5f0ef9ad-5701-4620-89bf-eb6937adccac</partId>


## Uburyo bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa: Gutahura ibibazo


<chapterId>020329e9-a2cb-464b-bb4c-ee4f0e5346c6</chapterId>


Kugeza ubu, twashize umutima canecane ku gucungera no gukoresha mudasobwa yawe. Ariko rero, ku bantu benshi, ubu telefone ngendanwa ni co gikoresho gikoreshwa cane mu buzima bwa misi yose.


Mu buryo butandukanye na orodinateri, amatelefone ngendanwa muri rusangi akoresha ubuhinga bufunze, bugenzurwa cane n’abayakora. Ni co gituma muri iki gice, ndasaba ko twosuzuma ingorane zidasanzwe zijanye n’ubuhinga bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa.


### Android: Kuva ku nkomoko yuguruye gushika ku bugenzuzi bwa Google


#### Amateka make ya Android


Android ubu ni yo itwara isoko ry’amatelefone ngendanwa kw’isi yose, ikaba ifise hafi 72% vy’ibikoresho bikoreshwa. Iterambere ryayo ryatanguye mu mwaka w’2003 aho Android Inc. Intumbero yabo ya mbere yari iyo guhingura uburyo bwo gukoresha amafoto y’ivyuma.


Inyuma y’aho abashoramari banse kenshi, Android Inc. yahisemwo guhindura umugambi wayo mu guhingura ubuhinga bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa. Kugira ngo tubone ivyo, mu myaka ya 2003-2004, isoko rya telefone ngendanwa ryari ririko riratera imbere cane, ahanini ryari riganzwa n’abahinguzi nka Nokia, Motorola, Sony Ericsson na Samsung. Ivyinshi mu bikoresho vyari "amatelefone y'ibidukikije", bifise ama keyboards y'umubiri, amabara mato mato, rimwe na rimwe na kamera y'ishimikiro. Telefone ngendanwa zari zisanzwe zihari, ariko ahanini zari zigenewe abahinga, kandi zitwarwa n’amashirahamwe nka BlackBerry.


Google yaguze Android Inc. mu mwaka w’2005 ku mahera ashika ku miriyoni 50 z’amadolari. Hagati y’umwaka wa 2005 n’uwa 2007, iyo sosiyete yarateguye ubuhinga bwayo bwo gukoresha imbere mu gihugu, ata n’umwe yakoze verisiyo ya bose. Muri ico kiringo, hariho ibihuha vy’uko Google yariko irategura igikoresho co gukoresha telefone ngendanwa, bishoboka ko yafashe ivyiyumviro kuri BlackBerry, ico gihe cariko kirakundwa cane.


Ariko muri Mukakaro 2007, hari ikintu cahinduye cane amateka ya telefone ngendanwa: Steve Jobs yashize ahabona iPhone y'uruvyaro rwa mbere. Iciyumviro rusangi c’uko klavye y’umubiri yari ngombwa cane caracitsemwo ibice. iPhone yashizeho igikoresho cagenewe gukoreshwa mu gukora ku mubiri, ico gikoresho kimwe gusa cahinduye ivyo isoko ryiteze.


Kubera iyo mpinduka, Google yaciye itegekwa gusubira kwiyumvira inzira y’umugambi wayo wa Android kugira ngo ushobore gukorana na Interface. Mu nyuma mu mwaka w’2007, Google yaratanguje ku mugaragaro Android nk’umugambi w’inkomoko yuguruye ushingiye ku nzira ya Linux yahinduwe, mw’izina *Umugambi w’inkomoko yuguruye ya Android (AOSP)*.


Igikoresho cambere gikoreshwa na Android cashitse kw'isoko, HTC Dream, casohotse muri 2008. Yatanga ibidukikije vyari bikiri mu ntango, ariko vyuguruye vyose: abahinguzi n'abakoresha bashobora guhindura sisitemu mu mwidegemvyo kuvyo bakeneye, mu gihe abahinguzi bashobora kurema no gukwiragiza porogaramu ata kwemeza mbere. Ubwo buryo bwaciye bwihuta gutsinda abantu benshi kandi bwatumye abahinguzi benshi bakoresha cane Android.


![Image](assets/fr/131.webp)


*Isoko : [Na Akela NDE - Ibikorwa vyiwe bwite](Ikinyamakuru c'Ivyabona vya Yehova 6680413), CC BY-SA 3.0*


Ariko rero, ukwo gufungura kwa mbere kuzogenda kugabanywa na Google. Inyuma y’itegeko ry’inkomoko yuguruye rya AOSP, iyo sosiyete iriko irategura urutonde rw’ibikoresho n’ama API, bihuriwe hamwe mw’izina *Google Mobile Services (GMS)*. Ivyo bizogenda birimwo Iduka ry’Imikino, Ikarata ya Google, YouTube, Ibikorwa vy’Imikino ya Google, Gmail, Chrome n’Umufasha w’Ijwi. Kugira ngo abahinguzi bashobore gushiramwo imbere y’igihe Play Store, ubu bategerezwa gusinyana amasezerano y’uruhusha na Google no kwemeza ko ibikoresho vyabo bihuye n’ingingo mfatirwako za GMS, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane ubushobozi bwabo bwo guhindura ibintu nk’uko bashaka.


Android yarateye imbere cane: yarengeye iOS mw'isoko kuva muri Nyakanga 2011, maze iba ubuhinga buhambaye bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa muri Ruheshi 2012, inyuma y'aho SymbianOS isenyukiye bukwi na bukwi inyuma y'aho Nokia ayihevye ikaja kuri Windows Phone. Android kuva ico gihe yagumye ari yo irongoye isoko ry’amatelefone ngendanwa ata n’umwe ahakana, kandi uno musi igira ubufatanye bubiri na iOS.


![Image](assets/fr/130.webp)


#### Inkomoko yuguruye na Google


Umugambi wa Android ushingiye ku bubiri bw’imiterere. Ku ruhande rumwe, AOSP (*Umugambi w’inkomoko yuguruye ya Android*) iserukira urufatiro rw’inkomoko yuguruye rwa sisitemu: rurimwo umurongo wa Linux, ikirundo ca porogarama ya sisitemu, ibishushanyo bikeyi vya Interface n’umugwi w’ama API. Iyi base isohorwa mu ruhusha rwa Apache 2.0, kandi iguma ishobora gushikirwa na bose. Ku rundi ruhande, ibidukikije mu vy’ukuri bikoreshwa n’abantu benshi bakoresha Android vyishimikije hafi vyose ku bihimba vy’ubuhinga vyakozwe na Google: *Google Mobile Services* (GMS).


Ivyo bice si ivy’ubuhinga bufunguye: ntibishobora gusuzumwa n’abanyagihugu mu mwidegemvyo, canke ngo bisubirizwe mu buryo bworoshe. Kugira ngo bashobore kubishira ku bikoresho vyabo mu buryo butegekanijwe n’amategeko, ababikora bategerezwa gusinya amasezerano y’uruhusha na Google kandi bagakurikiza ibisabwa bikomeye vy’ubuhinga n’ubudandaji. Ivyo bisabwa birimwo:



- Ubufatanye bw'ingorane bwa porogaramu nyinshi za Google nk'iporogaramu za sisitemu zidashobora gukurwaho
- gushira ahabona amashusho y'ibikorwa bimwebimwe (Ishakisha rya Google, Iduka rya Play, Gemini, n'ibindi) ku mugaragaro w'intango
- ikoreshwa ryihariye rya Google APIs ku bikorwa bihambaye nk'uguhuza, gusunika amatangazo n'aho umuntu ari


![Image](assets/fr/132.webp)


Ivyo biriko biratuma buhoro buhoro abahinguzi ba telefone ngendanwa bagira ivyo bakoresha, kandi bikaba bituma ugutanga amakuru y’abantu ku ma server ya Google biba hafi ataco bimaze ku muntu akoresha telefone ngendanwa. Izo serivisi zigamije gutuma umuntu akoresha neza, ariko kandi akagira ibikorwa bihambaye nk’ugucungera amakuru, gucungera aho umuntu ari, canke kwemeza umuntu ubudasiba biciye ku konti ya Google (kenshi bisabwa kugira ngo umuntu akoreshe neza igikoresho ciwe).


Naho Android iguma, mu vyiyumviro, ari ubuhinga bufunguye mu ntumbero yayo, amatelefone menshi ya Android agurishwa kw’isi yose akoresha verisiyo yahinduwe kandi ikomezwa na Google. Muri iyi verisiyo, Layer y’inkomoko yuguruye ahanini yihishije munsi y’igipfukisho c’umunyagihugu, gipfutse kandi gishobora kwinjira.


Kugira ngo vy’ukuri usubire kugenzura, ni ngombwa rero guhindukira ukaja ku yindi nzira nk’ama ROM y’ubuntu (GrapheneOS, CalyxOS, n’ibindi), ivyo tuzobiraba mu nyuma muri iki cigwa.


### iOS: umutekano mwinshi, ariko ni uburyo bufunze


#### Amateka make ya iOS


iOS ni uburyo bwo gukoresha bwakozwe na Apple ku matelefone yayo y'ubuhinga bwa none, bwashizweho na iPhone ya mbere mu 2007 (ico gihe yitwa "*iPhone OS*"). Kuva mu ntango, Apple yarafashe ubuhinga bwo gukorana n’ibindi vyose mu buryo buhagaze: ibikoresho, porogarama, uburyo bwo gukoresha, ibikorwa vyo kuri internet n’ububiko bw’ibikoresho vyose vyateguwe, bigenzurwa kandi bikabungabungwa na Apple. Mu ntango, porogarama z’ikirundi zitasohowe na Apple mbere ntizari zishigikiwe. Ubwo buryo buratandukanye cane n’ubwa Android, kuko ibidukikije vyayo vyari bifise ibice vyinshi kuva mu ntango, kandi n’ubu biracariho.


![Image](assets/fr/133.webp)


iOS mu ntango yari ishingiye ku buryo bwo gukoresha bukoreshwa na Mac: OS X. Ikoresha umurongo w’ivyuma biva kuri Darwin, ubwawo ukava kuri BSD Unix na Mach microkernel. Uyu mushinge w’ubuhinga ushoboza iOS kuragwa umubare w’ubukomezi n’ugushikama kw’imiterere yihariye kuri sisitemu za Unix. Ubuhinga rero bwateguwe bushingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako zikomeye z’umutekano, harimwo:



- guheza gukora sandboxing y'ibikorwa, kubuza iporogarama imwe kuronka amakuru canke imigenderanire y'iyindi
- umukono w'itegeko wa kode y'ikoreshwa, yemeza ubutungane bw'ibiharuro bibiri n'inkomoko yavyo (App Store gusa)
- gupfuka amakuru y'ibikoresho ku gicapo, biciye ku *Secure Enclave*, igikoresho co gupfuka amakuru gitandukanijwe n'ibindi bice vya sisitemu
- ivyagezwe vyihuta vy'umutekano, bishirwaho ataco bimaze na Apple ku bikoresho vyose, ata n'umwe abihuza


Ubu buhinga bufunze burashoboza Apple gutanga ubumenyi bw’abakoresha bugenda neza kandi butekanye. Iterambere ry’imbere mu gihugu na ryo nyene rituma habaho uguhindura neza ibikoresho n’amaporogarama, ata guhinduka guke hagati y’ibigereranyo, bitandukanye na Android. iOS rero ifatwa nk’imwe mu nzira zitekanye cane ku bitero vya orodinateri.


#### Inyungu zo gufunga iOS .


Ariko rero, uwo mutekano ushingiye ku gufunga cane uwukoresha igikoresho ciwe, kuko ata bubasha afise bwo kugenzura igikoresho ciwe. Ntibishoboka gushiramwo izindi porogarama atari biciye kuri App Store, kiretse biciye ku *jailbreak*, igikorwa gikomeye, gifise ingorane kandi kenshi kidashikamye gikuraho garanti kandi kigatuma umutekano wa sisitemu uhungabana. Iryo hame kandi rishigikira ubuhinga bwa Apple bwo gukora ubucuruzi, busaba komisiyo ku bikorwa bikoreshwa mu bikorwa vy’abandi.


Guhindura ibintu nk’uko umuntu abishaka na vyo nyene biragoye cane. Ntibishoboka guhindura cane inyifato ya sisitemu, guhindura mu mwidegemvyo ibidukikije vy'igihe co gukora, canke gushika ku madosiye ya sisitemu. Rero, mu bikorwa, iyo telefone y’ubuhinga bwa none iguma ari iya Apple, mbere n’inyuma yo kuyigura, kuko nta bubasha bwose uyigenzura.


![Image](assets/fr/134.webp)


Ikindi, ugushiramwo iCloud ku nguvu mu bikorwa vyinshi (gukora backups, ubutumwa, amafoto, ahantu, Siri...) bituma abakoresha bashobora gushiramwo amakuru yabo bwite. Naho Apple ivuga ko ifise uburyo bwibanda ku buzima bwite (kandi, bitandukanye na Google, uburyo bwayo bwo gukora ubucuruzi ntibushingiye ku gukoresha nabi amakuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe), hariho imipaka myinshi igumaho:



- bimwe bimwe Elements (nk’amakuru y’ihuriro, ibisabwa na Siri canke inyandiko z’amakosa) biracariko biraca ku maserukira ya Apple .
- uburyo bwo gusesangura inyifato ku vyiyumviro bishingiye ku vyo umuntu abona, gusubiramwo App Store canke gucungera ubutumwa gukoresha uburyo butagenzurwa
- gukoresha ibikorwa nka iCloud bisobanura kwizigira ibikorwa remezo vya Apple, ataco ugenzura aho canke igihe amakuru abikwa


Ubwa nyuma, ku bijanye n’ubusegaba bwa digitale, iOS igereranya ikibanza gipfutse: nta butegetsi bwo hanze (yaba uwukoresha canke ishirahamwe ryigenga) bushobora kugenzura canke guhindura uko ikora. Abakoresha rero baragoberwa no kwizigira Apple ku rwego rwose: ibikoresho, porogaramu, urubuga...


### Ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha inkomoko yuguruye na Android


Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​ubuhinga bwa Android busanzwe, bugenzurwa na Google, bushingiye ku buhinga bufunguye (AOSP) bufise ibice vy’ubuhinga (GMS). Imigambi myinshi y’inkomoko yuguruye iriko irakoresha neza AOSP kugira ngo itange ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha bubaha cane ubuzima bwite, ata n’ibintu bishobora kwinjiramwo, kandi bishobora kugenzura neza abakoresha. Ivyo bikoresho bitari vyo bishirwaho kugira ngo bisubirire uburyo bwa kera, mu buryo bw’ama ROM ahinduwe ku buryo bubereye. Bigufasha gusubira kugenzura porogarama, ariko kandi bisaba ko ukoresha ibikoresho bikeyi, kuko bihuye n’ibikoresho bikeyi gusa.


#### Ibisabwa ku bikoresho n'imburi


Imbere yo gushiramwo, birahambaye ko usuzuma ko telefone yawe y’ubuhinga bwa none ihuye na ROM wahisemwo. Vyinshi muri iyo migambi bishigikira urutonde rw’ibigereranyo bibujijwe. Akenshi, uzokenera gukoresha amatelefone ya Google Pixel, kubera ubufasha bwayo bwo gufungura bootloader n’abashoferi ba bose.


Gushiramwo bisaba gufungura bootloader, igikorwa gituma ishusho nshasha ya sisitemu yandikwa, ariko kigafuta burundu ibiri mu gikoresho c’intango. Ibindi bikoresho, nka F-Droid canke Aurora Store vy’amaporogarama, na vyo nyene bizobwirizwa gushirwamwo n’amaboko.


Hari abahinguzi babuza canke bagatera ingorane iyo nzira, canke mbere bagahagarika ibikorwa bimwebimwe (camera, sensors, n’ibindi) igihe bahindura ubuhinga. Ni vyiza rero guhitamwo telefone ihuye (kenshi ni Google Pixel).


![Image](assets/fr/135.webp)


#### GrafeneOS


[GrapheneOS](https://grapheneos.org/) ni ROM ya AOSP iteye imbere, yateguwe gutanga umutekano urugero rwo hejuru kuruta Android isanzwe. Itegurwa n’umugwi wigenga kandi igenzurwa n’abahinga. Graphene ishira mu ngiro uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano buteye imbere, harimwo:



- kugabanya cane igitero: guhagarika ibikorwa vyinshi (NFC, Bluetooth, n’ibindi), gufunga ivyuho vya USB iyo igikoresho kitakora, kugenzura neza amapin ya pogo, n’ibindi.
- isanduku y'umusenyi ya Android ikomeye
- uburinzi bw'ubwenge buteye imbere
- ubugenzuzi bw'uruhusha
- Ububiko bw'ibikoresho bwigenga kuri Google
- n'ibindi.


![Image](assets/fr/136.webp)


GrapheneOS nta bihimba vy’umunyagihugu ishiramwo. Ufise umwidegemvyo wo kwongerako ibikorwa vya Google canke utarivyo, ariko ivyo biri ukwavyo (bishizwe mu gasandugu k'umusenyi mu mirongo yihariye). Ivyo bituma iyo sisitemu ishobora cane guhangana n’ibitero vyo mu karere no gukoresha nabi ubugoyagoye bwa sisitemu.


Graphene ihuye gusa n’ibipimo vya Google biherutse gusohoka (ibipimo 6, 7, 8 na 9).


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/grapheneos-08d43d7a-0b22-4638-a151-578d48d32d88

#### CalyxOS


[CalyxOS](https://calyxos.org/) ni uburyo bwo hagati bugamije guhuza ubuzima bwite, umutekano n’uguhuza n’ikoreshwa rya misi yose. Ishingiye kandi kuri AOSP, ifise ivyiza vy’umutekano. Ikintu kidasanzwe ni ugushiramwo MicroG, ugusubira gukoresha ku buntu ibikorwa vya Google. Ivyo bituma bishoboka gukoresha porogarama nyinshi za Android zishingiye ku bikorwa vya Google, ataco bimaze guca mu bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none.


CalyxOS kandi itanga porogaramu zashizweho mbere (Ikimenyetso, F-Droid, Iduka rya Aurora, VPN yunze ubumwe...), na Interface nziza. Biroroshe gushiramwo biciye ku gikoresho c'ibishushanyo ku bakoresha Pixel. Calyx ahanini ikorana na Google Pixels, ariko kandi n’ibikoresho bimwe bimwe vya Fairphone na Motorola.


![Image](assets/fr/137.webp)


#### UruvyaroOS


[UmurongoOS] (https://umurongo w’uruzitiro.org/), uwukurikira CyanogenMod, ni ROM y’ubundi buryo ihuye cane. Ishigikira amajana menshi y’ibigereranyo, bishimira umuryango munini w’abatanga. Ishingiye kuri AOSP, ishimika ku guhindura ibintu nk’uko umuntu abishaka, ku kworosha no ku kwidegemvya mu gukoresha.


LineageOS iguha ubuhinga bwa Android ataco bushizeko, ata bloatware, uburongozi bw’uburenganzira bwose, guhindura vyoroshe na Interface itunganye. Ushobora kwongerako serivisi za Google canke ugahitamwo gukoresha 100% ku buntu.


Ariko ku bijanye n’umutekano, LineageOS ntishiramwo uburinzi bumwe bumwe bw’ibikoresho canke ubukomezi bw’ukwibuka buboneka muri GrapheneOS na CalyxOS. Uburyo bwayo bwo guhindura bushasha na bwo buvana n’abanyagihugu, bishobora gutuma habaho ugucerezwa mu bice vy’umutekano.


![Image](assets/fr/138.webp)


### Ni OS iyihe ya smartphone yo gukoresha iki?


Igihe uhitamwo uburyo bwo gukoresha telefone yawe, urakeneye kumenya ivyerekeye umutekano, ubuzima bwite, ukworoha gukoresha n’uguhuza n’ibikorwa. Umuti wose ufise ibintu vy’ubuhinga vyihariye bizogira ico bikoze ata guca ku ruhande ku bumenyi ufise ku musi ku musi, ubushobozi bwawe bwo kugenzura, n’ukuntu ushobora gushikirwa n’ugucungera canke gushikirwa n’ingorane z’ubudandaji.


Android isanzwe (ifise GMS) iguma ari umuti ukwiragiye cane muri iki gihe. Itanga ubushobozi bwo gukorana n’ibikoresho vyose vya Android, ukworohereza gukoresha no guca ubona ibikorwa vy’abantu benshi (Play Store, Maps, Gmail...). Ariko rero, ukwo kworoha gukoresha bishingiye ku gufatanya gukomeye kw'ibikorwa vya Google, n'ugukusanya amakuru mu buryo butunganye: ikibanza ca GPS, amateka yo gusura, amakuru y'amatelefone, ivyo ukunda mu kwamamaza... Rero ni amahitamwo mabi nimba uhangayikishijwe n'ubusegaba bwawe bwa digitale canke ubuzima bwite bwawe.


IOS ya Apple irafise umutekano mwinshi cane. Ariko rero, uwo mutekano ujana n’ugufunga cane ibidukikije: Uwukoresha ntashobora gushiramwo porogarama hanze ya App Store (kiretse mu bihe vy’inyuma), ntashobora guhindura inyifato za sisitemu, kandi yizigira Apple yose ku bijanye n’ugucungera ibikoresho, ububiko bwo mu gicu n’uguhuza. Ni ikibanza ciza kandi gikomeye, ariko gitanga uburyo bwose bwo kwihindura canke kwigenga.


GrapheneOS igenewe imirongo isaba cane mu bijanye n’umutekano n’ibanga. Urugero rw’umutekano wayo, ariko, rurashiraho inzitizi zimwe zimwe: ibikoresho bikeyi bihuye (ibigereranyo vya Google Pixel biherutse gusa), nta kwinjira kwihuta kw’ibikorwa vy’ibikorwa vy’uwundi muntu, n’ugukenera gutunganya n’amaboko ibindi bikoresho vyo guhindura, ububiko canke amatangazo. Nimba ubuzima bwite n’umutekano ari vyo ushira imbere, biragaragara ko ari ryo hitamwo ryiza kuruta ayandi yose.


CalyxOS itanga uburinganire bushimishije. Ubumenyi bw’abakoresha buguma hafi y’ivyo Android isanzwe, ariko ata kugenzura kwa Google. Ishigikira umubare ubereye w’ibigereranyo (cane cane Google Pixel), kandi ishobora gushirwako ata bumenyi buhanitse bw’ubuhinga. Ku bakoresha bashaka umutekano wo hejuru ataco batakaje ku bijanye n’uguhuza porogarama, CalyxOS ni umuti ukora, uringaniye.


Ubwa nyuma, LineageOS ni ugukwirakwiza AOSP ku bakoresha bashaka guhinduranya no kugenzura. Ihuye n’ibikoresho vyinshi, mbere n’ivya kera, iremesha guhindura uko umuntu ashaka, kandi itanga uburyo busanzwe bwo guhindura ibikoresho vy’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Ariko rero, ntiyinjira mu buryo bw’akavukire ivyiza vy’umutekano biteye imbere biboneka muri GrapheneOS canke CalyxOS, kandi ntiyama ivyungukira ku guhindura ubudasiba ku bikoresho vyose. LineageOS rero isaba indero kanaka y’abakoresha kugira ngo igumye itekanye mu gihe kirekire.


| System | Security | Privacy | Compatibility | Customization |
| ------ | -------- | ------- | ------------- | ------------- |
| Android | 🟡       | 🔴      | 🟢            | 🟢            |
| iOS     | 🟢       | 🟡      | 🟡            | 🔴            |
| GrapheneOS | 🟢       | 🟢              | 🟡            | 🟡               |
| CalyxOS    | 🟡       | 🟢              | 🟡            | 🟡               |
| LineageOS  | 🟡       | 🟡              | 🟢            | 🟢               |

Utitaye ku mahitamwo yawe y’uburyo bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa, mu kigabane gikurikira turaza kuraba uburyo bwiza ushobora gukurikiza kugira ngo ukingire neza telefone yawe no kubungabunga ibidukikije vyiza vy’ubuhinga bwa none.


## Gukingira telefone yawe kugira ngo uyikoreshe buri musi


<chapterId>37b9499e-32cf-42c3-8715-15c6884d2ec7</chapterId>


Mu kigabane ca mbere, twasuzumye ibibazo bijanye n’uburyo bwo gukoresha telefone ngendanwa, maze turarondera uburyo butandukanye bwo kuronka ububasha bwinshi kuri telefone yawe. Ariko guhitamwo uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha ntibihagije: kugira ngo ubone umutekano nyawo n’ibanga, birahambaye ko wemera ingendo nziza nkeyi mu gukoresha kwawe kwa misi yose.


Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba intambwe ku yindi impanuro zimwe zimwe z’ishimikiro zikora ataco zitwaye kuri Operating System yawe ya telefone ngendanwa.


### Ivyavuguruwe


Nzosubiramwo hano, ariko buri nkuru nshasha isohorwa n’abahinguzi ishobora kuba irimwo ibintu bihambaye vy’umutekano. Ikindi, amatelefone ngendanwa ashobora gushikirwa n’ingorane nyinshi kubera uburebure bunini bwo gutera: Biciye ku nzira z’amatelefone ngendanwa, ku bikoresho vy’abandi, ku guhanahana amakuru ata nsinga (Wi-Fi, Bluetooth, NFC, n’ibindi).


Kudashira mu ngiro ivyo bishasha bisigura gusiga n’ibigirankana ubugoyagoye buzwi, bwanditswe ku mugaragaro mu bitabo vy’amakuru nka CVE (*Ubugoyagoye n’Ibimenyetso Bisanzwe*). Izo nzira mbi rimwe na rimwe zica zikoreshwa n’ibikoresho biri kuri Internet, mbere ata n’ubuhinga buhanitse bisaba. Ivyo bituma telefone ya kera iba ikintu ciza cane co gutera, mbere no ku bitero vyinshi vy’ubuhinga bwa none.


![Image](assets/fr/139.webp)


Ni ngombwa rero ko ushobora gukoresha ibintu bishasha vyihuta mu mitunganyirize ya sisitemu yawe, kandi ugasuzuma n’amaboko buri ndwi ko igikoresho cawe gifise ibintu bishasha vyo gucungera umutekano. Kuri Android, ivyo bikorwa kenshi mu `Imiterere > Umutekano > Ivugurura rya Sisitemu`, no kuri iOS mu `Imiterere > Rusangi > Ivugurura rya Porogarama`.


#### Kuvugurura infashanyo


Si amatelefone yose y’ubuhinga bwa none yaremwe kimwe iyo bije ku bijanye n’ugufasha porogarama. Ivyuma vyinshi vyo mu rwego rwo kwinjira n’ivyo hagati birahagarika kwakira ibintu bishasha bihambaye inyuma y’imyaka ibiri canke itatu gusa, ivyo bikaba bigutera ingorane zikomeye cane.


Ariko rero, hariho amashirahamwe afise ubuhinga bwiza cane bwo gufasha, cane cane Google (imyaka 7), Fairphone (imyaka 5 gushika kuri 7), Samsung (imyaka 5 gushika kuri 7) na Apple (imyaka 5 gushika kuri 7). Ico kigereranyo ni ikintu gihambaye cane igihe ugura telefone nshasha: Igikoresho kiramvye ni co mbere na mbere igikoresho kibungabungwa.


#### Koresha amaduka yizewe


Porogaramu zo kuri telefone ngendanwa ni zo zitera ingorane nyinshi: Ni zo zicamwo amaporogarama menshi y’ubuhinga bwa Android yo muri iki gihe. Gushiramwo porogarama biciye ku dosiye `.apk` yaronse ku rubuga rutazwi, canke ku iduka ritaremejwe, bisigura gufata ingorane yo gushiramwo porogarama igira ububi n’ibigirankana, canke ihinduwe kugira ngo ishiremwo ibikorwa vy’ubutasi canke vy’ukwiba amakuru.


No ku maduka yemewe nka Google Play canke Apple App Store, urakeneye kuguma uri maso. Naho hari uburyo bwo kuyungurura, porogarama mbi zirashobora kwinjira mu buryo budasanzwe.Nk'akarorero, porogarama za "Sparrow wallet" zirashobora rimwe na rimwe kubonwa kuri Play Store, naho iyo porogarama iriho gusa kuri PC: Nta gukeka ko ari porogarama y'ubuhendanyi.


Imbere yo gushiramwo, fata umwanya wo gusuzuma ibintu bikeyi: uruhusha rusabwa, igitigiri c’ivyo mwaronse, igiharuro muri rusangi, itariki ya nyuma yahinduweko n’ivyo abakoresha basubiyemwo.


Kuri Android, amaduka y’ubundi buryo yuguruye nka [F-Droid](https://f-droid.org/) atanga umuti w’inyifato runtu kandi kenshi utekanye: porogarama yose ikoranirizwa hamwe ivuye mu masoko y’ubuntu, kandi igasuzumwa n’amaboko. Ku bikoresho bikenewe, ibikoresho nka [Iduka rya Aurora](https://auroraoss.com/) bituma umuntu ashobora kwinjira muri Play Store ata konti ya Google, ivyo bikaba bigabanya amakuru.


![Image](assets/fr/140.webp)


Uretse Operating System, porogarama zishizwe kuri telefone yawe y’amaboko na zo nyene zirakeneye kuguma zijanye n’igihe. Ushobora gukoresha ivyagezwe vyihuta biciye ku mitunganyirize y’ububiko bwawe bwa porogarama, maze ukagira akamenyero ko gukoresha isuzuma ry’amaboko n’imiburiburi rimwe mu ndwi.


Kuri Android, iyo ushizeho porogaramu biciye ku madosiye `.apk`, uzokenera gucunga ivyahinduwe n'amaboko. Nkako, izo porogarama zishizwe hanze y’imihora yemewe nta buryo bwo kwihindura zigira. Rero uzokenera gusuzuma ubudasiba verisiyo zasohowe n’abahinguzi kuri GitHub canke ku rubuga rwabo rwemewe.


### Gucungera uruhusha rw'ikoreshwa


Ku telefone ngendanwa, porogarama iyo ari yo yose irashobora gusaba gushika ku bintu bihambaye: Mikoro, kamera, ikibanza nyaco, igitabu ca Address, amadosiye, ubutumwa bwo kuri telefone, ibimenyetso vy’inyigisho, n’ibindi. Ni co gituma bihambaye gukurikiza ingingo ngenderwako y’uburenganzira bukeyi: guha ubusabe bwose ubwo burenganzira gusa buhambaye cane kugira ngo bukore neza cane.


![Image](assets/fr/141.webp)


Nk’akarorero, porogarama y’itara ntikeneye gushika ku bantu uvugana canke aho uri. Igikoresho c’ikirere gishobora gukorana n’uguhindura aho umuntu ari, ata GPS ishobora gukoresha. Igikoresho co gusoma PDF ntigikeneye gukoresha mikoro canke SMS. Niba ufise amakenga, wama wanka ku buryo busanzwe, hanyuma wongere usuzume nimba iyo porogarama idakora neza. Ku mirongo imwimwe, birashoboka kandi gutanga uruhusha mu gihe gito gusa: haba ku gukoresha rimwe, canke igihe gusa porogarama iriko irakora. Ivyo bibuza porogarama gukoresha uburenganzira bumwebumwe buri inyuma ataco uzi.


Android na iOS ubu zitanga uburenganzira bwo kugenzura. Ushobora kubicungera ukoresheje ubusabe canke ukoresheje ubwoko bw'uruhusha. Fata umwanya, rimwe mu kwezi nk’akarorero, kugira ngo usuzume uruhusha rukora biciye ku mirongo ya telefone yawe.


Hariho kandi ubuhinga bumwebumwe bushobora kuguha uburenganzira bwo gukuraho uburenganzira bwatanzwe ku gikorwa inyuma y’igihe kinaka kitagikoresheje. Ivyo bigabanya ingorane iyo wibagiwe gukuraho porogarama.


### Gufunga igicapo


Umutekano wo ku mubiri wa telefone ngendanwa utangura n’igicapo cayo co gufunga. Iyi ni yo nzitizi ya mbere iri hagati y’umuntu ashobora kukutera n’ukuronka amakuru yawe bwite. Uburyo bwo kwizigirwa cane buracari kode ya PIN canke ijambobanga rigoye.


Ku rundi ruhande, uburyo bwo gufungura nk’imigero y’ibishushanyo buraremeshwa cane. Mwene iyo migambi isiga ibimenyetso biboneka ku rubuga, biroroshe gufata mu mutwe umuntu agira gatatu ariko arihweza ikimenyetso cawe, kandi ntabwo ari kenshi iba igoye bihagije.


Uburyo bwo gupima ubuzima (kumenya mu maso canke gufata urutoke) buratanga uburyo bugaragara, ariko bukwiye gukoreshwa n’ubwenge. Iyo umuntu afise ingorane zo ku mubiri (ubusuma, igitutu c’abapolisi, n’ibindi), urutoke canke mu maso birashobora gukoreshwa ata kwemera kwawe. Mu bihugu bimwebimwe, gukoresha ubuhinga bwa biometric ntibirindwa n’amategeko nk’uko ibanga ry’ijambobanga rikingirwa.


Ku rundi ruhande, ubuhinga bwo gupima ubuzima burashobora gukingira (canke bushobora kuba muri kazoza) hakoreshejwe ubuhinga nk’ugusubiramwo mu maso canke gusubirana ibimenyetso vy’intoke vyihishije ku kintu. Ukwizigirwa kwavyo na kwo nyene kuva cane ku rugero rw’umutekano w’igikoresho cawe: Nk’akarorero, ubuhinga bwa Apple bwo kumenya mu maso umuntu bukoresheje Face ID burakomeye cane kuruta ubw’amatelefone amwamwe yo mu rwego rwo kwinjira.


Mu guca irya n’ino, ng’uru urutonde kuva ku buryo bwiza bwo gufunga telefone ngendanwa gushika ku bubi kuruta ubundi:



- Ijambobanga ry'inyuguti n'imibare
- Kode ya PIN
- Ivy'ubuzima
- Ibishushanyo
- Nta gufunga


![Image](assets/fr/142.webp)


Ku bikoresho bikomeye, umuti mwiza ni ijambobanga rifatanijwe n’uguhagarika biometric, n’ugufungura n’amaboko gusa. Ivyo vyoshobora gusa n’ibibuza, ariko ni uburyo bwiza bwo kwirinda. Biragaragara ko ku bijanye n’ijambobanga rya PIN canke ijambobanga ry’inyuguti n’imibare, uko rigenda rireha kandi rikagenda rihinduka ni ko bigenda neza. Itegerezwa kandi guhangana n’ibitero vy’inkomezi z’ubukazi.


### Gukoresha no gucapura amakuru


Nk’uko twabibonye mu bice vyabanje, gucapura ni umugenzo uhambaye wo kugabanya ingorane iyo habaye ugusenyuka kw’igice kimwe c’urutonde. Mu kurema ibidukikije bitandukanye vy’ibikorwa vyawe bitandukanye, urabuza igitero canke amakuru asohoka mu karere kamwe ngo ntahumanye igikoresho cawe cose. Kuri Android, iyo nzira ishobora gushirwa mu ngiro biciye ku buryo butari buke bushizwemwo.


#### Koresha umwirondoro w'umwuga utandukanye


*Work Profile* ni ikintu kivukiye kuri Android (kuva kuri Android 5.0), kigufasha gukora igice ca porogarama gitandukanye muri telefone imwe. Mu buryo bukora, iyo nkuru ikora nk’ikintu kiri ukwaco: Amaporogarama, amakonti n’amakuru abitswe muri iki kibanza ntibishobora gukorana n’ivyo mu nkuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ukwo gutandukanya bibuza amakuru gusohoka hagati y’ibibanza bibiri, kandi bikagabanya uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ibikorwa. Ico gikoresho akenshi gicungirwa imbere mu masosiyete, ariko kandi hari uburyo bwo kugikoresha ku giti cawe kugira ngo ushiremwo ibikorwa.


![Image](assets/fr/143.webp)


Igikoresho ca Shelter ni porogaramu yuguruye ikoresha iki kintu *Work Profile* ca sisitemu ya Android kugira ngo ihe abakoresha batari abahinga uburyo bworoshe bwo guhingura ikibanza kiri ukwaco. Shelter ishobora gukoreshwa mu gushiramwo no gukoresha porogarama zihambaye mu kibanza kirinzwe, bikagabanya cane ukuntu zishobora gushikirwa n’izindi porogarama zishizwe kuri telefone.


![Image](assets/fr/144.webp)


#### Koresha amatelefone menshi atandukanye


Kugira ngo ugutandukanya imikoreshereze bigende mbere kure, birashoboka guhitamwo gukoresha ibikoresho vyinshi vy’umubiri, kimwe cose kikaba kigenewe ubwoko butandukanye bw’igikorwa (c’umuntu ku giti ciwe, c’umwuga canke c’ubuhinga). Ukwo gutandukanya kw’umubiri gutuma umuntu yitandukanya n’abandi, bikaba bikomeye cane kuruta ugutandukanya porogarama, kubera ko telefone imwe imwe ikora yigenga.


Iyo telefone imwe y’ubuhinga bwa none iteye akaga, izindi ziguma zitagira ico zihinduye. Ukwo gucapura kw’umubiri na kwo nyene kurafise akamaro ko kworohereza uburongozi bw’ugushikira n’uburenganzira ku gikoresho cose, kandi bikagabanya ukuntu muri rusangi umuntu ashobora gushikirwa n’ibintu bishobora gutera ubwoba.


### Kugenzura uruja n'uruza rw'amakuru yawe


Telefone yawe y’ubuhinga bwa none iguma ivugana n’isi yo hanze, haba biciye kuri Wi-Fi, Bluetooth, NFC, GPS canke ku nzira z’amatelefone ngendanwa. Imwe muri izo nzira igereranya ahantu hoshobora gutera. Gutahura ingene zikora no kuzikingira rero ni ngirakamaro kugira ngo umuntu agabanye ingorane.


#### Wi-Fi ya bose


Ivyuma vya Wi-Fi vya bose, nk’ivyo mu bibanza vy’ibinyobwa, mu mahoteli canke mu binyabiziga vya bose, ntabwo bikunda gutekana. Naho basaba ijambobanga, akenshi risangizwa n’abakoresha benshi, kandi rimwe na rimwe ijambobanga ry’ibanga rikoreshwa rirarenganywa bitagoranye. Umuterabwoba ahuye n’urubuga rumwe arashobora gufata amapakete yawe, gufata amakuru y’ibanga canke akagutera ibintu bibi biciye ku bitero vya Man-in-the-Middle.


Kugira ngo wikingire, gusa wirinde gukoresha izo nzira za bose, canke ukoreshe VPN, izotuma haba umugende w’amazi hagati y’igikoresho cawe na server iri kure. Uwo mugende ushiramwo amakuru yawe, bikaba bigoye cane kuyafata canke kuyahindura.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mozilla-vpn-f55903d4-aece-4d59-b193-2eb073e59b67

Naho ku bijanye n’urubuga rwa Wi-Fi rwo muhira, ivyo tuzobivuga mu gice ca nyuma c’amashure ya SCU 202.



#### Uburuzu, NFC na GPS


Bluetooth (umurongo w’ivy’itumanaho udakoreshwa n’amashanyarazi), NFC (Ivy’uguhanahana amakuru hafi) na GPS (ugushinga ahantu h’inyenyeri) birakoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe ku matelefone menshi y’ubuhinga bwa none. Izo tekinoloji zishobora gukoreshwa nk’irembo ry’ibitero vyo mu karere: Gukora kode kure, gushika ku muntu ata wemerewe, gukurikirana aho umuntu ari, mbere no gufata amakuru y’itumanaho iyo ari Bluetooth (nk’akarorero, ubugoyagoye bwa BlueBorne).


Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo bibazo, wama uzimya ivyo bikoresho igihe utariko urabikoresha. Ivyo bigabanya cane ahantu umuntu ashobora gutera kandi bikabuza ko umuntu agerageza gukoresha nabi.


#### Imihora y'amatelefone ngendanwa


Amatelefone ngendanwa aguma avugana n’ibibanza vy’abakoresha amatelefone. Iryo tangazo rishobora gufatwa n’aba *IMSI Catchers* bamwebamwe, bigana ama base station kugira ngo bafate amakuru yawe yo kuri telefone ngendanwa. Ivyo bitero bituma uwundi muntu ashobora kumenya igikoresho cawe, gukurikirana aho ugenda, rimwe na rimwe no gufata amatelefone n’ubutumwa.


![Image](assets/fr/145.webp)


Hariho porogarama zimwe zimwe, nka SnoopSnitch kuri Android, zishobora kumenya inyifato iteye amakenga mu vyo uhanahana n’urubuga. Ivyo bikoresho birasuzuma amakuru y’ivy’itumanaho ry’amatelefone ngendanwa kandi birashobora kukumenyesha iyo habaye amahinduka mu bijanye n’imiterere y’iradiyo canke inyifato idasanzwe, ivyo bikaba bituma urushiriza kuba maso ku bijanye n’ukugerageza gufata amakuru.


Uburyo bwiza bwo gukingira ubutumwa bwawe ni ugukoresha ubutumwa butekanye, haba ubwo guhamagara canke ubutumwa. Izo porogaramu ntizikoresha urubuga rwa telefone ngendanwa, kandi zikora vyose kugira ngo amakuru ahindurwa ashizwe mu buryo bubereye. Ivyo tuzobiraba mu buryo burambuye mu kigabane gikurikira.


### Gukingira igikoresho cawe ngendanwa


#### Umugera wo kuri telefone ngendanwa


Akamaro k’amaporogarama yo gukingira virusi kuri telefone ngendanwa akenshi kararengerwa, ahanini bivuye ku masekeza y’ubudandaji akomeye. Ivy’ukuri bitera ubwoba kuri telefone ngendanwa, cane cane kuri Android, muri rusangi bifitaniye isano n’ugushiramwo porogarama mbi zivuye mu bibanza bitazwi. Ku gikoresho gihora gihindurwa, gitunganijwe neza (cane cane mu bijanye n’uburenganzira), kandi gikoresha gusa amakuru yemewe canke yagenzuwe, ingorane zo kwandura ni nto cane.


Kandi, ibikoresho vya Android birasanzwe bifise Google Play Protect, ikora nk’ikintu co gukingira umugera. Ivyo bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none bikoresha iyo scanner nyene yitwa Interface, iyo na yo ikaba yongerako gusa ibindi. Mu vy’ukuri rero, antivirus yo kuri telefone ngendanwa nta co itanga, yaba kuri Android canke kuri iOS.


Ikindi kandi, izo porogarama zirashobora gutuma abazikoresha bumva ko bafise umutekano w’ikinyoma, bikabatuma bemera ko zikingiwe rwose ku bitero, mu gihe mu vy’ukuri zitanga uburinzi bwo gusubiza gusa. Nta n’imwe itanga uburinzi ku bijanye n’ubuhendanyi, canke uruhusha rwinshi ruhabwa porogarama, naho nyene ingeramizi nyinshi zitera telefone ngendanwa ziva kuri izo nzira nyene.


Akamaro kavyo nyakuri rero ni gato cane, kandi ivyo bikoresho rimwe na rimwe biratwara amahera menshi, bikaba bitwara inguvu n’ubutunzi vy’amabateri ata co bimaze. Ni vyiza ko tutabikoresha, kandi gusa ugafata ingendo nziza zishikirijwe muri iki kigabane.


### Suzuma amahuza asohoka


Hariho kandi porogarama zikingira umuriro kuri telefone ngendanwa, nka NetGuard canke RethinkDNS, zikora nk’uruhome rw’umuriro rwo mu karere ku gikoresho cawe. Bakoresha VPN API ya Android kugira ngo bafate amakuru yose asohoka, ataco basaba ko umuntu akoresha root.


Mu majambo ngirakamaro, ivyo bisigura ko umuntu ku giti ciwe ashobora guhagarika Internet ku bikoresho bimwebimwe, gutyo akagabanya cane ingorane zo gukusanya amakuru udashaka canke guhanahana amakuru ata wemerewe.


NetGuard, nk’akarorero, iragufasha gucunga uburyo bwo gukoresha Internet ku buryo bubereye, ku makuru ya Wi-Fi n’ayo kuri telefone ngendanwa. RethinkDNS kandi itanga ibintu biteye imbere nk’ugucungera DNS, guhagarika amatangazo n’ugusuzuma ibibazo vya DNS kugira ngo umenye ibishobora gusohoka.


![Image](assets/fr/146.webp)


### Gukingira ububiko n'uburongozi mu gihe co gutakaza


#### Gushiramwo ububiko bwawe


Gukora backup y’amakuru yawe ya smartphone ni ikintu gihambaye cane ku mutekano wawe. Ariko iyo backup itegerezwa kuba ipfutse, kugira ngo amakuru yawe y’agaciro ntaboneke n’umuntu wese yoba afise ibiganza vyiwe ku bikoresho vyawe vy’ububiko. Ivyo birajanye n’amafoto, inyandiko n’amakuru y’ibisabwa.


Kugira ngo ubishikeko, ushobora gukoresha inyishu z’aho hantu zipfutse, nka disiki y’inyuma canke urufunguzo rwa USB rwapfutse (nk’akarorero na Veracrypt). Ivyo bishitse, inyishu z’igicu zitwakira ubwazo nka *Syncthing* canke *Nextcloud* ziguha uburenganzira bwo gucungera amakuru yawe kuri server y’umuntu ku giti ciwe, mu gihe uguma ugenzura vyose ku bijanye no kuyaronka n’ibanga. Mu buryo butandukanye n’ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji vyo mu gicu (Google Drive, iCloud...), izo nyishu zigabanya cane amakuru yawe ku bandi bantu.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/veracrypt-d5ed4c83-7c1c-4181-95ea-963fdf2d83c5

#### Guhanagura kure


Telefone ngendanwa yazimiye canke yibwe irashobora kuba isoko y’amakuru menshi ku muntu atera: Amakuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe, amateka y’ugusura, amakonti ahuye, n’ibindi.


Kuri Android, ushobora gukoresha *Rondera igikoresho canje* uhereye ku mategeko ya Google. Kuri iOS, *Rondera iPhone yanje* irafise uruhara nk’urwo nyene, ushobora kuyironka ukoresheje iCloud. Ivyo bikoresho biratuma ushobora guca ufunga uburenganzira bwo gukoresha, ugahamagara igikoresho kugira ngo kibone aho kiri, canke nk’uburyo bwa nyuma, ugahanagura amakuru yose uri kure. Hariho kandi ibikorwa bisa n’ivyo bicungiwe n’ibikoresho vy’abahinguzi, nka *SmartThings Find* ya Samsung.


![Image](assets/fr/147.webp)


Ariko rero, ivyo bintu birafise ingorane zikomeye: Bishira hamwe amakuru yawe y’agaciro (aho uri, kwinjira, gukoresha kure, n’ibindi) ku maserukira y’ishirahamwe ry’abikorera ku giti cabo, kandi bisaba ko uguma ukoresha aho uri.


Niwahitamwo kubishira mu ngiro uko biri kwose, gerageza ivyo bintu imbere y’igihe kugira ngo umenye neza ko bizokora neza ku musi uzoba ubikeneye vy’ukuri.


Canke rero, nimba ushaka kudakoresha izo nzira zo gukoresha telefone yawe, ndagusavye cane ko uhora ukora backup y’amakuru yo kuri telefone yawe kugira ngo ntutakaze amakuru yawe iyo igikoresho cawe kizimiye canke cibwe. Kugira ngo umuntu ntashobore kuronka amakuru yawe, nushireho ijambobanga rikomeye ry’ugufunga telefone yawe n’ikarata SIM yawe.


Twashitse ku mpera y’iki gice ku buryo bwiza bwo gukoresha telefone yawe y’amaboko. Mu gice gikurikira, nzokwereka inyishu zibereye cane zo kuvugana n’abandi mu mutekano kandi mu ibanga ukoresheje igikoresho cawe, haba mu guhamagara, guhana ubutumwa canke gucunga amatsinda yawe y’amakuru.


## Kuvugana ata wumva .


<chapterId>e60773c6-ee96-47b2-a9fa-08d1bdbd1108</chapterId>


Muri iyi si y’ubu ihuye, igice kinini c’ivyo duhanahana ku giti cacu, ku bijanye n’umwuga no ku bijanye n’ivy’ubuhinga bibera biciye ku butumwa bwo kuri interineti. Ariko rero, ibanga ry’ivyo bimenyetso riratandukanye cane bivanye n’amategeko akoreshwa.


Muri iki gice, tuzogerageza gutahura ibibazo vy’ubuhinga n’ivy’ibikorwa bijanye no gukoresha ibikoresho vy’itumanaho ry’ubuhinga bwa none, kugira ngo duhitemwo no gukoresha ivyo bitanga uburinzi nyakuri bwo gutega amatwi no gucungera.


### Ni kuki ubutumwa bwa SMS butarinda ivyo muhanahana?


SMS (*Short Message Service*) mu mateka yarakunzwe cane mu guhanahana amajambo, ariko ishingiye ku nzira y’ubuhinga bwa kera ya kera kuva mu mpera z’imyaka ya 1980. Iyi porotokole, yinjijwe mu ngingo ngenderwako za GSM (*Sisteme y’isi yose y’itumanaho ry’amatelefone ngendanwa*), nta buryo bwo gupfuka amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera itanga. Mu bikorwa, ubutumwa bwose bwoherezwa burungikwa mu nyandiko zitomoye biciye ku nzira z’abakoresha telefone ngendanwa (rimwe na rimwe bushirwa mu nzira ku maradiyo Interface gusa, ariko ntibushobora gushika ku mpera kugeza ku mpera). Ibi bisigura ko ubutumwa bushobora gufatwa ku rwego rwinshi:



- n'umukoresha
- n'umukinyi w'umubisha afata uruja n'uruza rw'abantu (nk'akarorero biciye ku bafata IMSI)
- canke n'inzego za Leta zifise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ibikorwa remezo vy'uruja n'uruza mu buryo butegekanijwe n'amategeko canke butemewe n'amategeko .


Kubera ko ubutumwa bwa SMS bubikwa kuri serveri nyamukuru z’abakoresha, n’ubugoyagoye bw’uburyo bwo kwemeza ko umuntu ari uwuriho (inomero ya telefone nk’ikimenyetso kidasanzwe), bituma ubutumwa bufatwa bitagoranye kandi bugashobora guterwa. SMS rero ntibereye rwose gutanga amakuru, haba mu bijanye n’umuntu ku giti ciwe, mu bijanye n’umwuga canke mu bijanye n’ibintu bikomeye.


Ivyo bipimo birakora no kuri MMS (*Multimedia Messaging Service*), ishingiye ku mishinge imwe y’ubuhinga, hakongerwako n’ibintu vyinshi (amafoto, amasanamu).


Mu myaka ya vuba, abakoresha n’abahinguzi bamwebamwe barashizeho RCS (*Ibikorwa vy’Itumatumanako vy’Ubutunzi*), ni ukuvuga ubuhinga bwo guhindura ubutumwa bwo kuri telefone. RCS irashoboza kohereza ubutumwa butunganijwe (amashusho, amasanamu, ivyemezo vy’ukwakira, n’ibindi) kandi igashiramwo ubuhinga bwo gufungura amakuru (TLS), ariko ivyo biguma bivana n’abakozi bakoresha kandi ntivyemeza ko ubutumwa buzoba buva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera mu bihe vyose. Ikindi, uguca ibice kw’ishyirwa mu ngiro ryayo hagati y’abayikoresha n’abayikora (hagati ya Android na iOS, nk’akarorero) biragabanya kwemerwa kwayo n’ukwizigirwa kwayo nyakuri.


Kuva muri 2021, ubutumwa bwa Google bwaremeye uburyo bwo gukingira amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera, ariko iyo nzira ishobora gukoreshwa gusa iyo abo bompi bakoresha ubutumwa bwa Google.


Muri Ntwarante 2025, ishirahamwe rya GSM ryasohoye *Universal Profile 3.0* (UP 3.0), ryashizeho amaherezo ingingo ngenderwako y’ugukorana n’abandi ku bijanye n’ugushiramwo amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera (E2EE) muri RCS. Ivyo bituma iyo Exchange ibaye biciye ku mukiriya wa RCS yubahiriza UP 3.0, ibirimwo ntibishobora gusomwa n’uwubikoresha be n’uwufata IMSI. Google na Apple zatangaje ko zizoshigikira ubu buhinga (biracariho nimba ivyo bizokorana). Ariko rero, iyo kimwe muri ivyo bikoresho kidahuye na RCS UP 3.0, canke iyo ata nzira ya IP iriho, ivy’uguhanahana amakuru birahita bihindukira bikaja ku butumwa busanzwe, butagiramwo amakuru, ivyo bikaba bituma gufata amakuru biba ata co bimaze.


Ku ruhande rwa Apple, iMessage (yatangujwe mu 2011) itanga ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru hagati y’abakoresha Apple, ariko iyo porotokole iguma yugaye kandi igarukira ku bidukikije vya iOS/macOS. Iyo umuntu ahana ubutumwa n’abakoresha bari hanze y’ivyo bidukikije, ubutumwa burasubira mu nzira ya kera, bugatakaza ibanga ryose. Encryption irashobora kandi gusenyuka iyo wewe canke uwo mugenzi wawe ubitse ubutumwa bwawe muri iCloud ata *Advanced Data Protection*.


Muri make, nta SMS isanzwe, canke MMS, canke mbere RCS isanzwe ishobora gufatwa nk’imiti yo kwizigirwa, y’isi yose yo kuzigama ibanga ry’uguhanahana amakuru. Gukoresha ubutumwa bwa Google, iMessage canke umurongo wa RCS UP 3.0 wo muri kazoza ni vyo vyonyene bishobora gutuma haba ibanga ryiza, igihe cose bompi bafashe umurongo umwe wo gupfuka amakuru. Kandi ni ho nyene umutego nyamukuru w’ubutumwa bwa SMS mu buryo bwagutse uri: Iyi porogarama yo gutanga ubutumwa, ibanza gushirwa ku matelefone menshi, ihuriza hamwe amategeko atandukanye cane, kandi iyo uwundi ashigikiye gusa amategeko ya SMS, ubutumwa bwawe buzorungikwa mu buryo butomoye, ataco uzi. Ni co gituma, gushika hashizweho ingingo ngenderwako y’ugushiramwo amakuru y’iherezo ry’isi yose kandi ikomeye, ndaguhanura cane kudakoresha ubutumwa busanzwe, kuko uguma uvyifatamwo neza cane mu guhitamwo kwa mugenzi wawe uburyo bwo gukoresha amakuru kugira ngo ushobore kwizigira umutekano wawe bwite.


Aho gukoresha SMS, noguhanura gukoresha ubutumwa bwihariye bukoresha ubuhinga bukomeye kandi buboneka, bushobora gutuma umuntu ashobora guhanahana amakuru mu buryo butekanye kandi bw’ibanga.


### Ubutumwa butekanye: ni ibihe bisubizo?


Kubera ko ubutumwa bwo kuri telefone bufise aho bugarukira, haradutse ubuhinga butari buke bwo muri iki gihe, bumwebumwe bukaba bufise ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera. Aha niho hari insiguro y’ibikoresho nyamukuru biriho uno musi, kugira ngo bigufashe kumenya ivyo bihuye neza n’ivyo ukeneye mu bijanye n’umutekano n’ibanga.


#### Ikimenyetso


Signal ni porogarama yo gutanga ubutumwa buca ikoreshwa kuva mu ntango kugira ngo itange ibanga ryinshi n’umutekano. Ishingiye kuri *Signal Protocol*, ishobora gutuma ubutumwa bwose, ijwi canke amasanamu, hamwe n’ugusangira amadosiye, haba ugushiramwo amakuru mu buryo bubereye. Iryo tegeko risubira gukoreshwa n’izindi nzira nyinshi zo gutanga ubutumwa, nka WhatsApp, Facebook Messenger, Skype n’ubutumwa bwa Google (mu gushirwa mu ngiro kwayo kwa RCS).


![Image](assets/fr/148.webp)


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, ikiyago cose kiri muri Signal kirindwa n’uburyo bwo gupfuka butaringaniye kandi bumara igihe gito: Imfunguruzo z’ikiganiro ziraganirwako mu buryo bukomeye kandi zigasenyuka inyuma yo gukoreshwa, gutyo bikagabanya ingorane zo gusenyuka. Uguseruka kw’iyi porogarama, kode yayo yose ikaba ari open-source ku ruhande rw’umukiriya n’urwa server, bisigura ko umuhinga mu vy’umutekano canke umushakashatsi wese ashobora kugenzura ubutungane bwayo n’uko yubahiriza ingingo ngenderwako z’ubuhinga bwa crypto zavuzwe.


Ariko rero, Signal irafise intege nke iyo bije ku bijanye no kutamenyekana: iyo porogarama isaba inomero ya telefone ibereye kugira ngo umuntu yiyandikishe kandi amenyekane. Naho iyo nomero itaboneka mu buryo butunganye ku bantu ushobora guhura na bo (ishobora guhishwa mw’izina ry’uruyeri), ico gisabwa kirazana ukuntu umuntu yizigira ibikorwa remezo vya telefone, bigatuma rero habaho ikinogo co gukurikirana.


Muri make, Signal ni umuti mwiza cane wo gutanga ubutumwa, ariko ikibabaje ni uko bisaba gufatanya n’inomero ya telefone.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/signal-8dfb5572-6962-4f1c-bfa5-3192da4e9a4e

#### WhatsApp


WhatsApp, ifise Meta (yahora yitwa Facebook), nayo ikoresha *Signal Protocol* mu bijanye n’ugushiramwo amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera. Rero, mu vyiyumviro, ibiyago vyawe vya WhatsApp birakingirwa neza kugira ngo ntibifatwe. Ariko rero, si ngombwa ko ari vyo vyiza kuruta ibindi vyose mu bijanye n’ibanga nyaryo: iyo porogarama ikoranya amakuru menshi cane (imibare, incuro umuntu ahinduranya, ahantu hafi, abo umuntu ashobora guhura na we...), ashobora gukoreshwa mu bucuruzi na Meta mu kwamamaza canke mu gusesangura.


Kandi, ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru bukoreshwa na WathsApp ntibushobora kugenzurwa, kuko kode yayo y’inkomoko ari iy’umuntu. Ni co gituma ntababwira ko mukoresha WhatsApp mu gihe ibanga n’umutekano w’ivyo muvugana ari ngirakamaro.


#### Itelegaramu


Telegram ni ubutumwa buzwi cane kubera ubuhinga bwayo n’ibintu biyikoresha (imirongo ya bose, ama bots, amatsinda manini...). Ariko rero, umutekano wayo uragabanutse cane ku buryo busanzwe: "uguhanahana kw'ibanga" gusa ni kwo kwungukira ku gushiramwo amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera. Ibindi biganiro vyose (ivyinshi mu biganiro abakoresha bavugana ku musi ku musi) bibikwa bitashizwemwo amakuru ku ma server ya Telegram.


![Image](assets/fr/149.webp)


Telegram rero irashobora mu buryo bw’ubuhinga gushika ku birimwo ibiyago vyinshi bitarinzwe mu buryo butomoye. Naho iyo sosiyete yofata ingingo ikomeye ku butegetsi bwa Leta, Telegram si umuti mwiza wo guhanahana amakuru y'ibanga canke y'agaciro, kiretse ukoresheje mu buryo butomoye "uguhanahana amakuru y'ibanga" yayo, ariko ntaco bimaze cane ku musi ku musi.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/telegram-account-09ab3cf3-7625-4267-97a1-24e59a9e5943

#### Batatu


Threema, yatangujwe mu Busuwisi mu 2012, iratandukanye n’izindi nzira nyinshi zo gutanga ubutumwa butekanye kubera uburyo bwayo bwo gukingira ubuzima bwite. Udakunze Signal, WhatsApp canke Telegram, nta nomero ya telefone isabwa kugira ngo umuntu akore konti. Uwukoresha ashobora guhabwa ikimenyetso kidasanzwe, kigatuma umuntu ashobora kwiyandikisha ata n’umwe amubona ata n’umwe ahuye n’akaranga nyakuri.


![Image](assets/fr/150.webp)


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Threema itanga ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera ku bijanye n’itumanaho ryose: ubutumwa, amatelefone, amadosiye, amatsinda, n’ibindi bikorwa. Kuva mu mwaka w’2020, kode y’inkomoko y’ibikoresho vyo kuri telefone ngendanwa yarabaye inkomoko yuguruye, bikaba vyatumye habaho igenzura ry’abantu bigenga. Ku rundi ruhande, ibikorwa remezo vya server biguma ari ivy’umuntu, naho nyene biri mu Busuwisi gusa, igihugu gifise amategeko meza ku bijanye no kurinda amakuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Iyi porogaramu ihuye na Android na iOS, kandi itanga urubuga rwa Interface rutekanye, hamwe n’umukiriya w’imvukira wa Windows, Linux na macOS. Ariko rero, kugira ngo utangure gukoresha telefone ngendanwa.


Ikindi kintu gihambaye ca Threema ni ubuhinga bwayo bwo gukora: iyo porogarama si ubuntu ahubwo ni iyo kugura (hafi €5.99). Iryo hitamwo ririnda kwizigira ivyitegererezo bishingiye ku gukusanya amakuru canke kwamamaza. Kugira ngo umuntu ntamenyekane igihe agura, imfunguruzo zo gukoresha zishobora kugurwa mu bitcoins canke mu mafaranga ataco uhinduye ku Threema Shop ya Android.


Ngira ngo uwo muti wo gutanga ubutumwa ni mwiza cane, ariko ikibazo cawo nyamukuru ni uko kode y’inkomoko y’abakozi bayo iguma ari iya nyir’umuntu.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/threema-24382d25-df7b-4e96-b332-6968f748df74

#### Ibiganiro vyoroshe


SimpleX Chat, yatangujwe mu 2021, irakuraho burundu iciyumviro c’indangamuntu y’ukoresha: nta nimero ya telefone, nta zina ry’uruyeri ry’abantu bose, nta rufunguzo rwa bose ruboneka. Uwukoresha wese amenyekana gusa biciye ku mahuza canke ku makode ya QR y’igihe gito. Iyi nyubakwa ituma ubucuti hagati y’abakoresha budashoboka, bikaba vyemeza ko haba ibanga ryinshi.


![Image](assets/fr/151.webp)


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, ubutumwa burashirwa mu mfuruka kuva ku mpera gushika ku mpera kandi bukaca ku bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Izo nzira z’ugutanga amakuru nta bumenyi zifise ku bijanye n’uwuzirungitse, uwuzironka canke imfunguruzo zazo. Ubutumwa bumaze gushikirizwa, buca buca bukurwaho kuri server. SimpleX ikoresha ubuhinga butagiramwo ubufatanye, bushizwe ahantu hamwe: abakozi ntibasangira ububiko bw’isi yose, kandi umukoresha wese arashobora gushiramwo umurongo wiwe bwite. Ivyo bitandukanye n’imiti nka Matrix, aho abakozi bahurikiye hamwe bakurikirana ivy’uguhinduranya.


Iryo porotokole ryose ni ry’inkomoko yuguruye: abaguzi, abakozi n’amaporotokole birashikira abantu bose kandi bikagenzurwa. SimpleX iboneka kuri Android, iOS, Linux, Windows na macOS, ifise ububiko bwo mu karere bufise amakuru, bushobora gutwarwa, ku buryo amakuru ashobora kwimurirwa ata server nyamukuru. Buri muntu wese akoresha arashobora kandi gucunga imirongo myinshi yitandukanije, imwe yose ikaba ifise ivyayo, izina ry’ibanga n’ifoto. Ukwo guhinduranya bituma bishoboka gutandukanya neza ubuzima bwite, ubuzima bw’umwuga n’izina ry’uruyeri.


Abahuza bongerako biciye ku mahuza y’igihe gito canke amaderesi adahinduka (ibimenyetso bihoraho ariko bishobora gusubirwamwo). Ushobora kandi guhitamwo hagati ya Exchange y’igihe gito canke uburyo bwa kera, bufise ubugenzuzi bwiza ku bijanye n’ukuboneka n’uburenganzira (nk’akarorero, guhisha izina ryawe ry’ukuri inyuma y’izina ry’uruyeri ry’umuntu wese).


Ku bijanye n’umutekano n’ibanga, SimpleX irarenga uburyo bwinshi bwo gutanga ubutumwa busanzweho, igabanya amakuru y’imbere mu gihugu ku rugero rutoyi kandi igakuraho ukuntu umuntu yizigira ububiko bwa mbere canke ikimenyetso kidasanzwe. Ariko rero, iyo nyubakwa irasaba ko habaho ibintu vyinshi bishobora gutuma umuntu ashobora gukoresha neza: rimwe na rimwe nta n’umwe ashobora gukoresha neza, bikenewe ko umuntu yiga gatoyi mu ntango, kandi bivana n’uko hariho ama server y’ugutanga amakuru.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/simplex-chat-7a1efa11-4d0a-49c4-92aa-e18bf22c22b9

#### Ikoraniro


Session, yatangujwe mu mwaka w’2020 n’ishirahamwe ryitwa Oxen Privacy Tech Foundation, ni porogarama yo gutanga ubutumwa yagenewe gutanga ubuzima bwite n’ukwihangana mu gihe umuntu ariko aragenzurwa. Session nta makuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe isaba ku kwiyandikisha: nta nimero ya telefone, nta e-mail, gusa imfunguruzo zibiri z’ubuhinga bwa none zivuye mu karere. Ivyo bituma umuntu ashobora kwemeza ko ari we atamenyekana.


![Image](assets/fr/152.webp)


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, Session ishira mu ngiro ubuhinga bwo gupfuka ubutumwa, amadosiye, amajwi n’amatelefone, hamwe n’imigwi (abashika ku 100). Ubutumwa burungikwa biciye ku rubuga rwigenga rushingiye ku bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa node vyahumekewe n’ubwubatsi bw’igitunguru bwa Tor. Ubwo buryo buratanga uburinzi buteye imbere ku gucungera urubuga, harimwo n’aba ISP n’abakozi ba Leta.


Umukiriya wa Session na server ni inkomoko yuguruye. Iyi porogarama iboneka kuri Android, iOS, Windows, macOS na Linux, ikaba ifise uburyo bwo gukorana hagati y’ibikoresho biciye ku majambo Mnemonic asa n’ayo akoreshwa mu bikoresho vya Bitcoin. Iri jambo riha uwuriko arakoresha ububasha bwo gucungera amakuru yiwe, ariko kandi ritanga inshingano ikomeye mu bijanye no gucungera amakuru.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/session-b0e3193c-2129-4f1b-9013-c211210724c3

#### Gukomeza


Keet, yatangujwe mu 2022 na Holepunch (isosiyete ishigikiwe na Tether na Bitfinex), iratandukanye cane n’uburyo bwayo bwo kwegereza abantu bose: Ivy’uguhanahana amakuru vyose (ubutumwa, amatelefone y’amajwi n’amasanamu, uguhanahana amadosiye, n’ibindi) bibera ataco bimaze hagati y’abakoresha, ataco bica kuri server n’imwe. Iyi nyubakwa ya P2P irakuraho abahuza kandi igatuma iyo sisitemu igira ibanga kandi ikaba ishobora gukomera.


![Image](assets/fr/153.webp)


Keet ipfuka ivy’itumanaho vyose kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera. Ukwiyandikisha ntibimenyekana rwose: nta nomero ya telefone, e-mail Address canke ikimenyetso kigaragaza umuntu bisabwa. Ivyo bituma haba ibanga ryinshi kuva igihe iyo serivisi itanguye gukora. Amatelefone yo kuri videwo ni ay’agaciro kanini cane, kandi ukwohereza amadosiye nta n’aho bigarukira, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kubikoresha mu buryo bw’umwuga no mu buryo bwiwe bwite.


Ku rundi ruhande, naho ibice bimwebimwe (ugushiramwo amakuru n’ugukorana n’abandi) bisohorwa nk’ivy’ubuhinga bufunguye kuri GitHub, umukiriya wa Keet Interface ntiyari yuguruye bimwe bishitse igihe SCU-202 yandikwa (Gitugutu 2025). Ariko rero, Holepunch yatangaje ko izosohora iyo kode yose muri kazoza.


Keet iboneka kuri Android, iOS, Windows, macOS na Linux, kandi ishobora guhurizwa hamwe hagati y’ibikoresho hakoreshejwe ijambo Mnemonic.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/keet-efdb759d-5e94-4bbf-b28c-5fa8669c809b

#### Olvid


Olvid, yatangujwe muri 2019, ni ubutumwa bwo mu gifaransa bufise amabanga. Iciyumviro caco gikomeye: Ukwiyandikisha ata makuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Imenyekanisha rishingiye ku Exchange itaziguye y’imfunguruzo z’ibanga hagati y’abakoresha.


![Image](assets/fr/154.webp)


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, ubutumwa buri kuri Olvid burashirwa mu mfuruka kuva ku mpera gushika ku mpera, hakoreshejwe uburyo bwihariye bwagenewe gukingira atari ibiri mu butumwa gusa, ariko n’amakuru y’inyuma: Nta n’umwe, harimwo n’umukozi wa mbere, ashobora kumenya uwuriko aravugana n’uwundi, canke ryari. Ico kigereranyo kigabanya cane ingorane zo gukora ubutasi no gucungera abantu.


Ariko rero, ibikorwa remezo vya server biguma ari ivy’umuntu kandi bikaba bishizwe hamwe, bishizwe kuri AWS (*Amazon Web Services*). Kode y’umukiriya imaze imyaka myinshi ari open-source, ariko kode ya server ntisohorwa, ivyo bikaba bigabanya uguseruka kw’ubuhinga bwa sisitemu.


Icogereranyo c’umutekano ca Olvid gishingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako ihambaye: Ukubura rwose umuntu agira gatatu yizigirwa mu gushinga akaranga k’ubuhinga bwa none. Udakunze uburyo bwinshi bwo gutanga ubutumwa bufise amakuru, bwishingikiriza ku bubiko bumwe kugira ngo bucunge akaranga k’abakoresha, Olvid ntiyizigira ibikorwa remezo vyose vy’ubuhinga bwo guhanahana amakuru kugira ngo bimenyeshe ubutungane bw’itumanaho. Iyi nyubakwa irakuraho ingorane zijanye n’ugusenyura ububiko.


Olvid ikoresha umukozi wo gukwiragiza ubutumwa hagati, ariko uruhara rwayo ni urw’ivy’ubuhinga: Ikora ivy’ugutanga ubutumwa bushizwe mu buryo butajanye n’igihe. Iyi server nta ntambwe iyo ari yo yose igira mu nzira yo gushiramwo amakuru, kandi ntazi akaranga nyakuri k’abakoresha, canke ibirimwo canke amakuru y’ubutumwa (uretse urufunguzo rwa bose rw’uwuronka, rukenewe kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gutanga inzira). Bishobora rero gufatwa nk’urwanko ku buryo busanzwe, ataco bihungabanya ku mutekano muri rusangi. Naho yoba yarahungabanijwe, ntiyari kwemera ko umuntu wese ashobora kuronka ibirimwo mu bimenyetso vy’itumanaho. Olvid rero yiyumvira ko ubutumwa buzokwiragizwa hamwe (kubera imvo z’ubushobozi n’uburyo bw’ibikorwa), mu gihe yizeza umutekano udashingiye kuri ivyo bikorwa remezo.


Olvid atanga amaverisiyo abiri:



- Verisiyo y’ubuntu, itanga ibikorwa vyose kiretse guhamagara amajwi n’amasanamu (kwakira gusa) no gukorana n’ibikoresho vyinshi
- Verisiyo yishurwa ku €4.99 ku kwezi ifungura ibiranga vyose


Iryo kete ryemejwe na ANSSI (*Ikigo c’Igihugu c’Umutekano w’Imirongo y’Amakuru*).


Olvid ikorana na Android, iOS, Windows, macOS na Linux. Ivy’ubuhinga bwayo biguma vyoroshe kandi bishoboka. Iyo porogarama irafise kandi uburyo bwo gucungera imfunguruzo n’abantu ushobora guhura na bo, kugira ngo ushobore kugarura konti yawe ku gikoresho gishasha.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/olvid-05038dc1-62c0-4a47-be4e-3d23c6155bfd

### Ubutumwa bwo kwirinda


Ubutumwa buzwi cane nka WhatsApp, WeChat, Facebook Messenger, Ubutumwa butaziguye kuri Instagram, Snapchat na LINE burakoreshwa cane ku musi ku musi. Ariko rero, mu vy’ubuhinga, izo nzira ntizihuye n’ingingo mfatirwako z’umutekano zo muri iki gihe zibereye gukoreshwa mu guhanahana amakuru ku giti cabo.


Muri rusangi, ibintu bibiri vy’ishimikiro umuntu akwiye kwitwararika igihe ahitamwo ubuhinga bwo gutanga ubutumwa ni ibi: Yoba itanga ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera, kandi kode yayo yoba ari iyo gufungura? Hanyuma hariho n’ibindi bishobora gushimisha, nk’ukwiyandikisha ata mazina canke gukoresha ubuhinga bwo gukorana n’abandi, ariko ivyo bibiri vya mbere Elements ni vyo vy’ishimikiro. Ugushiramwo amakuru y’ibanga bituma ivyo uhindura biguma ari ibanga, mu gihe gufungura kode y’inkomoko bigufasha kugenzura ko ugushiramwo amakuru y’ibanga vyashizwe mu ngiro ata nkomanzi.


Gukoresha ibikorwa bidashobora gushitsa ivyo bisabwa bibiri ni nk’uguha burundu uburinzi bw’amafaranga yawe abakinnyi b’ubudandaji inyungu zabo z’ubutunzi akenshi zivana no kuyakoresha nabi.


Aha niho hari urutonde rw’incamake rw’ibikoresho nyamukuru vyo gutanga ubutumwa biriho n’ibiranga, nk’uko bimeze mu gihe c’ukwandika (Gitugutu 2025):


| Application          | E2EE 1:1       | E2EE groups   | Anonymous registration | Client open-source license | Server open-source license | Decentralized server | Creation year |
| -------------------- | -------------- | -------------- | ------------------- | -------------------------- | --------------------------- | -------------------- | ------------- |
| WhatsApp             | ✅              | ✅              | ❌                   | ❌                          | ❌                           | ❌                    | 2009              |
| WeChat               | ❌              | ❌              | ❌                   | ❌                          | ❌                           | ❌                    | 2011              |
| Facebook Messenger   | ✅              | 🟡 (optionnel) | ❌                   | ❌                          | ❌                           | ❌                    | 2011              |
| Telegram             | 🟡 (optionnel) | ❌              | 🟡                  | ✅                          | ❌                           | ❌                    | 2013              |
| LINE                 | ✅              | ✅              | ❌                   | ❌                          | ❌                           | ❌                    | 2011              |
| Signal               | ✅              | ✅              | ❌                   | ✅                          | ✅                           | ❌                    | 2014              |
| Threema              | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ✅                          | ❌                           | ❌                    | 2012              |
| Element (Matrix)     | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ✅                          | ✅                           | 🟡 (federated)          | 2016              |
| Delta Chat           | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ✅                          | N/A                         | 🟡 (via email)       | 2017              |
| Conversations (XMPP) | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ✅                          | ✅                           | 🟡 (federated)          | 2014              |

| Keet                 | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ❌                          | N/A                         | ✅                    | 2022              |
