| Briar                | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ✅                          | N/A                         | ✅                    | 2018              |
| Tox                  | ✅              | ✅              | ✅                   | ✅                          | N/A                         | ✅                    | 2013              |

*E2EE = Ugushiramwo amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera*


Umutekano w’ivy’itumanaho ryawe ry’ubuhinga bwa none uvana canecane no guhitamwo ubuhinga bwiza no kwemera uburyo bwiza bwo kubikoresha. Gutahura uburyo bwo gucungera umutekano bushingiyeko, kumenya amakosa ari mu mirongo ngenderwako isanzwe no guhitamwo uburyo bwo kwizigirwa ni vyo bishingiyeko canecane kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kuvugana n’abandi ata wumva.


Kugeza ubu, twasuzumye ingene wokingira telefone yawe n’ingene wohitamwo porogarama yo gutanga ubutumwa yizigirwa. Mu gice gikurikira, ndasaba kwagura iyi nyigisho ku miryango yose ikomeye y’amaporogarama y’amatelefone ngendanwa, kugira ngo uronke uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha amaporogarama ukunda cane. Yaba ari email, ububiko bw’amadosiye, ikarita, amasanamu canke umuziki, ni ibihe bikoresho vy’inkomoko yuguruye ushobora gukoresha?


## ibikorwa vy'inkomoko yuguruye: ubundi buryo bwiza


<chapterId>9c0e056c-45ce-407c-b4b6-f648bbc1f7d5</chapterId>


Uretse porogarama zo gutumako ubutumwa, birahambaye kwibuka ko izindi porogarama ziri kuri telefone yawe zishobora gukoresha amakuru yawe mu ntumbero z’ubudandaji. Ikintu ciza, hariho uburyo bundi bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bufunguye bubaha ubuzima bwite bwawe. Ivyo nivyo nshaka kubamenyesha muri iki gice.


Sinzosubira ku bijanye n’ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha ama browser n’intumwa zica hano, nk’uko twamaze kubivuga mu buryo burambuye mu bice vyabanje.


### Imeyili z'abaguzi


Email iguma ari igikoresho gihambaye co guhanahana amakuru, ariko porogarama zizwi cane, nka Gmail canke Outlook, zitera ibibazo vyinshi vy’ubuzima bwite. Izo serivisi akenshi zisesangura ubutumwa bwawe, zibika amakuru y’imbere mu gihugu kandi zigagira uruhara mu kurema imirongo y’imenyekanisha.


**Ibindi**:



- [Imeyili y'ubutungane](https://imeyili.kode y'ubutungane.eu/)


FairEmail ni porogaramu ya Android yuzuye, ishingiye ku mutekano. Ishigikira abatanga IMAP/SMTP bose, ishoboza gupfuka ubutumwa biciye kuri OpenPGP, ibuza amashusho yo kure (akoreshwa nk’abakurikirana), kandi nta n’imwe ikoresha. Biguha ububasha bwiza ku mahuza, amatangazo n’inyifato yo guhuza.


![Image](assets/fr/155.webp)



- [Ikete rya K-9](k9ikete.app)


K-9 Mail ni umukiriya w’ubutumwa bwa Android bufunguye, buherutse kwinjira mu bidukikije vya Mozilla vya Thunderbird. Ifasha amakonti menshi, gupfuka PGP biciye kuri OpenKeychain, kandi ikora ata server iri hagati.


![Image](assets/fr/156.webp)



- [Itelefone y'inkuba](https://www.inyoni y'inkuba.net/itelefone/)


Thunderbird Mobile ni verisiyo y’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma vy’ivyuma. Mu buryo buhuye n’ubuhinga bw’uwo mugambi, iyo porogarama ishimika ku bijanye n’ibanga, uguseruka kw’amategeko no kutagira ubuhinga bwo gupima uburebure bw’ibintu. Thunderbird Mobile ishingiye kuri porogarama ya K-9 Mail, ariyo ikurikira ku mugaragaro kuri Android. Irafise uburongozi buteye imbere bwa konti za IMAP na POP, gukingira ubutumwa kuri interineti (biciye kuri OpenPGP), na Interface yoroshe kandi ikora neza.


![Image](assets/fr/157.webp)


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/thunderbird-91d02325-0361-4641-b152-8975890284a8

- [Tuta](ku rubuga rwa Tuta/)


Tuta (yahora yitwa "*Tutanota*") itanga umuti wuzuye w'imeli zifise amakuru y'ibanga, ariko umukiriya wayo w'itelefone ngendanwa ashigikira gusa amakonti ya Tuta. Ntibikorana n’abandi batanga. Interface ni iya none kandi nta n’ibintu vyinshi irimwo, kandi kwiyandikisha ntibisaba amakuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


![Image](assets/fr/158.webp)



- [Ikete rya porotoni](https://porotoni.me/ikete)


Proton Mail ni ubutumwa butekanye bushingiye ku Busuwisi butanga ubutumwa bushingiye ku mpera ku mpera hagati y’abakoresha Proton. Iyi porogaramu yo kuri telefone ngendanwa irafunguye, nta kwamamaza igira kandi nta makuru y’ibanga yegeranya iyo umuntu yiyandikishije. Proton Mail ifasha gusa amakonti ya Proton, ariko yemera kohereza amakuru mu buryo bupfutse mbere no ku ma aderesi yo hanze biciye ku jambobanga.


![Image](assets/fr/159.webp)


Uburyo bwa email bushingiye ku bice 2 bitandukanye: Uwutanga email (nka Gmail, Tuta canke Proton Mail), akora ivyo kwakira, kohereza no kubika ubutumwa biciye ku ma server; n’umukiriya wa imeyili, ari ryo porogaramu ikoreshwa mu kuraba no kwandika imeyili zawe (nk’iporogarama ya Gmail, Outlook, K-9 Mail canke Thunderbird). Umukiriya ashobora kwifatanya n’abatanga amakuru batandukanye biciye ku masezerano asanzwe nka IMAP canke SMTP.


Birashoboka rero gukoresha umukiriya w’inkomoko yuguruye afise ubuzima bwite mu gihe mu ntango afise konti n’umutanga amakuru asanzwe. Hariho porogaramu zimwe zimwe, nka Gmail, Proton Mail canke Tuta, zitanga abaguzi ba email na bo nyene bakora nk’abatanga ubutumwa, gutyo bagatanga umuti wuzuye ushizemwo ugusoma kwa Interface n’ugutuma/kwakira imeyili.


Aha hariho ivyiyumviro bike, aho uriko uhitamwo uwuguha imeyili:



- [Ikete rya porotoni](https://porotoni.me/ikete)
- [Tuta](ku rubuga rwa Tuta/)
- [Isanduku y'ubutumwa](https://isanduku y'ubutumwa.org/)
- [Gukuraho imizi](https://gukuraho imizi.org/)
- [Uruzitiro rw'ubutumwa](https://uruzitiro rw'ubutumwa.com/)


### Gukora ikarita no kugendera mu mazi


Ivyinshi mu bikoresho vya kera vyo gukora ikarita, nka Google Maps, Waze canke Citymapper, bikusanya amakuru menshi y’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Barandika aho wimuka, ivyo urondera be n’ingeso zawe, bakabikoresha mu vy’ubudandaji.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ikarita z'ibinyabuzima](https://amakarata y'ibinyabuzima.app/)


Ikarata y’ibinyabuzima ni porogaramu y’ubuntu yo kugendera ku nzira. Ishingiye ku makuru ava muri [Ikarita y’Ibarabara Yuguruye](https://www.ikarata y’Ibarabara Yuguruye.org), urutonde rw’amakuru rwuguruye kandi rukorana. Uca ufata amakarata y’uturere ushaka, hanyuma ukagendagenda ata n’urubuga.


Nta kwamamaza, gukurikirana canke gukusanya amakuru birimwo. Iyi porogaramu irabereye cane cane mu ngendo z’amaguru, ku nkweto canke ku modoka, ifise Interface yoroshe, yihuta kandi idasamaza.


![Image](assets/fr/160.webp)



- [OsmNa](urubuga rwacu/)


OsmAnd (*OpenStreetMap Ivyiyumviro vy'Ivyiyumviro*) ni indi porogarama y'ikarita y'inkomoko yuguruye. Itanga uburyo bwo kugenderamwo GPS ata n’umurongo, amakarata adondora neza (harimwo inzira, inzira z’amagare n’imiterere y’ubutaka), n’uguhindura vyinshi.


Ushobora gukoresha ibice bitandukanye (ibice vy’abagenda n’amaguru, ivy’ugutwara abantu bose, n’ibindi), gusobanura imburi z’umuvuduko canke gushiramwo amakarata yihariye nk’ayo gutembera mu misozi canke inzira zo mu mazi.


Verisiyo y’ubuntu irasanzwe ari itunze cane, kandi verisiyo y’amahera iragufasha gufungura mbere n’ibindi bikoresho no gushigikira umugambi.


![Image](assets/fr/161.webp)


### Ibiro n'inyandiko


Ibikoresho vya kera vy’ibiro nka Google Docs canke Microsoft Office birakora cane, ariko biratera ingorane zikomeye z’ibanga. Inyandiko zibikwa kuri server zazo, zigasuzumwa, rimwe na rimwe zigakoreshwa mu gutangaza canke mu gutoza abahinga mu vy’ubuhinga bwa none.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ibiro vy'ubufatanye](www.ibiro vy'ubufatanye.com/)


Ibiro vya Collabora ni verisiyo y’ibikorwa vy’ubuhinga bwa none, vyagenewe telefone ngendanwa n’ibikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none vy’i Android na iOS. Iragufasha gukora, guhindura no gusangira inyandiko z’ibiro utazokwigera uva ku gikoresho cawe canke mu gicu cawe bwite.


Porogaramu ishigikira guhindura mu bufatanye iyo ihuye n'intangamarara ya Nextcloud n'ukwaguka kwa Collabora Online. Ibi bituma bishoboka gusubiramwo ubumenyi bumeze nk'ubw'inyandiko za Google, ariko mu kwakira amadosiye yawe wewe nyene.


![Image](assets/fr/162.webp)



- [IBIRO GUSA](www.ibiro vyonyene.com/)


ONLYOFFICE ni ibiro vy’ubuhinga bufunguye. Iragufasha gufungura no guhindura inyandiko za Word, Excel na PowerPoint ukoresheje telefone yawe ngendanwa, mbere no mu karere. Ushobora kandi kuyifatanya n’ibikorwa bitandukanye vyo mu gicu kugira ngo ikoreshe neza, nka Nextcloud.


![Image](assets/fr/163.webp)


### Umuyobozi wa dosiye n'igicu


Servisi nka Google Drive canke Dropbox zibika amadosiye yawe ku ma server yo kure y’amashirahamwe yigenga. Amakuru yawe arashobora rero gucapurwa maze agakoreshwa mu kwamamaza canke mu gukora imibare. Ikindi kandi, ukeneye Internet be n’iyindi konti y’uwundi muntu kugira ngo ushobore kubironka.


**Ibindi**:



- [Igicu gikurikira](https://igicu gikurikira.com/)


Nextcloud ni umuti w’igicu c’umuntu ku giti ciwe ushobora kwakira wewe nyene canke ukawukoresha biciye ku muntu wizigirwa. Iragufasha gukorana, gusangira no guhindura amadosiye yawe ukoresheje telefone yawe, mu gihe uguma ugenzura vyose ububiko bwayo.


Kuri Android, urashobora gushiramwo porogarama yemewe ya Nextcloud kugira ngo ushikire igicu cawe bwite uri aho hose. Ushobora kandi kwongerako ibikorwa nk’ugucungera amafoto, ibiro, ikirangamisi n’ubutumwa.


![Image](assets/fr/164.webp)



- [Idosiye z'ibikoresho](github.com/zhanghai/Idosiye z'ibikoresho)


Dosiye z'ibikoresho ni umucungerezi wa dosiye yuguruye yoroshe kandi atagiramwo ibintu vyinshi. Iragufasha gusesa, kwimura, gukopa canke gufuta amadosiye mu karere kawe ku gikoresho cawe ca Android.


Porogaramu nta kwamamaza canke abakurikirana, kandi nta ruhusha rwo gukoresha nabi rusaba. Ni uburyo bushimishije bwo guhindura dosiye itangwa na Google, akenshi yinjizwa mu zindi serivisi z’igicu.


![Image](assets/fr/165.webp)


### Ikirangamisi / Igitabo


Abantu benshi bakoresha porogarama nk’ikirangamisi ca Google canke ikirangamisi ca Outlook kugira ngo bashobore gucunga amasaha yabo. Yamara izo serivisi zihuye n’amakonti yo kuri interineti ahurikiye hamwe akusanya amakuru yerekeye ingeso zawe, aho uhurira n’ingene ukorana.


**Ibindi**:



- [Etari](itsinda rya Etari/Ikirangamisi ca Etari)


Etar ni ikirangamisi coroshe, gikora neza kandi gifunguye rwose. Ishobora gukora mu karere, ariko kandi iremeza guhuza biciye kuri CalDAV, umurongo usanzwe wo guhuza ingengabihe n’ibikorwa vy’ubuzima bwite (nka Nextcloud canke EteSync).


![Image](assets/fr/166.webp)



- [Ikirangamisi coroshe](https://ibikoresho vyoroshe vy'amatelefone ngendanwa.com/ikirangamisi coroshe/)


Iyi porogaramu iri mu "*Ibikoresho vyoroshe vyo kuri telefone ngendanwa*". Nta konti canke urubuga bisaba, ivyo bikaba bituma ari vyiza gukoresha ata n’urubuga. Ushobora kwongerako ibintu, gushinga ivyibutsa no gutunganya ivyerekanwa ku musi, indwi canke ukwezi. Cokimwe n’ibindi bice vyo muri suite, Simple Calendar nta kwamamaza, nta n’umwe akurikirana kandi 100% ni inkomoko yuguruye.


![Image](assets/fr/167.webp)



- [Ikirangamisi ca Tuta](ku rubuga rwa Tuta.com/ikirangamisi)


Tuta Calendar, yateguwe n’umugwi uri inyuma ya Tuta Mail, ni ikirangamisi gifise amakuru yuzuye kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera, gikoreshwa kugira ngo ibintu vyawe bibe ibanga. Ikora kuri Android, iOS no biciye ku mukiriya w’urubuga. Mbere n’amazina, insobanuro n’amakuru y’ibintu vyawe birashirwa mu nzira, kugira ngo ata wundi muntu, harimwo na Tuta, ashobora gushika ku makuru yawe.


![Image](assets/fr/168.webp)



- [Ikirangamisi ca porotoni](https://porotoni.me/ikirangamisi)


Ikirangamisi ca Proton kandi gitanga ububiko bw'ibintu vyawe n'amakuru yavyo. Ishobora gukoreshwa kuri telefone ngendanwa (Android, iOS) no ku rubuga, ifise Interface igaragara kandi igaragara. Iyi serivisi irashoboza gukora ingengabihe nyinshi, kwinjiza/gusohora ibintu n’uburyo bwo gusangira. Urubuga rwo gukoresha ni open-source, ariko porogaramu zo kuri telefone ngendanwa ntizirafunguye bimwe bishitse.


![Image](assets/fr/169.webp)


### Gufata amajambo


Porogaramu nka Evernote, Google Keep canke OneNote zikoreshwa mu gufata ivyiyumviro, gutunganya ibikorwa canke kubika urutonde. Ariko rero, bose bizigira ibikorwa vyo kuri Internet vy’abanyagihugu, ivyo bikaba bishira amakuru yawe ku ma server yabo kandi akenshi bikasuzuma ibirimwo kugira ngo bikoreshe ubudandaji.


**Ibindi**:



- [Igitabo c'Ivyandikano](ku rubuga:


Quillpad ni porogaramu yoroshe yagenewe canecane gufata amajambo y’i Markdown. Bigufasha gupfuka amajambo yawe, gutunganya ibirimwo hakurikijwe ibimenyetso n’amabara, no kwongerako ivyibutsa. Ivyo vyose birakora ata konti canke connexion, kandi amakuru aguma abitswe ku gikoresho cawe. Bishobora kandi kubikwa mu buryo bupfutse kuri pCloud.


![Image](assets/fr/170.webp)



- [Joplin](urubuga rwa Joplin/)


Joplin ni umuti wuzuye, utanga uguhuza amajambo yashizwemwo amakuru biciye ku bikorwa bihuye nka Nextcloud, Dropbox canke WebDAV. Ushobora gucunga amajambo yoroshe canke atunganijwe (muri Markdown), gushikiriza inyandiko zawe, mbere no kwinjiza amadosiye afatanijwe.


Interface yayo irakomeye gatoyi kuruta iya QuillNote, ariko iracari nziza cane kuri telefone ngendanwa, kandi irabereye gukoreshwa ku giti cawe no ku kazi.


![Image](assets/fr/171.webp)


### Umuyobozi w'ijambobanga


Abakoresha benshi bareka ibikoresho vyabo bikabika amajambo banga yabo biciye ku mirongo nk’iyitwa Google Password Manager. Naho bibereye, ubwo bwoko bw'uburongozi buhurikiye hamwe ntibutanga ububiko bugenzurwa n'ukoresha, kandi bushira ahabona amakuru yawe y'ibanga iyo konti yawe ya Google ishobora guhungabanywa. Kugira ngo ushobore gucunga amajambo banga yawe mu buryo butekanye kandi bubereye, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo kuyakoresha.


**Ibindi**:



- [Umucungezi w'ibice](www.com/)


Bitwarden ni umwe mu bacungera ijambobanga ry’inkomoko yuguruye ry’inkomoko ryinshi cane. Ipfuka amakuru yawe yose yo mu karere, ikaguha amajambo y’ibanga akomeye ya generate, kandi itanga uguhuza hagati y’ibikoresho.


Ushobora gukoresha ama server ya Bitwarden, canke ukayikira nimba ushaka kugira ngo uyigenzure yose. Igikoresho caco ca Interface kiratomoye kandi kiragenda neza, kikaba gishobora gukorana neza na Android canke iOS.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9


- [KugumyaDX](www.gukomezaDX.com/)


KeePass ni umucungerezi w’ijambobanga ry’amateka ashingiye ku madosiye y’aho hantu yashizwemwo amakuru. Ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi, KeePassDX ni uburyo bwiza cane bwo gukoresha Android, bujanye n’amakuru yose ya KeePass. Ikora offline, ata gicu, bikaba ari umuti mwiza ku bashaka ko amakuru yabo aguma ari 100% yo mu karere.


![Image](assets/fr/172.webp)


Hariho kandi [KeePassium](https://keepassium.com/) ya iOS, porogaramu yinjijwe neza mu bidukikije vya Apple, ihuye n’uburyo bwa KeePass n’inkomoko yuguruye. Iyindi nzira ya iOS ku mukiriya wa KeePass ni Strongbox, ariko iyi porogarama imaze imyaka myinshi idafunguye.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246


- [Igihugu c'iporotoni](https://iporotoni.me/ibarabara)


Yatangujwe n’umugwi wa Proton (uzwi cane kubera Proton Mail na Proton Drive, n’ibindi), Proton Pass ihuriza hamwe ukworohereza gukoresha, gukingira amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera n’ibikorwa remezo vy’Ubusuwisi bifasha ubuzima bwite. Porogarama yo kuri telefone ngendanwa irasanzwe, iratuma wongerako amajambo atekanye, kandi irafasha guheza ubwawe. Ni uburyo bwiza cane ku bashaka umuti w’urufunguzo, ataco bitwararika ku bijanye n’uburongozi bw’ubuhinga.


![Image](assets/fr/173.webp)


### VPN


VPNs (*Virtual Private Network*) zigufasha gupfuka amakuru yawe yo kuri Internet maze ukayarungika biciye ku nzira y’ubuhuza iri kure. Ivyo bipfuka IP yawe Address, bikagukingira amahuzu yawe ku mbuga za bose (Wi-Fi y’ikibuga c’indege, ama café...) kandi bikakurinda uburyo bumwe bumwe bwo kugucungera.


Ariko rero, si VPN zose zaremwe zingana. Ibikorwa bikundwa nka NordVPN canke ExpressVPN bikora neza, ariko uburyo bwavyo buguma ari ubw’ubudandaji, n’akarorero gashingiye ku gukurikirana abakoresha kugira ngo ubudandaji bube bwiza. Bisaba kandi gukora konti kandi kenshi bikorakoranya amakuru menshi kuruta ayo bireka.


**Ibindi**:



- [VPN ya Mullvad](urubuga rwa Mullvad/)


Mullvad ni imwe mu VPN nziza cane mu bijanye no kurinda ubuzima bwite. Nta email canke ijambobanga bisaba: Konti yawe ihuye n’umubare woroshe w’imburakimazi. Ukwishura bishobora gukorwa mu bitcoins canke mu mafaranga. Ico gikoresho gikoreshwa kuri telefone ngendanwa ni open-source, coroshe gukoresha kandi gifise ububasha. Mullvad nta nkuru ibika, ntikurikirana abayikoresha, kandi ihora isohora igenzura ry’umutekano ryigenga.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8


- [IVPN](imbuga ngurukanabumenyi/)


IVPN ni ubundi buryo bwiza cane bwibanda ku buzima bwite. Itanga Interface igendagenda yoroshe kandi ikora neza, nta nkuru ishobora gukusanywa, kandi iremesha kwiyandikisha ata wuzi. Ushobora kandi kwishura mu ma bitcoins. Iyi porogaramu irimwo uruhome rw’umuriro ruzibira uruja n’uruza rwose rutari rwa VPN, rushobora kuba ngirakamaro cane kuri telefone ngendanwa. Abaguzi ni abafunguye.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68


- [Iporotoni VPN](imbuga ngurukanabumenyi/)


Iyi VPN yateguwe n’umugwi wa Proton, itanga umugambi w’ubuntu, ata kwamamaza. Proton VPN ikorera mu Busuwisi, ikurikiza amategeko akomeye agenga ivy’ubuzima bwite, kandi itangaza igenzura ridasanzwe. Abaguzi bayo na bo nyene ni abafunguye.


![Image](assets/fr/174.webp)


### 2FA kwemeza


Ivyemezo vy’ibintu bibiri (2FA) ni Layer y’inyongera y’umutekano hejuru y’ijambobanga ryawe. Akenshi bishingiye kuri kode y’igihe kimwe ivuye mu masegonda 30 yose n’ikoreshwa ry’ivyemezo. Iyi kode ishingiye kw’ibanga risangiye hagati y’igikoresho cawe n’igikoresho co kuri Internet, hakurikijwe umurongo wa TOTP (*Ijambobanga ry’Igihe kimwe*) rishingiye ku gihe. Porogaramu izwi cane ni Google Authenticator, ariko ntabwo ari iyo gufungura kandi ituma wizigira ibidukikije vya Google.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ivyemezo vya Aegis](urubuga rwa getaegis/)


Aegis ni porogaramu y’inkomoko yuguruye yuzuye. Ipfuka urutonde rwawe rwa 2FA n’ijambobanga, itanga amakuru yoherezwa hanze (na yo nyene ipfutse), kandi ikagufasha gutoranya amakonti yawe hakurikijwe ububiko. Interface iratomoye, iragezweho kandi yoroshe gusubiramwo ku gikoresho gishasha, igihe cose ufise dosiye y’ububiko n’ijambobanga rijanye na yo.


![Image](assets/fr/175.webp)



- [Ukwemeza kw'injira](https://inyandiko.io/ukwemeza/)


Ente Auth ni umuti w’ubuhinga bwa none, ufunguye, ukoreshwa ku mbuga nyinshi ufise ububiko bushingiye ku mpera ku mpera. Iragufasha gukoranya amakode yawe ya 2FA mu buryo butekanye kuri telefone ngendanwa, kuri mudasobwa no ku rubuga. Ushobora kandi kuyikoresha utari mu nzira, ataco ukora mu gicu canke ngo ukore konti.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/ente-auth-1928e65a-3b43-40f3-9efd-457ee2d79bb9
Ente Auth itanga ibintu vyinshi vy’inyongera: Gutunganya hakurikijwe ibimenyetso, ibishushanyo vy’ibikorwa vyose, amajambo, ivyo ukunda, ubushakashatsi buhuriweko, gusangira kode y’umugwi itekanye.


![Image](assets/fr/176.webp)



- [Uburenganzira](www.uburenganzira.com/)


Authy itanga 2FA synchronization ku bikoresho vyinshi, bishobora kuba vyiza, ariko porogaramu ntabwo ari open-source kandi isaba inomero ya telefone kugira ngo umuntu yiyandikishe. Ariko rero, ku batangura, iratunganye kuruta Google Authenticator, cane cane kubera igikorwa cayo co gucungera amakuru mu gicu.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/authy-a76ab26b-71b0-473c-aa7c-c49153705eb7

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/proton-authenticator-047ca2eb-a922-4e0e-8f75-1b89d23951ae
Niba wifuza kumenya vyinshi ku bijanye n’abacungera ijambobanga, kwemeza 2FA na VPNs, ndagusavye gusoma ibice vyihariye mu nyigisho ya SCU-101:


https://planb.network/courses/99c46148-7080-4915-a7e0-9df0e145cd47

### Ikirere


Ibikoresho vya kera vy’ikirere nka AccuWeather canke Météo France akenshi bikusanya amakuru y’ibanga, harimwo n’aho uri nyaho, ingeso zo gukoresha rimwe na rimwe mbere n’ibimenyetso vy’ibikoresho, ku ntumbero z’ubudandaji canke zo kwamamaza. Izo serivisi kandi zishingiye ku ma API y’uburenganzira, zigabanya ububasha bwawe ku makuru yerekanwa canke arungikwa.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ikirere c'Igihugu] (Ikirere c'Igihugu)


Geometric Weather itanga ubuhanuzi burambuye n’ibikoresho bishobora guhindurwa, vyose ata kwamamaza canke gukusanya amakuru. Kode yayo ni iyo gufungura. Iryo koraniro rishigikira abatanga ibihe vyinshi.


![Image](assets/fr/177.webp)



- [Ivyiyumviro](ku rubuga rwa Github.com/Davidtakac/Ivyiyumviro)


Prognoza ni porogaramu y’ubuhinga buke cane ishika ku ciyumviro: Kwerekana ibihe vy’ubu n’ivyo bizoshika. Itanga ibikoresho vyinshi. Prognoza nta kwamamaza igira, nta n’uwukurikirana kandi nta ruhusha rudakenewe rusaba.


![Image](assets/fr/178.webp)



- [Ubuhanuzi](ku rubuga rwa github.com/martykan/ubuhanuzi)


Ikoreshwa ry'ikirere ryoroshe, rishingiye kuri OpenWeatherMap, ry'inkomoko yuguruye, rishobora guhindurwa, rifise ibikoresho.


![Image](assets/fr/179.webp)


Muri rusangi, ku bikorwa vy'ikirere, ni vyiza gutunganya n'amaboko ahantu ushaka kuruta gukoresha ubuhinga bwo kumenya aho uri.


### Gutangaza amajwi/amasanamu


Ivyuma bikundwa nka Spotify canke YouTube bitanga ubumenyi bw’abakoresha butagira umurongo, ariko bikaba bifise igiciro c’ugusenyuka gukomeye ku bijanye n’ubuzima bwite. Izo serivisi ziguma zikwegeranya amakuru yerekeye inyifato: Amateka yo kuraba canke kwumviriza, umwanya umaze, ivyo ukunda, igikoresho ukoresha. Aya makuru akenshi akoreshwa mu gutanga urutonde canke mu gutora abantu.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ikinyamakuru](https://ikinyamakuru.dev/)


LibreTube ni porogaramu ya Android ishobora kugufasha kuraba amasanamu ya YouTube ata Google ikukurikirana. Ivyo usaba vyose birungikwa biciye ku nzira y’ubuhinga bwa Piped, iyo na yo ikaba ituma umuntu adashobora kubona amasanamu. Interface yayo ni iya none, iranyaruka kandi nta kwamamaza igira. Porogaramu nta konti ya Google isaba, kandi iragufasha kwiyandikisha ku mihora canke gukora urutonde rw’indirimbo zo mu karere.


![Image](assets/fr/180.webp)



- [Umuyoboro mushasha](https://umuyoboro mushasha.net/)


NewPipe ni uwundi mukiriya wa YouTube. Iremereye, nta kwamamaza, nta n’umwe akurikirana kandi yose ifunguye, iragufasha kuraba, gukura canke kwumviriza amasanamu kuri YouTube (n’izindi nzira nka SoundCloud canke PeerTube) mu nyuma. Nta guhuza na Google bisabwa. NewPipe ikora yigenga rwose ku gikorwa ca YouTube, kandi ntibisaba igikorwa na kimwe ca Google kugira ngo ikore.



- [VLC Android](ku rubuga rwa Android)


Igikoresho gikundwa cane ca VLC kiraboneka no kuri Android. Ishigikira uburyo bwinshi bw’amajwi n’amasanamu, kandi iragufasha gukina amadosiye mu karere canke ku rubuga, vyose ata kwamamaza canke gukusanya amakuru. Ni umuti mwiza cane wo gucunga ububiko bwawe bwite bw’ibitabu vyinshi mu karere, ata guhuza n’igikorwa c’uwundi muntu.


![Image](assets/fr/181.webp)



- [Ikiyaga](https://ikiyaga.amajwi/):


Funkwhale ni urubuga rwigenga rwo gusangira no kwumviriza umuziki, n’abaguzi bahuye.


### klavye


Ivyuma bikoreshwa mu buryo bw’impwemu nka Gboard ya Google canke SwiftKey ya Microsoft biri hose kuri telefone ngendanwa. Ariko rero, biratera ingorane zikomeye z’ubuzima bwite: Inyuguti yose yanditswe irashobora kwandikwa, gusesangurwa canke gurungikwa ku bikoresho vyo kure. Naho ayo mashirahamwe yovuga ko atamenyekana, gukusanya amakuru birashoboka.


**Ibindi**:



- [Urubaho rwuguruye](ku rubuga: github.com/dslul/urubaho rwuguruye)


OpenBoard ni klavye ya Android ifise inkomoko yuguruye, ishingiye kuri klavye ya AOSP (*Umugambi wa Android yuguruye*). Nta bihimba vy’umunyagihugu canke abakurikirana, kandi ntiyigera ivugana n’abakozi bo kure. Gukosora, kwandika imbere y’igihe n’inkoranyamagambo y’umuntu ku giti ciwe bikora mu karere gusa.



- [Ikigo c'amashurwe](https://ikigo c'amashurwe.org/)


FlorisBoard itanga uburyo bugezweho, bufise ibice. Kandi ni open-source, ihuriza hamwe ibikorwa biteye imbere nk’ugushiramwo ibimenyetso, ugushiraho urufunguzo rw’umuntu ku giti ciwe n’ugucungera indimi nyinshi. Ivyo gukora amakuru vyose bikorwa mu karere, ata guhuza n’ama server yo hanze. FlorisBoard iracariko irategurwa, ariko irasanzwe ikoreshwa neza ku musi ku musi ku bashaka klavye ikomeye ataco batakaje ku buzima bwite bwabo.


![Image](assets/fr/182.webp)


### Igiharuro


Porogaramu ya Google Calculator, naho ikora neza, iracari igicuruzwa ca Google kandi izana n’ingorane zisanzwe zijanye n’ugukusanya amakuru no kwizigira ibidukikije bihurikiye hamwe.


**Ibindi**:



- [Igiharuro gifunguye](github.com/Umwami w'umwijima78/Igiharuro gifunguye)


OpenCalc ni igiharuro cihuta kandi coroshe gukoresha, gihuye neza n’ivyo umuntu akeneye buri musi. Nta makuru yegeranya kandi ikora ata n’imwe ikora, ata kwamamaza canke kwizigira igikorwa ico ari co cose co hanze.


![Image](assets/fr/183.webp)


### Iduka ry'ibisabwa


Iduka rya Google Play ni ryo ry’imbere ry’ibikoresho ku matelefone menshi y’ubuhinga bwa Android. Ariko rero, irafatanye cane n’ibikorwa vya Google kandi ijana n’ugukusanya amakuru mu buryo butunganye, mbere no mu gihe c’ugushaka canke guhindura ibintu vyoroshe.


**Ibindi**:



- [F-Cold](ubutumwa bushasha/)


F-Droid ni urutonde rw’ibikoresho vy’inkomoko yuguruye gusa. Porogaramu zose ziriho zirashobora gusuzumwa no gukurwa ku buntu, ata kwamamaza, gukurikirana canke kwizigira ibikorwa vya Google. Porogarama ya F-Droid ubwayo nta konti y’ukoresha isaba.


![Image](assets/fr/184.webp)



- [Iduka rya Aurora](ku rubuga rwa Auroraos/)


Iduka rya Aurora rigufasha gushika ku rutonde rw'iduka rya Google Play ata wuzi, ata konti ya Google. Ni umukiriya w'ubuntu akorana n'abakozi ba Google, mu gihe yihisha akaranga kawe biciye kuri konti rusangi. Ni umuti w’agaciro wo kubandanya ukoresha ibintu bimwe bimwe bikenewe: Ibikoresho, mu gihe wirinda Google Play telemetry.


### Amakuru


Porogaramu y’amakuru ya Google, naho ikora kandi igenewe umuntu, yizigiye gusuzuma neza ivyo ukunda, amateka yo gusura n’ingeso zo gusoma kugira ngo utunganye impanuro zayo. Ivyo birimwo kwegeranya amakuru menshi yerekeye umuntu, akenshi akoreshwa mu kwamamaza.


**Ibindi**:



- [Amakuru](ku rubuga rwa github.com/bubelov/amakuru)


Porogarama ya *News*, yateguwe na Bubelov, itanga uburyo butandukanye cane. Ni umusomyi wa RSS mutoyi, yagenewe kurondera amakuru ata bakurikirana, kwamamaza canke ubuhinga bwo gutanga impanuro butaboneka. Ushobora guhitamwo n’amaboko amasoko yawe (itangazamakuru, ama blogs, podcasts, ibinyamakuru vyigenga, n’ibindi), ugatanga icemezo c’uko ushobora gusoma ataco ukora, ataco ukora. Ivyo bikoresho ntibiteye akaga, amakuru arahindurwa ubwayo, kandi nta makuru ashikirizwa abandi.


### Guhanahana amakuru


Google Contacts, nk'ibindi bikoresho vyinshi bikoreshwa kuri Android, bihuza ibitabu vyawe vya Address n'ibikoresho vya Google. Ivyo bisigura ko amakuru yose y’abantu ushobora guhamagara (amazina, inomero, ubutumwa bwo kuri interineti, rimwe na rimwe amaderesi y’iposita canke amafoto) abikwa kuri Internet kandi afitaniye isano na konti yawe. Ukwo gushiramwo ibintu vyose bifasha gukora ububiko n’uguhuza, ariko bivyura ibibazo bikomeye vy’ubuzima bwite.


**Ibindi**:



- [Uguhuze](https://github.com/wewe-amaporogarama/Uguhuze)


Connect You ni uburyo busanzwe, butagiramwo ibintu vyinshi, bugenewe abashaka gucunga abo bahuriyeko mu karere, ata gukusanya amakuru canke gukorana n’igicu c’uwundi muntu ku nguvu. Itanga Interface yoroshe, ituma vyoroha gutoranya, kurondera no guhindura ivyo winjije, kandi ishobora gukorana n’ibikorwa vya CalDAV nimba uriko ukoresha umukozi w’ivy’uguhamagara (biciye muri Nextcloud, nk’akarorero).


### Ubuyobozi bw'amafoto


Amafoto ya Google ni meza cane mu kubika amashusho mu gicu, kuyatunganya canke kuyaronka biciye mu kumenya mu maso. Ariko ukwo kworoha guhisha uburyo amakuru yawe akoreshwa mu buryo bubereye: Ishusho yose irasesangurwa, igashirwa mu rutonde kandi igahuzwa n’ayandi makuru yawe ya Google. Amafoto yawe arashobora kuba isoko y’inyongera y’amakuru, akoreshwa mu vy’ubudandaji.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ibarabara ryoroshe](https://github.com/Ibikoresho vyoroshe/Ibarabara ryoroshe)


Simple Gallery ni porogaramu y’inkomoko yuguruye ikora yose ata murongo. Ni kimwe mu bigize *Ibikoresho vyoroshe vyo kuri telefone ngendanwa*. Iragufasha gucunga, gutoranya, kuraba no guhindura amashusho yawe ata makuru ava ku gikoresho cawe. Irafise kandi retouching, gukingira ijambobanga n’igitereko c’imyanda co gusubiramwo ibintu vyasimbujwe. Nta gukurikirana, nta guhuza ku nguvu: Amafoto yawe agumana nawe.



- [Aves](urubuga rwa github.com/umuhinguzi w'amaguru)


Aves ni ubundi buryo bufise Interface y'ubu. Itanga uburyo bwo kugendagenda neza muri album n’imitunganirize iteye imbere (ibimenyetso, amayunguruzo, gutoranya, n’ibindi). Nta nzira ya Internet isaba kugira ngo ikore, kandi nta makuru y’abayikoresha yegeranya.


![Image](assets/fr/185.webp)



- [Amafoto y'i Ente](ku rubuga rwa Ente.io/)


Ente Photos ni serivisi y’inkomoko yuguruye (abaguzi + abakozi) yo gucungera amafoto yihuta n’ugushiramwo amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera. Amashusho yawe arashirwa ku gikoresho imbere y’uko yoherezwa, kugira ngo mbere n’abakozi ba Ente badashobora kuyaronka. Ente kandi itanga verisiyo yikorera ku bakoresha bateye imbere.


![Image](assets/fr/186.webp)



- [Amafoto ya Stingle](https://Stingle.org/)


Stingle ni ikibanza co gushiramwo amafoto n’ivyo gufata amafoto, bifatanijwe n’igikorwa co gucungera amafoto. Cokimwe na Ente, amafoto arakingirwa n’ugushiramwo amakuru kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera. Ushobora gukoresha igikorwa cabo co mu gicu (1 GB ku buntu) canke wiyakira server ya Stingle kugira ngo uyigenzure vyose. Interface ni yoroshe, nta n’amatangazo canke abayikurikirana.


![Image](assets/fr/187.webp)


### Umusomyi wa PDF


**Ibindi**:


Adobe Acrobat Reader, ikoreshwa cane mu gusoma canke gutanga ibisobanuro ku nyandiko za PDF, izana n’ibikorwa vyinshi vyo kuri internet bishobora gushikiriza amakuru yawe: Telemetry ikora, gukorana n’ibicu no kwegeranya amakuru ku madosiye yawe canke ingeso zo gusoma.



- [Umurorerezi wa MuPDF](ubutumwa bw'ibara ry'umubiri/amapaki/com.artifex.umurorerezi w'ibintu.


MuPDF Viewer ni igikoresho co gusoma PDF gifise umuco mwinshi cane, gica vuba kandi gifise inkomoko yuguruye. Ifata ubutunzi buke cane. Naho idatanga ibintu vy’agaciro nk’ugushiramwo ibisobanuro canke gusinya, ikora akazi kayo neza cane: Kwerekana inyandiko zawe, ata gutahura.



- [Umusomyi wa PDF wa MJ] (umusomyi wa Pdf wa MJ)


MJ PDF Reader ni porogaramu yoroshe, ifunguye, ishobora kugufasha gusoma amadosiye ya PDF ata kwamamaza canke gufatanya na konti yo kuri Internet.


### Telefone


Porogarama ya Google yitwa Phone, ishirwa ku matelefone menshi y’ubuhinga bwa Android, ikora neza ariko ikorakoranya amakuru menshi y’ikoreshwa.


**Ibindi**:



- [Koler](ku rubuga rwa Github.com/Chooloo/koler)


Koler ni porogaramu y’amatelefone yuguruye yakozwe kugira ngo ibe nziza, yoroshe gukoresha kandi idashobora gukingira ubuzima bwite. Itanga Interface igenda neza kandi ishobora gukoreshwa neza mu gucunga amatelefone yawe, ata bakurikirana canke gusesangura amakuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ariko rero, ubu ntabwo harimwo ugucungera amatelefone canke gufatanya n’ibikorwa vy’abandi.


![Image](assets/fr/188.webp)


### Ubuhinduzi


Google Translate ni co kigereranyo mu guhindura bwite, ariko gukoresha kwayo mu buryo butegekanijwe birimwo kohereza ibibazo vyawe vyose kuri Google, n’ugukurikirana kwubatswemwo n’ugukusanya amakuru y’agaciro (Ivyanditswe vyahinduwe, amateka, n’ibindi).


**Ibindi**:



- [Guhindurawewe](https://github.com/wewe-amaporogarama/guhindurewewe)


TranslateYou ni porogaramu y’ubuhinduzi yuguruye yubaha ubuzima bwite bw’abayikoresha. Ikora nka Interface ku bikoresho bitandukanye vy’ubuhinduzi (LibreTranslate, LingvaTranslate, Mozhi, DeepL, n’ibindi), kandi ikagufasha guhitamwo igikorwa kidakoresha nabi amakuru yawe.


Nta kwamamaza, nta gukurikirana, na Interface yoroshe gukoresha bituma TranslateYou iba ubundi buryo bwiza bwo guhindura Google.


![Image](assets/fr/189.webp)


### Igikoresho co gupima igicuruzwa


Yuka ikoreshwa cane mu gupima ibifungurwa n’ibintu vyo kwisiga no gusuzuma uburyo bwavyo, ariko ishingiye ku citegererezo kitaboneka, gifise ingingo ngenderwako ziteye amakenga, urutonde rw’amakuru rw’igice c’umuntu n’ikoreshwa ritagira inkomoko yuguruye. Ikindi, igikorwa caco gisaba gufatanya na server iri hagati, n’ubushobozi bwo gukusanya amakuru y’ikoreshwa.


**Ibindi**:



- [Ivy'IvyokuryaVyuguruye](https://isi.ivy'IvyokuryaVyuguruye.org/ivy'Ivyokurya-vyuguruye-app-ya-telefone)


OpenFoodFacts ni uburyo buboneka cane kandi bushobora gukingira ubuzima bwite. Uyu mugambi w’ubufatanye w’inkomoko yuguruye utanga urutonde rw’amakuru kw’isi yose, rugaburirwa n’intererano z’abakoresha. Amakuru yerekeye ingaburo, ibirungo n’ibimenyetso bishobora gushikirizwa mu buryo buboneka, ata gukusanya amakuru atari yo.


Iryo koraniro ryo kuri telefone ngendanwa rituma ushobora gucapura amakode y’ibiharuro, ugaca ubona amakuru yerekeye ibintu, kandi nawe ubwawe ugatanga umusanzu ku rutonde rw’amakuru. Ni ubuntu gukoresha, ata kwamamaza canke abakurikirana.


### Gusangira hafi


Ibikorwa nk’ivyo gusangira vyihuse (Android) canke AirDrop (iOS/macOS) bigufasha kohereza amadosiye hagati y’ibikoresho biri hafi biciye ku Bluetooth no kuri Wi-Fi itaziguye, ata n’imwe ikoresha Internet. Birakora, ariko bishingiye ku mirongo yugaye, rimwe na rimwe ihuye n’amakonti ya Google, Samsung canke Apple.


Gusangira vyihuse ubu ni co gisanzwe kuri Android. Iyi porogaramu, yashizweho ubwa mbere na Samsung, yashizwe hamwe mu mwaka w’2024 na Nearby Share na Google, bituma haba porogaramu imwe yo gusangira amadosiye kuri Android.


**Ibindi**:



- [Igishushanyo](https://github.com/Igishushanyo/igishushanyo)


Snapdrop ni uburyo bwo gukoresha ku buntu, bufunguye, butasaba ko umuntu ashiramwo. Bigufasha gusangira amadosiye hagati y’ibikoresho bihuye n’urubuga rumwe, biciye ku mucukumbuzi w’urubuga. Ukwimurira ni direct (peer-to-peer) kandi amakuru ntashobora guca kuri server iri kure.


Iyindi nzira iryoshe cane ni [PairDrop] (Fork ya Snapdrop), itanga ibintu bikeyi vy’inyongera.



- [Umuvugizi w'intambara](ku rubuga rwa github.com/linuxmint/umuvugizi w'intambara)


Warpinator, yakozwe na Linux Mint, ituma vyoroha gutanga amadosiye hagati y’ibikoresho bifatanye n’urubuga rumwe rwa Wi-Fi. Ikorana n'abandi, ata gicu canke server y'uwundi muntu, ifise Interface yoroshe. Hariho ivyuho vya Android, bituma amadosiye ashobora guhererekanwa hagati ya telefone na mudasobwa.



- [Ivyoherezwa mu karere](https://ivyoherezwa mu karere.org/)


LocalSend ni ubundi buryo bwo ku buntu, bufise ubushobozi bwose bufise Interface. Iyi porogarama yose ikoreshwa n’inkomoko yuguruye, ishobora gutuma amadosiye ashobora guhererekanwa hagati y’ibikoresho bifatanye n’urubuga rumwe rwo mu karere. Nta serveri zo hagati zikoreshwa, kugira ngo amakuru yawe ntazokwigera ava ku rubuga rwawe rwo muhira.


![Image](assets/fr/190.webp)


### Ibitabo


Amaporogarama nka Goodreads, naho akoreshwa cane, aravyura ibibazo bikomeye vy’ubuzima bwite. Iyi nzira ni iya Amazon, ikoranya amakuru menshi cane ku vyo usoma, ivyo ukunda, ivyo ubona n’ivyo usubiramwo. Ikindi, Interface yizigira cane gukurikirana abakoresha no gusuzuma inyifato yabo ku ntumbero z’ubudandaji.


**Ibindi**:



- [Gufungura](gufungura gusoma)


Openreads ni uburyo bufunguye bwo gukurikirana ibisomwa bifise ubuzima bwite. Iyi porogaramu iragufasha gukora ububiko bw’ibitabu bwawe bwite, gukurikirana ingene usoma, gupima no gutanga ibitekerezo ku bitabu, no kuronka impanuro zishingiye ku ngingo zawe bwite, ata gusuzuma canke gukurikirana hamwe. Amakuru yose aguma ku gikoresho cawe canke akoranywa biciye ku bikorwa vy’ukwikorera.


### Isaha, inkengeri n'ibihe


**Ibindi**:



- [Igihe](ku rubuga rwa github.com/vicolo-dev/igihe)


Iboneka kuri F-Droid kandi ikaba ifunguye yose, Chrono itanga Interface y’ubuhinga bwa none, idafise ibibazo, ata kwamamaza canke gukusanya amakuru. Bigufasha guhingura inkengeri zishobora guhindurwa: Gusubiramwo hakurikijwe imisi canke amatariki yihariye, guhitamwo ijwi, uburemere butera imbere, guhungabana, canke mbere ibikorwa vyo gukora kugira ngo inkengeri izimye (Gutorera umuti igiharuro, gusubira gusoma icanditswe, n’ibindi).


Iryo koraniro kandi rifise igiharuro c’igihe n’igiharuro c’igihe, n’ugufata amajwi y’ibihe, imibare, kugereranya igihe n’ugucungera ibiharuro vyinshi. Ushobora gutunganya amasaha menshi, ugahindura insanganyamatsiko (amabara, imiterere, amashusho), mbere ugatunganya inkengeri zawe n’ibiharuro vyawe bifise ibimenyetso.


Kugira ngo ushobore gutohoza neza iyo nkuru, ndagusavye gusura urubuga [*Ibanga ry’Ibanga*](https://awesome-privacy.xyz/), rufise urutonde rw’ibintu vyiza kuruta ibindi vyose bishobora gukoreshwa mu gukingira ubuzima bwite kuruta porogarama ukoresha ku musi ku musi.

___


⚠️ ***Iciyumviro**: Naho uburyo bundi buvugwa muri iki gice ahanini ari ubw’ubuhinga bufunguye kandi bushingiye ku bwiherero, ntibutagira aho bugarukira canke ingorane. Bimwe bishobora guhagarika gutunganirizwa, bikaba bifise utunenge tutavuzwe, bikaba ari ivy’umuntu canke mbere, bishobora kuba ari ibintu bibi. Bimwebimwe vyoshobora kandi kuba bitemewe n’amategeko mu karere iwanyu. Nanditse iki kigabane muri Ruheshi 2025, ariko ivy’ivyo bisabwa bishobora kuba vyahindutse kuva ico gihe.*


Ikindi kandi, jewe ubwanje sinasuzumye kode y’ibikoresho vyose vyavuzwe, kandi impanuro zanje ntizikwiye na gato gufatwa nk’ivyemezo vy’ukuri. Ni ngombwa rero ko umuntu wese akora ubushakashatsi bwiwe bwite imbere yo gukoresha izo porogarama.


___


# Gukingira urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere


<partId>23e49e48-34c9-435c-a36f-1c86b0254275</partId>


## Gutahura neza urubuga rwawe rwo muhira


<chapterId>8a7577e0-4a27-4331-a6d9-7a4c838fa720</chapterId>


Umutekano wa digitale akenshi utangura n’ukumenya neza urubuga rwo muhira. Igikoresho cawe co muhira ni co kibanza ca mbere Internet yinjiramwo mu bidukikije vyawe bwite, kandi ni co gitera ingorane nyinshi umutekano wawe n’ubuzima bwite bwawe.


Gutahura ingene urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere rukora, ingene amakuru yawe agenda n’ibikoresho bijejwe gucunga ayo makuru ni ikintu gihambaye cane ku busegaba bwawe bwa digitale.


Muri iki gice, tuzokwihweza buhoro buhoro ivyiyumviro nyamukuru vy’ugukorana n’abandi mu rugo, kuva ku nsobanuro y’ico Internet ari co gushika ku bintu vy’ukuri nk’ugutanga amaderesi IP yo mu karere n’uruhara rwa router. Intumbero ni ugusubira ku vyiyumviro vy’ishimikiro bihambaye kugira ngo umuntu atahure neza ikigabane gikurikira, kizovuga ku bintu vyinshi bikora.


### Internet


#### Amateka make y'Internet


Amateka ya Internet asubira mu mpera z’imyaka ya 1960, mu gihe c’ubushakashatsi bwa siyansi n’ubw’igisirikare. Umugambi wa mbere, witwa "ARPANET", watangujwe n'ishirahamwe ry'Abanyamerika ARPA (ubu ryitwa DARPA) kugira ngo bihuze ibibanza vyinshi vy'ubushakashatsi, bishobore gusangira ibikoresho.


![Image](assets/fr/191.webp)


Intumbero yari kandi iyo guhingura uruja n’uruza rushobora gukomera, rushobora kubandanya rukora naho igice c’imirongo yarwo coba carasambutse (ivyo vyari bikenewe hagati mu ntambara ya Cold). ARPANET ni yo yatumye habaho uguhanahana amakuru kwa mbere hagati ya mudasobwa ziri kure mu 1969.


![Image](assets/fr/192.webp)


Mu myaka mirongo iheze, uwo mugambi waragutse, cane cane mu gutuma amategeko ya TCP/IP ashirwa ku rugero rumwe mu 1983, ivyo bikaba vyacitse umushinge w’ubuhinga rusangi wa Internet yose. Mu myaka ya 1990, ukuza kwa *World Wide Web*, twavuganye mu kigabane c’imbere, kwatumye abantu bose bashobora gukoresha Internet mu kworohereza abantu kuronka inyandiko biciye ku bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Iryo hinduka rikomeye ryahinduye Internet iba igikoresho co guhanahana amakuru no gutanga amakuru ku bantu bose.


#### Internet ni iki?


Internet, bisobanura "urubuga rufatanye", ni ibikorwa remezo vyo kw'isi yose bishoboza amamiliyaridi y'ibikoresho guhanahana amakuru. Si igikorwa kimwe, canke ahantu kanaka, ahubwo ni ihuriro ry’imirongo ya mudasobwa ya bose n’iy’abikorera ku giti cabo, ihuye ku rugero rw’imibumbe. Buri mukinyi (umuntu ku giti ciwe, ishirahamwe, ubutegetsi bwa Leta, n’ibindi) arashobora gufatanya urubuga rwiwe n’isi yose, igihe gusa yubahiriza amategeko amwamwe y’ubuhinga agezweho atuma ibikoresho bishobora gutahurana.


Ibikorwa remezo vya Internet bishingiye ahanini ku masezerano abiri:



- IP** (*Iporotokole ya Internet*) Imenyesha igikoresho cose gihuye kandi irungika amapakete y’amakuru.
- TCP** (*Protocole de contrôle de la transmission*) Icapura uruja n’uruza, igenzura amakosa maze igasubiza ibice mu rutonde.


→ Ku bikorwa vy’igihe nyaco aho ukwizigirwa ataco bimaze kuruta guhagarara (VoIP, DNS, streaming, n’ibindi), akenshi hakoreshwa uwundi murongo wo gutwara abantu aho gukoresha TCP: UDP (*User Datagram Protocol*).


Ivyo bipimo bibiri birakorana kugira ngo ubutumwa bwoherezwa buva ahantu hamwe buja ahandi bushike bushitse kandi bujanye n’urutonde rwiza.


Mu majambo nyayo, iyo usuye urubuga, nk’akarorero mu kwandika Address mu mucukumbuzi wawe, ibikorwa vyinshi biratangura inyuma. Ubwa mbere, mudasobwa yawe canke telefone yawe ngendanwa itegerezwa guhindura Address isomwa (nk’iyitwa `planb.network`) ikayigira IP Address, ukoresheje igikorwa citwa DNS (*Sisteme y’izina ry’itongo*). Iyo IP Address ya server y’urubuga imaze kuronswa, ayo makuru arashobora kwoherezwa aho aja.


Ivyo bimenyetso rero bica bikurikira inzira igoye. Ubwa mbere, ica muri router yawe yo mu nzu na modem, imbere y’uko ishika ku bikorwa remezo vya ISP yawe. Ivuye ng’aho, irashobora kujabuka imirongo myinshi iri hagati (rimwe na rimwe intsinga zica mu kiyaga, ama routeur y’inzira, ama points ya Internet Exchange, n’ibindi) imbere y’uko ishika aho ija: Server y’urubuga wipfuza gusura. Ivyo na vyo nyene birungika amakuru (ibirimwo ku rubuga) mu buryo bunyuranye.


![Image](assets/fr/193.webp)


Internet rero irashobora gusobanurwamwo mu ncamake nk’urubuga runini cane rwigenga, rushingiye ku mategeko rusangi, aho igikoresho cose gishobora kuvugana n’ikindi, aho coba kiri hose kw’isi. Ariko naho ukwo gufungura gutuma habaho uguhanahana amakuru ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi, bisaba kandi ko ufata ingingo yo kwiyubara: Igikorwa cose ukora kuri Internet gica mu bikorwa remezo udashobora kugenzura, kandi ibanga ry’uguhanahana amakuru yawe rivana n’ingene utunganya ivyo bikoresho no kubikoresha.


### Uruhara rwa modem na router


Mu mihana myinshi yo muri iki gihe, umuntu ashobora gukoresha Internet biciye ku gikoresho co hagati gikora nka modem be n’ivyo gukoresha Internet. Izina ry'iki gikoresho riratandukanye ku gihugu ku kindi (mu Bufaransa, citwa "Internet Box"). Ico gikoresho gikora vyinshi gitangwa na ISP ni co kiguhuza n’ibindi bikoresho vyo kuri Internet.


→ *ISP = Uwutanga amakuru kuri Internet.*


Iki gikoresho gihuza ibikorwa 2 nyamukuru:



- Uruhara rwa modem**


Modem (mu ncamake "*modulator-demodulator*") ni co gice gihuza urubuga rwawe rwa ISP n'inzu yawe. Ihindura ibimenyetso vy’umuyagankuba canke vy’amaso vyakiriwe (biciye mu nzira y’amatara, umugozi w’amaso, ADSL canke urubuga rwa telefone ngendanwa) bikagira ibimenyetso vy’ubuhinga bwa none bishobora gutahurwa n’ibikoresho vyawe. Ku rundi ruhande, ihindura amakuru ava mu bikoresho vyawe mu buryo bushobora gutangazwa ku bikorwa remezo vy’uwubikoresha. Iyo ntambwe ni ngirakamaro nimba urubuga rwawe rwo muhira ruzovugana na Internet.



- Uruhara rwa router**


Router ni umutima w’urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere. Itanga uruja n’uruza rwa Internet ku bikoresho vyawe vyose: Mudasobwa, amatelefone ngendanwa, ibintu bihuye, amacapiro, n’ibindi.Iha kimwe cose muri vyo IP yo mu karere Address (Itandukanye n’IP yawe ya bose iboneka kuri Internet). Ico gikoresho gica gitunganya amakuru yinjira n’asohoka, kugira ngo amakuru ashike ku gikoresho kibereye. Ishobora kandi gushiramwo uruhome rw’umuriro, gucungera amapakete y’urubuga canke gucunga amategeko yo gurungika ivyuho. NAT ipfuka urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere amaso ya Internet, ikoresheje IP imwe ya bose Address kugira ngo iserukire ibikoresho vyawe vyose. Router yonyene ni yo izi igikoresho co mu karere catanguje igisabwa.


Mu bihugu bimwebimwe, ivyo bikorwa bibiri rimwe na rimwe biragabanywa hagati y’ibikoresho bibiri bitandukanye: Modem na router.


Mu bikorwa, routeur ya modem y’ubu akenshi irimwo ibindi bikorwa vy’inyongera: Igikoresho co gukoresha Wi-Fi, igikoresho co guhindura Ethernet, igikoresho co gukoresha Interface, rimwe na rimwe mbere n’igikoresho co gukoresha amadosiye n’ibindi.


Gutahura uruhara rwa router-modem ni ikintu nyamukuru co gukingira urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere. Mu buryo bumwe, ico gikoresho ni co gikora urubibi hagati y’isi yo hanze (Internet) n’ibidukikije vyawe vy’ibanga vy’ubuhinga bwa none. Gutunganya nabi, amajambo banga agoyagoya canke porogaramu zitagikoreshwa bishobora guhindura iri rembo ngo ribe umwobo ufunguye. Ku rundi ruhande, modem-router itunganijwe neza iba igihome co gukingira abayitera.


Mu kigabane gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene twotuma iyo ntunganyo igenda neza, tukamenya utunenge dusanzwe dufise, maze tugasubira kugenzura iyo ntunganyo.


### Urubuga rw'aho hantu (LAN)


Igikoresho co mu karere, canke "LAN" (*Igikoresho co mu karere*), ni amahuriro yose y'ubuhinga bwa none ari mu nzu yawe. Harimwo ibikoresho vyose bifatanye na router yawe: Mudasobwa, amatelefone ngendanwa, amatablette, amacapiro, n’ibindi.


Mu buryo butandukanye na Internet, iyo na yo ikaba ari urubuga rwo kw’isi yose, rw’abantu bose, urubuga rwo mu karere ni ikibanza c’ibanga, igice kimwe kiri ukwaco, gigenewe gutuma ibikoresho bishobora kuvugana, ata guhanahana kwavyo kuva mu nzu yawe. Nk’akarorero, iyo wohereje dosiye kuri orodinateri yawe ku gicapo gifatanye na Wi-Fi, canke ugacungera urumuri rufatanye biciye ku telefone yawe, ivyo bimenyetso bibera aho hantu gusa, ataco biciye kuri server iri kure.


![Image](assets/fr/194.webp)


Ivyo bishingiye ku buhinga n’amategeko agezweho, ahambaye cane muri yo ni amategeko ya IP. Igikoresho cose kiri ku rubuga rwawe rwo mu karere gihabwa IP yo mu karere Address (kenshi mu buryo `192.168.x.x`), ikoreshwa mu kugimenya mu buryo budasanzwe muri urwo rubuga. Iyi Address ntiboneka kuri Internet. IP yawe ya bose Address, isangiwe n’ibikoresho vyose biciye kuri modem, ni yo yonyene igaragara hanze y’inzu yawe.


Ariko ivyo bisa n’uko witandukanije n’abandi ntibikwiye kuguha inyiyumvo y’ikinyoma y’uko ufise umutekano. Urubuga rw’aho hantu rwatunganijwe nabi rushobora kuba irembo ry’ibitero, cane cane mu bihe bikurikira:



- Niba ibikorwa vyuguruye (nk’ugusangira amadosiye canke imirongo y’uburongozi) bishobora gushikwako kuri Internet .
- Niba Wi-Fi idatekanye (ijambobanga rigoyagoya canke uburyo bwo gupfuka amakuru butagikoreshwa)
- Nimba ibintu bimwebimwe bihuye bivugana n’isi yo hanze mu nyandiko zitomoye canke bikasiga ivyuho vyuguruye


Ni ngombwa rero gutahura ingene urubuga rwawe rugenda imbere, no kugenzura ibikoresho bishobora gukorana, hagati yavyo canke n’isi yo hanze.


### Wi-Fi


Wi-Fi (mu ncamake "*Wireless Fidelity*") ni ubuhinga bwo guhanahana amakuru ata nsinga bushobora gutuma uhuza ibikoresho vyawe n'urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere, ata n'umugozi ukeneye. Ubu buhinga bushingiye ku gutanga amakuru biciye ku mirongo ya radiyo, muri rusangi mu mirongo y’incuro 2,4 GHz na 5 GHz (canke mbere 6 GHz ku nzira za Wi-Fi 6E na Wi-Fi 7).


Ariko ukwo kworoha gukoresha biraza n’ingaruka zavyo. Mu buryo butandukanye n’ivyuma bikoreshwa n’amashanyarazi (nk’ivyo bita Ethernet), ibimenyetso vya Wi-Fi bica mu bihome kandi bishobora gutorwa biri ku metero amajana n’amajana. Ivyo bisigura ko abantu bari hanze y’inzu yawe (mu nzira, mu nyubakwa iri hafi, mbere n’abavuye mu modoka ihagaze hafi) bashobora kugerageza kumenya urubuga rwawe maze bakarufatanya na rwo iyo rudakingiwe neza.


![Image](assets/fr/195.webp)


Uwutera afise uburenganzira bwo gukoresha urubuga rwawe rwa Wi-Fi yoshobora rero:



- Gufata amakuru atashizwemwo amakuru arenga ku rubuga (nk'ibisabwa vya DNS canke uruja n'uruza rwa HTTP)
- Kugera kuri dosiye zawe canke ibikoresho vyawe nimba bitarinzwe neza
- Injiza ibintu bibi muri mucukumbuzi yawe
- Koresha uruja n’uruza rwawe rwa Internet ataco uzi, canke mbere ukore ibitero vyo kuri Internet ukoresheje IP yawe ya bose Address .


Kugira ngo wirinde ivyo bintu bitera ubwoba, urakeneye gukingira urubuga rwawe rwa Wi-Fi. Tuzorabira ingene ivyo twobikora mu bigabane bikeyi bikurikira.


### Aderesi za IP zo mu karere


Iyo uhuje igikoresho n'urubuga rwawe rwo muhira, kironka IP yo mu karere Address. Iyi Address igizwe n’imibare ine itandukanijwe n’utudomo (nk’akarorero `192.168.1.14`). Ikoreshwa mu kumenya mu buryo budasanzwe igikoresho cose kiri mu rubuga rwawe rwo mu karere. Ni kubera iyo Address ko router yawe imenya igikoresho co koherezako amakuru (nk’akarorero, urubuga canke videwo wasavye).


Ni vyiza gutahura ko izo IP zo mu karere zitaboneka kuri Internet. Biri mu migwi yabitswe, isobanurwa n’ingingo mfatirwako mpuzamakungu, idashobora gukoreshwa ku rubuga rwa bose. Ivyiyumviro bitatu bikunze gukoreshwa cane mu karere ka IP Address ni:



- `192.168.0.0` kugeza `192.168.255.255` (muri rusangi ku bakoresha b'ibanga)
- `10.0.0.0` kugeza kuri `10.255.255.255` (muri rusangi ku masosiyete)
- '172.16.0.0` kugeza '172.31.255.255'


Ico gikoresho nyene rero gishobora kugira IP Address nka `192.168.1.42` muhira, mu gihe uwundi mukozi wo mu kindi gihugu azogira ikindi gikoresho gifise iyo IP Address ku rubuga rwiwe bwite rwo mu karere, ata n’umwe yigeze agira amakimbirane, kuko ayo maderesi ntava ku rubuga rwo muhira. Ni router itanga uruja n'uruza hagati y'urubuga rwawe rwo muhira n'urubuga rwa bose, igahindura izo aderesi biciye ku buryo bwitwa "NAT" (*Ubuhinduzi bw'urubuga Address*).


Aderesi za IP zo mu karere muri rusangi zitangwa mu buryo buhinduka, hakoreshejwe DHCP (*Iporotokole y’Itunganywa ry’Umushitsi*). Iyo uhuje igikoresho gishasha n’urubuga, kirungika ubusabe bwa DHCP bwa Address, maze router ikagiha Address y’ubuntu iriho mu rugero rwategekanijwe. Iyi Address ishobora guhinduka uko igihe kigenda kirarenga.


Ariko rero, birashoboka gutunganya amaderesi IP adahinduka y’ibikoresho bimwebimwe. Ivyo bisigura kubika Address yihariye ku gikoresho kinaka, ku buryo budahera. Ivyo ni ngirakamaro mu bihe bitari bike, nk’akarorero:



- Kugira ngo ushobore gushika ku server y'umuntu ku giti ciwe canke NAS ukoresheje ikindi gikoresho
- Kugira ngo ucape kure ku gicapo c’urubuga ataco ukeneye kurondera Address yayo
- Kugira ngo ureme amategeko yo kuyungurura canke yoherezwa imbere muri router yawe


### Ivyambu vy'urubuga


Kugira ngo utahure ingene urubuga rwo mu karere rukora, ukwiye kumenya ko IP yose Address (yaba iyo mu karere canke iya bose) ifatanye n'urutonde rw'ibibanza vy'imibare, bifise inomero kuva kuri `0` gushika kuri `65535`. Ivyo bibanza ntibiboneka: Ni ibibanza vy’injira canke vy’ugusohoka vy’ukuri bituma porogarama n’ibikorwa bishobora kuvugana ku rubuga rwose.


Igihe cose igikoresho kivugana biciye kuri Internet canke ku rubuga rwo mu karere, kibigira mu gufatanya IP Address n’inomero y’ibarabara. Ivyo bituma umuntu adashobora kumenya igikoresho co koherezako amakuru gusa, ariko kandi akamenya n’igikoresho canke igikorwa kidasanzwe kiri kuri ico gikoresho. Nk'akarorero:



- Icibutso `80` gikoreshwa mu gushika ku mapaji y'urubuga HTTP
- Icibutso `443` gikoreshwa mu gushika ku mapaji y'urubuga HTTPS (ihuriro ry'ibanga)
- Icibutso `22` gikoreshwa mu guhuza SSH
- Ivyambu `25`, `465` na `587` bikoreshwa mu kohereza ubutumwa kuri interineti (SMTP)
- Icibutso `110` gikoreshwa mu kugarura ubutumwa kuri interineti biciye ku nzira ya POP3
- Icibutso `143` gikoreshwa mu kugarura ubutumwa kuri interineti biciye ku masezerano ya IMAP
- Icibutso `21` gikoreshwa mu gutanga dosiye biciye ku masezerano ya FTP
- Icibutso `53` gikoreshwa ku bibazo vya DNS...


Ivyo bibanza bikoreshwa kandi mu mirongo nka Bitcoin canke Tor, aho ivyambu vyihariye bikoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe ku bijanye n’uguhanahana amakuru hagati y’abandi canke inzira y’imiduga:



- Icibutso `8333` gikoreshwa ku guhuza P2P kuri Bitcoin Mainnet
- 18333` ikoreshwa mu guhuza P2P kuri Bitcoin Testnet
- Icibutso `8332` gikoreshwa kuri Interface RPC y'urudodo rwa Bitcoin
- Icibutso `9050` gikoreshwa n'umugenzuzi wa Tor SOCKS5
- Icibutso `9150` gikoreshwa n'umucukumbuzi wa Tor


Mu yandi majambo, icigwati kimeze nk’umuryango wihariye. Iyo usuye urubuga, mudasobwa yawe irafungura icuma c'inkomoko maze ikarungika ubusabe kuri IP Address y'urubuga rwa kure, ikaba igenewe icuma `443` nimba ari ihuriro ry'ibanga. Serveri iri kure ica igarura inyishu biciye ku muhora umwe. Ku router, iki ciyumviro c’icuma ni ikintu gihambaye: Gikeneye kumenya igikoresho n’icuma co mu karere co guhinduramwo amakuru yinjira.


Ariko ubwo bushobozi bwo gufungura ivyambu na bwo burazana ingorane z’umutekano. Icibutso gisigaye kifunguye ataco kivuze gishobora kumenyekana n’ibikoresho vyo gupima urubuga maze kigakoreshwa n’abatera iyo gifitaniye isano n’igikorwa gishobora guhungabana canke gitunganijwe nabi. Ni nk'ugusiga urugi rwuguruye. Ariko ivyo tuzobivugako mu nyuma.


Gutahura rero ingene urubuga rwawe rwo muhira rukora ni ikintu gihambaye cane. Gutahura neza ivy’ishimikiro vya modem yawe, Wi-Fi, routers, IP addresses zo mu karere n’ama ports biragufasha kumenya ingorane zishobora gushika maze ugakora bihuye n’ivyo kugira ngo ukomeze umutekano wawe wa digitale.


Muri iki gice, twavuze ivyiyumviro bihambaye vyo gukorana n’abandi mu rugo. Mu kigabane gikurikira, turaza kuraba ingene wokingira ibikorwa remezo vya Internet vyo mu karere kawe mu bikorwa, n’ingene wotunganya neza Wi-Fi yawe kugira ngo umutekano wawe ube mwiza.


## Gukingira urubuga rwawe rwo muhira mu ntambwe nke gusa


<chapterId>d5577b2e-5247-4d10-8685-4906391e2cc1</chapterId>


Nk’uko twabibonye mu kigabane ca mbere, gukingira urubuga rwawe rwo muhira ni ikintu gihambaye cane kugira ngo ukinge ubuzima bwite bwawe, amakuru yawe bwite, no kugira ngo ushobore gukingira ubusegaba bwawe bw’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none.


Amaze gusubiramwo ivy’ishimikiro vy’ivyiyumviro, iki gice kizokuyobora mu ntambwe zitomoye, zikora kandi zikora neza zo kwongereza umutekano w’urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere.


*Ibuka: Amakuru atangwa ngaha ni rusangi, kuko Plan ₿ Network igenewe abantu bo kw’isi yose. Bivanye n’ivyo mu karere iwanyu be n’ivyo ISP yawe ikora, hari ingendo nziza zimwezimwe zishobora kutavugwa ngaha, canke zishobora gukoreshwa mu buryo butandukanye.*


### Guhitamwo no gucungera ibikoresho vyawe vy'urubuga


Umutekano w’urubuga rwawe rwo muhira utangura n’uguhitamwo neza ibikoresho: router, canke mu bihe bimwe bimwe router ya modem. Ico gikoresho kiratanga uruja n’uruza hagati y’urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere na Internet. Ni co gituma gifise uruhara runini mu kurinda amakuru yawe.


Ni vyiza guhitamwo ibikoresho vya none, bibungabungwa n'uwabikoze, kandi bihuye n'ingingo ngenderwako z'umutekano ziherutse gushirwaho. Uyu musi (Kamena 2025), birakenewe ko umuntu ahitamwo igikoresho gihuye n’umurongo w’ugushiramwo amakuru WPA3 (*Wi-Fi Protected Access 3*), ukaba ushobora gukurikira WPA2 kandi ugakosora amakosa menshi. Cane cane, WPA3 iratuma umuntu ashobora guhangana n’ibitero vy’inguvu z’ubukazi ku majambo y’ibanga ya Wi-Fi, kandi igatuma habaho ukwitandukanya neza hagati y’abaguzi b’urubuga.


Router ihuye na Wi-Fi 6, Wi-Fi 6E canke Wi-Fi 7 izoguha umuvuduko mwiza kandi, ikiruta vyose, ubufasha bw’akavukire bw’ubuhinga bwa none bwo gucungera umutekano. Ku rundi ruhande, ibikoresho vya kera cane, canecane ivyo bitagishobora guhindurwa, vyoshobora kuba birimwo utunenge tuzwi kandi tutarakosorwa. Bigereranya rero ingorane ku rubuga rwawe rwose, naho woba ubitunganije neza. Ugereranije n’amatelefone ngendanwa canke orodinateri, ama router ni ibikoresho dukunda kubika imyaka myinshi. Ariko rero, vyoshobora kuba vyiza ko ubisubirira ubudasiba, kugira ngo wungukire ku citegererezo gishasha kandi gitekanye.


Rero urabe ko uhindura mu buryo bubereye porogarama ya router yawe. Ivyo bishasha bikosora ubugoyagoye, vyongerako ibintu bishasha kandi bikongera ugushikama kwa sisitemu muri rusangi. Hari abahinguzi batanga ivyagezwe vyihuta, ariko mu bihe bimwebimwe uzokenera kuvyisuzuma n’amaboko biciye ku gikoresho co gutwara Interface ca router yawe. Nk’uko biri kuri telefone yawe, mudasobwa, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha na porogarama, birahambaye ko uhora uhindura router yawe. Ushobora guhindura iki gice c’ibikorwa vyawe vy’indwi - Nk’akarorero, buri musi w’Imana - mu gukora urutonde rw’ibintu vyose ukeneye kugenzura no kuguma ubimenya.


Niba router yawe itagitunganijwe ariko ikaba ikora neza uhereye ku bijanye n’ibikoresho, urashobora gushiramwo ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bufunguye, nka:



- OpenWrt, ni urudandazwa rwa Linux rwihariye mu bijanye n'ama router, rutanga uburyo bwinshi bwo guhindura ibintu no guhindura ibintu bihoraho
- pfSense na OPNsense, ni uburyo bubiri bushingiye kuri FreeBSD (bumeze nka Unix) bw'ibihome vy'umuriro vya x86 n'ibikoresho vyo gukoresha


![Image](assets/fr/196.webp)



https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/opnsense-90c2785d-a0d7-4981-be8d-d290bbeb8263

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/operating-system/pfsense-24eea96a-2fdc-42a6-a77b-89bc29149864

Izo nzira zituma umuntu ashobora kugenzura neza amategeko agenga uruhome rw’umuriro, amahuzu asohoka n’ayinjira, gucapura urubuga (VLANs) n’ugucungera DNS, ariko zigenewe cane abakoresha bateye imbere.


**Mu ncamake, ndabagira inama**:



- Hitamwo umurongo uheruka
- Gumana sisitemu yawe ku gihe
- Niwiyumvire ubundi buryo bwo gukoresha porogarama nimba bikenewe


### Guhindura ukwinjira mburabuzi n'amajambobanga


Imwe mu makosa asanzwe (kandi ateye akaga) ni ukuguma ufise amakuru y’ibanga yatanzwe n’uwakoze router, canke gukoresha ijambobanga ry’intege nke.


Mu mateka, ivyemezo vya router vyari bifise umutekano muke cane kandi kenshi vyari bisa ku bakoresha bose, nk'uwuzwi cane `admin/admin`. Ivyo vyemezo vy’ishimikiro vyari vyerekanwa na bose, vyanditswe mu bitabu vy’abakoresha kandi vyanditswe cane mu bitabo vy’amakuru vyakoreshwa n’abatera. Muri ivyo, umuntu wese abona ko router yawe iriho yoshobora kugerageza kwinjira ata wemerewe gusa mu kugerageza izo nzira zizwi.


Muri iki gihe, benshi mu bahinga baraha ijambo banga ry’umwihariko kandi rikomeye kuri router yose. Ariko rero, no muri ivyo, ndabahimiriza guhindura ivyemezo vy’imbere. Ivyo bigabanya ingorane z’uruzitiro rwa Supply, kandi bikabuza ijambobanga ry’intango (rimwe na rimwe ryacapwe ku rupapuro rwa router) guhungabanya umutekano wawe.


Ni ngombwa rero ko uhindura ibimenyetso vyawe ubwo nyene umaze gushiramwo router yawe:



- Izina ry'ukoresha (niba ririho) ry'ubuyobozi Interface
- Kandi ikiruta vyose, ijambobanga ry’ubuyobozi, ririnda gushika ku mirongo yose y’urubuga, hamwe n’ijambobanga rya Wi-Fi .


Iryo jambobanga ritegerezwa kuba rirerire (inyuguti 40), rigoye (imibare, inyuguti nto, inyuguti nini n’ibimenyetso), ridasanzwe (ritazosubira gukoreshwa ahandi), kandi ridasanzwe. Biragaragara ko nsaba gukoresha umucungerezi w’ijambobanga kuri generate no kubika neza ivyo bimenyetso.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/bitwarden-0532f569-fb00-4fad-acba-2fcb1bf05de9

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/authentication/keepass-f8073bb7-5b4a-4664-9246-228e307be246

Imburi: ntuvange ijambobanga ry’uburongozi bwa router (rikingira ukuntu umuntu ashobora gushika ku ntunganyo zayo) n’ijambobanga rya Wi-Fi (rituma ushobora kwifatanya n’urubuga rwa wireless). Izo ni Elements zibiri zitandukanye, kandi zompi zikeneye guhindurwa.


Ubwa nyuma, ama routeurs amwe amwe yo muri iki gihe arafise uburyo bubiri bwo gucunga: Urubuga rwo mu karere Interface (rushobora gushikwako biciye ku Address nka `192.168.1.1`) n’igicu Interface (bishoboza gucungera kure biciye kuri Internet). Nimba iyo ya nyuma ikoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe, ndaguhanura ko woyizimya nimba utariko urayikoresha, canke ukomeze umutekano wayo ukoresheje ijambobanga rikomeye kandi bishoboka ko n’ukwemeza ko umuntu ari uwundi (2FA) nimba biriho.


### Gutunganya umurongo w'umutekano


Router ni umutima w’urubuga rwawe rwo muhira. Ivyo ikora birafise uruhara runini mu gucungera umutekano w’ibikoresho vyose bihuye. Ikibabaje ni uko vyinshi mu bikorwa bikoreshwa kuri ivyo bikoresho bishobora gutuma urubuga rwawe ruterwa n’abantu bo hanze ataco bizi. Ni co gituma bihambaye gukora isuzuma ryuzuye ry’amahitamwo yakoreshejwe, no guhagarika ayo adakenewe cane ku ntumbero zawe.


Hari ibiranga bikwiye kwirindwa canke gukurwaho mu buryo butegekanijwe:



- UPnP (*Igikoresho cose co gushiramwo n'ugukina*)**:


Ivyo bituma ibikoresho biri ku rubuga rwawe bisaba router gufungura ports ubwavyo. Naho ivyo vyorosha gukoresha ibintu bimwebimwe (imikino yo kuri Internet, amakamera ahuye, n’ibindi), birafungura kandi urugi rw’ibikoresho bibi bishobora guhindura imiterere y’urubuga ata ruhusha rwawe. UPnP ni kimwe mu bituma ibikorwa vyo mu mutima bishikirizwa hanze ataco bigamije.



- WPS (*Imiterere irindwa na Wi-Fi*)**:


Mu ntango, iyo nzira yari igenewe kworohereza abantu gufatanya ibikoresho na Wi-Fi ata jambo banga winjije, ikaba ishingiye kuri kode ya PIN akenshi igoyagoya kandi iterwa bitagoranye n’inguvu z’agahomerabunwa. Ndaguhanura ngo uyizimye.



- Ugushikira kure (*Uburongozi bwa kure*)**:


Hariho ama routeurs ashobora kuguha uburenganzira bwo kwifatanya n’ubuyobozi bwabo Interface uri hanze, biciye kuri Internet. Ivyo bituma router yawe igira ubushobozi bwo gutera. Izimye burundu, kiretse iyo ufise ivyipfuzo vyihariye vyo gucungera kure. Naho ari ukwo, wama ukoresha VPN.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/tailscale-9acbd7de-04d9-40f6-ab80-35f0dfedb632


- Amasezerano ya kera canke adatekanye**:


Guhagarika ibikorwa vyose vy'ubuyobozi bikoresha amasezerano y'inyandiko rusangi nka Telnet, FTP, HTTP idashizwemwo amakuru canke SMBv1. Aya masezerano ntatuma amakuru ahindurwa aba ibanga canke ubutungane, kandi akenshi araterwa n’ibintu bibi. Niba ukeneye gushika ku nzira yo mu karere canke kure, koresha gusa amahuzu biciye kuri HTTPS (Interface yashizwemwo), SSH canke SFTP, nk’uko bikwiye.



- WAN/ICMP**:


Hariho ama router yishura ku vyo ICMP isaba bivuye hanze (itegeko rya `ping`). Ivyo bituma uwugutera ashobora kugenzura ko urubuga rwawe rukora kandi ko rushobora gushikirwa. Niba udakeneye, zimya iyo nyishu mu ruhome rw’umuriro rwa router.


Ubwa nyuma, wibuke guhagarika uburenganzira bwo gukoresha uburongozi bwa router Interface ku bikoresho vyizigirwa gusa, ugahagarika uburenganzira bwo gukoresha aderesi IP zimwe zimwe, nimba Interface ibirekura. Hariho porogaramu zimwe zimwe, nka OpenWrt, zitanga ubugenzuzi bwiza cane kuri ivyo bipimo.


### Gukomeza umutekano w'urubuga rwa Wi-Fi


Akenshi urubuga rwa Wi-Fi ni rwo rukunda kwinjiramwo kugira ngo umuntu yinjire mu bidukikije vyo mu rugo. Ntiboneka n’amaso ariko ushobora kuyironka uri hanze y’inkuta z’inzu yawe, ni ikintu coroshe umuntu wese ari mu nzira ishobora gushikako.


Intambwe ya mbere ihambaye ni uguhitamwo uburyo bwiza bwo gushiramwo amakuru. Igihe cose ukoreshe "*WPA3-Personal*", urugero rwa nyuma kandi rutekanye. Ntibirinda gusa amakuru ahindurwa, ariko kandi irabuza ibitero bimwebimwe bizwi.


Izina ry'urubuga rwawe rwa Wi-Fi, ryitwa "SSID" (*Indangamuntu y'Ishirahamwe ry'Ibikorwa*), rikwiye kuguma ritagira aho ribogamiye. Irinde gushiramwo izina ryawe, Address canke ikimenyetso ca router. Izina nka `MaisonDupont_WiFi6` rirasanzwe ritanga amakuru menshi cane ku muntu ashobora gutera. Hitamwo izina rusangi, ritagira insobanuro yihariye. Ivyo bigabanya amakuru aboneka kugira ngo umuntu akurikirane canke akoreshe abantu.


Ikindi kintu ciza ni ugukora urubuga rw’abashitsi rutandukanye n’urubuga rwawe nyamukuru. Uwo muhora w’uruja n’uruza, akenshi utangwa mu buryo bw’akavukire ku bikoresho vy’ubuhinga bwa none, uragufasha guha abashitsi bawe uruja n’uruza rwa Internet ataco bashobora gukoresha ku bindi bikoresho vyawe (ordinateri, amacapiro, NAS, n’ibindi). Bisigura kandi ko udategerezwa kubaha ijambo banga ry’urubuga rwawe nyamukuru. Kugira ngo ugende kure, nushireho uburyo bwo kwitandukanya n’abaguzi kuri uru rubuga rw’abashitsi: Ivyo bizotuma kandi abashitsi badashobora kuvugana, bigabanye n’ingorane zijanye n’ibikoresho bishobora gukoreshwa nabi.


Ubwa nyuma, nuhindure ubushobozi bwo gutanga amakuru bw’aho ukoresha Wi-Fi. Kubera ko ari vyo, ama router menshi atanga ikimenyetso gikomeye cane, rimwe na rimwe kikaba kigaragara kure cane y’inkuta zawe. Ivyo bituma urushirizaho gushikirwa n’ibintu. Mu mirongo iteye imbere ya router yawe, nugabanye ubushobozi bwo gutanga amakuru ku rugero rutoyi rukenewe kugira ngo upfuke inzu yawe. Nimba router yawe ibirekura, urashobora kandi guhindura Wi-Fi yica iyo udakoresha.


### Ugucapura urubuga


Imwe mu nzira nziza zo gukomeza umutekano w’urubuga rwo mu rugo ni ugucapura. Ivyo birimwo gucapura urubuga rw'aho hantu mu mirongo myinshi yigenga yitwa "VLANs" (*Virtual Local Area Networks*). Izo VLAN zituma bishoboka gutandukanya ubwoko butandukanye bw’ibikoresho canke ikoreshwa, naho nyene zikoresha ibikoresho bimwe (router, cabling, terminal ya Wi-Fi, n’ibindi).


VLAN yose ikora nk’urubuga rutoyi, rwigenga rufise amategeko yarwo yo guhanahana amakuru. Ivyiyumviro hagati ya VLANs birabujijwe ku buryo busanzwe canke bikagenzurwa cane. Ivyo birabuza nk’akarorero televiziyo ihuye n’ibindi bihuye n’ibintu bitari vyo gushika kuri mudasobwa yawe bwite canke kuri NAS. Ubwo buryo bushingiye ku ngingo ngenderwako 2 z’ishimikiro z’umutekano wo kuri internet twamaze kwiga mu bice vyabanje: Gucapura n’agateka gatoyi.


![Image](assets/fr/197.webp)


Mu majambo nyayo, ng’izi ingero zimwe zimwe z’ugucapura woshobora gukora:



- VLAN y’umuntu ku giti ciwe: Ku bikoresho vyawe wizigira nka mudasobwa, amatelefone ngendanwa canke ama server y’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Ico ni co gice nyamukuru aho amakuru yawe y’agaciro agendagenda.



- IoT VLAN: Ku bintu bihuye (amatara, amajwi, ama kamera, amateleviziyo y’ubwenge, n’ibindi). Ivyo bikoresho kenshi ntibitekanye, ntibijanye n'igihe, kandi ni vyo bikunda guterwa. Kuzitandukanya biragabanya cane ingorane zo kuzitera nk’inzira yo kwinjira mu rubuga rwawe.



- VLAN y’umushyitsi: Igenewe abagenzi bawe canke umuryango wawe iyo baje kubana nawe. Itanga uburyo bwo gukoresha Internet, ariko nta buryo bwo gukoresha ibikoresho vyawe vy’ibanga.


Ubwa nyuma, ubu buryo buratanga kandi inyungu mu bijanye n’ugukora n’ugucungera: Bugufasha gushiramwo imbere ubwoko bumwebumwe bw’uruja n’uruza, gukoresha amategeko yihariye y’umutekano bivanye n’ivyo VLAN (firewall, rate limiting, DNS filtering, n’ibindi), no kugenzura neza inyifato idasanzwe y’urubuga. Ni akamenyero ndabashimira cane.


### Ubuyobozi bwa DNS buteye imbere


DNS (*Izina ry'Ikibanza*) ni igikorwa ca Internet gihindura amaderesi y'urubuga atahurwa n'abantu (nk'akarorero `planb.network`) mu maderesi ya IP atahurwa n'imashini. Iyo igikoresho kiri ku rubuga rwawe gishaka gusura urubuga, kirabaza umukozi wa DNS kugira ngo kironke Address y’uwo mukozi co guhamagara. Kubera ko ari vyo, ivyo bibazo vya DNS akenshi birungikwa mu nyandiko zitomoye (zitagiramwo amakuru) kuri ISP yawe, bikayishoboza (canke uwundi muntu nka leta) kubona imbuga zose usura, naho ibirimwo vyoba vyashizwemwo amakuru biciye ku HTTPS.


Kugira ngo wongere ubuzima bwite bwawe bwo gusura no kubuza ibintu bimwebimwe udashaka kuva ku muzi, urashobora gufata ububasha ku bijanye n’ugutorera umuti DNS mu rubuga rwawe rwo muhira. Tangira mu gusubirira ama serveri ya DNS yatanzwe n'ubundi buryo bwo gukingira ubuzima bwite nk'ubundi :



- [Quad9](https://quad9.net/): Harimwo urutonde rwo kubuza imbuga mbi kandi ntizigama amazina y'igihe kirekire



- [DNS y'igicu](https://www.cloudflare.com/ibikorwa-vy'ibikorwa/ibicuruzwa/dns/): Yihuta kandi yiyemeje gukurikiza ingingo ngenderwako zikomeye zo kudakora



- [NextDNS](https://nextdns.io/): Ishobora guhindurwa cane, ifise ubuhinga bwo kuyungurura n'imibare



- [AdGuard DNS](https://adguard-dns.io/): Biroroshe gutunganya, n'amahitamwo yo guhagarika amatangazo n'ugukurikirana


![Image](assets/fr/199.webp)


Inyuma y’aho, fungura porotokole yo gupfuka ibibazo vya DNS kugira ngo ibibazo vya DNS ntibifatwe canke ngo bikurikiranwe. Hariho amategeko 2 nyamukuru yo gukora ivyo:



- DoH (*DNS kuri HTTPS*)**: Ishiramwo ibisabwa vya DNS mu masezerano ya HTTPS, bikaba bituma bidashobora gutandukanywa n'uruja n'uruza rw'urubuga rwashizwemwo amakuru



- DoT (*DNS kuri TLS*)**: Ikora umurongo wihariye ushizwemwo amakuru hagati y'igikoresho cawe na serveri ya DNS



- DoQ (*DNS kuri QUIC*)**: Itwara ibisabwa vya DNS biciye ku nzira ya QUIC ishingiye kuri UDP


Mu majambo ngirakamaro, ugushiramwo amakuru ya DNS n’uguhindura server bishobora gushirwa mu ngiro ku nzego zitandukanye:



- Ku rugero rw’ibikorwa: Ibikoresho bimwe bimwe vya porogarama, nk’umucukumbuzi wa Firefox, biguha uburenganzira bwo gutunganya amasezerano y’ugushiramwo amakuru ya DNS, nka DoH, ataco uhinduye. Ariko rero, uwo muti ukingira gusa ivyo usaba biciye kuri iyo porogarama, nturinda ibindi bice vya mudasobwa yawe.


![Image](assets/fr/198.webp)


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/firefox-11814cec-3415-4ed9-a06e-f6fda5c9510f

- Ku rugero rwa sisitemu ikoreshwa: OS zimwe zimwe zishiramwo ubufasha bwa DNS (DoT canke DoH), bucungera ibisabwa vyose vya DNS bica mu rutonde rw’urubuga rwa sisitemu. Ariko rero, ivyo ntibishobora gukingira orodinateri yose canke telefone yose: Amaporogarama arashobora guca muri iyo nzira iyo atunganijwe gukoresha uburyo butandukanye bwo gutorera umuti canke uburyo butandukanye bwo gutorera umuti DNS.



- Ku rugero rw’urubuga: Ugushiramwo amakuru ya DNS gushobora gukoreshwa ku rubuga rwose rwo mu karere biciye ku gutunganya urubuga. Na none, router itunganijwe kuri DoH/DoT ibona gusa uruja n’uruza rwoherezwa kuri yo vy’ukuri. Rero umucukumbuzi yatunganijwe kugira ngo akoreshe umucukumbuzi wo kure arahunga ata guca ku ruhande iyo nzira. Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo bihengeri, ukeneye guhagarika port 53 mu nyandiko zitomoye no kubuza aho DoH/DoT ija ata wemerewe biciye ku ruhome rw’umuriro rwa router.


Kandi, ama routeurs ya modem atangwa na ISP ntabwo yama ashigikira ivyo bintu. Iyo router ifise aho igarukira, hariho uburyo bwinshi bwo kuyikoresha. Ushobora gushiramwo umukiriya wa DNS yashizwemwo amakuru n’amaboko kuri buri gikoresho, ukongerako umurongo w’umuntu ku giti ciwe inyuma y’uwa ISP (ushobora gukorana n’ugushiramwo amakuru ya DNS) canke ugashiraho umukozi wa DNS wo mu karere (nk’akarorero, kuri Raspberry Pi) ashinzwe gushiramwo amakuru no guhindura ibisabwa vya DNS ku resol itekanye.



Kugira ngo ibintu bigende imbere, urashobora kandi gushinga umuti wo kuyungurura DNS yo mu karere nka Pi-hole canke AdGuard Home.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/pi-hole-46a735c5-8af3-4cc3-a2c2-1d4f6a7dc428

Ivyo bikoresho bikora nk’agace gatoyi ka DNS kari mu rubuga rwawe, bikabuza ibisabwa ku mbuga zizwi ko zakira amatangazo, abakurikirana umucukumbuzi, ubuhendanyi canke imbuga mbi. Ivyo bikoresho kandi biragufasha kwikorera urutonde rwawe rwo kubuza canke guhindura ukuyungurura bivanye n’ibikoresho bihuye.


![Image](assets/fr/200.webp)


### Ukwinjira kure biciye kuri VPN


Mu bihe bimwe bimwe, birakenewe ko ushobora gushika ku rubuga rwawe rwo muhira igihe uriko uragenda: Raba amadosiye kuri NAS, ukoreshe node ya Bitcoin na Lightning, ushikire server yikorera, canke urongore urubuga rwawe. Ariko rero, iyo nzira yo guhuza kure itegerezwa kuba itekanye.


Impanuro ya mbere ni ukutazokwigera ufungura port kuri router yawe kugira ngo ushikire igikoresho (nk’akarorero biciye kuri RDP, SSH canke FTP), kuko ivyo bica bigaragaza iyo serivisi kuri Internet yose, ivyo bikaba ari ubugoyagoye. Ibitero vy’ubuhinga bwa none bitera ivyambu vyuguruye ni vyinshi.


Umuti ndababwira ni ugukoresha VPN (*Virtual Private Network*), ni ukuvuga umurongo w’amazi hagati y’igikoresho cawe co kure (mudasobwa, telefone ngendanwa, n’ibindi) n’urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere. Iyo umaze kwifatanya na VPN, urashobora gushika ku bintu vyo mu nzu yawe nk’aho woba uri ng’aho ku mubiri, kandi mu buryo butekanye.


Inyishu zibiri nyamukuru ku bakiriya b’abikorera ku giti cabo ni:



- WireGuard: Ivya none, vyihuta kandi biremerera
- OpenVPN: Ya kera, ariko irakuze cane kandi ishobora gutunganirizwa


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/wireguard-81fdd0db-b2bd-4a6c-a082-2de269e26779

Aha niho hari inyigisho yuzuye kuri Tailscale, umuti woroshe gutunganya VPN ukoresha WireGuard:


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/tailscale-9acbd7de-04d9-40f6-ab80-35f0dfedb632

Ushobora kwakira iyo VPN ataco uhinduye kuri router ihuye, kuri mudasobwa ntoyi (nk’iya Raspberry Pi) canke kuri server yihariye muhira. Ushobora kandi kuyishiramwo nk’umukiriya ataco uhinduye ku gikoresho ico ari co cose.


Ariko VPN si iyo gukoresha kure gusa. Ushobora kandi gukoresha umukiriya wa VPN wa kera ku bikoresho vyawe kugira ngo ushiremwo amakuru yawe yose asohoka, mbere n’igihe uri kure y’i muhira (Wi-Fi ya bose, hoteli, kaminuza, n’ibindi). Muri ivyo, igikoresho cawe gifatanya na server ya VPN y’uwundi muntu (y’ubudandaji canke iyo kwikorera), iyo serveri igaca irungika amakuru yawe kuri Internet. Ivyo bihisha IP yawe nyayo Address kuri ISP, bikarinda amakuru yawe ubutasi bwo mu karere kandi bikarinda uburyo bumwe bumwe bwo gucengera.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/mullvad-968ec5f5-b3f0-4d23-a9e0-c07a3e85aaa8

https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/ivpn-5a0cd5df-29f1-4382-a817-975a96646e68

Ubwa nyuma, birashoboka kandi gushinga VPN ataco uhinduye kuri router yawe, bikagufasha kurinda ibikoresho vyose vyo mu nzu yawe ataco ukeneye gushiramwo umu client wa VPN kuri kimwe cose muri vyo.


### Gukurikirana no kumenya


Igihe urubuga rwawe rwatunganijwe neza kandi rwaciwemwo ibice, birahambaye ko urenga umutekano udakora. Gukurikirana neza urubuga rwawe rwo mu karere birashobora kumenya inyifato idasanzwe, amahuzu atemerewe canke ibimenyetso vy’ukwinjira. Intumbero ni ukumenya ingorane hakiri kare, imbere y’uko zitera ingorane.


Intambwe ya mbere ni ugushira hamwe ibitabo vy’umutekano. Igikoresho cose gifatanye n’urubuga kiratanga amakuru arimwo amakuru yerekeye amahuza, amakosa canke igikorwa giteye amakenga. Aho kurondera ivyo bitabo umwumwe wese, ndabagira inama yo kubirungika kuri server ishobora kubishira mu migwi, kubitoranya no kubisuzuma. Inyishu nka Graylog canke Elastic Stack (ELK) zigufasha gukoranya izo nyandiko mu gishushanyo Interface aho ushobora kurondera ibintu vyihariye, gukora imburi canke kubona ibikorwa vy’urubuga.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/graylog-3a7f0377-1d95-4446-abe0-d7866a551455

Inyuma, kora ama scanners active y'urubuga rwawe, nk'akarorero na Nmap. Ivyo bizokuronsa inyishu y’ibikoresho vyose biri ku rubuga rwawe, n’ibibanza vyafunguye. Iyo ubonye igikoresho kitazwi canke igikorwa kidasanzwe, ivyo vyoshobora kuba ikimenyetso c’igitero.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/communication/nmap-862300d7-6dfb-4660-970d-f56a9f58f60d

Kugira ngo ugende mbere n’imbere, urashobora gushiramwo IDS (*Sisteme yo kumenya abaje kwinjira mu nzu*), canke mbere IPS (*Sisteme yo gukingira abaje mu nzu*). Ivyo bikoresho, nka Suricata canke Snort, bigenzura uruja n’uruza rw’urubuga mu gihe nyaco kandi bikamenya imikono y’ibitero bizwi (ugupima port, injections, amahuzu akekwa, n’ibindi). IDS iragabisha, mu gihe IPS ishobora kwibuza ibikorwa bimwebimwe.


Ubwa nyuma, gukurikirana ukuntu bandwidth ikoreshwa na vyo nyene ni ikimenyetso ciza c’ibikorwa bidasanzwe. Iyo igikoresho gifunguye amakuru menshi mu buryo butunguranye ata mvo igaragara, ivyo vyoshobora kwerekana ko umuntu yayakuye ata wemerewe, ko amakuru yasohotse canke mbere ko igikoresho coshobora guhungabanywa. Ibikoresho nka ntopng canke vnStat bigufasha kubona ivyinjira n'ibisohoka ku gikoresho.


https://planb.network/tutorials/computer-security/data/ntopng-77435bd3-674a-4f35-81d9-0a5325bbdcbd

### Gusubiza inyuma no kwihangana


Naho woba ufise urubuga rutekanye neza, ukunanirwa kw’ibikoresho, amakosa yo gutunganya canke ibintu bitateguwe (ugucika kw’amashanyarazi, ugucika kw’amashanyarazi, ukunanirwa kwa disiki ya Hard, n’ibindi) birashobora gutuma amakuru atakaza canke ibikorwa vyawe bihagarara. Kugira ngo ushobore gukomeza ibidukikije vyawe vya digitale no kwirinda gutangura uhereye ku ntango iyo habaye ingorane, birahambaye ko ushira mu ngiro ubuhinga bwo gusubiza inyuma no kwihangana.


Tangana n’ugukora backup y’ibikoresho vyawe vy’urubuga, cane cane router. Izo dosiye z'imiterere zishobora gurungikwa hanze biciye ku buyobozi Interface. Kubika kopi biratuma ushobora gusubizaho ningoga ubuhinga bukora neza iyo igikoresho cosubirwamwo canke kigasubirwamwo. Ndabagira inama kandi yo gupfuka iyi nkuru.


Ubwa nyuma, kugira ngo urusobe rwawe rushobore guhangana n’amashanyarazi iyo umuriro wacitse, shiramwo UPS. Ico gikoresho kiratanga ubushobozi bwo gusubiza inyuma iminota mikeyi iyo umuriro wacitse, kikagufasha kubandanya ukoresha Internet canke ukamenya neza ko ibikoresho bihambaye (NAS, router, Wi-Fi access point, n’ibindi) bifunga neza. Hari n’ibikoresho bimwebimwe birashobora kohereza itegeko ryo guhagarika ubwavyo ku bikoresho bihuye iyo bibonye ko bateri iri hasi.


Niwakurikiza izi ntambwe nke, uzoba wubaka urubuga rukomeye kandi rutekanye rwubaha ubuzima bwite bwawe.
